shes pa 'dug de na yod pa rnams jo bo dang kha che paN chen nas brgyud par 'dug go/ // ! gnyis pa bod du bstan pa ji ltar byung ba'i tshul la/ snga dar dang phyi dar ba'i
tshul gnyis kyi dang po ni/ slob dpon shes rab go chas skya seng bu lnga dang / dgra ngan dpung tshogs yan lag bcu gnyis 'thabs pa'i tshe/ rgyal po ru pa ti zhes pa dmag
stong phrag gcig dang bcas pa bud med kyi chas su zhugs te ri gangs can gyi dbus su bros pa las mched pa bod do zer te/ 'khrug pa de ni rtsod pa'i dus thog mar byung
ba'i tshe yin la/ rdzogs ldan gyi dus gsungs pa'i 'khor lo sdom pa'i rgyud du/ bod ces yul nyi shu rtsa bzhi'i ya bar bgrangs pas des gnod/ des na da lta bod lung zhes grags
pa 'di'i ming las spyi la de skad du grags pa ste/ rdo rje mkha' 'gro'i rgyud las/ bod yul du ni lhan skyes te/ /zhi zhing gsal ba'i gzugs can ma/ /chu srin rgyal mtshan
lag na thogs/ /brag gi khyim la brten te gnas/ /rang byung gi ni skyes gnas can/ /zhes byung zhing / 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis ral gcig ma'i sgrub thabs spyan drangs pa'ang
'di las yin pa dang / 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud kyi srong btsan sgam po lung bstan du/ lha ldan yul zhes bya ba yi/ /gangs can ri yi nang gnas pa'i/ /zhes pa'i lha ldan
gyi gangs can yang yul de'i ming gi rnam grangs yin la/ de la de hi ma la ya zhes 'byung bas so/ /don da lta tsa ri trar grags pa 'di yin no/ /bod spyi 'di dang po mi ma
yin rnams kyis bzung bas ming yang mi 'dra ste/ sngon bdud kyis bzung bas de'i tshe bdud yul kha rag mgo

mgo dgu zhes thogs skad pa sogs/ de dag la rgyal phran sil ma bcu gnyis su grags te rim par 'ongs pa de dag thams cad ni mi ma yin 'ba' zhig go /'jam dpal rtsa rgyud du/ nga
ni 'das nas lo brgya na/ /kha ba can du mtsho bri nas/ /sA la'i nags ni 'byung bar 'gyur/ /zhes lung bstan pa bzhin/ ston pa 'das nas lo brgya na kha ba can sngon mtshor
yod pa bskams pa'i 'go zug cing sA la'i nags tshal chags par gsungs pa dang / bod rnams sngon yul 'di thams cad la shugs pa'i nags yod ces gleng ba dang mthun no/ /de ltar
yul chags nas mi ring ba na 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dang / jo mo sgrol ma'i sprul pa spre'u dang brag srin las thog mar sprel phrug de dag rim gyis mir song ba yin
la/ de dag gi grong chags pa'i snga ma ni kong yul spre sna/ mi yul gyi lding du grags pa de yin la/ der li tsa byi'i rigs kyi bu zhig 'khyar ba lha ri gyang thor babs pa
de dag gi rje bor bsten pa ni rje la snga ba gnya' khri btsan po yin no/ /de nas rgyal rabs nyi shu rtsa drug na lha tho tho ri gnyan btsan byon/ yum bu bla sgang btab pas
mkhar la snga ba yin/ der nam mkha' nas rin po che'i sgrom bu zhig babs pa kha phye bar/ za ma tog bkod pa'i mdo/ spang kong phyag rgya pa/ gser gyi mchod rten gcig tsinta
ma Ni'i gzungs rnams thon/ de'i rmi lam na mi rabs lnga na 'di shes pa 'byung zhes lung bstan/ 'on kyang de dus ci yin ngo ma shes kyang ya mtshan du gzung nas/ ming
gnyan po gsang bar btags te mchod pas rgyal po lo brgya nyi shu thub/ de nas mi rabs bzhi pa gnam ri srong btsan dang / btsun mo tshe spong bza' 'am/ 'bri bza' thod dkar
du grags pa'i sras su 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs rgyal bu mgo bcu gcig yod pa zhig skyes te/ mtshan khri lde srong btsan du grags so/ /dbu lhag ma dar le brgan gyis dkris/
lo bcu gsum na rgyal sar byon/ des mtha'i rgyal phran thams cad dbang du bsdus/ blon po mgar zhes pa phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa des/ bal po'i rgyal po 'od zer go cha'i
sras mo sgrol ma khro gnyer can gyi sprul pa dang / rgya nag nas sgrol ma sngon mo'i sprul pa lha cig kong jo bsus/ jo bo shAkya rnam gnyis sogs

kyi sku rten byin rlabs can mang po spyan drangs/ sku rgyu spungs pa la rang byon bcu gcig zhal byon/ de'i tshe bod la yi ge med pas thon mi a nu'i bu 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul
pa sambho Ta kha cher yi ge slob tu btang / des slob dpon lha rig pa'i sengga zhes bya ba las sgra legs par bslabs/ bod du log nas bod kyi skad dang bstun nas gsal byed
sum cu/ dbyangs gug kyed bzhir bsdus/ dbyibs kha che'i yi ge dang bstun nas lha sa'i sku mkhar ma rur bcos/ sgra'i bstan bcos brgyad mdzad/ rgyal pos kyang yi ge dang sgra
legs par slob pa'i tshul bstan/ rgyal pos mi dge ba bcu bgags shing / dge ba bcu spyod pa'i khrims bcas pa dam pas rgyal po'i mtshan srong btsan sgam por grags zer/ btsun
mo gnyis kyis gtsug lag khang 'gran nas rtsig par chas pa la/ khri btsun gyi gtsug lag khang thog mar byed pa'i sa 'o thang gi mtsho la lung bstan pas rtsig ma thub/
rgyal po la zhus pas/ bod spyi srin mo gan kyal du sgyel ba 'dra ba'i 'di snying ka yin/ der lha khang 'debs pa la sa'i dpyad gzhan rnams mnan dgos gsungs nas/ dpung pa g.yas
la ska tshal g.yon la khra 'brug rkang pa g.yas la gtsang 'gram/ g.yon la grom pa rgyang / ru bzhi'i gtsug lag khang zer/ gru mo g.yas la kong po bu chu/ g.yon la lho
brag mkho mthing / pus mo g.yas la ska brag g.yon la pra dum rtse re/ mtha' 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang zer/ lag mthil g.yas la byang tshal gyi rlung gnon/ g.yon la khams
kyi glong thang sgron ma/ rkang mthil g.yas la mang yul byams sprin/ g.yon la mon bum thang / gzhan yang sa non gyi lha khang / mchod rten brgya rtsa brgyad sprul pa bkye
nas bzhengs/ gdod 'o thang gi mtsho la rdo'i khar brtsigs shing gis phub/ klu'i 'dag pas zhal zhal byas/ ras sa bskyal de brdal ba la lha khang brtsigs te/ bzo khyad las
'phrul lta bur snang bas ra sa 'phrul snang zhes grags/ kong jos ra mo che bzhengs/ rgya gar gyi slob dpon ku sa ra/ bram ze shang ka ra/ bal po shrI la manydzyu/ rgya nag
gi slob dpon mahA de wa tsho spyan drangs/ lo tsA ba thon mi/ de'i slob bu dharmA ko sha sogs kyis byas/ gsung rab kyi skad bcos/ mdo sde za ma tog bkod pa sogs bsgyur/
rgyal pos gdam ngag gnang nas yer par sgom grwa btsugs te rab byung med/ rgyal pos lo drug cu rtsa dgu rgyal srid

bzung ste brgyad cu rtsa gnyis la yab yum gsum rang byon 'phags pa'i thugs kar thim/ de dus kong jo'i zhal chems la/ lha shAkya mu ne ra mo che nas gdan drongs la 'phrul snang
gi blo bur du sbos la zhal zhal gyis/ logs dang steng du 'jam dbyangs kyi sku re bris shig gsungs/ de ltar byas pas rgya nag gi dmag sleb dus rig kyang 'jam dbyangs kyi
sku bshig ma phod/ de nas rgyal rabs lnga pa la khri lde btsug bstan gyis lha sa'i brag dkar la sogs pa'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ li yul nas don pa'i dge 'dun dang rgya
nag ha shang spyan drangs te mchod/ bran ka mu la ko sha sogs kyis mdo sde las brgya/ gser 'od bsgyur/ ljang tsha lha dbon la rgya'i sras mo gyim shing kong jo bslangs
pas bu shi mes rang dang 'dus nas lha shAkya mu ni btsal te mchod pa byas/ de gnyis la 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul pa'i sku gcig 'khrungs mtshan khri srong lde btsan du
btags/ de chung ba'i dus su rgya'i yul du sang shi la sogs pa mi bzhi chos 'tshol du btang / de dag gis rgya'i rgyal po'i drung du phyin/ de la zhus nas sgom pa'i lung 'bogs
pa'i ha shang dang mjal nas legs par mnos/ ha shang de mngon shes mnga' bas sang shi la/ ston pas gdong dmar can gyi yul du dam pa'i chos dar bar byed pa'i byang chub
sems dpa' lung bstan pa de khyod yin/ bod ni rgya gar gyi mkhan po zhi ba 'tsho zhes bya ba des 'dul skal yin/ de ma yin pa gang gis kyang phan mi thogs zer/ de rnams kyis
rgya nas chos bam po stong tsam blangs/ ha shang zhig kyang spyan drangs te 'ongs pa bod du sleb pa'i tshe rgyal po 'das/ rgyal bu chung / blon po rnams kyi chos khrims
bshig ste/ dam chos byed pa byung na spyug par byas/ lha shAkya mu ni rgya yul du skyel bar brtsams pa la/ mi sum brgyas ma theg nas bye thems su sbas/ lha sar bshas ra
byas so/ /de'i tshe sna nam khri thog rje thang la 'bar zhes bya ba rgyab gas nas shi cog gru skyes bzang rgyal/ mgo byad bskams nas shi bas lha bye 'og tu bcug pas len
zer nas bton/ dre'u gnyis kyis bteg nas mang yul skyi grong du bskyal/ mkhar brag dang mgrin bzang bshig go /des khong tshos chos

sbas ha shang slog gsal snang mang yul gyi blon por bskos te brdzangs so/ /de nas rgyal bu lo bcu gsum lon pa na rgyal sar bton/ yab mes kyi le'u tshe gtam du mdzad pa na chos
kyi gtam byas chos sbas pa blangs te gzigs pas dad par 'gyur/ rgya me mgo dang / kha che A nandas bsgyur/ de blon po zhang grom pa skyes la sogs pas bkag go /blon po
chos la dkar ba rnams kyis sang shi mang yul du brdzangs/ gsal snang gis mang yul du ma bsdad par/ rgya gar du phyin/ ma hA bo dhi dang byang chub shing / nA lendra rnams
la mchod pa chen po byas bal yul du log mkhan po bo dhi sa twa dang mjal te mang yul du spyan drangs/ gtsug lag khang bzhengs/ mkhan po'i gsungs nas/ bod kyi btsan po dang
/ khyod dang / nga dang gsum 'od srung gi bstan pa la bya rdzi ma'i bu gsum du gyur nas bod du bstan pa spel bar smon lam btab pa yin te/ btsan po'ang ma skyes/ khyod
kyang nar ma son pas ngas 'di na bod kyi rgyal rabs dgu'i bar du dgug cing bsdad pa yin gsungs slar bal por gshegs/ sbas chos sbas te pho brang rlung 'tshubs su rgyal po
dang mjal te chos kyi bka' mchid byas/ bo dhi sa twa'i lo rgyus bsnyad pas khyod yib cig ngas zhang nyam bzang khad kyis gsol du gzhug go gsungs/ zhang nyam bzang dang 'gos
khri bzang la sogs pa chos la dga' ba'i blon po kun la chos byed par mol btab pas/ nyam bzang na re/ ma zhang dbang che la chos la gnag pas mi 'grub mchi zer/ 'gos na
re/ thabs bgyi bar rngo thog gi kho bo'i rting gnon mdzod cig zer bas/ rgyal blon chad mdzad/ 'gos kyis g.yo byas ma zhang grom pa skyes gson por dur du bcug sba A tsArYa
bo dhi satwa spyan 'dren du btang / lang gro Na ra sogs gsum bsu ru btang / khong tsho dang mang yul du mjal/ rim pas spyan drangs/ kha che A nanda la A tsArYa ci 'dra rtog
tu bcug pas/ bzang po zhig ste thugs khrig mi 'tshal zer bas pho brang du spyan drangs/ kha che des lo tsA byas/ pho brang rlung 'tshub tu zla ba bzhir dge bcu/ khams
bco brgyad dang rten 'brel bcu gnyis kyi chos bshad pas bod kyi lha srin khros

te/ 'phang thang chus khyer/ dmar po ri la thog rgyab/ mi nad phyugs nad byung bas/ bod 'bangs yo log chos byas pas len zer nas A tsArYa bal por log de nas cung zad lon pa
na/ sba gsal snang rgya yul du chos tshol ba la brdzangs/ sang shi sogs A tsArYa spyan 'dren du btang ngo / /de'i tshe ha shang mngon shes can zhig gis/ da zla ba drug zhag
drug na 'phags pa rta skad kyi sprul pa 'di 'dra zhig 'ong zhes 'bag byas/ sleb pa dang ji lta bas de la rgya rjes bya dga' byin/ ha shang la sgom lung blangs/ 'khor ba
na de skyes su phul bas/ A tsArYa da dung spyan ma drongs khyod song zhig gsungs bal por phyin/ mkhan po spyan drangs pa ma byon par/ der mkhan po'i gsungs nas/ bod kyi
lha srin thu/ chos byed mi ster/ de 'dul ba la slob dpon padma sambha wa zhes bya ba 'dzam bu gling na che ba'i rig sngags mkhan zhig bzhugs de spyan drangs dgos gsungs
pa bzhin/ sna nam rdo rje bdud 'joms sogs lnga btang ba slob dpon gyis mkhyen nas mang yul gung thang du byon pa dang mjal/ lha mtsho srid mtsho'i rtsa bar bstan ma bcu gnyis
dam la btags nas byang lam brgyud/ bod kyi 'dre srin gdug pa can thams cad dam la btags te mal gro'i phu nas byon/ bsam yas su spyan drangs/ mkhan po spyan 'drongs/
jo bo shAkya mu ni slar lha sar bzhugs su bcug sa chog mdzad/ mkhan pos bkod pa mdzad de o tantra pu ri'i gtsug lag khang la dpe blangs te/ dbu rtse ri rab/ gling bcu gnyis/
nyi zla/ mtha' ma lcags ri nag pos bskor ba bsgrubs/ btsun mo che ba tshe spong bza' dkar rgyal me tog sgrol mas zangs khang gling / pho yong bza' rgyal mo btsun gyis
bu tshal gser khang / 'bro bza' byang chub sman gyis dge rgyas li ma gling bzhengs/ me mo yos la bting nas sa mo yos la tshar/ A tsArYa rnam pa gnyis kyis rab gnas mdzad/
lo bcu gsum du dga' ston byas/ lug gi lo la yod smra'i dge 'dun bcu gnyis spyan drangs/ bod la btsun pa btub mi btub sad pa'i phyir du mi bdun rab tu byung ste/ de dag
gi mkhan po ni bo dhi sa twa'o/ /de las rgan gsum ni/ sbas ratna rakShi ta/ rin

chen srung ba zhes bya ba/ sbas dznyyA nandra rakShi ta/ ye shes dbang po srung ba ste/ dam pa'i chos 'dzin pa'i mkhan po chen po bod la sku drin che ba yin zhing / mkhan po
bo dhi satwa sku gshegs nas 'dis mkhan po'i gdan sa mdzad/ ratnendra rakShi ta/ rin chen dbang po srung ba ste gsum mo/ /bar pa ni/ glang su ga ta warma rakShi ta/ bde
bar gshegs pa'i go cha srung ba zhes bya'o/ /gzhon nu gsum ni/ pa gor bai ro tsa na rakShi ta/ rnam par snang mdzad srung ba zhes bya ba/ nges pa'i don theg pa'i rtse mo
la shin tu sku drin che ba/ 'khon nA gendra rakShi ta/ klu'i dbang po srung ba zhes bya ba/ gtsang de wendra rakShi ta lha'i dbang po srung ba dang gsum mo/ sad mi mi bdun
la/ ka ba shrI ku Ti rakShi ta dpal rtsegs srung ba la sogs pa lo tsA ba che ba brgya rtsa brgyad kyis blo sbyangs la/ de dag la cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan la sogs pa lo
tsA ba stong rtsa brgyad kyis blo sbyong mdzad do/ /zhes sngon gyi bka' chems kyi yi ge rnying pa las byung ngo / /rgyal po nyid kyi ring la khams yan chad du chos kyi grwa
chen po bcu gnyis btsugs/ paNDYi ta mang po spyan drangs/ theg pa che chung gi sde snod mang po bsgyur/ sngags 'chang dharma kIrti zhes pa byon/ rdo rje dbyings sogs
dang / sangs rgyas gsang ba gangs ri ti se na bzhugs pa thos nas spyan 'dren pa bran ka mu ti ka dang / sbas manydzyu shrI gnyis brdzangs pa ma byon par bod kyi don du de
nyid 'dus pa/ rnam snang mngon byang / bsam gtan phyi ma gsum la 'grel pa mdzad/ de gnyis la mkhas par bslabs te log gsang sngags bla med rnams bsgyur du ma gnang ste/ lkog
tu slob dpon padmas rje 'bangs brgyad dam nyer lnga la gdams so zhes grags rje 'bangs dgu'i mnga' bdag la che mchog gnubs nam mkha' snying po la yang dag sangs rgyas
ye shes rin po che la 'jam dpal/ rgyal ba mchog dbyangs la padma dbang chen/ mtsho rgyal la phur pa/ 'brog mi dpal gyi ye shes la ma mo/ rlangs dpal gyi ye shes la 'jig rten
mchod bstod/ bai ro tsa na la dmod pa drag sngags kyi bka' babs/ de la mnga' bdag gis tshe zad nas lo lnga sring ba/ nam mkha'i snying po nyi zer la zhon pa/ sangs rgyas
ye shes brag la phur pa 'debs pa/ rgyal ba mchog dbyangs rta mgo bton nas

rta skad thengs gsum 'don pa/ mtsho rgyal bsad gso/ 'brog mis mkha' 'gro ma dngos su 'khor ba/ rlangs kyis sde brgyad bran du bkol ba/ bai ros lha srin dbang du bsdu shes so/
/gzhan ldan ma rtse mang sogs mang ngo / /rdzogs chen pa bi ma la de dus byon/ des rje/ gnyags/ nyang ting nge 'dzin gsum la bshad/ nyang gis sbas blo gros dbang phyug
la gdams zer/ sgyu 'phrul pa rnams de ral pa can gyi dus su byon rma dang gnyags la bshad zer ro/ /spyi'i lo rgyus la slob dpon padmas ngam shod kyi bye ma ne'u gsing du
bsgyur ba dang / gtsang po sbubs su 'dzud par gsungs pas bsam yas kyi mtsho ni thang du bsgyur/ phu'i ri la nags dngos su byung nas/ blon pos phra ma byas te slob dpon brdzangs
pa mang yul nas nam mkha' la 'phur nas byon zhes grag la/ rnying ma'i lo rgyus las mu ne btsan po rgyal sa 'dzin gyi bar du bzhugs te/ bod yul 'di thams cad byin
gyis brlabs pa la gnas re re lo zla du ma bzhugs zer/ de ni dus gcig la sku'i bkod pa sna tshogs ston pa'i rdzu 'phrul can yin pas de dag la go rim mi dgos kyi/ gtan tshigs
su sgrub dka' 'o/ /mkhan po mya ngan las 'da' kha'i zhal chems su/ bod du padma sambha was bstan ma bcu gnyis la bka' bsgos pa'i phyir mu stegs ni mi 'byung gi sangs rgyas
kyi bstan pa kha gnyis su gyes te rtsod par 'gyur pas/ de'i tshe nga'i slob ma kA ma la shI la spyan drongs la rtsod pa byed du chug des rtsod pa chos phyogs su zhi
bar 'gyur ro zhes gdams te/ rtas phra brgyab pa'i rkyen gyis zhi bar gshegs/ ye shes dbang po mkhan por bskos te/ ring zhig bstan pa bskyangs/ des dpal dbyangs tshab tu bskos
te lho brag mkhar chur bsgom du byon/ de'i ring la rgya'i ha shang ma hA ya Na'i slob ma dar te/ lus ngag gi chos spyod dge ba byas pas sangs mi rgya ba dang / yid la
mi byed pas sangs rgya zer ba'i lugs dar/ de la ston mun du grags/ dpal dbyangs dang / sba ratna la sogs pa nyung shas shig mkhan po'i rjes su 'brang / de la rtsen min
rgya'i skad yin/ bod skad du cig car ba dang rim skyes la zer/ de dag ma mthun par rtsod pa na/ rgyal pos A tsArYa bo dhi satwa'i lugs bzhin du gyis shig gsungs pas/ ston
mun pa rnams khros

te/ rtsen min pa ril gsod zer/ rgyal po thugs ma bde/ ye shes dbang po 'bod du btang bas lan gnyis su ma khugs/ gsum pa la ma khugs na sod cig bsgo bas khugs/ rgyal po la mkhan
po'i zhal chems gsos btab nas rgya gar nas ka ma la shI la spyan drangs/ btsan po dgung la bzhugs/ ha shang g.yas gral/ slob dpon g.yon gral du bkod de/ btsan pos gnyis
ka'i lag tu me tog gi 'phreng ba gtad de/ khyed gnyis gang rgyal ba la pham pas me tog gi 'phreng ba phul cig pham pa de 'dir ma sdod ces bka' stsal/ rtsod pas slob dpon
rgyal/ ha shang gis me tog gi 'phreng ba phul te/ rgyal pos deng phyin chad lta ba klu sgrub kyi lugs gzung / spyod pa chos spyod bcu dang pha rol tu phyin pa la slobs/
ston mun gyi lugs byed du mi dbang ngo zhes bcad de/ ha shang rgya yul du brdzangs/ de'i dpe rnams gter du sbas/ ka ma la shI las 'grel pa du ma brtsams/ mi ring bar ha
shang gis mngags pa'i rgya'i gshan pa mi bzhis dku mnyes te grongs so/ /btsan po'ang dgung lo drug cu rtsa dgu la gshegs so/ /de'i sras mu ne btsan pos rgyal sa gzung /
bsam yas su mchod pa bzhi btsugs te/ bod kyi ltogs phyug lan gsum bsnyams/ chab srid lo gcig dang zla ba bdun mdzad/ yum gyis dug btang ste grongs/ de nas sad na legs mjing
yon nam/ khri lde btsan lo bzhi pa la rgyal sa gtad/ des dkar chung rgyal sde'i lha khang bzhengs/ chos kyi srol cher bzung / rgyal srid lo bcu bdun bskyangs/ de nas
khri ral pa can zhes bya ba snying rje padma dkar po'i mdo las gsal bar lung bstan pa/ mtshan ni khri lde srong btsan/ phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa'i sku des rgyal sa bzung
/ 'di sad na legs kyi sras su 'chad mkhan mang zhing / glang dar ma'ang 'di'i mched do/ /sgra sbyor bam gnyis pa las/ 'di khri srong lde btsan rang gi sras su 'chad de/
'di skad du rta'i lo la btsan po khri lde srong btsan pho brang gi 'on ljang ngo na bzhugs/ stod smad kyi dmag dang rkun chen btul/ gar log gi pho nyas phyag 'tshal/ blon
chen po zhang khri zur ram shags dang / blon mang rje lha lod la sogs pas bya las gnangs mang po bcad de/ rnga rta dang ba mar phal mo che phyag tu phul/ zhang blon man
chad so sor byas/ dga' stsal

ba'i lan la/ nyi 'og gi mkhan po A tsArYa dzi na mi tra dang / su randra bo dhi dang / shI lendra bo dhi dang / dA na shI la dang / bo dhi mi tra dang / bod kyi mkhan po ratna
rakShi ta dang / dharma tA shI la dang / lo tsA ba mkhas par tshud pa dznyyA na se na dang / dza ya rakShi ta dang / manydzyu shrI warma/ ratnendra shI la la sogs pas
theg pa che chung gi gzhung las 'byung ba'i rgya gar gyi skad las bod kyi skad du 'gyur zhing ming du btags pa rnams dkar chag tu bris te/ nam du'ang gzhung lugs de las
mi bsgyur zhing kun gyis slob tu rung bar gyis shig ces bka' stsal nas/ sngon lha sras yab kyi ring la A tsArYa bo dhi sa twa dang / ye shes dbang po dang / zhang rgyal nyen
nyam bzang dang / blon khri sher sang shi dang / lo tsA ba snying de wa ko Sha dang / lce khyi 'brug dang / bram ze A nanda la sogs pas chos kyi skad bod la ma grags
pa las ming du btags pa dag ci mchis pa'i nang nas/ kha cig chos kyi gzhung dang / byA ka ra Na'i lugs dang mi mthun te/ mi bcos su mi rung ba rnams kyang bcos/ skad kyi
ming gces so 'tshal gyis kyang bsnan nas theg pa che chung gi gzhung las ji skad byung ba dang / gna'i mkhan po chen po nA gArdzu na dang / ba su bandhu la sogs pas ji ltar
bshad pa dang / byA ka ra Na'i lugs las ji skad du 'dren pa dang yang bstun te 'jal dka' ba rnams kyang tshig so sor phral nas gtan tshigs kyis bshad de gzhung du bris/
skad rkyang pa bshad mi 'tshal ba sgra bzhin du bsgyur ba'i rigs pa rnams kyang sgra btsan par bgyis te ming du btags/ skad kha cig don bzhin du gdags pa'i rigs pa rnams
kyang don btsan par bgyis te ming du btags nas/ btsan po'i spyan sngar bande chen po yon tan dang / bande chen po ting nge 'dzin la sogs pa'ang tshogs te/ rje blon gdan
'dzoms pa la zhus nas dharma bsgyur ba'i thabs dang rgya gar gyi skad las bod kyi skad du ming gdags pa'i rnam gzhag gtan la phab ste bkas bcad pa/ dam pa'i chos bsgyur
ba'i lugs ni sgra dang mthun la/ don dang yang mi 'gal ba la/ bod skad las yang gar bde bar gyis shig dharma bsgyur ba la rgya gar gyi skad go rim las mi snor bar bod kyi
skad du bsgyur na don dang tshig tu 'grel zhing

bde na ma bsnor bar sgyur cig bsnor na bde zhing go ba'i skyed cig yod na/ tshigs bcad la ni rtsa ba bzhi pa'am drug pa'ang rung ste/ tshigs su bcad pa gcig gi nang gar bde
bar bsnor cing sgyur cig rkyang pa la ni don gar bsnyegs pa yan chad kyi tshig dang don gnyis ka la gar bde bar bsnor cing sgyur cig skad cig la ming du mar 'dren pa ni
ltag 'og dang bstun la gar bsnyegs pa bzhin du ming thogs shig gau ta ma lta bu/ gau'i sgra las tshig dang / phyogs dang / sa dang / 'od dang / rdo rje dang / ba lang dang
/ mtho ris la sogs pa rnams du mar bsnyegs pa dang / kau shi ka lta bu/ rtsa ku sha thogs pa lta bu/ mkhas pa dang padma la dga' ba dang / 'ug pa dang mdzod ldan la sogs
pa sgra'i lugs las drangs shing bsgyur na rnam grangs mang po zhig tu snyeg la/ bsgyur ba rnams gcig gi nang du ni rnam grangs de kun 'dur yang mi btub ste/ gcig tu chad
par byar yang gtan tshigs chen po med par rnams ni mi bsgyur yang rgya gar gyis skad so na zhog cig gar yang drang du rung ba'i tshig byung na phyogs gcig tu chad par mi
bsgyur bar spyir snyegs su rung bar gyis shig yul dang / sems can dang / me tog dang / rtsi shing la sogs pa'i ming bsgyur ba mi go zhing tshig mi bde ba dang / 'ol phyir
bsgyur du rung yang don du de ltar yin nam min gtol med pa rnams ni 'go la yul zhes sam/ me tog ces bya ba la sogs gang bya ba ming zhig bla thabs su snon la rgya gar
gyi skad so na zhog cig grangs la rgya gar gyi skad bzhin du bsgyur na/ dge slong brgya phrag phyed dang bcu gsum zhes 'byung ba la sogs pa ni/ stong nyis brgya lnga bcu
zhes tha mal par bod kyi skad kyi lugs bzhin du bsgyur na don dang mi 'gal la/ bod kyi skad la'ang bde bas grangs sdom du rung ba'i rnams bod kyi skad kyi lugs bzhin du thogs
shig pa ri dang / sam dang / u pa lta bu la sogs te/ tshig gi phrad dang rgyan lta bur 'byung ba rnams bsgyur na don mthun zhing 'byor pa'i thabs ni/ yongs su zhe'am/
yang dag pa zhe'am/ nye ba zhes sgra bzhin du sgyur cig don lhag par snyegs sa med pa rnams ni tshig gi lhad kyis bsnan mi dgos kyi don bzhin du thogs shig rnam grangs
su

btags pa'i tshig rnams ni ma 'dom na ming gang bod skad du spyir gdags shing tshig tu gang bde bar gdags so/ /'dom na so sor btags pa bzhin du thogs shig sangs rgyas dang /
byang chub sems dpa' dang / nyan thos la sogs pa la zhe sa dang ko long gi tshig gi rim pa ni/ sangs rgyas la zhe sa'i tshig tu bsgyur/ gzhan la tshig 'bring po man chad
tsam du bya ste/ sngon lha sras yab kyi spyan sngar mkhan po dang lo tsA ba mkhas pa tshogs pas/ dharma dkon mchog sprin dang / langkar gshegs pa bsgyur te gtan la phab
pa'i lugs bzhin du sgyur cig skad kyi lugs 'di ltar bkas bcad pa las so so nas su 'ang 'chos shing 'og tu ming gsar du 'dogs su mi snang gi bsgyur ba dang 'chad pa'i grwa
so so nas skad gsar du ming gdags dgos pa zhig na/ so so'i grwa grwar ming chad par ma gdags par chos kyi gzhung dang sgra'i lugs las ji skad 'byung ba'i gtan tshigs dang
chos la ji skad du gdags par dpyad de/ pho brang du bcom ldan 'das kyi ring lugs kyi 'dun sa dang / dharma zhu chen tshal ba'i grwar phul la snyan du zhus te bkas bcad
nas skad kyi dkar chag gi dkyus su bsnan no/ /gsang sngags kyi rgyud rnams gzhung gi gsang bar bya ba yin te/ snod du ma gyur pa rnams la bshad cing bstan du'ang mi rung
la/ bar du bsgyur zhing spyod du gnang gis kyang / ldem po'i ngag gi bshad pa ma khrol nas/ sgra ji bzhin du 'dzin cing log par spyod pa dag kyang 'byung / sngags kyi rgyud
kyi nang nas 'thu zhing bod skad du bsgyur ba dag kyang 'byung zhes bdas kyi/ phyin chad gzungs sngags dang / bla nas bka' stsal te bsgyur du bcug pa ma gtogs pa sngags
kyi rgyud dang / sngags kyi tshig 'thu zhing bsgyur du mi snang ngo / /zhes gsungs pa las gsal bar mthong zhing / lung rgyas par bris pa ni chos bsgyur ba dag la gus pa
bskyed par 'dod pas so/ /de yan na bod 'di na grong zhing thor bu las ma chags la/ phal cher 'brog brdal rta dang rnga mong nor gyis gtso bor byed pa da lta'i sog po lta
bu ste/ de'i dbang gis bod kyi dmag gis rgya nag lan du mar bcom/ rgyal po 'di'i thog nas dbon zhang 'dums byas/ lha sa dang / rgya bod kyi mtshams

dang / pho brang blta na sdug gsum du rdo ring bslangs/ de la chad rdo'i yi ge btab bo/ /rgyal po des 'on ljang rdo'i gtsug lag khang btab/ rab tu byung ba re la 'bangs mi
khyim bdun bdun sbyar zhing / rang gi ral par ras yug btags te/ de la dge 'dun bzhugs su bcug pas/ de dag la dbus sde gnyis su grags pa sogs bstan pa rin po che la bkur sti
kham che ba mdzad pas/ sdig blon rnams mi dga' chos khrims bshig pa'i gros byas/ lha sras gtsang ma spyugs/ btsun mo ngang tshul ma dang bande chen po dpal gyi yon tan
gyis nal bshams so zer phra ma bcug ste bande chen po bkum/ btsun mo lcebs/ btsan po dgung lo so drug pa la dbas rgyal gto re dang co ro legs sgra gnyis kyis zhal ltag par
bstan te bkrongs/ glang dar ma 'u dum btsan la rgyal srid gtad/ dbas rgyal gto re nang blon du bskos/ sna nam rgyal tsha khri gsum la sogs kyis chos khrims dang 'gal ba
mang du byas/ lo paN gyis chos bsgyur ba'i grwa bshig bsgyur 'phro bcad/ paNDYi ta rang yul du brdzangs/ lo bzhi chab srid bskyangs/ de'i bar la rab tu byung ba kun phab/
btsun pa'i rtags bor du ma 'dod pa kun mda' gzhu bskur nas rngon pa byed bcug mi nyan pa rnams bsad/ shAkya mu ni sbas sgo brtsigs te bzhag po sti phal cher lha sa'i brag
la sbas/ de nas skabs shig na lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje la dpal lha mos bskul te/ des btsan po lha sar bsad nas bros pas thar/ des mngon pa kun las btus/ 'dul ba 'od
ldan/ karma sha tam gsum khyer nas khams su phyin/ myang ting 'dzin bzang po dang / rma rin chen mchog la sogs pa grir bkum/ lo tsA ba la la bros/ bstan pa med par byas so//
// ! gnyis pa bstan pa phyis dar ba'i tshul la bstan pa'i me ro smad nas langs tshul/ stod nas gsos tshul/ dbus gtsang du 'bar tshul gsum las/ dang po ni/ dar mas bstan
pa bsnubs pa'i dus/ gtsang rab gsal/ g.yo dge 'byung / dmar shAkya mu ni dang gsum chu bo rir bsgom zhing yod pa na/ btsun pa khyi ra byed pa mthong / gtam dris pas rgyal
pos bstan pa bsnubs tshul thos pas

dngangs te 'dul ba dre'u la bkal nas mnga' ris stod du bros/ gar log nas lam thon nas hor yul la phyin/ skad rigs mi gcig pa'i yul du bstan pa dar bar bya snyam yang ma nus
nas mdo smad du byon/ der sgom zhing bzhugs pas tsong khar skyes pa/ bon bzhon nu mu zu gsal 'bar zhes bya ba zhig khong rnams la dad pas gtugs shing / khyad par dam pa'i
chos 'dul ba la lhag par mos nas bstan pa la rab tu 'byung bar zhus pas gnang ste/ der gtsang gis mkhan po byas/ g.yos slob dpon byas/ dge tshul bsgrubs/ mkhan slob kyi
mtshan las dras te dge ba rab gsal du btags/ phyis thugs rab che bas dgongs pa rab gsal du grags/ des kyi rgyal ba'i gtsug tor la dbu tshad/ nam dga' ldan byang chub la
yo ga gsan/ bsnyen pa rdzogs pa ran pa dang dge slong lnga dgos pa ma tshang nas/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje glong thang du 'dug bgros thos nas spyan sngar phyin te zhus pas/
ngas rgyal po bsad pas las kyi kha skong mi 'os/ ngas btsal rogs bgyi gsungs nas/ rgya nag ha shang ko bang dang / gyi ban bya ba gnyis rnyed de/ sngar gyi mkhan slob/
dmar gyis gsang ston/ rgya'i dge slong gnyis kyis kha skong byas te lnga tshogs kyi dbus su bsnyen par rdzogs/ de'i ring la mkhan slob dang gong sengge grags la 'dul ba
legs par bslabs/ de nas lo lnga lon pa na dbus nas klag pa lam pa klu mes tshul khrims shes rab/ 'bring ye shes yon tan/ rakShi tshul khrims 'byung gnas/ sba tshul khrims
blo gros/ sum pa ye shes blo dang lnga/ gtsang nas 'gur mo rab kha ba lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug shab sgo lnga'i tshong btsun shes rab sengge/ mnga' ris pa 'od brgyad
spun gnyis/ bo dong pa u pa de dkar ba dang lnga ste mi bcu 'ongs nas gtsang la bka' drin zhus pas/ nga rgas nas mkhan po mi 'khyongs pas bla chen po la zhus gsung / der
zhus pas nga bsnyen par rdzogs nas lo lnga las ma lon pas gzhan gyi mkhan po mi btub gsungs pa la/ gtsang na re/ dmigs bsal la btub pas gyis gsungs nas/ bla chen pos mkhan
po byas/ gtsang dang g.yo las

slob dang gsang ston/ dmar dang ha shang gis kha skong byas te thams cad tshig rdzogs byas so/ /de nas bla chen gyis lo ston mthu che bas bstan srung gyis/ klu mes btsun pas
mkhan po gyis/ tshong dge blo rno bas ston pa gyis/ 'bring bkod mkhas pas gnas gzhi gzung gsungs/ de nas sba sbar gnyis/ ja cog gnyis/ bzhad srags gnyis/ 'al gnubs gnyis/
zong 'tshur gnyis rnams bsnyen par rdzogs/ zhang 'od mchog grags la sher phyin byang sa sogs mdo sde dang mngon pa gsan mkhas par mdzad/ de'i dus su rakShi'i gcung dang
/ sba'i gcung gnyis pho bo bsu ru 'ongs pa dang klong thang du mjal bas dad de/ los mkhan po byas/ phu bo gnyis kyis slob dpon byas te rab tu byung / de nas byin po yar
log klu mes kyis grum ye shes rgyal mtshan la 'dul ba gsan zhing lo gcig bsdad/ de nas klu mes kyis mkhan po la kho bo dbus gtsang du 'gro bas mchod gnas cig zhu byas pas/
ban po'i 'obs zhu phog nas de tshun du bzhes pa'i zhwa sa ser btab pa zhig gsol 'phro gnang / 'di gyon la nga dran par gyis gsung / zhwa ser por byed pa de nas dar ba
yin/ dbus pa lnga bsam yas su gdan 'dzom/ klu mes kyis ka chu/ sba mched kyis bu tshul dang dbu rtse/ rakShi mched kyis dge rgyas/ 'bring gi zangs khang bzung / dbus su dge
'dun gyi sde mang bar btsugs/ lo tshong gnyis kyis gtsang du dge 'dun gyi sde mang du btsugs la/ klu mes kyi slob ma glan ye shes 'bar/ rngog byang chub 'byung gnas/ sna
nam rdo rje dbang phyug gru mer ye shes 'byung gnas bzhi la ka bzhi/ klu sum gnyis la gdung gnyis/ khu dang ring gnyis la sgo glegs gnyis zer/ phyams zhes bshad pa rnams
ni klu sum gyi mkhan bu/ gral bu ni de dag gi'ang mkhan bu rnams la bzhag par 'dug ste/ klu mes rang la'ang thug dngos slob gzhan dge bshes yam shud sogs mang ngo / /smad
'dul ba'i bshad rgyun la klu mes gtso che ste/ de'ang gru mer gyi mkhan bu rlung skyogs gzus/ gzus kyis klu mes rang la'ang gtugs/ de la bu bzhi ste/ 'jims dang / sne
pho/ glan dang / spo chung nge / de'i 'jims

pa ma gtogs gsum la rgya 'dul ba 'dzin pas gtugs/ 'jims pa'i slob ma ko khyim pa ye shes bla ma/ sne pho'i slob ma sog tshul khrims bla ma/ spo chung pa'i slob ma myang mtshams
rin chen bla ma rnams dang / phyi ma'i slob ma skam gsal ba'i snying po kun la rgya 'dul gyis gsan/ 'di myang stod mang ra ba sku 'bras ngan pas gnas gzhi bya rog tshang
du ma chug par dga' ba gdong du byon/ mdo rtsa la klog dar byas pas zhar la gzhung zin nas so ga can du 'dul ba slob tu byon nas/ gzhan yang 'dul ba mkhas zer tshad
la gtugs/ dgung lo so bzhi'i bar du 'dul ba la sbyangs pa mdzad/ de nas dge bshes kyi cha bzung ste bzhugs sa ma mo dga' ba gdong du mdzad/ dgon pa chu mig lung yang bzung
nas chos gzhi mang du btsugs/ 'dul ba'i bshad pa rgya cher mdzad/ brgyad cu bzhes nas 'dul ba'i thun re tsam gsungs/ bshad pa'i rkang zhar chos pa tsho 'dzin btsug dgung
lo brgyad cu rtsa lnga la shangs su sku gshegs/ de'i slob ma ka ba bzhi/ gdung ma bcur grags pa'i ka ba rma tsho'i slob ma bya 'dul 'dzin te gtsang rong g.yung du 'khrungs/
'dre chen po las rab tu byung / sog dang khyad par rgya dang rma tsho las 'dul ba mkhas par bslabs/ rgyal tsha zhang ye la dbu tshad/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba la yo ga stod
lung pa chen po la bka' gdams/ zul phur bshad grwa btsugs/ dpe dkar gyis btsun chung du sprul nas glags blta bas 'dul ba dang 'gal ba char byung ba zhig la na bza' spu
phyir bstan pa gcig pu las ma mthong bas dad de nye gnas byas/ slob ma 'gro ba la phan thogs nus pa bdun cu rtsa drug byung / dgung lo bdun cu rtsa drug la zul phur gshegs/
de'i slob ma rtsis pa gzhon seng / de'i slob ma bya'i snang dpon chos dbang / de'i slob ma chos byang / chos kyi brtson 'grus/ chos grags rin chen dpal/ de tshun zul
phu'i mkhan po rkyang yin/ de nas tshogs chos lung pa'i mkhan chen ka bzhi pa dang / de'i slob ma chos lung mkhan po bsod grags/ de gnyis bu ston rin po che'i bsnyen rdzogs
kyi mkhan slob kyang yin/ 'dul ba'i bshad pa'ang tshar phyin pa gsan/ kha che pan chen gyis

snar klas mo cher dbyar gnas mdzad/ me tog 'phreng rgyud gsungs pa sengge zil gnon dang shangs pa jo brtan gyis gsan/ sengge zil gnon la tshad ma'i skyes bu bsod nams mgon
pos gsan/ de la bu ston gyis zhus so/ /yang phyis paNDYi ta nags kyi rin chen la rong ston pa shes bya kun rig gis kyang gsan no/ /rgya'i ka ba jo brtan nag po dar tshul
gyis lo drug cu lon nas rab tu byung / klog bslabs/ bdun cu lon pa na 'dul ba la mkhas par gyur te/ yar klungs tsha rong du bshad pa'i slob ma sha mi/ de'i slob ma klungs
dkar tshul khrims grags/ de'i slob ma gra mi/ de'i slob ma rgya dur gyi mkhan po dar ma ye shes/ de'i slob ma zangs chen pa dar ma bsod nams/ de'i slob ma mtsho sna pa shes
rab bzang po'am/ yang sha mi'i slob ma ka ba dar seng / de'i slob ma thag ma rdo gzhon/ de'i slob ma spal ti ste/ mdor na bod du 'dul grwa bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung
ngo / /smad 'dul stod 'dul gnyis ka'i sdom rgyun klu sgrub la thug phyis kha che'i paNDYi ta chen po shAkya shrI bha dra'i mkhan bu rdo rje dpal dang / byang chub dpal gnyis
las tshogs sde bzhir grags pa byung ba'i sdom rgyun yang klu sgrub la thug pa yin no/ /chos mngon pa'i brgyud pa/ kha che dzi na mi tra nas ska cog zhang gsum des lha
lung dpal gyi rdo rje/ nam nad zla ba'i rdo rje/ dbas rgyal ba ye shes gsum la bshad la/ dang po gnyis kyis sgom mdzad bshad pa ma spel/ dbas kyis dbus nas khams su byon/
de la slob ma mang du byung ba'i ra khri bzang bar la brang ti dar ma snying pos gsan/ des gtsang rong du ngur smrig btab bshad grwa bskyangs pa'i slob ma shin tu mang
ste/ bshes gnyen mu dra chen pos bo dong btab/ paNDYi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa spyan drangs te/ 'jal du rngog lo dge slong sum brgyas bskor te byon pa'i tshe/ lo tsA ba'i dge
slong re re la brang tis kho rang gi dge slong bcu gsum bcu gsum bsnyen bkur byed du bcug ces grags/ brang ti la ko bo ye byung / de la 'ban/ tho gar gnam lde/ 'jad pa
byang skyabs/ 'jad pa gzhon byang / 'brang mchams zhang / bo dong rin rtse/ khro phu ba bsod nams sengge/ tshad ma'i skyes bu/ bu ston rin po che'o/ /shes rab kyi pha rol
tu phyin pa'i bshad pa ni 'dre chen po shes rab 'bar gyis rgyas par mdzad pa bstan pa snga dar gyi bshad rgyun khams su 'phos pa las kyang byung zhing / de la slob ma shin
tu mang yang bshad rgyun ar byang chub ye shes kyis bzung ngo

zhes grags so/ /tshad ma ni bstan pa snga dar gyi dus su mkhan po bo dhi satwa yis tshad ma de kho na nyid bsdus pa zhes bya ba mdzad cing / phyis ka ma la shI las rigs thig
dang / de'i 'grel pa dul lhas mdzad pa dang / nyid kyi phyogs snga ma bsgrigs pa rnams bsgyur/ de tsam las ma dar la/ de'i rgyun yang mi snang ngo / /de ltar bstan pa stongs
pa rang lo bdun cu 'o bu gsungs// // ! gnyis pa stod nas gsos tshul ni/ glang dar gyi sras 'od srung dang yum btsan gnyis/ dang po la mnga' bdag dpal 'khor btsan/ de
myang stod du snyags kyis bkrongs pa nas rgyal srid 'thor/ khong gi sras bkra shis brtsegs pa dpal dang / skyid lde nyi ma mgon gnyis byung ba'i phyi ma mnga' ris stod
du spyugs pa la sras dpal gyi mgon/ lde gtsugs mgon/ bkra shis mgon gsum byung ba stod du rgyal srid zhwa tsam chags/ ya rtse rgyal po'ang de rnams la zer/ smad du bkra shis
brtsegs pa bzhugs/ de la dpal lde/ 'od lde/ skyid lde gsum byung / dbus gtsang gi ru lag bzhi bskyangs pas smad du rgyal srid lham tsam chags zer/ bkra shis mgon gyi
sras 'od kyi rgyal mtshan/ de'i sras srong nge dang kho re gnyis/ srong nges gu ger mtho lding gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i gros mdzad/ sa pra mkhan po na re/ brtsigs
kyang lo brgya na 'jig par 'dug zer/ 'o na bzhag gam gsungs pas/ lo brgya po de bstan pa la nan ltar phan pa zhig 'ong bar 'dug zer ba la/ 'o na bzhengs rin chog dgongs te
bsam yas ji lta ba la/ khyad par shar phyogs su gser gyi mchod rten chen po zhig bzhengs pas nyi ma shar ba'i tshe/ de'i 'od nang na yar phog pas lha khang thams cad gser
gyi mdog tu lhag ger 'char bas mtho lding gser khang du grags/ phyis bsam yas gzigs pa na/ nga'i yab mes bod tshang ma la dbang sgyur ba'i phyag rjes las nga mtha' 'khob
kyi rgyal phran zhig gi sug las mi chung bar 'dug gsung / des mtshan nyid kyi theg pa bkar shes kyang / ar tsho bande bco brgyad la sogs pa'i sngags pa rnams kyis sbyor
sgrol byas pas/ de dag bka' yin min the tshom zos/ rje rigs kyi bu thams cad bsags te lo bcu las mar mi gzhon/ nyi shu las yar mi rgan pa mang du 'tshogs pa'i blo la

brtags nas blo rab 'bring dgur phye/ blo rab kyi rab tu gyur pa bdun/ de rnams kyi g.yog po bdun/ yang g.yog byed pa bdun te nyi shu rtsa gcig pha ma la rin byin nas nyos te
kha cher brdzangs/ der kho rnams la gser mang po bskur nas 'di skad du bsgo'o/ /kha che'i yul na mkhas pa rin chen rdo rje zhes bya ba yod pas de spyan drongs/ rgya gar
shar phyogs na dharma pA la bya ba yod pas de spyan drongs/ nub phyogs ka ru na paNDYi ta nor bu gling pa bya ba yod pas de spyan drongs shig dbus 'gyur 'chang na paNDYi
ta pradznyyA ba li bya ba yod pas/ de la 'dus pa rnam gnyis bya ba'i chos mu stegs kyis kyang rtsod par mi nus pa yin/ de shes par gyis shig de nyid 'dus pa la kun dga'
snying po'i 'grel pa yod zer bas/ de shes par gyis shig nor bu gling pa dang dharma pA la gnyis la las kyi sgrib pa rgyun gcod pa'i rgyud dang / de'i 'grel pa slob dpon dpyid
kyis mdzad pa dang / dkyil 'khor gyi lha sum brgya bzhi bcu pa slob dpon rgyal ba'i lhas mdzad pa yod zer bas/ de shes par gyis shig dpal gsang ba 'dus pa la sangs rgyas
ye shes zhabs dang / 'phags pa klu sgrub kyis mdzad pa'i dkyil chog yod zer ba dang / rin chen rdo rje la dus 'khor dang / rdo rje gdan bzhi'i rgyud 'grel yod zer bas
tshol la shog gzhan bi kra ma la shI la na paNDYi ta brgya rtsa brgyad/ mkhas pa bdun cu rtsa gnyis/ 'gran zla med pa sum cu rtsa bdun/ gtsug gi nor bu lta bur bcu gcig
'dzam bu'i gling gi rgyan lta bu brgyad/ khams gsum gyi spyan lta bu gnyis yod zer bas/ de rnams las gang byung re/ rab gser la ma rtseg par spyan ci drongs kyis/ 'bring
gdams pa ci thob gyis/ tha ma'ang paNDYi ta chos gang mkhas pa dang / gdam ngag gang che ba rtsad chod la lung zhus dpe longs pa gyis la shog byas te btang ngo / /khong
rang mkhan slob med par bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan ye shes 'od/ sras gnyis kyang rab tu byung / rgyal srid gcung gi sras lha lde la gtad/ de la sras gsum/ 'od lde byang chub
'od/ zhi ba 'od do/ /byang chub 'od la thugs rtsis che/ rab tu byung du bcug go /de ltar rgya gar du brdzangs pa rnams/ dang po kha cher phyin/ bcu dgu kha che grib bstan
du shi

rin chen bzang po dang / legs pa'i shes rab gnyis lus/ rin chen bzang pos 'jig rten snang byed kyi dal du zhugs/ 'jam dpal rdo rje zhal gsum phyag drug pa la me tog phog kha
che rin chen rdo rje la sogs par yo ga'i rgyud dkyil chog dang bcas pa/ rdo rje rnal 'byor mas lung bstan nA ro pa la gtugs te/ gsang 'dus lugs gnyis gsan/ dbus 'gyur gyi
paNDYi ta 'das nas/ slob ma dharma pA la yin zer btsal yang ma rnyed/ nor bu gling pa la ngan song sbyong rgyud dang / thabs kyi rgyud lnga/ khyad par mi 'khrugs pa'i
rgyud gdam ngag dang bcas pa zhus so/ /rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor du lha grangs dang mnyam pa'i dbang thob/ bi kra ma la shI lar paNDYi ta mar me mdzad bzang po dang
/ mi thub zla ba dang / rgyal ba'i 'byung gnas gsum la sngags mtshan nyid mang po zhus/ spyir paNDYi ta sum cu rtsa lnga la dbang thob/ rgyud sde bzhi'i sgro 'dogs kha che'i
paNDYi ta dang nor bu gling pa la bcad/ dgung lo so gsum pa la bod du byon/ der yo ga kha che lugs btsugs/ mnga' ris rgyal blon spros pa la dgyes nas/ gzhung na med
pa'i mchod 'phreng dang / khyad par lo chung legs shes gre ba bde bas dbyangs bcos/ dgung lo zhe dgu pa la paNDYi ta zla 'od bzang po dang / bhi na se dang / ka ma la rakShi
ta la bsnyen par rdzogs/ dbus gtsang stod smad kun tu chos gsungs/ de nas lo brgyad nas paNDYi ta shrIddhA ka ra warma bla ma nor bu gling pas bod du btang nas rdo rje
'byung ba dang ye shes zhabs lugs gsungs/ ka cog gi 'gyur la cung zad bcos/ bod spyi mthun gyi bsod nams la grub nas rgya gar shar phyogs kyi paNDYi ta dharma pA la bal
po'i rten khyad par can rnams bskor ba la byon pas/ paNDYi ta tshad pas bsnyungs nas bod kyi gangs ri mthong bar byon na phan zer bas/ rgyal blon chos la dgyes bod la phan
thogs par dgongs nas mnga' ris su byon/ der yo ga gsan pas slob dpon kun dga' snying po'i gdams pa ma nor ba zhig byung bas shin tu mnyes te/ gser 'khar sder gang phul
ba ma bzhes/ khong nor gyi 'dod pa dang bral ba yin gsung / de nas yo ga kha che lugs bzhag nas rgya gar shar phyogs pa'i lugs gzhung gdam ngag dang bcas pa la nyams len
dang bshad pa byas pas

yo ga'i bdag por gyur/ de'ang sku tshe'i stod la kha che lugs/ smad la shar phyogs lugs dar bas yo ga la bod 'dir stod lugs dang smad lugs gnyis su grags so/ /de la slob ma'i
mchog bzhi byung ba ni/ lo chung legs pa'i shes rab/ grwa ba gzhon nu shes rab/ kyi nor ye shes dbang phyug gung shing brtson 'grus rgyal mtshan zhes grags so/ /paNDYi
ta dharma pA la dang mjal nas sgro 'dogs chod de bye ba bdun gyi dam bca' mdzad/ lha bye ba phrag gcig sgom pa gtor ma brgya rtsa bye ba phrag gcig bskor ba bye ba phrag
gcig tsha tsha bye ba phrag gcig yan lag bdun pa bye ba phrag gcig bzlas pa bye ba phrag gcig ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang bye ba phrag gcig bzhes mdzad pas spyi gtsug tu rus
pa dkar po ngang pa'i sgo nga tsam zhig byung / de 'jam dpal dpa' bo'i sprul pa yin skad/ lo tsA ba des sngags log sun 'byin mdzad/ klu dkar rgyal btul/ paNDYi ta dharma
pA la la zhang zhung ba rgyal ba'i shes rab kyis sdom pa blangs/ de bal por byon/ 'dul 'dzin pre ta ka la 'dul ba'i lag len bshad pa zhus pa las mched pa rnams la stod
'dul ba zhes grags/ gzhan yang lha btsun pas paNDYi ta du ma spyan drangs/ mdo rgyud bstan bcos mang du bsgyur/ 'chad nyan gyis gtan la 'bebs su bcug sku tshe smad la jo
bo rje'i snyan pa gsan/ spyan drangs ba'i thugs 'dun drag po byung nas/ blon po sa 'og gi gter mthong ba zhig yod pa de la gser tshol gsungs pas/ des gser ling pa chen po
zhig rnyed pa phul/ de nas gtsang ltag tshal du 'khrungs pa'i lo tsA ba rgya brtson 'grus sengge la bod phrug brgya tsam grogs su btang de rnams la gser ling pa de/ gsil
ma mang du bskur nas spyan 'dren par brdzangs/ zhu yig tu/ khyed kyi thugs rje phyogs ris mi mnga' zhing / /sangs rgyas bstan la thugs ni sem byed na/ /kha ba can 'dir sngon
ni phun tshogs kyang / /deng sang dus na sems can bsod nams nyams/ /de yi stobs kyis bod kyi rgyal po nga / /mya ngam thang la tshad pas gdungs pa na/ /chu yi 'du byed
yid la byed pa ltar/ /nyin dang mtshan du mgon po khyod bsam na/ /bdag la thugs kyis brtse bar mdzad du gsol/ /zhes

bris nas bskur ro/ /de nas rgya brtson sengges bi kra ma la shI lar brtol/ jo bos kyang bod rgyal pos slob gnyer ba zhig brdzangs 'dug zer ba gsan/ gsan ma thag tu bu'i 'du
shes 'khrungs/ de nas rgya brtson sengges jo bo dang mjal te gser ling pa de phul/ bod du byon par zhu ba byas pas/ jo bos bod du 'gro ba la rgyu gnyis yin te/ 'dod pas
gser tshol du'am/ rang bas gzhan gces kyi byang chub sems kyis 'gro ba la/ nga la de gnyis ka med pas mi 'gro gsungs nas gser tshur gtad/ lo tsA bas chos gos kyi gsham la
'jus nas bshums pas kyang ma gnang / de'i res la lo tsA ba'i 'khor rnams phal cher tshad pas gum/ gser bsil ma de zad/ jo bos khyod bod rnams snying re rje gsung / tshur
log gser ling ba rgyal po la gtad/ jo bo spyan ma 'drongs/ lo rgyus snyan du gsol bas/ lo tsA bas dka' ba dang bsdos/ lus srog thed la bor nas byon pa thugs la btags/ jo
bo spyan ma drang pa'i thabs med gsung / khong la de res nag tsho lo tsA bas mngon pa nyan pa'i zhu ba phul bas/ nga slar rgya gar du log nas 'gro bas long mi 'ong gsung
/ 'o na nga 'ang rgya gar du 'gro zhus pas/ khyod rang gi snying khams kyis pher na 'dong gsung / dpon slob lnga drug tsam rgya gar du byon no/ /de'i dus lha bla mas gser
btsal la jo bo spyan drang dgongs/ mtha' 'khob tu gser tshol ba la dmag du ma zhig dang bcas te byon pas/ gar log gis shes nas dmag btang / de dang thug 'thabs pas pham
nas lha btsun rang btson la shor/ gar log gi rgyal pos brtags pas bod kyi rgyal por shes nas btson khang du bcug dar yug gi sku bsdams te 'dug go /lha bla ma 'dzin pa'i
phyir gar log gi dpung song zer ba lha btsun byang chub 'od kyi mched kyis gsan nas/ byang chub 'od kyis rta pa brgya dang bcas te khu bo slog par byon pas/ gar log gi lag
tu thal zin nas ldog ma thub/ dmag gtos che ba khrid nas 'thabs nas lhogs srid de mi bsad mang du 'byung bar yang snang la/ gal te nyid la bar chad byung na jo bo mi 'drongs/
khu bo'ang btson nas mi thon par 'dug dgongs te/ kho la thabs kyis bstun na legs par gzigs nas phan tshun lab sna sbrel ba dang / gar log na re khyod nang

pa sangs rgyas pa'i rgyal po yin pas/ khyod rang gi rgyal khams thams cad mu stegs pa'i lta ba la 'god na bslus ma mi 'dod kyi steng du bya dga' chen po ster/ paNDYi spyan
ma 'dren/ khyod rang nga'i 'og tu zhugs/ de mi byed na gser rgyal por rang dang mnyam pa khyer la shog de nas btang gi zer/ gser sprod pa la gdams nas gser srang brgya khyer
nas bslu bar phyin pas ma btub/ der log nas dbus gtsang gi rab tu byung ba la sde pa brgyad yod de/ gtsang nas lo tshong gnyis/ 'a 'dre gnyis te bzhi/ dbus su klu mes
dang sba rag gnyis/ 'bring tsho dang rma tsho gnyis te bzhir byas pa la sham thabs kyi khral blangs/ bod khams gsum gling dgu 'bangs rnams la rin bsdus/ mnga' ris su gser
bsgrubs pas sku lus byin dang mnyam pa rnyed/ dbu tsam ma rnyed/ de khyer nas lha btsun rang gis blur byon/ lha bla ma rang la'ang gar log gis khyod rang dkon mchog gsum
la skyabs su 'gro ba gtong na nged kyis btson las gtong / de ltar ma yin na lus ril po dang ljid mnyam pa'i gser byung na gtong zer/ skyabs su 'gro ba ni ma btang / gser
rnyed pa la tshegs che bas btson du yun ring du lus/ gar log gis sku'i rtsa sgo mes bsregs so/ /der dbon byang chub 'od bslebs nas gar log la blur thong byas pas/ dbu'i
tshad ma longs rin mi gtong zer/ der lha bla mas gsan nas byang chub 'od la 'phrin btang ba/ khyod kyis bya thabs de las med/ gser de tshos nga ma slu bar rgya gar nas jo
bo spyan drang na rab yin te mi 'drongs/ jo bo'i 'og nas su che ba'i paNDYi ta zhig spyan drongs/ mtho lding la mchod pa chen po gyis/ yab mes kyi lha sa bsam yas sogs
kyi zhig ral gsos zhes bskur byung ba dang / byang chub 'od kyi dgongs pa la da dung gser btsal la slu dgos de la da res khu bo dang mjal na legs par 'dug snyam nas/ gar
log la khu bo dang mjal du chug gsungs pas/ khu bo'i btson khang gi sgo drung du btang bas/ byang chub 'od kyis drung de nas khu bo la bos te/ bka' drin chen po sngon gyi
las thog tu bab pa yin pas/ ngas kho la dmag brgyab nas log na ni skye bo tshan po che 'phung la gtang nas rang re gnyis

po ngan song du 'gro dgos par snang / paNDYi ta gdan ma 'dren par khyed rang nga'i 'og tu 'dug zer ba la ni chos blos btang nas sdig rgyal gyi 'og tu zhugs pa las khyod chos
ldan du gshegs pa drag snyam du bsam/ des na gser khyod rang tsam zhig dgos zer ba la gser btsal bas khyod kyi sku lus dang mnyam pa'i tshad tsam zhig rnyed de khos ma
nyan/ da ngas dbu tsam zhig rnyed pa dang slur 'ong gi de bar du sngon gyi las su sems pa dang / dkon mchog gsum la gsol ba 'debs pa dang / snying po che brang 'og tu bcug
pa'i so nam mdzad dgos pa yin zhes zhus pa dang / khu bo bzhad kyin/ khyod la da gces phrug snum zan ma'i dpags shig yod/ dka' spyad dang snying rus mi nus snyam pa yin
te/ nga rang shi'ang khyod kyis yab mes kyi phyag srol skyong nus par snang / khyod kyi de rnams go ba che/ da des chog nga'i bsam pa la bod 'dir chos khrims shig ma bcos
par nga rang shi na mi rung snyam pa yin te/ da nga na so yar song / 'dir ma shi ba'i dbang du byas na'ang tshe lo bcu tsam e thub yin/ nga'i rtsa sgo mes btsas bsregs
nas dud 'gro lta bur yod/ sngar tshe 'khor ba thog ma med pa nas chos phyir gcig kyang shi ba med/ da lan chos kyi phyir shi na legs pa yin pas/ rgyal po 'di la gser ra ti
gcig dgos kyang mi ster/ gser nga rang tsam rnyed pa shin tu kham che na/ da mgo tsam ga na rnyed/ gser de rnams thams cad rgya gar du khyer la da dung paNDYi ta de spyan
ci drongs gyis/ paNDYi ta chen po'i snyan du'ang / ngas khyod dang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa'i phyir lus srog gar log gi rgyal po la rngan par byin yod pas tshe rabs thams
cad du bdag la thugs rjes 'dzin pa dang / nga'i bsam pa'i gtso bo khyod bod du byon nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar bar byed pa yin pas/ de kho na bzhin du mdzad pa
dang / skye ba 'di'i 'og rol tu nges par khyod dang mjal bar byin gyis brlab tu gsol zhes pa'i 'phrin mdzod cig de ltar lags pas nga blos thong la sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa
la soms shig gsungs/ de skad gsungs pa'i bar la byang chub 'od kyis sgo'i bar la gzigs pas sku lus rnams ni dar gyis bcud/ spyan ni khung na lhung

sngar las rnam pa thams cad 'gyur ba'i sku bung ba tsam du song / de'i khong na'ang bod kyi sems can dang / sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang / jo bo 'ba' zhig sems pa 'o brgyal
bzhin par bzhag ni ma phod/ thabs ni med/ spyan chab dang bcas par yul du log de'i bar la lha bla ma gar log gis shig dong du bcug nas bkrongs/ 'grongs kar/ 'di nas bzung
ste tshe rabs thams cad du/ /chos phyir srog la phangs pa med pa dang / /dkon mchog gsum dang 'bral ba med pa dang / /snying stobs chen pos gzhan don byed par shog /ces
smon lam mdzad/ de nas lha btsun byang chub 'od kyi thugs dgongs khu bo ni grongs/ khong gi thugs dgongs rdzogs par bya ba'i phyir rgya gar nas paNDYi ta spyan 'dren/ khong
gi sku gdung la mchod pa byed/ dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya chen po bya dgos snyam nas/ sku gdung bslus te mchod rten du bzhugs su bcug sku rjes su gser gyi mchod rten bkra
shis sgo mang shig bzhengs/ da jo bo spyan 'dren/ de la bang chen pa'i 'os gzigs pas dge bshes gung thang pa de rgya gar du bzhud pa'i thugs gda' bas 'os snyam/ gung thang
lha btsun gyi gdong byas de'i 'khrungs sar byon/ khong rgya gar nas ma log par snang ste/ mi chos pa rnams la khyed kyi 'dul ba 'dzin pa de rgya gar nas byon byung na
nga la skad thong bya ba'i 'phrin bzhag gung thang pas rgya gar du rgya brtson seng la mngon pa gsan/ lo tsA'ang mkhas par lobs/ chos kyang 'ga' re bsgyur te tshur byon pa
la mi chos pa rnams kyis 'phrin sprad de/ khyod lha btsun pa'i gan du bzhud dgos byas pas der byon/ don ci bdog zhus pas/ gung thang pa gdan gyi gung la bzhag nas bsnyen
bkur bzang po byas te 'di gsung / lags 'dul ba 'dzin pa la zhu ba/ nga'i pha mes rgyal blon byang chub sems dpa' de rnams kyis sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dbu rnyed/ srol
gtod dar zhing rgyas par mdzad pa yin pa la/ dus deng sang bstan pa nyams dmas pa mkhas btsun thams cad shes pa skyo/ jo bo ni spyan ma 'drongs/ de'i 'og ma che ba zhig spyan
'dren dgos pas khyod la zhu ba lags zhes thugs chad pas de skad gsungs/ sngar rgya brtson seng btang ba dang / khu bo gnas skabs ji ltar gyur pa dang / nga'i khu bo
de 'o rgyal/ ngas khu bo bzhag nas yong phod pa/ khu bo de btson dong na bzhugs pa'i nang na'ang sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dang jo bo 'ba' zhig thugs la sems

nged mtha' 'khob kyi sems can ma rig pa rnams kyi snying stobs de 'dra na/ khyod 'gro ba'i skyabs gnas thugs rje can rnams ci tsug song zhes zhus shig da res nga dga' ba dang
/ phyis 'dul ba 'dzin pa dga' bar yang byed do/ /da 'di na gser srang bdun brgya yod/ 'di phar khyer la bdun brgya po 'di bla ma'i phyag tu phul/ nged bod pre ta pu ri
lta bu'i grong khyer na gser lug shig tsam re la'ang dka' las chen po yod pa yin pa la/ da 'di dang lha bla ma ye shes 'od kyis dbu bgyis/ mi nor thams cad yongs su rdzogs
nas yod kyi/ da lan 'di la mgon po bod du ma byon na khyod dam pa rnams kyi thugs rje'ang de ltar bas pas nged kyang bya ba ci bder spyod par bgyi'o/ /khyod 'dul ba 'dzin
pas zhu ba 'di rnams jo bo la zhus nas 'byon du ma bzhed pa'i gzhug mtha' ma la snyan du thegs par gyis shig gsungs nas spyan chab kyis pang khebs dang cog rtse bangs
pa tsam du bshum zhing gsung byon pas/ dge bshes gung thang pas tshig zur tsam yang zhu ma nus/ gsung shin tu bden pa de rnams thos/ chos rgyal de ma mthong yang rnam pa
dran pa dang / khong khu dbon gyi mi nor mang po zad pa rgyus yod pas/ khong khu dbon sdug ches/ nged rnams skyid ches pa dang / lha btsun mi chen po zhig gis de ltar bshums
pa'i stobs kyis lo tsA ba lus 'dar/ mchi mas gdong gang ste lha btsun gyi zhal yang lta mi nus/ de'i stobs kyis lus srog dang / bar gyi dka' tshegs dang / tshe 'di'i
bde skyid gang la'ang ma bsam par 'o lags so zhes dbang med par zhal gyis bzhes so/ /de nas lha btsun gyis 'khor lnga brgya tsam gtong ba'i grabs mdzad pas/ lo tsA bas de
tsam mang lnga tsam gyis chog phar lam tshur lam gyi rgyags dang bcas pa gser du dgos zhus pas/ paNDYi ta la gser thig po gcig la srang bcu drug yod pa/ ling ba gcig la
srang bdun cu/ gser phye bre gang / lo tsA ba la srang bdun/ phar lam gyi brgyags la srang bdun sogs dgos pa thams cad brdzangs te/ lha btsun pas thag ring por skyel thung
mdzad/ dge slong khyod kyis nga'i phyogs su bya ba byas da lan dka' las che na'ang phar byon la don grub pa zhig mdzod/ 'khor nas byas shes bka' drin gzo bar bya zhes
lo tsA ba dpon slob la phyi mig gzigs kyin gshegs/ yang gsung

chen po zhig gis bos nas/ dge bshes lo tsA ba jo bo thugs rje chen po la gsol ba 'debs kyin gshegs pa zhu gsung / bal por nas rgyal phran bi kra ma la shI lar 'gro ba dang
'dzom pas lam la skyon med/ nyi ma rgas khar ganggA'i 'gram du slebs/ gru pas mgron po tshan gcig bcug gru bsdus nas song / skad btang bas/ da res mi thongs phyi res bsu'o
zer/ srod 'khor ba na gru byung na'ang / rgyal po mi che bas sngon la sgrol/ khong rnams lus/ phyogs der mi ni med/ a tsa ra rnams ni spyod pa ngan/ bdud rigs ni chos la
sdang / gser mang po yod pas sngangs/ gab sa dang yib sa med/ ci drag la gya ba'i dus su mnyan pa dkar po zhig gru dang bcas te byung / lo tsA bas khyod gar gshegs byas
pas/ khyod dpon slob bsu ru 'ongs pa yin zer te grus bsgral/ da nam phyed yol/ chu 'khris dang sngo gseb tu nyal na dug sbrul gyi 'jigs pa 'ong / do nub bi kra ma la shI
la'i sgo spe'i 'og tu brtol/ chom rkun pa'i 'jigs pa ye mi yong zer ga shed du song / de nas der phyin te 'di na bod su yod ces lan gsum bos pas/ rgya brtson seng sgo khang
gi steng du bzhugs pas gsan nas bod nga yod/ khyed kun ga nas 'ongs/ nged mnga' ris stod nas 'ongs pa yin byas pas/ 'o na sgo na byis pa yod/ de la khyed rang gi chas
chol gar yang ma 'gro/ do nub de rang du sdod cig nang par mjal lo zer bas de bzhin byas/ sang rgya brtson seng gis rtsad bcad nas mjal/ ci la 'ongs gsung / lo rgyus rnams
zhus pas/ jo bo'i 'og na che ba lta mang po yod de/ de kun gyis bod la phan mi thogs/ jo bo 'di la lhag pa'i thugs rnam dag yod pa yin/ da dung jo bo rang spyan 'dren
dgos/ khyod nga'i slob mar snang ba ngo ma shes/ da 'dir a ti sha gdan 'dren du 'ongs ba skad ma zer slob gnyer la yongs kyis/ gnas brtan shI la A ka ra bya ba yod/ de 'di
na dbang che bas de'i sems gzung / da lta rang song gser srang phyed phul la nged bod nas 'ongs pa yin/ paNDYi ta ni spyan ma drongs/ da khyod kyi zhal snga nas paNDYi
ta spyan drangs pa dang khyad med pa'i slob gnyer cig thugs la 'dogs par zhu zhes zhu ba phul/ de nas kyang rings rings dang blo ma phebs pa ye ma byed par slob gnyer gyis
la ngal gsos/ de nas 'o cag thabs mkhas pos jo bo chags phebs pa'i dus su zhu ba byed pa yin gsungs pa bzhin byas so/ /

de dus der jo bo ma bzhugs/ rten khyad par can la mchod pa 'bul du gshegs par 'dug de nas byon dus gzhan kun gyis gsangs/ sprang phrug gcig gis a ti sha zer nas phyi la brgyugs
pas ngo shes te/ lo tsA ba yus kyis dngangs mchi ma 'don zhing phyi la brgyugs pas khye re bzhugs/ bod kyi tshe dang ldan pa bden/ mchi ma ma 'don khyod bod kyi rgyal
blon 'bangs dang bcas pa la kho bo snying thag ring ba min/ 'di ltar na so rgas/ lde mig mang po 'dzin dgos byung / da dung khyed blos ma btang bar yod pa yin gyi/ dkon
mchog la gsol ba thob/ de skad gsungs pa tsam gyis kyang re che ba dang yus pa'i stobs kyis mig mchi mas gang zhing gtam ma thon/ gsung chen pos ngan pa ci zer gsungs pas/
bred nas mchi ma sangs/ de nas nyin gcig dben pa'i dus su rgya nas shog gsungs jo bo'i gzims khang du khrid/ dbu sngas mgo na thugs dam gyi maNDYal yod pa'i khar gser
ling pa de bzhag gser gsil ma rnams tshom bur bkod nas jo bo la phul te/ rgya bod kyi lo rgyus/ nga yang / bod kyi rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' des tshe dang ldan pa spyan
'dren du btang nas gda' bas/ na ning skad mi gsung bar bod la thugs rjes gdags par zhu 'tshal zhus pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas/ bod kyi rgyal po byang chub sems dpa' yin par
'dug byang chub sems dpa'i bka' yang bcag tu mi btub/ rgyal po de la ngo'ang mnong bar yod/ nga'i phyir du khong gi mi nor mang po chud zos la song gsungs spyan chab nyil
mdzad de byon par zhal gyis bzhes/ der jo bo'i mdzad pa'i 'phro b.ratal ba la zla ba brgyad tsam sgug sdod byas/ 'byon par zug dus nag tsho la gnas brtan shI la a ka ras
jo bo lo gsum na 'khor ba'i chad byas te/ jo bo dpon slob nyi shu tsam tshur byon khar/ gser rnams cha bzhir byas te/ gcig bla ma rnams la phul/ gcig rdo rje gdan du mchod
pa/ gcig bi kra ma shI la'i dge 'dun la/ cha gcig rgyal po la gtad de jo bo nyid kyi shul gzigs par gsol te rim pas byon/ bal por rgyal pos zhabs nas bteg thang bi ha
ra'i gtsug lag khang brtsigs/ lha btsun pa'i bsu bas shing kun tu slebs/ der rgya brtson seng grongs/ de nas rim pas mnga' ris su phebs/ mchod yon mjal bas shin

tu gus te/ 'jig rten gyi mgon po bod du byon no zhes snyan pas khyab/ lo chen paNDYi ta pas nga rang yon tan che dgongs yod kyang / lha btsun gyis spyan drangs pa yin pas zhabs
tog byed dgos snyam/ mtho lding du spyan drangs/ der rgyud sde bzhi'i lha rnams rgyud sde'i go rim bzhin thog so'i mtho dman la byas yod pa gzigs te/ so so la mngon
rtogs dang mthun pa'i bstod pa re mdzad/ gdan la bzhugs pa na lo tsA bas bstod pa de sus mdzad zhus pas/ kho bo rang gi 'phral du'o gsung / des lo tsA ba 'jigs zhum song
/ der khyod kyis chos ci dang ci shes gsung / mkhyen tshul zhus pas/ khyod lta bu bzhugs bzhin du nga bod du yong mi dgos par 'dug pa la gsung / de thams cad gang zag gcig
gis nyams su len na ji ltar byed gsungs/ so so'i gzhung nas bshad pa ltar byed zhus pas/ lo tsA ba rul nga bod du yong dgos pa 'dug gsungs te gsang sngags 'phrul gyi me
long bya ba'i bshad pa mdzad/ lo chen thugs ches/ de nas gsung rab du ma bsgyur/ de nas slar bal yul thang bi ha ra'i rab gnas la bskor cig gshegs/ slar mnga' ris su phebs
nas/ spu rangs kyi rgyal zhing zhes par bzhugs dus 'brom ston phebs/ de gdung rus bzher/ yab rta gsum bzher/ yum khu lto bza' lan gcig pa gnyis kyi sras su 'khrungs/ yul
stod lung phu/ chung chung nas jo bo bse btsun lho bal du byon nas log pa'i phyag phyir 'brang 'dod/ tshong pa dang bsdebs khong bzhugs sar brtol/ slob gnyer legs par
mdzad/ nye logs na paNDYi ta sgra'i tsher ma zhes bya ba zhig las bi brta mang po bslabs/ da lta rgya gar na su che dris pas/ nged rgya gar na yod dus nA ro pa che ba yin/
da lta rgyal rigs las rab tu byung ba'i dge slong dI paM ka ra shrI dznyyA na bya ba yod pas/ de da lta bzhugs na khong che bar 'ong gsung / mtshan thos pas mos pa chen
po skyes/ tshe 'di la mjal ba srid dam snyam pa byung / jo bo mnga' ris su phebs pa'i skad cha thos nas bse btsun la zhus pas/ khong dgyes bzhin chas dang bcas te gnang
/ phan yul du zhang chen po la dge bsnyen zhu sa yin pas phyag skyal du byon/ ka ba shAkya dbang phyug dang yang mjal/ nga paNDYi ta mjal du 'gro /dbus su spyan 'drong pa
srid na yi ge 'bul bas

khyod mi chen rnams kyis mdun ma mdzad de 'ong dgos zhus byang lam brgyud 'ong ba jo bos mkhyen/ nga'i u pa si ka sleb ces dgyes dgyes mdzad thugs yid 'dres so// // ! gsum
pa dbus gtsang du 'byon tshul ni/ 'brom gyis dbus kyi phyogs na lha sa bsam yas sogs gtsug lag khang dge 'dun stong phrag mang po yod pa'i bsngags pa brjod pas/ jo bo'i zhal
nas tshangs par spyod pa grangs mang po de tsam rgya gar na'ang med/ dgra bcom pa'ang yod mchi gsung phyogs gtad de phyag mdzad/ des spobs pa rnyed dbus su 'byon par
gsol/ kho bo dge 'dun gyi bka' byung na 'gro gsungs/ lo chen la lo tsAr 'gro dgos gsungs pas/ dbu dung lta bu gzigs phul mtshams kyi dam bca' mdzad de mkha' spyod du gshegs
kyang zer/ gshegs nas gdung bya mo'i sgo nga tsam gsum byung ste/ de yal zer ro/ /der dbus su/ shing rta'i dbyibs 'dra 'dzam gling gi sogs zhu 'phrin brdzangs pa ka ba
la 'phrod/ des do dam cher bgyis rgyal gyi zhang chen po la sogs la gros zhus nas jo bo gdan 'dren du 'byon par brtsams pa'i tshe khu ston khong rang yi ge na mi 'dug pas
ma dgyes nas sngon la ngas mjal ba zhig bya snyam brgyugs/ des gzhan rnams la lcags bcug pa bzhin song / dbus gtsang gi mi chen thams cad dpal thang du phebs/ skyid grong
du sngar zhu ba song bas jo bo dpon g.yog kyang der phebs/ bod ston rnams zhwa sna ring na bza' ber dang rtar bcas pa rgyang nas gzigs pas/ jo bos u pa si ka mi ma yin
mang po byung gsungs dbu gtums/ de nas khong rnams kyi rta babs/ zhwa dang ber bzhag snam sbyar gsol ba sha stag tu byas nas byung bas/ jo bo mnyes nas dge 'dun la spyi
phyag mdzad/ de nas bod ston rnams log jo bo dpon g.yog rim gyis 'byon par byas te/ lho byang myang rong dbus kyi sol nag thang po che bsam yas sogs su 'phrin las bskyangs
nas/ 'brom gyis zhang ston la yi ge btang / khong gis snye thang du spyan drangs/ der bzhugs gdan chags sa'i ma mo mdzad/ bur du dgon pa ba la sogs pa'i sgom grwa btsugs/
rngog legs shes lha sa dang / rngog byang chub 'byung gnas kyis yer pa/ ka ba chen pos 'phan yul du spyan drangs/ slar snye thang du log ste sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin
po che

legs par bskyangs so/ /mthar jo bos 'brom la khyod kyi gnas gzhi chung ngu zhig brtsigs/ nga'i bstan pa khyod la gtod pas zung gsung / de la 'brom gyis/ spyir bdag 'khos ka
chung bye brag tu rten dge bsnyen du song nas bya ba chen po sgrub mi nus zhus pas/ jo bos bslabs pa bzhin du gyis/ nga rang gis byin gyis rlob pas sems khral mi dgos gsung
/ 'brom la rgyal tshab bkod/ dgung lo bdun cu rtsa gsum la dga' ldan du gshegs/ sku gdung zhugs la phul ba'i dus gser gyi char bab/ jo bos bod du lo bcu gsum bstan pa
bskyangs so/ /'brom gyis shul 'dir ji ltar bya snyam thugs las che ba la/ ka ba shAkya dbang phyug de ma thag tu byon nas gdung rnams bzhu/ rngog la sogs pa bu chen rnams
la 'tsham par bkye/ rten dang thugs dam gyi lha rnams 'brom la gtad/ khu rngog 'gar dge rnams kyis gdung la dngul gyi gdung khang legs pa re'ang grub/ ka bas do dam mdzad
nas 'dad dang shul du gtsug lag khang brtsigs/ 'brom gyis jo bos skyong ba'i tshogs pa rnams phyag phyir khrid de stod lung du byon nas gnam gyi bye ma lung du thog cig
bzhugs/ de'i tshe 'dam pa'i gtso bo rnams kyis kyang gros byas/ 'brom ra sbreng du spyan 'dren par thag bcad/ 'phrang kha ber chung gis kyang zhu bas slebs nas me pho spre'u
lo gsar la ra sbreng du phebs gnas gzhi btab/ de rting nga 'jig rten blos gtong gsungs nas chos gsung ba ma gtogs 'jig rten gyi 'dun ma mi mdzad/ dgung lo drug cu pa
la mya ngan las 'das/ 'di ni snying rje padma dkar po'i mdo las dge bsnyen chos 'phel zhes lung bstan pa de yin par kun bden/ 'tshims pas 'phags pa'i gnas brtan bcu drug
gi nye gnas dharma ta/ de dag gi gdugs tshod la bab pa na snang ba mtha' yas mdun gyi nam mkhar byon nas bskul ba'i dge bsnyen ni 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs te 'brom/ 'od
dpag med jo bo yin no gsung / de ltar jo bo la bod rang du'ang slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ba'i sras kyi dam pa 'brom yin no/ /de la'ang slob ma mang yang / phu
chung ba dang / spo to ba/ spyan snga ba gsum la sku mched gsum zhes grags te/ phu chung bas tshogs pa ma bskyangs/ /spo to ba la rgyun du tshogs pa stong lhag pa re rjes
su 'brang / gzhan gyis gnod na'ang spyir dge

slong khas nyen/ bye brag tu byang chub sems dpa' khas nyen gsungs nas gnod lan ye mi mdzad/ lam sgom pa gtso bor 'don/ mdo sde rgyan dang byang sa/ bslab btus dang spyod 'jug
skyes rabs dang ched du brjod pa'i tshoms drug nan tan du 'chad pas/ de dag la bka' gdams gzhung drug de nas brgyud pa la bka' gdams gzhung pa zer ro/ /slob ma gtsang
na rab snang gnyis/ byang phag gnyis/ gnyal gyi glang gnyos gnyis/ dol gyi 'be rog gnyis rnams la chen po brgyad/ glang ri thang pa dang dbus kyi shar pa chen po gnyis la
dbus kyi ka chen zer ro/ /glang ri thang pas glang thang btab/ tshogs pa nyis stong tsam rgyun du 'dus/ sha ra ba chen po thugs rab che bas bka' 'gyur thugs su bzhugs par
grags/ tshogs pa sum stong drug brgya tsam 'dus/ bshad pa'ang gzhung lugs chen po kun la mdzad/ slob ma 'gro don nus pa mang po zhig byung ba'i gtum ston gyis snar thang
btab/ khyad par bya 'chad ka ba la blo sbyong gi bka' babs/ spyan snga ba tshul khrims 'bar ni 'brom rnal 'byor ba gnyis/ dgon pa ba chen po rnams la brten bsam gtan grub
pas rdzu 'phrul che/ lta ba la 'gran du med/ 'brom la sngags kyi man ngag mang po gsan/ lo dang smyug rum du bzhugs/ slob ma 'gro phan nus pa bsam gyis mi khyab/ gtso
bo bya yul ba gzhon du 'od kyis bya yul gyi gnas gzhi btab/ grwa pa nyis stong re byung ba'i nang nas ting nge 'dzin skyes pa lnga brgya/ dge bshes jag rtse 'chab brgya
dang bcu/ de dag gi nang nas phyi'i chen po dgu bar gyi chen po brgyad/ nang thugs kyi sras gsum zer ro/ /jo bo'i dngos slob dgon pa ba chen po ni/ rus 'dzeng / mtshan dbang
phyug rgyal mtshan/ khams nas byon te jo bo myang stod nyan tshor phebs dus mjal dar yug brgya phul nas sgom gnang bar zhus pas/ jo bo'i zhal nas nga'i zan zo gsung ba
la/ bdag rang la brgyags yod zhus pas/ khyod nga'i zan za na gdam ngag ster/ de lta min na mi ster gsung ba la/ de nas bzung ste jo bo'i mchod gnas mdzad/ legs par bsgoms
pas gegs mang po byung ba jo bos bsal/ mngon par shes pa rgya chen po mnga'/ de la slob ma nye gnas 'grogs yun ring ba rgya yon bdag yin/ gzhan sne'u zur pa/ zhang ka
ma la/ gnyan lha mo ba/ 'bro ko de lung bzhi la dgon gyi

bu bzhir grags/ rgyas lcags ri gong kha btab/ sne'u zur pa mtshan ye shes 'bar/ gzhon nu nas ting nge 'dzin rang 'khrungs/ de'i gtam sgom pa shes rab dbang phyug gis dgon pa
ba la zhus pas/ kho'i de dge ba'i bshes gnyen gyis zin na legs par 'ong ste ma zin na smyon par 'gro gsung ba des bskyar bas de res la ma thon/ phyis ra sbreng du byon/
dgon pa ba bsten/ jo bo'i gdams pa ji lta ba gnang / sne'u zur btab/ ting nge 'dzin dang rdzu 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab/ rje btsun mi la dang mtshan thos pa'i grogs po yin/
tshogs pa stong tsam re 'dus/ slob ma 'gro don nus pa mang du byung ba'i/ sgyer sgom khu dbon/ sgyer sgom bya yul ba'i yang slob ma yin/ de'i dbon po ni rgya ma'i sangs
rgyas dbon ston du grags pa byang chub sems dpa' skal ldan shing rtar singgha la'i dgra bcom pas lung bstan pa de'o/ /de'i rgya ma'i gtsug lag khang btab/ 'phrin las mtha'
klas/ de'ang jo bo bod du byon nas bla chen gyi brgyud 'dzin kun kyang jo bo'i zhal slob tu song ba'i stobs kyis gnas gzhi phal cher bka' gdam ngag tu smra bas bka'
gdams par grags pa der song / de dang dkar brgyud rin po che dar ba'i dus rab tu byung ba thams cad de gnyis la 'dus pa 'dra zhing / gzhan rnams nyung bas/ snar thang bcom
ral thugs mug ste/ sangs rgyas bstan pa bka' phyag sprin gyis bsgribs/ /zhes gsungs so/ /gzhan jo bo'i slob ma rngog legs shes ni yar 'brog sgog mkhar du 'khrungs/ 'bring
ye shes yon tan las bsnyen par rdzogs/ sde snod slob pa'i phyir du khams su bse btsun gyi rtsar byon/ 'brom yar byon pa'i phyi lo log lha sar bshad grwa btsugs/ jo bo
dang mjal/ chos kyang du ma bsgyur/ de'i skabs jo bos gsang phu'i phyogs su phyag mdzad/ byams 'jam dbyangs rtsod pa mdzad kyi 'dug bshad grwa btsugs na shin tu legs par
'ong gsungs pa khong gis thos nas/ de gzhan la mi gsung ba zhu/ bdag gis dgon pa 'debs pa lags zhus pas gsang phur thogs/ phyis de la dgon pa btab/ rang gi gcung po chos
skyabs kyi sras shig rab tu byung mtshan blo ldan shes rab tu btags/ 'dis mdo sde rgyan zhogs rgyugs gcig la zin pa yin zer/ dgung lo bcu bdun tshun khu bo rang gis sgra
la sogs pa legs par bslabs/

de nas kha cher brdzangs/ lo bcu bdun lho bal du bzhugs nas gsan sbyong mdzad/ bal po'i mtha' 'khob zhig tu slob dpon chen po Dombi he ru ka mngon sum du gzigs nas mkha' spyod
du 'dong gsungs nas stag gi 'phongs steng du bskyon nam mkha' mthon por slebs pa dang / bod kyi thad gzhan pas ngoms nag ba mun pa'i gling lta bur gzigs nas ma gi gang
lags zhus pas bod rmongs pa'i gling ngo gsungs/ brtse ba mi bzod pa 'khrungs/ mkha' spyod du mi 'gro bar der 'chad nyan btsugs te/ blo gros kyi snang bas de dag nyin mor
bya'o snyam dam bcas nas slob dpon la gsol bas legs so gsungs te sngar gyi sar babs zhes gro lung pa'i gsung las byung / des bod du phebs nas gtso bor gsang phu dang /
gzhan chos par mdzad de lo bcu bdun du 'chad nyan mdzad pa'i slob ma gsung rab kun la mkhas pa'i gro lung pa blo gros 'byung gnas/ phar phyin la mkhas pa 'bre chen po shes
rab 'bar/ tshad ma la mkhas pa gangs pa she'u/ dbu ma la mkhas pa khyung rin chen grags/ sku dngos kyi gdan sa pa zhang tshe spong ba sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa byon/ des
phar phyin rgya gar gyi paNDYi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa'i lugs bzhin Tikka mdzad/ tshad ma la rnam 'grel rgyan bshad/ rnam nges/ mngon rtogs rgyan/ spyod 'jug sogs la Tikka
mdzad pas dbus gtsang du legs par dar/ khyad par gangs pa she'u dang khyung gnyis ka'i dngos slob stod lung rgya dmar ba byang chub grags/ dbu tshad la de'i slob ma mang
yang phywa pa chos kyi sengge gtso bo/ des phar phyin sogs gro lung pa dang / spyod phyogs zhang la gsan/ gzhung lugs kun la bsdus pa re/ khyad par tshad ma la yid kyi
mun sel zhes pa bod kyi blo gros kyi padmo 'byed pa la nyi ma lta bu de brtsams/ 'chad nyan legs par mdzad pa'i slob ma seng chen brgyad/ seng chung brgyad/ jo sras mi bzhi
grub thob mi gsum sogs mtha' yas so/ /de phyin nas gzhung lugs kun spom yor du mi 'jog par dpyad bdar zhib mor byed pa 'di byung / de nas ring zhig tu spyi ma Tikka dar/
de las phyi rabs rang 'dir spyi ma thal dar/ gzhung lugs kyi tshugs ci bder bzhag pas da lta jo bo mtshan nyid pa rnams thal ma bsdus shig la dbu bsnyung ngo / /'bre'i
slob ma ar/ de'i slob ma khu dang dkar chung ba/ de'i slob ma zhang g.ye ba/

de'i slob ma gnyal zhig gzhan de phya ba'i yang slob rgyun de la bu dgur grags pa byung ba'i bzang rings kyis khro phu/ phu thang dar dkon gyis stod lung dang yar klungs/ gtsang
pa gru gus zhwa lu/ 'u yug pa bsod nams sengge sa skya/ khong gis 'jam pa'i dbyangs kyi sprul pa'i sku sa skya paNDYi ta kun dga' rgyal mtshan la rnam 'grel gsan de
bshad pas/ da lta'i tshad ma ba thams cad kyi thug sar gyur pa yin/ bo dong rin rtses brag ram du/ 'jam gsar pas rkyang 'dur du/ 'di rgya nag ri bo rtse lngar byon zer ba
'jam dbyangs mgon po dang nor ba yin/ skyel nag grags sengges snar thang du btsugs pa'i slob ma skyi ston grags 'bum/ de'i slob ma bcom ldan ral gri dang / de'i slob ma
'jam sgeg dpon slob de gnyis kyi bka' 'gyur dang bstan 'gyur gang rnyed bzhengs/ rgya 'ching ru pas snye thang bde ba can btab ste/ gtsang pa jo brtan ma gtogs pa gnyal
zhig gi bu rnams kyis bshad grwa legs par bskyangs/ khro phu ba'i bshad rgyun bu ston la 'khril/ des zha lur bskyangs shing / de la g.yag phrug sangs rgyas dpal gyis btugs/
des sa skya dga' ldan gyi bdag mdzad/ bu dol gyi slob ma nya dbon kun dga' dpal sogs la red mda' ba gzhon nu blo gros kyis btugs/ de'i sa skya'i brag dmar bzung 'gran
bshad mdzad pa'i stobs kyis mdo slob 'dod thams cad der tshogs pas kun sa skya par song / g.yag pa la slob ma mang yang mchog tu gyur pa rgyal mo rong pa mtshan shAkya rgyal
mtshan shes bya kun rig tu grags pa de yin/ des nA lendra btab kyang bshad grwa ma byung / khong gi slob ma mkhyen rab grags bzang gis bi lung / kun mkhyen don yod dpal
bas gser mdog can btab/ de paNDYi ta chen po shAkya mchog ldan gyis bskyangs pas mkhas pa'i 'byung khungs su gyur/ kun mkhyen chen po byams chen rab 'byams pas skyed tshal
btab/ 'di mes ston tshon po la mar pas lung bstan pa de yin pa la nor/ gnas gzhi bting nas mar pa byon te bag tsam mthos 'dug gsungs pa de la ba thor thogs/ ma 'ongs
pa 'debs par zhus pas kun mkhyen sangs rgyas 'phel du 'khrungs pa yin zer/ 'di 'chad nyan mkhas pas slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab

pa thon/ de'i nang nas mus chen sems dpa' chen pos sa skya pa'i mi gcig po zhes bsngags pa kun mkhyen go bo las thub bstan go gnyis/ sde bdun pa bstan pa rab gsal gyis ra ba
smad/ mkhas pa'i dbang po 'bum phrag gsum pa byams pa chos grub kyis gnyan yod byar gshongs/ gzhung brgya bas chos 'khor lhun po btab pa sogs legs par dar ro/ /gdan sa
'jam dbyangs chos rjes gzung / red mda' ba'i slob ma 'gran zla med par bsngags pa tsong kha pa chen po/ rtsod pa'i khyu mchog dar ma rin chen snga mas 'brog ri bo dga' ldan
rnam par rgyal ba'i gling btab/ thams cad du snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen par grags shing btsun pa'i snyan pas 'phrin las che/ phyi ma'ang de'i mdo'i brgyud 'dzin du
song bas rjes 'jug rnams de la bsngags pa che'ang / kho bos bltas na 'brom ston gyi sprul par grags pa dge 'dun grub/ 'dis bkra shis lhun po btab/ sprul pa'i sku rim par
byon nas dge ldan pa'i bstan pa bskyangs pas tsong kha pa'i slob ma la 'di lhag go /de'ang rong ston dang rgyal tshab dar ma rin chen gnyis gsang phur rtsod/ rgyal rnga
rong ston gyis brdungs/ de nas rong po'i slob rigs rnams sa skya pa/ tsong kha pa'i slob ma rnams dge ldan pa zhes gnyis su song ba 'di byung zhes grags la/ g.yag gzhon
ma byon phan bod du 'dul grwa/ mngon grwa/ mtshan nyid pa zer lugs tha dad du byed do/ /dbu ma thal 'gyur ba'i srol ni bod du jo bos gtod mod kyang / gzhung rnams la de nas
brgyud pa'i 'chad nyan ma dar/ 'phan yul du pa tshab stod smad gnyis yod pa'i stod par 'khrungs pa nyi ma grags zhes pas gzhon nu nas kha cher byon/ paNDYi ta sadzdza
na dang / dza ya a nanta sogs la gtugs shing / lo nyi shu rtsa gsum du gzhung lugs mtha' dag dang / khyad par dbu ma la sbyangs/ 'phan yul du log pa la gdul bya ni che nas
dge ba'i bshes gnyen sha ra bas bdag rkyen mdzad de/ rang gi grwa pa mang po dbu ma slob tu brdzangs pa nas grags thon/ rtsa 'jug bzhi gzhung phran 'grel pa dang bcas pa
bsgyur/ phyis ra mo cher paNDYi ta ka na ka warma dang lhan cig dag par bcos/ 'chad nyan mdzad pa'i slob ma gtsang pas rbos/ rma bya

byang chub ye shes/ dar yon tan grags/ zhang thang sag pa/ phya pa'i seng chen rma bya byang brtson gyis pa tshab rang dang rang gi khu bo rma bya byang yes la gtugs/ zhang
thang sag pas thang sag btab/ da lta'i dbu ma'i bshad rgyun de la thug byams chos lnga ka lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab dang / btsan kha bo che gnyis sadzdza na gsan mnyam
yin kyang bshad lugs mi mthun/ btsan gyi lo rgyus la theg chen rgyud bla ma rtsa 'grel/ chos chos nyid rnam 'byed gnyis paNDYi ta gzhan la ma grags/ mai tri pas mchod rten
zhig gi ser kha nas 'od 'byung gi 'dug nas gzigs pas dpe gnyis thon/ de rje btsun ma pham pa la gsol ba btab pas sprin gyi mthongs su byon te/ de gnyis legs par gnang
/ mai tri pas paNDYi ta dga' ba'i grags pa la bshad/ des sprang po'i cha byad kyis kha cher byon/ sadzdza nas de ngo mtshar can du gzigs nas bsnyen bkur byas/ gzhung gnyis
po zhus/ dpe'ang kha yar bris nas mkhas pa dznyyA na shrI la sogs la phul/ btsan kha po che grwa pa mngon shes kyi mkhan bu/ sadzdza na la nga rgas pas chos mang po mi
lobs/ bcom ldan 'das byams pa'i chos la 'chi chos byas pas/ de'i bshad pa yang dag pa zhig gnang ba zhu zhus pas/ sadzdza nas lo tsA ba gzung dga' ba'i rdo rje la bcol nas
btsan kha bo che la gdam pa dang bcas pa gnang ngo zer ro/ /btsan gyis yar stod brag rgya btab/ dge bshes lcang ra ba sogs la bshad do// // ! de ltar mtshan nyid kyi 'chad
nyan byung ba rags pa tsam brjod nas/ da ni sngags kyi tshul ji ltar dar ba la/ sngon 'gyur ba'i rgyud sde phyi ma gsum gyi glegs bam rnams bstan pa bsnubs dus sngags
'chang khyim pa'i rten can rnams kyis gtsigs byas/ phyis bstan pa'i me ro langs pa'i dus dge ba'i bshes gnyen rnams la phul bas dpe sngon gyi dkar chag dang mthun par byung
la 'chad nyan gyi rgyun ni chad do/ /de dus kyi bla med rnams la rnying ma zhes bya/ de rgyas par ni gter du sbas pa yin/ rags tsam ni so so'i dbon dang slob mas bshad
pas 'jam dpal sku/ padma gsung / yang dag thugs/ bdud rtsi yon tan/ phur pa 'phrin las/ ma mo rbod gtong / dmod pa drag sngags bdun gyi rgyud man ngag gi rigs sngon nas
da lta'i bar du byung / lhag par gnubs sangs rgyas rin po che sgrags su 'khrungs/ gnubs nam mkha' snying po'i tsha bo/ slob

dpon padma sogs la thug bal po'i rgyal po ba su dha ras rjes su gzung / yul de'i dpon sangs rgyas ye shes la sras gnyis yod pa 'bangs kyis ngo log rje'u dang khengs kyis 'khrugs
pa la grongs/ yab tshan rnams thor/ khong gi mthus sgrags grong bdun cu brlag par byas/ 'khrug pa 'di khong gis bal por glang dar bsgral nus pa'i mthu slob tu byon/
de yan sngags pa dkar po/ de nas sngags nag hU~M shi phaTa? 'gyel ba zhig tu gyur/ tshur log dus glang dar bsad zin bsgral ma dgos/ khong rang gi dgra tsho kha phung la
btang / des thugs skyo ba la phor bldab rtsis/ gtsang rong du so ye shes dbang phyug dang phrad/ sos bzhugs zhus/ khong gis grogs po spa skor/ sru legs pa'i sgrol ma gnyis
la sbran/ ltag tu dgon pa mdzad nas bzhugs te/ sa la phur pa/ spa sgor la bdud rtsi/ sru la yang dag bshad/ de dus khu lung yon tan rgya mtsho shwa ba shor nas ma sod pa
ltogs chad 'dzom pa zhig dgon par byung lto slong pas/ nang du btang zas byin nas lo rgyus dris pas rus gnubs su 'dug 'di dang nga nye bar 'dug dgongs/ 'o cag nye bar 'dug
ngas slob gnyer slob/ rngon pa bshol gsungs pas kho'ang dad pa skyes/ rta sga dang bcas pa phyag rten du btang / slob dpon gyi thugs la btags bsam phur gshin gsum gyi
gdam ngag zab tshad gnang / khu lung pas drin gzor gser mang po 'bul snyam byang gi brag rar gser rdol ba gsan nas 'byon pa'i gnang ba zhus pas/ jo bo nas nga rgas gser
gyi dgos pa med ma 'gro gsung rung nan byas te byon/ de'i shul du jo bo la grongs rtags byung / gdam ngag 'phro tshar ba mdzad/ gnubs yon tan rgya mtsho'i chos skal gru gu
dmar nag tu gtums nas stag sgro gzig sgror bcug ste so la gtad nas/ 'di khu lung pa la gtod cig gsungs te gshegs/ de tsa na khu lung pa rang gi rmi lam na/ jo bo byon nas
nga tshe'i dus byas zin/ la 'ur yul du song zer/ mnal sad pa dang snying ma dga' ste 'phral yul du 'ongs/ so dang phrad nas dris pas grongs zer/ nga la zhal chems 'dra
med dam byas pas/ yod de sngon la spur gyi rtsar song zer/ der phyin gser spur la gtor bshums brgyal/ de'i snang ba la jo bo byon nas nga la mya ngan ma byed/ khyod rang
gi chos rnams so la gtad yod/ sos bsha' ma byed byed mi 'dra/ kho'i 'og khang gi ka gzhu

la bkal nas yod bya ba byung / rta bzang po zhon nas phyin/ sos khyim du bos/ phyin tsa na ji lta bar 'dug nas/ de rta la bkal te bros pa sos bdas pas ma slebs/ jo bo 'di gtsang
rong du rgya zhang khrom du 'khrungs rang gis chos sbas pa bton no/ /rgyud kyi bshad rgyun ma chad pa ni sgyu 'phrul gsang ba snying po'i skor te/ bi ma las rma rin
chen mchog des rin chen gzhon nu dang gye re mchog skyong gnyis la/ de gnyis kyis dar rje dang zhang rgyal yon la bshad nas brgyud pa dang / bi ma las gnyags dznyyA na ku
mA ra dang sog po dpal gyi ye shes/ de gnyis kyis gnubs sangs rgyas ye shes rin po che/ des so ye shes dbang phyug spa sgor blon chen 'phags/ dan yon tan mchog sru legs
pa'i sgrol ma/ sras kyi dam pa yon tan rgya mtsho lnga la gdams pa'i chos skor thams cad tshang ba yon tan rgya mtsho/ de la sras padma dbang rgyal dang ye shes mtsho/ dang
po'i sras 'jam dpal/ de'i sras lha rje ye shes gzungs/ rje mi la'i bla ma de'o/ /yon tan rgya mtsho yab sras dang so ye shes dbang phyug gsum ka'i slob ma myang sher
chog des myang ye shes 'byung gnas/ de'i slob ma zur po che shAkya 'byung gnas/ 'dis dge gong gi ce shAkya mchog la bdud rtsi/ tho 'bar nam mkha' sde la mdo dang spar khab/
myang stod kyi 'bre khro chung la rdzogs chen dang lam/ 'ching phu'i rog shAkya 'byung gnas la yang dag de sogs mkhas pa mang po bsten/ sgrub pa'i rtags thon/ bshad nyan
legs par mdzad/ 'bangs rtse mo bzhi lkog dang lnga/ sgom chen brgya rtsa brgyad la bshad/ de'i nang nas lta dgongs kyi rtse mor gyur pa zur chung shes rab grags/ brag
rgya bo dgu 'dus kyi rtser bsgrub pa mdzad pas bde gshegs rgya bo zer/ de la slob ma ka bzhi gdung brgyad/ phyam bcu drug gral ma sum cu rtsa gnyis/ sgom chen mi gnyis/ yul
po che gcig dkyus pa mi gnyis/ sta gur mi gnyis/ go chod mi gsum la sogs du ma byung bas/ so zur gnubs gsum sngags pa'i rgyal po yin zer ba 'di byung / ding sang gi bar
du dar ro/ /man ngag rdzogs pa chen por grags pa la/ sems sde/ klong sde/ man ngag gi sde gsum/ sems sde ni lnga bai ro tsa na dang / bcu bi ma la nas/ klong sde bai ro
tsa na/ man ngag gi sde ni snying thig ces grags shing / bi ma la las byung / de'i slob ma myang

ting 'dzin bzang po las brgyud de bod khams su dar ro/ /de las rma rin chen mchog gnyags dznyyA na ku mA ra/ gnubs sangs rgyas ye shes gsum las bka' ma shas cher byung bas/
'gos kyis rnying ma khong gsum gyi brtsams chos yin zer ba 'di byung ba yin/ de la bod rnams rnying ma yang dag pa min zer ba la sngags ma dag zer te/ rgya skad oM la ring
