po med ces zer nas oM la 'a btags pa la skyon 'dogs te/ rgya skad oM rang ring po yin pas ring po med smra ba rang 'khrul/ de ring por shes par bya ba la 'a btags pas
skyon ci'ang med/ rgya skad sor bzhag na auM sogs zhugs pa la sna ru nyis brtsegs las mi 'byung rgyu la/ de bod du klog pa la go'u ta ma'am/ ko'u shi ka sogs sngon gyi lo
tsA ba mkhas pa dag gis bkod pa lta bu/ yang ma mo'i rgyud du nyid zhi mu khal zhes gsungs/ de la rgya min bod min zer skyon gtong ste/ sngags thams cad legs sbyar gyi skad
min/ sha za dang zur chag rang bzhin skad kyang yod pa la ci'ang ma bsams par smras pa'i skyon yin/ dper na bal po'i longs sku sing zer ba lta bu dang khyad ci yod/ de'i
longs sku de bod skad ni min/ ghu ru/ dha ki sogs kyang u rgyan 'gro lding ba'i skad la de ltar yod cing / dzo gi skad gyong po dag kyang mngon sum sgrog dper na bod
skad gcig la khams pas smras na gyong ba lta bu yin/ lo tsA gsum pos byas pa'i shes byed yod na des chog sangs rgyas dang mnyam pa'i rig 'dzin yin/ lar rnying ma'i rgyud
rnams rig 'dzin rnams kyis 'khrugs bsdebs/ gab pa phyung bas kha gsal/ gsar ma'i rnams lung de khar bzhag pas kha dam pa yin/ rgyud rnam dag yin min don ci ston brjod dgos/
de nas bskyed rdzogs sangs rgya ba'i lam ston pa la khyad med pas cal brgyugs kyi rjes su mi 'brang 'tshal lo/ /gter snga shos gra pa dang rags sha phyis mnga' bdag myang
nyi ma 'od zer/ chos dbang sogs mang po zhig gis bton/ rnam par dpyad na ngo mtshar ba kho na bas/ gter nas chos tshad ma ma don smra ba'ang rigs pa ma yin no// // !
lo chen rin chen bzang pos yo ga rtsal du bton/ zangs dkar lo tsA ba dang shes rab bla mas kyang legs par bshad/ dang po gnyis kyi lugs rgyun phyis bu ston gyis gsal bar
mdzad/ bya spyod rgyud re tsam 'chad pa dang /

sgrub thabs kyi yi ge shin tu mang ngo / /gzhan lo chen gyis gsang 'dus bde mchog sogs gsang sngags mang du bstan/ nag tshos kyang jo bo dang kha che A kA ra siddhi sogs la
gsan/ gsang 'dus sogs bsgyur cing bshad/ rnal 'byor ma'i rgyud la ni ru gnon du brtsigs pa'i g.yas ru gtsang 'phrang ru lag na grom pa rgyang zhes grags pa de sogs smad
kyi btsan po sde gsum gyis bdag mdzad nas yod cing / lha rtser mched gsum bka' bgros te/ 'o cag la bla'i mchod gnas shig dgos par 'dug zer nas/ lo tshong gnyis la zhus pas/
rgya shAkya gzhon nu dang / so ye shes brtson 'grus gnyis byon/ grom pa rgyang du rgyas mkhan po/ sos slob dpon byas rab tu byung ba mang po bsgrubs/ de'i tshe mkhan slob
gnyis la mkhan bu mang du byung ba bsags nas/ rgya gar du chos slob tu gser bskur nas rdzong bzhed pa la dris pas khas len ma byung / mkhan slob rang gis 'brog mi shAkya
ye shes dang / stag lo gzhon nu tshul khrims gnyis sdug sran che/ dpyad pa che bar dgongs nas 'gro dgos gsungs/ de gnyis kyis khas blangs/ 'brog mis de tsa nas rang 'phral
skad legs par mkhyen pa yin/ de gnyis la mkhan slob kyis gser mang po bskur/ zhal bkod gsum mdzad de/ bstan pa'i rtsa ba yin pas 'dul ba/ bstan pa'i snying po yin pas
phar phyin/ bstan pa'i nying khu yin pas gsang sngags slobs gsungs brdzangs/ de gnyis kyis bal por lo gcig bzhugs/ bal po zhi ba bzang po bya ba'i paNDYi ta la btugs/
sgra bslabs dbang bskur dang rgyud sde mang du gsan/ bdag cag rgya gar du 'gro bas/ rgya gar du mkhas pa du yod/ ji ltar byas na 'thad zhus pas/ spyir rgya gar na o tantra
pu ri'i gtsug lag khang sogs mang bar yod kyang / da lta bi kra ma la shI la'i gtsug lag khang na bstan pa dar/ de na mkhas pa sgo drug bya ba yod/ de'i nang nas shar sgo
srung ba'i mkhas pa chen po shAnti pa snyigs dus kyi thams cad mkhyen pa yin/ de nga'i bla ma yin pas der song gsung ba bzhin shAnti pa'i drung du lo brgyad bzhugs/ mkhan
slob gsung ba bzhin 'dul ba/ phar phyin/ dgyes rdor rgyud gsum/ bde mchog sogs sngags mang du gsan/ nA ro pa sogs sgo drug gzhan rnams la chos 'brel zhus/ dus 'khor ba
dang a mo gha badzwa gnyis la sngags mang du gsan/ de nas bod

du log 'byon dgongs shar phyogs kha sarpa Ni grags che bas mjal du byon/ de dang nye ba ku ba tshal bya ba'i nags khrod na dge slong chos gos gsum lhung bzed dang bcas pa zhig
shing sdong la gsil byed thug thug byed 'dug pas/ de'i ser kha nas tshur lus mi snang / lag pa rin po ches brgyan pa zhig gis bsod snyoms 'bul ba mthong / shin tu dad
de rjes su 'dzin par zhus pas ci don du gnyer gsung / chos/ de'i nang nas gsang sngags don du gnyer zhus pas/ 'o na dbang bskur dgos gsung / sngar thob tshul zhus pas/ nga'i
chos 'dod na nga rang gis dbang bskur dgos gsungs nas/ de'i drung du lo bzhi bzhugs/ dgyes pa rdo rje rgyud gsum/ Dombi ba'i rjes su 'brangs ba'i 'brel pa dbang sgrub
thabs bsam gyis mi khyab sogs man ngag du ma dang / lam 'bras rtsa ba med pa zhig kyang gsan/ de mi thub zla ba'i dngos slob/ pradznyyA indra ru tsir bya ba/ bod skad du
shes rab dbang po mdzes pa zhes zer/ gsang mtshan dpa' bo rdo rje/ /phyis myu gu lung du'ang byon/ rin chen 'bar ba brtsams gser phul ba ma bzhes/ ci la byon zhus pas bod
kyi gangs lta ba yong gsungs/ lo gsum bzhugs te nyi zer la zhon nas log da lta'ang bzhugs zer/ de ltar lo bcu gsum song / stag los slob gnyer ma byas tshur mnyam du log
mkhan slob bla chen la dgyes/ stag lo la khyod kyis chos mi shes pa ci yin zer/ rdo rje gdan gyi byang chub chen po la mos par byung nas skor ba byed cing bsdad zhus/ tshul
khrims mgo thon pas phyis stag lo'i sde pa bzang la mang ba byung / 'brog mis myu gu lung dang lha rtse'i brag la bzhugs/ lha lcam gcig la sras indra dang rdo rje gnyis
byung / skabs shig tu gnam thang dkar po bya ba na yod pa'i 'brog pas spyan drangs chos 'chad pa na/ bla ma ga ya dha ras 'phrin btang nas paNDYi ta yong gi yod pas bsu
ru shog gsung / bris pas rdo rje theg par mkhas pa zhig tu dgongs te bsur byon/ mang yul gyi la der mjal/ lha rtser gdan drangs/ zla ba drug dpon slob kyi 'brel btags/
paNDYi ta lo lnga bzhugs/ lo tsA bas gser srang lnga brgya 'bul ba'i chad mdzad/ myu gu lung du spyan drangs/ gsung ngag lam 'bras gtso bor gyur pa'i chos rdzogs par gnang
/ lo gsum song ba dang rgya gar du 'gro gsung /

chad lo lnga bzhugs par zhal gyis bzhes pa lags mod/ bdag gis gser yang ma 'grub zhus pas/ chos thams cad ni tshar/ khyod rang gser phri la phul gsung / 'brog mi'i dgongs pa
la gser phri bas mi rung / tshang bar 'bul dgongs bsgrubs pas gser srang brgya ma gtogs rnyed/ brgya zur po che snga nas kyi slob ma yin pas/ kho nga la gser khur la chos
'dod na sbyin gyi shog gsungs pas khong gis phul/ khong la bsam mi khyab gnang / khong nas bla ma chen po'i bka' drin gyis kho bo'i sems phyogs nor du btang gsungs/ paNDYi
ta la gser rnams phul bas mnyes nas khyod ci dga' bya yi gsungs/ gsung ngag gi lhag ma yod na rdzogs par zhig zhu byas pas/ lhag ma lus par byin pa yin lhag ma med gsungs/
gzhan ci 'dod yang yang gsungs/ gsung ngag 'di bod du gzhan la mi gsung ba zhu zhes zhu 'phul bas zhal gyis bzhes te rgya gar du gshegs ga ya dha ra phyis mgos kyi'ang
spyan drangs/ de dus kyang mjal/ gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer gyi'ang spyan drangs/ de res gnyos 'byung pos gdan drangs/ kha rag tu byon/ der bsnyung nad kyis thebs/ 'pho
ba mdzad nas gshegs so/ /bla chen 'brog mi de man ngag gsungs pa'i slob ma la gzhung mi gsungs/ gzhung gsungs pa'i slob ma la man ngag mi gsung ba yin pas/ gzhung yang lnga
phan la mi gsung bas rna ba drug pa chos kyis dben zer ba byung / man ngag ni re re'am gsum las mang ba la mi gnang / gnang dus dmigs pa re la tshogs 'khor re mdzad kyin
gnang / gzhung tshar ba'i slob ma/ man ngag tshar ba'i slob ma/ grub thob kyi slob ma gsum las/ dang po la lha rtse'i gyi ljang dbu dkar/ shangs kyi brag rtsa se nag
pa/ 'phrang 'og gi 'drang ston dkon mchog rgyal po dang 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po/ gnyis pa 'brom mdo pa ston chung / lha btsun ka li/ se mkhar chung ba/ gsum pa grub pa
thob pa pho gsum/ mo bzhi/ gzhan yang rje btsun mar pa dang mgos sogs mang du byon/ bla chen la sku che ba'i yon tan gnas lnga rigs pa'i paNDYi ta yin/ bskyed rim la brtan
pa thob/ lus gcig las gnyis su sprul pa dang / sbyin sreg gi thab nas yo byad len nus pa/ nam mkha' la skyil krung 'cha' ba dang / bsams na shes pa'i mngon shes yod/ 'pho
ba grong 'jug byed nus pas nga'i

ro 'di zhag bdun ma bsgul bar zhog de nas nga'i rig pa phung po 'di la zhugs nas lam gyi lhag ma bgrod nas phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob par byed do gsung / sras
ma smad kyis ma nyan par tshos btang gi me la phul/ de tsa na drod ma yal bar yod zer ro/ /'khon dkon mchog rgyal po ni/ rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyi nang mir gtogs
pa 'khon dpal po che'i rgyud du 'khrungs/ bla chen 'brog mi la dgyes rdor rgyud gsum gyi bshad pa legs par gsan/ gzhan yang paNDYi ta shes rab gsang ba/ ba ri ba/ mal
gyo/ spu rangs lo chung sogs bla ma mang po bsten/ 'dis sa skya btab/ sku tshe ring sgrub pa dang 'chad nyan spel te bstan pa la bya ba che'o/ /se khar chung bas lo bcu
bdun du bsten yang lam 'bras bu'i skabs ma tshang / phyis sras indra bsten nas rdo rje'i tshig zhabs ma tshang ba rnyed/ bla chen nyid lo gcig bskyar nas bsten pas gdam ngag
tshang zhing / de'i rjes su lam bsdus te sgrub pa lung byin mdzad pas bum pa gang 'byo'i tshul du byung / bshad pa 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po la zhus/ de la man ngag phar
phul/ yon tan ni bskyed rim la brtan pa cung zad thob/ rtsa sngags kyi sgo nas nus pa brnyes/ khang chung gi klu sin mo thu ba zhig btul nas gzhan du sbas/ 'og rlung
la dbang thob/ byang sems zin pas jo mo yod kyang sras la sogs pa med/ sku'i bkod pa'ang du mar ston nus/ mdor na gnas sbyong bzhi cu rtsa gnyis kyi nyams thams cad skyes
shing 'byongs pas phyir mi zlog pa yin gsungs/ des man ngag rab tu byin pa zhang sku mched/ 'bring du sbyin pa zha ma lcam sring / 'di las ko brag pa'i lam 'bras byung /
mtha' mar sbyin pa se sgom byas yas las/ dang po zhang ston chos 'bar dang / gcung gzi byin 'bar/ gsung rab kyi rtsi dras mkhan/ ses mdo mang bzhengs pa'i rtsi dras la yong
/ 'brel thogs/ 'bul ba dang spyod lam gyis mnyes par byas/ gzhung rdzogs par gnang / zhang chos 'bar la yon tan/ khams 'dus pa bar ma'i thad sor slebs/ ting nge 'dzin
dpag tu med pa mnga'/ mngon shes brtan po yod/ gnyen lcug bzhi la mnga' brnyes pas lus stag dang bya sogs gzhan du sprul nus/ lus kyi bkod pa bdun tsam du ston no/ /

de la rje sa chen gyis gtugs/ de ni 'khon dkon mchog rgyal po dang zhang mo'i sras su 'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu gcig lon pa dang yab gshegs/ gdan sa ba ri lo tsA la gtad/ des
a ra pa tsa na'i sgrub thabs gnang bas zla ba drug nas 'grub/ bcu gnyis pa la rong ngur smrig tu byon/ brang sti la mngon pa/ zur chos pa byang chad sogs la sa sde/ nyang
stod du khyung rin chen grags la rnam nges sogs gsan nas sa skyar phebs/ ba ri bas gdan sa gtad/ de'i gdam ngag bla ma gnam kha 'u ba/ 'khon sgyi chu ba bsten/ bar der se
dang mjal tsam byung / mal lo tsA ba bsten/ de nas sag thang du phebs/ thags mkhan tsho gcig 'dug pas zhang dgon pa la mjal gyis byas pas/ pha ki ka yin zer/ gzigs pas
mi mang po zhig gi gseb na sham thabs cig gsol/ sha 'gag med par ra thul phyir log tu gyon nas yog ga byed cing gtam chal chol mang po mdzad kyin 'dug der drung du phyin
phyag dang phyag rten phul bas nor ba yin gsungs zhal gyis ma bzhes/ sa chen rang yang nor 'dug log 'gro dgongs tsa na/ jo sras 'od mchog zer ba'i phas zhang la/ 'o skol
rang mkhar chu ba na yod tsa na/ sgyi chu ba'i grwa pa zhig la nga'i bla ma'i sras po yin gsungs nas pang du len pa de 'dra na ldog pas cang mchi'am zhus/ 'o na dam tshig
gi nyes par 'gro nyen yod bos gsungs/ bos lo rgyus zhib tu mdzad pas thugs ches/ ngas da ci ngo ma shes par rdzun byas/ man ngag yod de sngar ma bshad pas bsam mno 'dra
gtong / phyis 'dir byon gsungs pa bzhin byon/ lo bzhi bzhugs/ gsung ngag ma lus pa/ lam skor dgu phra mo nyi shu rtsa brgyad/ kye rdo rje rgyud rkyang gi bshad pa/ gsang
'dus mnyam sbyor la sogs rgyud sde dang gdam ngag mang po gsan/ gdam ngag rdzogs te sgrub pa lung byin gyi skabs su/ lo bco brgyad kyi bar du chos 'di gzhan la ston pa lta
zhog 'di 'dra yod tsam dang shes pa ming tsam yang ma 'don/ yi ger ma bri/ de nas gzhan la 'chad dam/ yi ger 'dri'am/ gang byed kyang khyod rang chos kyi bdag po yin gsungs
bka' rgyas btab/ spyir khyod kyis sgrub pa gtso bor byas na tshe 'di la phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob/ nyan bshad

byas na gdul bya dpag tu med pa'i don du 'gyur/ khyad par sku lus ma spangs par phyag rgya chen po mchog gi dngos grub thob pa'i slob ma gsum/ bzod pa thob pa'i rnal 'byor
pa bdun/ rtogs pa dang ldan pa'i rnal 'byor pa brgyad cu tsam 'byung zhes lung bstan/ lo bco brgyad pa la bla ma a seng gis khungs chod nas nyid la gsung ngag rin po che
mnga' bar gda' bas/ sngar nga la yod kyang mi gsung bar 'dug da lam tshar gcig gsungs pa dang yi ge zhib pa zhig kyang mdzad par zhu gsungs/ bka' rgya thems pas tshar gcig
gsungs/ lam 'bras bsdus don ma de mdzad/ de nas lo bzhi ma gsungs/ ru mtshams pa dga' thed bya ba bla ma yun ring du bsten pa zhig gis zin bris la gnad 'chugs pa gzigs
nas/ nyams dogs khong gi don du dga' thed ma mdzad/ de nas klog skya ma sogs snga phyir 'grel pa bcu gcig tsam mdzad/ thams cad kyi rjes ma gnyags ma tshig nyung don rgyas
tshig sdeb legs/ 'chad sla bar dgongs nas ding sang gi bar du phyag len mdzad do/ /gzhan yang bi rU pa byon nas rgyud sde bdun cu rtsa gnyis dang / sgrub thabs lam 'bras
bshad/ bla ma'i rnal 'byor gegs sel gyi gnad/ grub chen bcu/ rnam 'joms lus dkyil/ bi rU pa nyid kyi sgrub skor sogs chos mang du gsungs/ byin gyis brlabs/ sku che ba'i
yon tan sdom pa gsum dang 'gal ba'i nyes pa phra mos kyang ma gos/ byams pa dang thugs rjes rgyud brlan/ dngos po gang la'ang mi chags/ dad pa dang sgrub pa'i sgo nas bla
ma mnyes par mdzad/ nang du rten 'brel 'grig pas yi dam lha'i zhal gzigs/ chos thams cad la mnga' brnyes/ mngon shes dang rdzu 'phrul thogs pa mi mnga' ba yin la/ zhang
ston gyis lung bstan pa bzhin gyi slob ma'ang byon/ de la sras bzhi/ che 'og slob dpon rin po che bsod nams rtse mo yab dang / gsang phur phya pa las mkhas pa chen por gyur
gyi bar sbyangs/ bstan bcos du ma brtsams/ phal cher dben par gzhol/ tshul khrims kyi phung po bu gcig pu lta bur bsrungs te/ dgung lo zhe gcig la sku ma spangs par bde
ba can du byon no/ /gsum pa rje btsun chen po grags pa rgyal mtshan/ dgung lo bcu bzhi pa la

dgyes rdor rgyud gsum gyi glegs bam gsol ba'i mnal lam byung bas chos thams cad kyi de kho na nyid thugs su chud/ sa chen la sogs pa las mdo rgyud kyi thos pa mthar phyin/
dgung lo bcu gsum nas bdun cu'i bar 'chad nyan mdzad/ yi dam lha mang po'i zhal gzigs/ mthu stobs bi rU pa dang mnyam/ 'byung po 'jigs byed lta bu'ang mtshan bsgrags pa tsam
gyis 'bros skad do/ /rdo rje dril bu gnam la 'jog pa sogs rdzu 'phrul du ma bstan no/ /de'i gcung po'i sras chos rje sa skya paNDYi ta/ mtshan kun dga' rgyal mtshan/
sku gzhon nu nas rje btsun pa la thos pa/ bco brgyad pa la mnal lam du dbyig gnyen la mngon pa gsan pa dang / gzhan phyogs kyi glang po'i phug yin zer ba zhig tu tshad ma'i
po ti mang po 'dug pa kun gyi lde mig gtad pa rmis pa dang / bcu dgu pa la 'phreng du dge bshes gzhu la tshad ma/ nyi shu la rkyang 'dur du tshur gzhon seng la tshad ma
dang rig tshogs/ chu mig ring mor kha che paN chen dang mjal/ tshad ma chos mchog rgya dpe'i steng nas/ paN chung dA na shI la la sgra tshad/ lhag par sanggha shrI sgra
la mkhas pas sgra sogs tha snyad/ paN chen dbus 'khor nas dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdun pa la bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan po dang rtsegs dbang phyug sengge/ spyi bo lhas pa sogs
bla mar bsten te yongs su rdzogs pa'i paNDYi ta chen por gyur/ 'phrog byed dga' bo rtsod pas btul/ sdom rig sogs bstan bcos mang du mdzad/ sku che ba'i yon tan gsang ba'i
gnas ltar mi mngon pa dang / dbu'i gtsug tor gsal por 'phags pa dang / smin mtshams kyi mdzod spu dung ltar 'khyil ba dang mngon par shes pa mnga'/ 'jam dbyangs kyi sprul
pa yin/ rgya nag tu rgyal po go dan gyis spyan drangs/ re lnga pa la de dang mjal/ rgyal po theg chen la btsud/ de sogs gdul bya mang po smin pa dang grol bar mdzad/
dgung lo bdun cu pa la ngo mtshar ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang bcas te gshegs so/ /de la bshad bka' 'dzin pa 'u yug khang gnyan zhang gsum/ man ngag gi brgyud 'dzin
dmar dang / lho ba kun mkhyen rin chen dpal/ rtogs pa'i brgyud 'dzin tshogs sgom pa kun dga' dpal ba/ grub thob yon tan dpal/ de'i dbon 'phags pa rin po che/ khu bo la
sogs pa dam pa

mang du bsten nas mkhas pa dang / se chen gyis bod 'bangs su bcug ste/ de thams cad 'phags pa rin po che la phul bas/ bod rgyal po'i rjes la 'phags pa rin po che bod khams
kyi sa'i cha la lung gtong rgya che/ chos lugs thams cad rang rang gi lugs kho na la spyad chog pa'i lung stsal/ bsgyur bsgyur ye ma mdzad/ 'chad nyan kyang mdzad cing sa
skya lugs gnyis kyis 'gran du med pa bzos/ slob ma bshad pa'i srol 'dzin shar nub gung gsum dang / bla ma grags pa 'od zer/ bla ma bkra shis dpal la sogs mang du byung /
gsung ngag legs par rdzogs pa zhang dkon mchog dpal dang / dge slong kun dga' blo gros gnyis las ma byung zhes grags so/ /de'i dbon sras dpal ldan bla ma dam pa mkhyen rab
sa paN dang mnyam/ gzhan theg chen chos kyi rgyal po sogs da lta'i bar du rim par byon pa'i chos kyi rje de dag gi ring lugs las ding sang gi bar du dpal ldan sa skya
pa zhes rgya bod hor gsum du khyab pa/ bshad pa'i bka'/ sgrub pa'i lung / nyams len thams cad dpyad pa gsum gyis dag pa 'di rnams byung ba yin zhing / de'i sngags kyi lugs
'dzin sa skya kun dga' rnam gnyis su grags pa dang / kun dga' rnam rgyal te/ rdo rje 'chang mngon sum pa de dag las ding sang ngor rdzong du bye ba dag yin/ sa skya pa
bying ngor par gyur to/ lo chen/ 'brog mi/ 'gos sogs kyis bde mchog bsgyur bshad mdzad kyang bshad rgyun med/ klog skya shes rab rtsegs kyis pham thing pa'i gcung la gsan/
de la mal gyos zhus/ slad kyi de nyid kyis bal por byon nas nA ro pa'i slob ma byang chub bzang po dang / ka na ka shrI'i slob ma bal po thugs rje chen po/ pham thing ba
dpon slob la nyan/ spu sreng lo tsA ba grags mchog shes rab/ de mar do'i lo chung yin pas bla ma gcig spu sreng lo chung zhes grags te/ des 'ja' lus byas so/ /mal gyo las
sa chen sogs dang / spu sreng lo chung nas dmar chos rgyal ba/ mnga' ris kyi ston pa dkon mchog 'bar/ des thur la'i mkhan po tshul khrims skyabs/ de la thang spel ba sogs
nas bu ston gyi bar du lo dril nag po sogs dar ro/ /mar do lugs kyang / des gze ba/ de'i slob ma khang gsar ba/ de la yang rtse ba/

bu ston/ mar do ni yar 'brog bla ngo'i rgyags su 'khrungs/ mtshan chos kyi dbang phyug paNDYi ta dang / rong zom dang / go rub lo tsA ba rnams la skad bslabs/ rgya gar du byon/
bal por mar pa tshur log pa mjal/ nA ro pa ti ra hu tir phebs pa yud cig mjal/ lho brag pa'i gsung bzhin nA ro pa'i slob ma ka na ka shrI/ pradznyyA rakShi ta/ kha che
byang chub bzang po/ pra mu ra badzwa rnams la bde mchog gi dbang rgyud man ngag legs par gsan/ paNDYi ta mang po bsten/ phyir bal por log dus bal po mched/ ka na ka shrI/
phyag na'ang mjal/ khyad par su ma ti kIrti la brten nas bde mchog gi skor tsho bsgyur/ bod du phebs nas mkhas pa rgya bsam/ de'i gze ba blo ldan/ khams kyi cog ro chos
rgyal/ lho'i la yag pa byang chub dngos grub sogs dang / sras nam mkha' 'od sogs mang po/ bshad bka'ang dar ro/ /phag mo'i skor ni de dang lo tsA ba blo ldan shes rab
kyis bsgyur/ dpyal 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan zhes pa nA ro pa dang smr-i ti'i slob ma yin/ des smr-i ti bod du phebs nas ra rdzi mdzad pa jo bo rnams la gser byin nas bslus/
smr-i ti la sku bsod skyes/ bzhugs par zhus kyang ma gsan khams su bzhud/ der 'gyur yang 'ga' mdzad/ mtshan brjod sgeg pa'i rdo rje lugs kyi bshad pa gnang / bshad rgyun
'di rngog la yod/ dpyal 'byung gnas rgyal mtshan gyi dbon se che nor rgyal bal por byon/ pham thing pa la btugs/ kye rdo rje nA ro lugs kyi bshad pa bskyangs/ de nas
thar lo'i bar du lo tsA ba mkhas pa mang du byon/ jo bo bod du byon dus smr-i ti dang dam nyams yin gsung / thar pa la yol ba btang ma gzigs par mdzad zer ba cal brgyugs
su zad do/ /gsang ba 'dus pa ni jo bo dang paNDYi ta A ka ra siddhi gnyis nas nag tsho/ des rong pa rgya sor pa/ des zhu lan pa/ des lha ri ston pa/ des ngor rje las brgyud
pa dang / khyad par rta nag phu'i sa'i cha khug pa zhes bya bar 'khrungs pa/ rus 'gos mtshan lha btsas/ des dang por zur pa'i slob ma byas pas las kho na bcol chos ma
bslabs pas 'brog mi'i thad du byon/ chos kyi 'brel tsam tshugs kyang rgyud nyan 'dod pa la gser khyer shog gsung / gser legs par 'grub pa dang bdag nyid rgya gar du 'gro
ba'i spobs pa skyes te rgya gar du byon/ paNDYi ta rnams la chos gsan pa'i tshe brtson 'grus ma bskyed na

'brog sdom de la ngo tsha bar yod gsungs nas 'bad pa chen po mdzad/ khong la bal po phan chad na paNDYi ta'i bla ma bdun cu dang / mkha' 'gro'i bla ma gnyis rnams yod/ de dag
las gtso bo ni bhangga la'i mngon shes can/ za hor gyi mkhas pa btsun mo can/ kong ka na'i rgyal bu sprin gyi shugs can/ rdo rje gdan gyi nag po dam tshig rdo rje/ jo
bo rje/ kha che grib brtan gyi mkhas pa tsandra rA hU la/ rgyal po'i khab kyi zhi ba bzang po/ bal po thugs rje chen po/ bal po rdzong gi na ba ku Ti pa/ nA ro pa'i slob
ma kha che dznyyA nA kA ra rnams so zer/ ngor rje/ klu byang / des tilli nA ro/ des ku sa li che ba/ des ku sa li chung ba/ des gser gling pa/ des piNDYo pa/ bsod snyoms
pa dang / mngon shes can dang / btsun mo can dang / dznyyA na A ka ra bzhi la bshad gsungs/ de bzhin chag chos rje dpal pa'i spyi rnam du'ang bgrangs so/ /lo tsA ba des gsang
ba 'dus pa rtsa 'grel/ dgyes rdor rgyud gsum 'grel pa/ bde mchog rgyud 'grel pa dang bcas pa/ rdo rje gdan bzhi bshad pa dang bcas pa/ ma hA ma yA sogs rgyud mang po
'grel pa dang bcas pa bsgyur/ mkhyen pa rgya chen po dang ldan pas mang du bshad/ slob ma'i mchog mang ra sengge rgyal mtshan/ brdog ge sa ra/ ngab mi byang chub rgyal mtshan/
lho pa rdo rje snying po/ gnyal pa mgar chos kyi rdo rje/ dbus pa sna drug de las deng sang gi bar du bshad pa'i rgyun snang ste/ bu ston mar 'gos chu bo gnyis 'gril
du bzhed la/ de nas brgyud pa tsong kha pa chen po bshad pa 'gos gtso bor mdzad pas/ da lta dge ldan pa rnams bshad pa 'gos kho na las byung ba 'dra zhig gleng ngo / /mar
'gos gnyis kas ye shes zhabs lugs kyang bshad/ gzhan 'dus pa bsgyur mkhan gnyos 'byung po/ phyag lo chos rje dpal sogs mang ngo / /gshin rje gshed skor rnams ni snye
nam snang yul du 'khrungs/ byis pa'i dus na lha mo re ma tis phu dung nang du bcug zla ba gnyis su rgyal khams bskor zhing / de nas ma la gtad/ rab tu byung zhing bsnyen
par rdzogs/ bal yul du byon/ bal po thugs rje chen po/ 'ba' ro phyag rdum sogs bsten/ nA ro pa nas pra dznyyA rakShi ta/ des bal po thugs rje chen po la gsungs/ de la rwa
los legs par gsan zhing mang du mkhyen pa na/ bde mchog rtsa rgyud/ sampu Ta/ rdo rje 'jigs byed

kyi skor/ gshed nag po'i skor/ gdong drug gi skor/ mtshan brjod sogs bsgyur/ de yang 'bre shes rab 'bar gyi gsungs nas/ bod du bsgyur ba'i chos la dge bshes rwa lo tsA ba'i
chos las zhe zhim pa med/ paNDYi ta mkhas pa'i dgongs pa lon cing / bod chos kyi bsres lhad med pas so gsungs/ de 'chad nyan mdzad/ 'jigs byed/ dgra nag gdong drug gsum
bshad pa'i slob ma nyis stong tsam yod par grags/ de dag las lha btsun sngon mo sogs che dgu /bshad pa'i rgyun khong rang gi dbon po rwa chos rab/ rwa ye shes sengge/ rwa
'bum seng / rje btsun rga lo yab sras rnams las brgyud de/ de ding sang 'jigs byed rwa lugs zhes g.yer che'o/ /rngog ston chos kyi rdo rje sambu Ta'i bshad pa de la gsan
no/ /dus kyi 'khor lo ni/ kha che zla ba mgon po bod du byon/ kha rag gnyos la babs/ 'grel pa dri ma med pa'i 'od bsgyur/ gser srang brgya brdzang bar chad pa la ma brdzangs
pas/ paNDYi ta ma mgu bar 'grel pa phyed las ma bsgyur/ 'gyur byed 'phro bsnams nas 'phan yul grab tu byon/ zhang ston chung bas bla mar bzung / 'bros lo tsA byas nas
yongs su rdzogs par bsgyur/ gnyos kyis zhang ston la khyod kyis nga'i bla ma phrog pa yin pas wa gseb tu yungs kar gtsang nge ba zhig bya yi zer ba la/ khro bo brgya yis
sdigs kyang mi 'jigs/ lha mo brgya yis 'dzum bstan kyang mi chags pa yin zer nas zhabs tog mdzad/ gnyos ston ye shes mchog la sogs la 'bul ba cher phul yang sod spor tsam
las ma gnang / 'phan yul grub tu sku 'khrungs pa sgom pa dkon mchog srung gi 'byor pa thams cad bsdus pas gser srang drug byung / de dang dar yug ske la btags te lus phul
nas zhabs tog mdzad/ ji ltar gsung ba bzhin bsgrubs pas gzhung man ngag ma lus pa gnang / de la sgro ston gnam la brtsegs kyis paNDYi ta rtsad chod nas gser srang bcu
gnyis dang rta nag po zhig phul zhabs tog yun ring por mdzad kyang so sor spong ba ma gtogs ma gnang / de dus dkon mchog srung la zhus kyang ma gnang / paNDYi ta rgya gar
du log nas shul du lo gsum/ yer par lo gsum ste drug la gzhung man ngag tshang bar zhus/ des gangs ti se'i 'brog pa rngam khrom pa dad pa rgyal po zhes bya ba'i sras grub
chen yu mo

la/ des de nyid kyi sras dharma shwa ra la/ des nam mkha' 'od/ des se mo che bar grags pa/ dharme shwa ra'i sras nam mkha' rgyal mtshan la/ des 'jam gsar la/ de la rong pa
rga los gsan/ 'di la 'bro'i 'gyur la brten pa dang / paNDYi ta dang sgom pa dkon mchog srung gi bar du lo tsA ba shes rab grags bcug kyang chog pas 'bro lugs zer/ rwa lugs
ni/ rwa rdo rje grags kyi dbon po chos rab kyi rwa lugs kyi chos skor mthar phyin/ dus kyi 'khor lo don du gnyer nas bal por byon/ paNDYi ta sa manta shrI la lo lnga zla
ba bcu zhag lngar bar ma chad par bsten rgyud dbang man ngag rdzogs par gsan/ paNDYi ta bod du spyan drangs/ rgyud 'grel bsgyur/ gser srang sum brgya phul/ gshegs skyel
yang skyi rong tshun mdzad/ des sras 'bum seng / des rong pa rga lo la/ 'di ni gtsang rong du 'khrungs/ dpal rga lo'i skye ba yin pas mtshan rga lor thogs/ kha che paN chen
dang mjal/ yab dang dpyal chos bzang bsten sbyangs pa rgya chen po mdzad/ 'od gsal chung na bzhugs te bsnyung / rgyal po'i bar chad thu bas zin/ thar par gshed dmar gyi
dbang zhus nas bar chad las grol/ gzhan yang sa paN/ 'jam gsar/ rwa 'bum seng / bi bhU ti tsandra dang khro lo sogs bsten/ dus kyi 'khor lo bshad pas man lung gu ru sogs
mkhas pa mang po thon/ 'phags pa rin po che dang chos phar zhu tshur zhu/ de'i sras shes rab sengge yab dang / bla ma dpyal pa dang / stag sde ba sengge rgyal mtshan sogs
las sde snod/ rgyud sde/ khyad par dus 'khor la mkhas pa chen por gyur gyi bar sbyangs te/ slob ma lo tsA ba yang bar pang gsum sogs mang po thon/ sras bla ma rdo rje
rgyal mtshan/ des yab la sogs pa las thos pa mthar phyin mdzad/ rgya nag tu rgyal pos gdan drangs/ thams cad dad par byas te grongs/ de la bu ston gyis gsan/ bu ston ni
'khrungs sa shab sgom gnas/ khro phur tshad ma'i skyes bu yang rtse ba sogs la gtugs/ grags par gyur la yab dang bcas te dbus gtsang la grwa skor mdzad pas/ pha ston pa bu
ston pa 'dug ces pas mtshan bu ston du grags/ zha lu'i 'chad nyan du bskos/ thar lo la sgra/ bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan la dus 'khor/ rgyang mkhar jo tsha'i 'phags 'od
yon tan rgya mtsho la 'phags yo ga dus gsum sogs te/ bla ma du ma las ngoms pa med pa'i

thos pa mdzad/ bod phrug gcig la thos pa che ba yin/ khro phu ba'i mdo'i 'chad nyan kyang der 'phos/ ding sang mdo rgyud sgra rig kun la lab lab byas chog pa 'di khong gi bka'
drin no/ /de la slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa byon pa las mchog gyur thugs sras lo tsA ba dpal ldan bla ma dam pa/ gong gsum pa dharma shrI sogs las dus kyi 'khor lo
mched de/ 'di khro phu ba'i khongs su gtogs la/ 'on kyang 'phrin las che bas bod rnams zha lu ba zhes lugs chen po logs pa zhig tu 'dren no/ /yang 'jam dbyangs gsar ma'i
slob ma kun mkhyen chos sku 'od zer/ de'i slob ma kun spangs thugs rje brtson 'grus/ 'dis jo nang btab/ de'i slob ma byang sems rgyal ba ye shes/ de la 'phags 'od yon tan
rgya mtsho dang mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho gnyis byon pa'i dang pos bu ston/ gnyis pas jo nang pa'i bla ma mdzad/ de'i slob ma dol po ba ste mnga' ris smad dol po'i
ban tshang zhes par sku 'khrungs/ gzhon nu la skyi ston 'jam dbyangs grags pa la gtugs nas ka chen bzhi dang / dus 'khor rwa lugs la thos pa mdzad/ khong rong pa shes rab
sengga'i slob ma yin/ sa skyar sku gzhon nu la bka' bzhi'i bshad pa mdzad/ dbus gtsang du grwa skor mdzad pas ston pa bzang bar grags/ des bu ston ri phug na bzhugs dus
rtsod du byon pas/ bu ston gyis ma nus/ thal skad bton pas gzims khang gas zer ba'i gtam khungs gzhan na mi 'dug jo nang pa'i sgom ma rnams kyi nyams las so snyam mo/ /gzhan
yang bla ma mang po la gsan pa mdzad/ khyad par jo nang du mkhas btsun yon tan rgya mtsho la dus 'khor rgyud 'grel man ngag dang bcas pa gsan/ man ngag sku nyams su bzhes
pas/ dpe med pa'i myong ba 'khrungs/ jo nang gi gdan sa gzung / sku 'bum mthong grol chen mo bzhengs/ gzhan stong ston pa'i bstan bcos mang du mdzad/ 'chad nyan gyis
bstan pa la phan thogs rgya chen po byung ba'i slob ma kun spangs chos grags dpal bzang sogs thun mong ma yin pa dang / bu dol gnyis thun mong ba ma ti rnam gnyis dang /
mnga' ris pa phyogs las rnam rgyal/ nya dbon kun dga' dpal de gsum phyis jo nang pa shas che/ de dag sogs mkhas shing yan lag drug gi rnal 'byor lhur len pa mang pos dbus
gtsang mnga' ris khams khyab par mdzad do/ /dus kyi 'khor

lo de las mched pa rnams la jo lugs su grags so/ /dus 'khor lugs gzhan ni/ dus zhabs pa'i slob ma shrI bha dra bo dhis/ gyi jo zla ba'i 'od zer/ des dus 'khor gyi bshad pa
yun ring po mdzad kyang / slob ma dus 'khor shes pa bzhi las ma byung / de dag gis bshad ka ma zin/ dA na shrI'i slob ma rma dge blo/ mda' 'od blo snying / byang she sogs
kyis bshad ka ma tshugs/ a bhya'i slob ma khe gad 'khor lo grags/ rga lo/ ro lings lo tsA/ steng pa lo tsA sogs kyis bshad ka ma tshugs/ se los rtsa mi lo tsA ba sangs rgyas
grags la zhus nas gnyos 'od la gnang / de nas rim gyis brgyud de rtsa mi lugs kyi bshad ka byung / de ltar dus kyi 'khor lor 'gyur mi gcig pa nyi shu rtsa lnga tsam
yod la bod du dar bar gyur to/ /rtsa mi lo tsA ba 'di 'khrungs yul mi nyag gi phu rtsa mi shing mi ba yin pas mtshan de ltar thogs/ rdo rje gdan pa chen po'i slob ma/ gdan
pa chung ba dang phar zhu tshur zhu/ bod mi rgya gar du phyin pa la 'phrin las che/ rga lo gzhon nu dpal yang rgya gar du grub thob kyi grags pa thon/ bod du chos skyong
phyag bzhi'i skor la khong dang steng lo/ khe gad rnams sku drin che/ bo dong rin rtse'i slob ma stag sde pa sengge rgyal mtshan/ de la mkhas pa shong sku mched dang dpang
los gtugs pa shong ston ni/ sbyin lung shar kha'i bong ra zhes par 'khrungs mtshan rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ stag sde par phar tshad mngon pa/ dus 'khor 'gro lugs gsan/ u
rgyan pa'i gcen po go lung pa mdo sde dpal rgyal mtshan la'ang dus 'khor sogs sngags mang du gsan zhing / bla ma 'phags pa bod du byon pa na/ bstod pa tshigs su bcad pa
tshig rgyan gyis mdzes pa phul/ lo tsA slob tu 'gro bar zhus pas/ de lta bu'i blo skye ba bzang / gzhung lugs gsar pa bsgyur nus pa 'ong bar dka' ste/ paNDYi ta la slob gnyer
dri gtugs legs par gyis/ kho bo kyang chos rje bsten yun thung pas sdeb sbyor me tog gi chun po dang / tshig gter la sogs pa tshul bzhin du mi shes par snang bas/ 'di
dag shes pa zhig ci nas kyang gyis shig de dag gi dpe dang gser srang lnga/ dar yug bcu rnams gnang / bal yul du byon nas paNDYi ta lakShIM la sogs pa bsten te/ rig pa'i
gnas chung ba lnga la sbyangs/ khyad par sgra rig phul du phyin/ sa skyar byon dus 'khor 'grel pa dang bcas pa'i 'gyur mdzad/

de la 'phags pa rin po ches kyang bsngags bsngags mdzad/ dpag bsam 'khri shing la gzhi 'gyur sgra snyan dngags ming gi mngon brjod rnams kyi srol legs par btsugs/ rang gi gcung
blo brtan la'ang legs par bslabs shing / lo tsA ba mchog ldan sogs slob ma legs par thon/ 'di sku mched gnyis kas grub thob chen po u rgyan pa'i spyan sngar gdams pa
mang du gsan te/ khrid chen brgyad bsnyen sgrub sogs la zin bris mdzad/ gcen bal por byon nas gshegs/ dpang lo gyam du 'khrungs/ yum snga mor grongs nas lug gi 'o mas gsos/
dbu skra rgod tshang pa'i gdan sa rgyal sras byang gling pa la bcad/ de ni sengge dgu tshar gyi sengge shes rab yin/ de dang u rgyan pa la'ang chos mang po gsan/ mkhan
po gser khang pa las dge tshul mdzad de mdo rtsa bslabs/ de nas stag sde pa las sngags mtshan nyid/ khyad par dus 'khor gsan/ bcu dgu bzhes pa'i tshe stag sde pa gshegs
nas/ lo tsA ba mchog ldan la gtugs te/ ka tsan snyan dngags mngon brjod sogs mkhas par bslabs/ gzhung de dag 'gyur mdzad/ bal por lan bdun byon/ bo dong e'i gdan sa mdzad/
bu dol gnyis/ dpal ldan bla ma dam pa sogs kyi zhabs la btud/ de nang nas bu ston mkhas pa chen por gzigs nas/ rang gi dbon po lo chen byang chub rtse mo khong la sbyar
te/ khyod rang dang mnyam pa zhig bzos gsung / byang rtses bu las sgra tshad dus 'khor sogs mkhas par bslabs/ 'di'i slob ma lo tsA ba nam mkha' bzang po/ de'i slob ma sgra
pa thugs rje dpal te/ sgra snyan dngags la sku drin che'o/ /byang rtse'i dbon po lo chen grags pa/ byang rtse dang lo grags gnyis ka sngags la bu'i brgyud 'dzin rang
yin/ de'i dbon bo dong pa chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ paN chen phyogs las rnam rgyal du grags pa mkhas pa'i dbang po dbyangs can mas dngos su byin gyis brlabs pas mkhyen pa la
mtha' med/ de kho na nyid 'dus pa zhes bya ba'i bstan bcos brtsams/ bod du bstan bcos brtsams pa la 'di mang / 'di las bo dong pa zhes bya ba'i lugs byung ngo / /gzhan phyis
paN chen nags kyi rin chen bod du byon/ dus kyi 'khor lo la sogs pa gnang ba'i slob ma/ grags pa 'byung gnas/ bdag po kun dga' legs pa/ 'gos gzhon nu dpal/ byams gling
pa bsod nams rnam rgyal/ khrus khang lo

tsA ba sogs mang la/ byang chub sems dpa'i rgyud 'grel gsum/ dpe med 'tsho'i sbyor drug bde phag gi man ngag gnang bas ji snyed pa'i mkhyen pa shar ba ni rgyal dbang chos rje'o/
/pha dam pa sangs rgyas kyis/ dang po tsa ri'i rong 'bri thad nas thon te tsa rir re ma ti la rkang mgyogs gsan te/ kong yul khams su byon te slar log gnyis pa kha
che nas byon/ gsum pa bal po nas/ bzhi pa mtsho sna'i sha 'ug stag sgo nas gnyal du byon nas/ lnga pa bod nas rgya nag slar bod du phebs pa yin/ des slob ma dpag tu med par
smin par mdzad kyang grags che ba zhi byed brgyud pa snga phyi bar gsum/ snga ma kha che dznyyA na gu la/ de od po lo tsA bas bsgyur/ brgyud pa bar pa/ rma/ so/ skam gsum/
dam pas gnyal nas yar stod du phebs/ rma dang mjal te/ de yar stod skyer snar rma smon lam zhes pa'i sras su 'khrungs/ mtshan chos kyi shes rab/ yab la padma dbang chen/
spyod phyogs/ dbu ma do ha sogs bslabs/ bcu dgu pa la khong khams ma bde bar rang gi khang thog tu bzhugs pa'i tshe/ a tsa ra nag po ras rkyang phrag la bkal ba zhig
byung ba sgo'ang ma bstan par mkhyen te nang du byon byin brlabs mdzad pa tsam gyis bsnyun dengs/ phyag rgya chen po btab pas rma la nyams rtogs khyad par can skyes/ zhag
bco brgyad song ba dang dam pa byon 'phan yul du shog gsung / bsgoms pas drod kha rnyed de so chung ba khrid nas 'phan yul du byon gdam ngag tshar/ bsgrub pa mdzad bu chen
lnga sogs byung / so ni yar stod ra me nang mi rnams sprad de 'ongs/ bu spun gnyis yod pa'i pho bo gzugs chung bas so chung / nu bo gzugs ring pas so ring zer/ der rma'i
phyag phyir khrid nas dam pa mjal/ rma log nas yun ring du bsten gdam ngag che/ de'i slob ma sgom chen slon lam 'bar sogs so/ /skam gra pa'i slob ma phar phyin shes pa
skran nad kyi zin pa zhig dam pa spyan drangs/ tshogs pa'i gseb tu brda'i ngo sprod cig mdzad pas/ skam nges shes skyes nas/ mi mang gi gseb tu re 'phangs snyam pa dang
/ dam pa'i zhal nas brda mig can gyis mthong ba yin/ mig med kyis mi mthong gsung ba bzhin gzhan go ba mi gda'/ gdam ngag rdzogs/ nad las grol/ rtogs pa shar/ slob ma bskyangs
so/ /brgyud pa phyi ma la dam pa ding rir byon/ der slob ma bskyangs pa'i mchog shar na dam pa

phyar chen/ lho na badzwa kro dha/ nub na phyar chung / byang na byang chub sems dpa' kun dga' rnams las/ kun dga' sras thams cad kyi gtso bo yin/ ding ri'i shar phyogs tsha
gud du 'khrungs/ skye ba lngar dam pas rjes su bzung ba/ sku tshe 'di la de'i gdam ngag gi mdzod/ de'i slob ma pa tshab sgom pa 'phan yul ba yin no/ /de'i slob ma rgyal
ba te ne/ de'i slob ma rog shes rab sengge/ zhig po nyi ma sengge gnyis las mched de/ zhi byed la gces pa'i lugs 'dzin mang por byung ba yin no/ /dam pas bal po nas byon
res gtsang du skyo bsod nams bla ma dang / sma ra ser po la spyod yul gyi gdams pa gnang / dang pos ma gcig lab sgron/ de gzhon nu nas grwa pa mngon shes la rab tu byung
/ de'i bla mchod byas sher phyin klog pas stong pa nyid gsha' mar go dam pa dang mjal/ 'dam bur klog la byon pas/ cer grong pa thod pa bha dra bya ba dang 'dus pas bza'
mir song / kong por byon/ de nas g.yer phebs/ gangs par spel gcig mar sbas snying po grub pa/ grub chung yang grub gsum/ sras mo gnyis 'khrungs/ skyo bsod nams bla ma khams
nas log pa'i lam du sgyu 'phrul gyi dbang gsan/ dbang gral du rtogs pa shar/ spyod kyi gdams pa gsan/ gdul byar gyur pa la gdam ngag bshad/ phyis zangs ri khang dmar gyi
phug par bzhugs/ gcod kyi gdams pas bod gang bar byas/ slob ma mchog bzhi la/ yar stod nas snyags pa rgyal mtshan/ yar smad nas an ston rin chen dpal/ bar na 'dreng jo
sras/ shung bu lo tsA ba zer/ gzhan yang mang ngo / /sras snying po grub pa rjes su bzung bas 'khrul zhig chen po zhig byung / de la sras tshe dbang / khu byug rdor grags/
kham bu ya le bzhi/ che ba'i sras rgyal ba ston gzungs/ thod smyon bsam 'grub skye med 'od gsal lo/ /thod smyon bsam 'grub la mdze byung / sham po gangs la bsgrub pa mdzad
mdze thon/ grub thob tu grags/ slob ma pho mo nyi shu rtsa gcig sras mo grub thob bco brgyad byon zhes grags te/ de dag las mang du mched pa ni mo spyod/ yar klungs
kyi sma ra ser pos nyams su blangs/ 'gres khar rang gi nye gnas smyon pa be ro la bshad par gnang / des ce ston dang sum ston gnyis la gnang / ce ston gyis gnyen ston/ sum
ston gyis skal ldan sras mo/ des

gtsang ston/ shes gnyen ston sogs las mched pa la pho spyod ces grags so/ /de lta bu'i spyod yul pa rnams zhi byed du rtogs kyang lugs tha dad du bye'o// // ! dpal nA ro pa'i
lcam ni gu ma'i lugs bod du byung ba ni/ yul snye mor mang su rus khyung po/ btsas ma thag tu rgya gar gyi grub thob a mo gha badzwa gyis lung bstan pa/ gzhon nu la klog
dang bon/ rdzogs chen sems sde bslabs/ stod lung sho ma rar kong ni ru pa'i chos ma lus pa gsan/ de nas gser mang po bsnams nas bal por paNDYi ta su ma ti las lo tsA bslabs/
kri yog gi chos gsan/ a tu lya badzwa gyis grogs mdzad/ rdo rje gdan pa mjal/ dge tshul mdzad/ de nas shrI bha dra sa dznyyA na/ bai ro tsa na/ kha che dgon pa ba/
mai tri pa'i slob ma zhing gi rdo rje/ mi mnyam rdo rje/ rin chen rdo rje gsum/ de wi ko Ta DA ki ma ka na shrI/ bram ze ratna pha la rnams la gsang sngags kyi chos mang
du gsan/ bod du byon/ gu lang gi gser kha rdol ba dang thug gser mang po byung bas slar bal por byon/ pham thing pa la bde mchog nA lendrar nA ro pa'i slob ma dA chen po/
mai tri pa'i slob ma na treng ka ba sogs mang du bsten/ lhag par mai tri pa dang mjal/ de'i tshe rdo rje 'chang dngos la thug pa su yod dris pas/ nA ro pa'i lcam ni gu
ma zhes bya ba yod/ de 'ja' lus brnyes pas su rung gis mi mthong / so sa gling gi dur khrod du mkha' 'gro ma'i tshogs dpon la 'byon pas sems dag na der mthong srid zer/ so
sa gling du byon/ na mo buddhA ya'i gsol ba btab pas ta la bdun srid tsam gyi nam mkha' la mkha' 'gro ma sku mdog smug nag rus pas brgyan pa/ phyag na kha TsAM ga dang
thod pa bsnams pa gcig dang du ma la sogs pa'i gzugs ston pa zhig mthong nas/ ni gu ma yin par nges te phyag dang skor ba byas/ yang dag pa'i gdams pa zhu 'tshal zhus pas/
nga ni sha za'i DA ki yin gsung / yang btud de zhus pas/ gsang sngags kyi gdams pa zhu na gser dgos/ srang lnga brgya phul bas nags su gtor/ sha za'i mkha' 'gro ma yin
nam snyam du the tshom zos/ spyan nam mkha' la gzigs nas mkha' 'gro ma mang po 'dus nas dkyil 'khor sprul/ der sgyu lus rmi lam gyi dbang bskur gnang / mkha' 'gro mas gser
gyi ri bo'i khar bzhag der rmi lam du chos drug tshar gcig

dngos su tshar gsum/ rdo rje'i tshig rkang / sgyu ma lam rim/ gzhan yang rgyud sgrub thabs mang po gsungs/ brgyud pa bdun rdzogs pa'i bar du chig brgyud gyis/ ngas byin gyis
rlob cing lung yang ston gsungs/ de nas sbas pa'i rnal 'byor pa dang / bi rU pa'i slob ma mkha' 'gro ma su kha siddhi mjal/ khyod nas brgyud pa rnams la'ang ngas sku dngos
su ston cing byin gyis rlob bo gsungs/ tshur byon glang ri thang pa la bsnyen par rdzogs/ 'phan yul 'jog por 'chad dkar dgon pa btab/ der ri nag po'i khong seng gi rnal
'byor pa rA hu la gupta badzwa byon/ rgyud sde lnga'i dbang sogs mang du gsan/ de nas shangs su byon lo gsum gyi nang du zhong zhong la sogs pa'i dgon gnas btab/ de'i
slob ma rme'u ston pa/ g.yor po rgya mo che/ rdul ston rin dbang / la stod pa dkon mchog khar/ rmog cog pa/ zhang sgom chos seng yin/ rmog cog pa dang por de nyid dang /
phyis sgam po par gtugs nas phyag rgya chen po'i rtogs pa shar ba yin/ de'i slob ma 'khrungs yul stod lung rnam pa/ gdung rus 'bal/ skyer sgang par grags/ rmog cog pa las
khyung po'i chos yongs su rdzogs pa gsan/ de'i slob ma sangs rgyas gnyan ston chos kyi shes rab/ 'khrungs yul yol gyi mda'/ gdung rus gnyan/ skyer sgang pa las gdam ngag
rdzogs par thob/ de'i slob ma sangs rgyas ston pa bsil mar bon gyi brgyud du 'khrungs/ sangs rgyas gnyan ston la thug de yan la brgyud pa rin chen bdun brgyud zer/ de la
mkhas grub bshangs ston dang / mkhas btsun gzhon nu grub gnyis/ dang po las 'jag pa dang / gnyis pas pa snam bsam sdings btab pas 'jag bsam gnyis su gyes la/ shangs pa bka'
brgyud ces grags so/ /yang jo bo mai tri pa'i slob ma rnams las phyag rgya chen po bod du 'gyur ba la snga phyi bar gsum/ snga ma kong ni ru pa las brgyud pa ste/ de'ang
mai tri pa'i slob ma ka ro pa/ de'i slob ma mchog tu gyur pa ni ru pa ta'i rnal 'byor pa/ de bla ma dang mkha' 'gros lung bstan pas bod du byon pa'i lam bgres ches nas
bal por kong chung pa 'das pa'i ro la grong 'jug mdzad pa yin/ zangs gling pa'i paNDYi ta'i cha byed du byas nas byon pas zangs gling pa byon par grags/ bar pa la stod
smad gnyis las

stod 'gyur/ rgya gar phyag na 'brog jo sras kyis spyan drangs/ gtsang gi chu sgor bzhugs nas lha rje gtsang shod pa sogs bod ston chen po sum cu la gdams pa phyi ma u su te
bal po skye med du grags pa la/ slob ma sgom ka ba bzhi/ gdung drug yor po ba'i bu gsum/ dmag pa sgang pa la sogs pa'o/ /phyi 'gyur mnga' ris pa nag po sher dang skyis rgya
gar du byon nas phyag na sku bgres khar thug phyir log bod du dar ba rnams so/ /de ltar nyan bshad yod pa rags rim ste/ gzhan lo tsA ba dang paNDYi ta du mas bsgyur bshad
mdzad pa dpag tu ma mchis so/ /mdo sde lung rgyun rnams gro lung pa chen pos bskul nas steng pa lo tsA bas rgya gar nas btsal ba dang / phyis 'phags pa rin po ches thugs
rtsol mdzad pas bka' 'gyur ro cog gi lung rgyun yid ches pa 'di byung ngo // // ! gangs can 'dir rdo rje theg pa'i bshad pa dang sgrub pa thams cad kyi sgo nas bstan
pa'i bdag por 'jog 'os pa ni rje btsun mar pa lho brag pa ste/ 'khrungs yul lho brag chu khyer/ gdung mar pa/ yab dbang phyug 'od zer dang / yum skal ldan skyid gnyis la
lcam sring lnga yod pa'i lnga tshigs pa/ gzhon nu nas bri klog mkhas par mkhyen/ shin tu gdug rtsub che bas shed bye re nas yab yum gyis ka ca mang du bskur te dgung lo
bcu gnyis lon pa na chos la brdzangs pa ste/ lo bcu gnyis lon nas chos dang phrad/ de sngon sbyangs kyi bag chags sad pa 'dra/ der bla ma su grags che ba rtsad bcad pas/
de'i dus 'brog mi lo tsA ba skad che bar 'dug nas/ mang mkhar du byon myu gu lung gi dgon par mjal/ phyag rten kyang che bar byas/ chos sgor zhugs sgra skad lo tsA mkhas
pa'i tshad du bslabs te/ dpal myu gu lung gi dgon par phyin/ /sgra bsgyur 'brog mi lo tsA la/ /sgra thad klog skad kyi yig tshad bslabs/ /khong bka' drin mi chung che bar
'khums/ /der gsang sngags kyi chos 'dod kyang yon che la bka' dog pas ma thob ste/ dpal myu gu lung gi dgon pa ru/ /gsang sngags chos kyi mu ge la/ /sems yi dwags byed cing
lo gsum bsdad/ /de nas rgya gar du 'gro ba'i spobs pa skyes te/ yul nas ka ca blangs gser du bsgyur/ sngar gyi ka ca rnams stag ris su gser du btsongs/ der zla bo ma
'byor bar zhag 'ga' bsdad/ sgyer phu'i klog skya chen po de stag sde mig mang su

slob ma gcig gis spyan drangs/ 'bul ba mang po byung ba bsnams te slar log 'gro ba'i zla la byon pas/ dge bshes des shin tu bkur sti che bar mdzad sgyer phu tshun bsdebs jo
bo de la nga lho bal du lo tsA slob tu 'gro rgyu yin/ da res khyod kyi thugs la btags/ tshe'i bar chad ma byung na phyis 'bab sa'ang zhu dgos byas pas/ nga rgas pas phrad
mi 'ong / bu 'di kun la byed 'jug pas cis kyang byon zhig gsung / rdzong pa'ang mdzad/ mang yul du byon/ der gnyos 'byung po dang phrad de khong dang bsdebs nas byon pas/
bdag bal yul gyi lam du zhugs tsa na/ /gcan 'phrang chu la thar dus med/ /nags 'thug po zhig la thon dus med/ /lam ring po zhig la bgrod dus med/ /lam de kun gyi bde dog
mthong tsa na/ /bya dgung la 'phur ba gshog pa 'dar/ /'on kyang ngal dub bya rin mchog /yul lha las babs pa'i bal po mthong / /phyi 'dod yon lta bas chog mi shes/ /mi
'dod khams kyi lha phran yin nam snyam/ /der lo gsum tshad pa la 'dris su bcug de'i ring la byin rlabs can gyi bal po pham mthing pas rnam rgyal dbang po'i sde la gsan pa'i
gdan bzhi'i bshad pa gsan/ sgra dang tshad ma gso ba la zhar chos mdzad/ de nas b.ratal zhugs spyod pa penda pa chen po des rgya gar du khrid/ de nas rgya gar 'gro tsa
na/ /mtha' 'khob kyi jag pa shi skyid la/ /srog ci bder thon pa cung ma bsams/ /gcan gzan gyi ngar skad thos tsa na/ /yid brtan par phyin kyang gom tshugs 'khyor/ /lam de
kun gyi bde dog bshad tsa na/ /dus da lta dran yang glo snying 'dar/ /chu grags pa can gyi ganggA brgal/ /'on kyang bka' ba spyad rin chog /yul dbus 'gyur 'chang gi bkod
pa mthong / /dpal rdo rje gdan gyis sna drangs nas/ /rten khyad par can la mchod pa byas/ /der bi kra ma shI lar slebs/ dge tshul shes rab sengge dang mjal/ da lta bla
ma rgya gar shar phyogs su byon nas ma bzhugs zhag shas ngal gsos gsungs/ der pho nya byung nas bla ma yang dgon par phebs grub/ khyod kyi der bod kyi slob gnyer ba zhig
kyang yod 'dug pa khrid shog gsungs te shar phyogs su byon/ ljongs me tog rgyas pa ri bo gser gling gi dgon par dpal nA ro pa dang mjal/ der tshogs dang mchod pa gu lang
gser gyi maNDYal phul nas chos gnang

dgos zhus pas zhal gyis bzhes/ thog mar dgyes rdor gyi dbang gnang bar tshugs/ der bla mas dgyes rdor lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor mngon sum du sprul nas lo tsA ba khyod dbang lha
la zhu'am nga la zhu gsungs/ lha la dbang dngos su thob na ya mtshan snyam dbang lha la zhu/ rgyud gdam ngag bla ma rang la zhu zhus pas/ de thugs kar bsdus nas/ byin rlabs
kyi rtsa ba bla ma yin pa la/ khyod kyis bla ma las yi dam lhag snyam 'dems pas khyed la mi brgyud kyi phan mi thogs/ chos brgyud chu bo'i gzhung lta bu 'byung gsungs
lung bstan/ dbang dus der mthong lam gyi rtogs pa rgyud la 'khrungs/ theg chen gyi sa dang po non te/ ma skal ba bzang mos rjes gnang ba/ /byin rlabs kyi chu rgyun ma chad
pas/ /dbang bzhi'i don la ngo sprod mdzad/ /zag pa med pa'i ting nge 'dzin skyes/ /zhag bdun bar du brtan pa thob/ /srog rtsol 'pho ba nyi zla gnyis/ /g.yo med nam mkha'i
khyim du bcug /rang byung lhan cig skyes pa'i nyams/ /bde gsal mi rtog khong nas shar/ /bag chags gnyis kyi 'khrul pa de/ /'od gsal lam gyi ngo bor rtogs/ /yid kyi g.yo
ba gzung 'dzin gnyis/ /spros bral chos kyi dbyings su bstim/ /phyi snang ba sgyu ma'i 'khrul 'khor 'di/ /skye med bde ba chen por rtogs/ /nang 'dzin pa yid kyi rnam shes
'di/ /sngar 'dris mdza' bo phrad pa bzhin/ /sems nyid rang ngo rang gis shes/ /lkugs pas rmi lam rmis pa bzhin/ /brjod du med pa'i don cig rtogs/ /gzhon nus bde ba myong
ba bzhin/ /smra ru med pa'i nyams shig shar/ /dang / ljongs me tog rgyas pa'i dgon pa der/ /dbang bzhi'i chu bo rdzogs par bskur/ /zhes pas so/ /de nas dbus dang kha cher
byon/ khyad par puShpa ha rir bzhugs nas/ dgyes rdor rgyud gsum gyi bshad pa/ dbang lung man ngag bsre 'pho gnad kyi mtshams sbyor/ bka' srung gur dud sol dang bcas pa
gnang ste/ gnas ngo mtshar mkha' 'gros lung bstan pa/ /sa byang phyogs kha che'i yul du phyin/ /dpal puShpa ha ri'i dgon pa der/ /sgo srung gi nA ro paN chen la/ /rgyud
zab mo dgyes pa'i rdo rje zhus/ /bsre 'pho gnad kyi mtshams sbyor thob/ /khyad par gtum mo las rgya zhus/ /chos skyong dud sol lha mo thob/ /der bar zhig la gnyos dang phrad/
/dgyes rdor

la chos skad byas pas mar pa rgyal/ /pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa zhes bya ba rlung sbar 'dzin du bya ba de dgos zer nas de la lan 'debs rgyu ma byung / log nas bla ma la zhus
pas/ nub tu la kShe tra'i dgon pa na paNDYi ta ye shes snying po bya ba pha rgyud kyi bdag po zhig bzhugs der song gsung / phyin pa'i lam du chu mi zan dug gi chu brgal
na sha lpags zul bshus 'gro ba zhig yod pa la de'i 'gram na yul chung zhig 'dug pa'i mi la rngan pa byin pas/ nags gseb nas shing lo zhig blangs/ de btags te lus la byugs
nas da brgal bas chog zer/ brgal bas sbrul bzhin shun pa brjes/ gzhan skyon ma byung / der ye shes snying po dang mjal gsang ba 'dus pa 'phags lugs rgyud 'grel pa dbang
man ngag dang bcas pa zhus te/ chu mi zan dug gi chu la brgal/ /lus dug sbrul bzhin du shun pa brjes/ /srog dor bar phangs so chos la bsams/ /nub la kShe tra yi dgon pa
ru/ /dpal ye shes snying po'i zhabs la gtugs/ /pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa nyan/ /sgyu lus 'od gsal gyi gdam ngag thob/ /lam rim pa lnga yi don la bslabs/ /de nas tshur log
bla ma'i drung du kha che paNDYi ta chen po A ka ra siddhi byon nas gsang 'dus zhu ba dang 'grig gsol ba btab pas dus la bab pa yin gsungs gnang bas bshad pa la khyad med/
man ngag zab pa tsam byung bas/ bla ma rang gi mkhyen bzhin du bdag de nas phar gtong ba zhus pas/ khong la gsang 'dus kyi bka' babs pa yin gsung / der gnyos dang phrad
chos skad byas pas rgyal/ khong nas ma rgyud mahA ma yA bya ba dgos zer/ bla ma la zhus pas/ bla ma'i zhal nas lho dug mtsho'i gling na paNDYi ta zhi ba bzang po bya ba
ma rgyud kyi bdag po zhig bzhugs/ der song gsungs lam 'jigs pa che bas bar chad mi 'byung ba'i byin brlabs mdzad de byon pas ha la pa Ta dug mtsho khol ba'i gling gi do
ri la btsal bas nyi ma'i dgung la smag rum mun pa 'thibs/ dmod btsugs nas gsol ba btab pas mun pa sangs/ rje btsun dang mjal/ der pho nya dang phrad dam gsungs/ stag gzig
'dra las gzhan su dang yang ma phrad zhus pas/ de ka yin mod gsung / der tshogs dang gser gyi maNDYal phul/ mahA ma yA'i rgyud dbang sgrub thabs rnal 'byor gsum la sogs
pa'i man ngag kun gnang ste/ lho dug mtsho khol ma'i gling du phyin/ /dus nyi ma'i

dgung la smag rum 'thibs/ /lam da ci gsal ba da lta stor/ /srog yal bar bor nas rje btsun btsal/ /dpal zhi ba bzang po dngos dang mjal/ /ma rgyud ma hA ma yA thob/ /dbyibs
rnal 'byor gsum gyi don la bslabs/ /sgyu ma gsum 'khyud kyi gdam ngag thob/ /tshur log bla ma nyid kyis snga ma las bshad pa rgyas tsam gzhan khyad med pa zhig gnang / de
nas gnyos dang phrad/ chos skad byas pas khong la lab rgyu ma byung / khyod kyis mahA ma yA su la bslabs zer/ ngas bla ma thar pa'i lam ston la bslabs/ de gar bzhugs/ grong
khyer ser skya na'o byas/ de bla ma la zhus pas gsang mi dgos khos bgrod par mi nus gsung / der rje btsun mai tri pa'i snyan pa gsan pa dang / bla mas kyang gnang ste
rgya gar shar phyogs su byon/ ri bo me ltar 'bar ba'i dur khrod dngos grub can gyi dgon par mnga' bdag mai tri pa dang mjal/ thugs rjes lhag par gzung / mtshan brjod gsan/
snying po skor gyi gdam ngag rnams gnang / des sgom pa'i lam la bogs phyung ste/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa ji lta ba rtogs/ sa drug pa brnyes/ shar dngos grub kyi
chu bo ganggA brgal/ /ri rab tu 'khrugs pa'i dur khrod kyi/ /dngos grub can gyi dgon pa ru/ /rje mnga' bdag mai tri'i zhabs la btugs/ /rgyud zab mo bstod pa glur blangs
thos/ /chos phyag rgya che la rtogs pa bskyangs/ /sems dngos po'i bzhugs tshul gtan la phab/ /der char zim pa zhig byung nas bla ma gyang sna breng nge zhig na char yibs
byed cing bzhugs pas/ lha khang zhig gi bya 'dabs kyi kha na bud med cig bya brun 'phyag gi 'dug bud med de'i phyags ma shod du lhung bas phar cer tshur cer bltas nas mi
med pa 'dra bas steng nas lag pa nar byas nas phyags ma blangs song / su yin bltas pas jo bo mai tri pa'i mu dra yin/ chu shing gi snye ma can bya ba de 'dug de mkha' 'gro
mar go nas/ de rang du gser gyi maNDYal phul nas bdag rjes su gzung 'tshal zhus pas/ gsang gdan le'u dang po'i dbang bskur/ yum bka' dang rdzogs rim chu shing gi me tog
gsang gdan gyi bshad pa byung / de nas log nas nA ro pa'i spyan snga na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ khrus mdzad pas srung 'khor khwa tas khyer ba rje btsun nA ro pas sdigs mdzub
mdzad pas khwa ta sa la lhung / slar bzhes de dang dus mtshungs par rgya tshad theng gsum grongs pa la thug pa byung / drag

nas bla mas so sa gling gi dur khrod na mkha' 'gro ma bzhugs pas der song la gdan bzhi zhus gsung / der byon rnal 'byor ma mi rus kyi rgyan cha can dang mjal/ 'di nA ro pa'i
lcam ni gu mar grags pa de kha yin/ der gdan bzhi gsan/ 'di la gdan bzhi ka'i bshad pa byung / log nas bla mas gnang / tshig ches rgyas pa don khyad med par byung gzhan
yang dpal singga li pa sogs bsten/ rgyud man ngag mtha' dag zhig gsan te/ rje nA ro chen pos sna drangs pa'i/ /grub thob bla ma rnams dang mjal/ /spyir rgyud sde bzhi la
nyan bshad byas/ /khyad par ma rgyud mtha' dag bslabs/ /pha rgyud gsang ba 'dus pa thob/ /dang / lar dur khrod nyul ba'i rnal 'byor pa/ /shing drung gnas pa'i ku sa li/
/yongs su ma grags 'ga' yod de/ /rdzogs rim kha 'thor mang du zhus/ /ngo mtshar can gyi sgrub thabs dang / /phran tshegs gdam ngag rtsis las 'das/ /chos 'brel ba tsam gyi
bla ma mang / /dpal singga li pas sna drangs nas/ /mngon shes rig pa mnga' brnyes shing / /snang ba 'gyur nges bcu gsum bzhugs/ /dang / chos smon lam gyi 'brel pa bcu gsum
dang / /khyad par grub thob zhal lnga bzhugs/ /rje 'gran gyi do med rnam gnyis te/ /gtso bo paN chen nA ro pa/ /de 'og rgyal sras mai tri pa/ /der dpe rnams la gzhi 'gyur
mdzad/ bla ma rnams la zhus te gtan la phab bo/ /de nas gser yang zad tshur byon pas gnyos kyi 'tsho chas kyang 'dzad nas log 'ong ba dang 'grigs nas bsdebs byon pa na/
gnyos kyi bsam pa la/ gser nga mang rung chos kho mkhas par 'dug bsam/ ngan zhugs te/ khong la khur tsa 'khur ba'i a tsa ra 'dug nas de la bslabs/ lo tsA ba bya ba khres
po 'khur nas phyin na mi'i mthong mi 'byung / dpe 'di la khol zer nan che bas dpe khres a tsa ra la gtad pas/ des gangga'i dbus su chu la shor skad byas te bskyur/ chu
khar a tsa ra bzung nas rgyal po la gtug byas pas/ gnyos kyis bslabs pa dang rngan pa byin pa zhib par bshad byung / der gnyos la khrel 'ded tsam mdzad/ myur du rgya gar
la log pa'i thugs dam mdzad de/ bal po'i mtha' 'khob tu sho gam pas bskyil/ de dus sa ra has mnal lam du byin gyis brlabs/ do ha rdo rje'i mgur stsal/ bal po nas rim gyis
bod du phyags phebs/ der sgyer

phu klog skya chen po gshegs/ de'i sras po shes rab brtsegs kyis zhabs nas bteg thog mar mahA ma yA'i chos btsugs/ rim gyis yul du byon/ lho la yag gi ba rang lba ba can sogs
'dus/ dpe med kyang gdam ngag rnams thugs la byang bar bzhugs pas 'chad nyan smar bar byung / de nas slar byang nam ra'i gser kha rdol ba dang thugs gser mang du rnyed
nas rgya gar du byon/ bla ma rnams la btang rag gi maNDYal tshogs dang mchod pas mnyes par byas te/ sngar ma gsan pa rnams gsan pa dang gsan pa rnams kyi dpe bod na 'gyur
grub pa rnams gzhi de khar bzhag nas/ bcos dgos pa rnams bla ma rnams la zhus te gtan la phab/ 'ga' zhig ma bsgyur bar rgya dpe rang bsnams/ jo bo nA ro pa la de res bde
mchog rang lugs kyi tshogs bshad tsam/ lo dril nag po'i skor/ 'dus pa ye shes zhabs lugs sogs gsan/ mai tri pa la dgyes rdor sangs rgyas thod pa gsan nas/ bod du 'byon
khar rje btsun nA ro pas phyag dbu thog tu bzhag nas/ nam mkha'i me tog skyes bu yis/ /mo sham bu yi rta zhon nas/ /rus sbal spu yi thun brabs te/ /ri bong rwa yi phur pa
yis/ /dgra bo chos nyid klong du bsad/ /lkugs pas smra zhing dmus long lta/ /'on pas nyan zhing zha bos rgyug /nyi zla gar mkhan dung 'bud cing / /'khor lo bu chung skor
bar byed/ /lan gcig cis kyang shog cig gsungs/ /'byon pa'i dam bca' phul/ de nas bod du phebs mes rngog mtshur dbang de la sogs pa rjes su bzung / slar 'phan yul nas byang
'dam gyi bar byon/ snying drung du mar pa mgo yags kyis gser srang bzhi bcus yol go chen po zhig bkang ste phul ba sogs gser gtos che ba rnyed/ der tho rangs mnal lam
na dar gyi gos gyon/ rus pa'i rgyan btags pa'i bu mo gsum bsgrigs nas/ mkha' 'gro nam mkha'i me tog gis/ /snyan rgyud mo sham rta zhon nas/ /brjod med rus sbal spus brabs
te/ /skye med ri bong rwa phur bus/ /te lo chos nyid klong du bsad/ /te lo lkugs pa smra bsam brjod med kyis/ /nA ro 'on pa chos nyid chos sku'i ri bo la/ /blo gros zha
bo 'gro 'ong med par rgyug /nyi zla dgyes pa rdo rje ste/ /gar mkhan du ma ro gcig yin/ /dung ni snyan pa phyogs bcur grags/ /'bud pa snod ldan dag

la 'bud/ /'khor lo bde mchog 'khor lo ste/ /bskor ba snyan rgyud 'khor lo nyid/ /bu chung zhen pa med par bskor/ /zer mnal sad pa dang dpal nA ro pa'i drung du 'gro ba la bskul
bar dgongs te/ chos 'phro rnams 'phral la bsgril lho brag tu byon/ rgya gar du chas pa la grwa bu slob rnams kyis nan gyis zhus kyang ma gsan/ nga bla ma la dam nyams
na mi rung / lan gcig cis kyang shog gsungs pas 'gro gsungs/ cis kyang thegs na phyag phyi ba dang bcas te thegs dgos zhus pas ma gsan par gcig pur bzhud par chas/ der
grwa pa thams cad kyis gser ci rnyed byas pas gtos che ba byung ba bsnams te byon/ nyang stod du jo bo rje phebs pa dang mjal/ chos 'grel gsan skad cha zhus pas/ rje btsun
nA ro pa na ning gi lo gsar gyi nya la spyod pa la gshegs gsungs pa thos pas thugs thon 'gro ba lta bu zhig byung / 'on kyang bla ma grongs pa ni min mjal ba zhig cis kyang
yong snyam pa'i re bas gsos/ der nga'i lo tsA la sdod gsungs/ bla ma la dam bca' phul pa'i lo rgyus zhus pas/ 'o na bden/ rje btsun thugs rje che bas mjal ba'i skabs
dbye ste 'ong gsungs/ de nas bal por phebs/ dgun de nyid la rgya gar du byon/ dge tshul pa dang mjal lo rgyus rnams zhib tu dris pas/ jo bo dang mthun par byung la/ spyod
pa la gshegs khar kho cis kyang sleb 'ong / de la 'di gtod gsung byin rlabs rten 'ga' zhig gtad/ der khong nas rje btsun thugs rje che bas dang khyod rang mos gus kyi gdung
shugs che ba 'dzom pas mjal rang 'ong / de la yo byad 'di tshos tshogs 'khor bskor la gsol ba thob gsungs pa bden snyam/ thog mar mai tri pa'i drung du byon/ de'i dus
su dpal gnyis med rdo rjes thugs la btags/ dus de'i tshe ngo mtshar ba'i ltas ni sna tshogs pa byung ste/ sku rgyab gtad pa'i ljon shing gis yang yang g.yo ba dang mgul
ba/ sprul pa'i ce spyang dmar mo bdun nam mkha' nas dngos su gtor ma len pa/ sa gsum gyi mkha' 'gro rnams gar bsgyur sngags kyi rang sgra sgrog pa/ bar snang gang ba'i zhing
skyong gi mkha' 'gro rnams rol mo 'bul ba/ sgron shing mar me mdzub gang zhag bdun du 'bar ba/ mnga' bdag gi gsungs nas/ khyod skye ba gsum gyi 'og rol tu sangs rgya
bar 'gyu ro zhes dang / ljongs kha ba can gyi rgyud du gdul bya snod ldan

yod pa dang / rje btsun nA ro pa dang mjal bar lung bstan/ lho dug mtsho'i gling du byon/ de'i dus su dpal zhi ba bzang po de tshogs kyi 'khor lo mdzad/ bud med kyi ro zhig
tshogs gral du 'dug pa'i thod pa rlon pa khrag tsa re ba'i nang du/ dpal zhi ba bzang pos gu ya ma tri'i chu ltem nas klad pa dang dri chu bsres pa de dam tshig tu brim
zhing 'dug pa mar pa'i thad du sleb pa dang / thod pa'i rdzas chil chil khol gyin 'dug nas nang du gzigs pas mahA ma yA'i yig 'bru sngags kyi 'khor lo zhal gzigs/ zab mo
sngags kyi rnal 'byor gyi rtogs pa dang mthar thug de kho na nyid kyi don khong du chud par byas so/ /de yang nA ro pa dang mjal bar lung bstan/ de nas nub tu la kShe trar
byon/ dpal ye shes snying po gang na bzhugs dris pas/ rigs ngan ma zhig gis nye gnas byas nas nags gseb ya gi na bzhugs/ rigs ngan ma de da lta chu 'chu ru 'ong zer/ chu
mig rtsar bsdad pas de byung nas bla ma la mjal ba'i zhu ba bskur bas spyil por song / de nas rigs ngan mo des bum pa zhig khyer nas 'ong ste chu 'di'i sum gnyis kyis khrus
gyis sum gcig kha ru 'thung zer nas/ rigs ngan ma des wa ti la chu bzed kyi 'dug pas chu bum pa'i nang du blugs pa dang / de thams cad byang chub sems su skya mer gyis
song / de nas bud med de rang bum pa'i steng du lus kyi 'khrul 'khor bcas nas 'dug pas/ gsang ba'i gnas nas rakta'i rgyun babs pas byang sems dkar dmar du 'dres pa de'i
sum gnyis kyis khrus byas/ sum gcig 'thungs/ lhag ma yod dam snyam bum nang du bltas pas/ bum nang na dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i dkyil 'khor rten brten par bcas pa khra sram
me gzigs/ de ma thag tu dpal ye shes snying po byon nas phyag phul bas/ zhal nas khyod nyon mongs pa'i 'ching ba las grol lam/ rgyud yongs su sbyangs sam/ de kho na nyid
kyi don khong du chud dam/ zhes gsungs nas byin gyis brlabs so/ /der sa brgyad pa brnyes/ de nas so sa gling du byon pas lam pa li pa Ta zhes bya bar brtol/ der bu mo
zhig shing thog dpal 'bras srung gin 'dug de la shing thog bslangs pas/ de na re nga'i ma la bslang dgos zer nas des ma la sbran byung / de rnal 'byor ma'i chas can du 'dug
des ltung ba'i lta stangs byas byung ba'i mod la shing

thog rnams sa la 'byar te bab byung / de nas gang 'dod zo zer/ bsgrubs te gcig za bar brtsams te kha phye bas/ de'i nang du gdan bzhi ba'i dkyil 'khor rten brten par bcas pa
mngon sum du gzigs te/ bud med ma smad mkha' 'gro mar mkhyen/ rnal 'byor ma mi rus kyi rgyan cha can gyis byin gyis brlabs pa yin/ de nas ri ri pa dang / ka so ri pa dge
tshul can du phyin tshogs kyi 'khor lo bskor/ de thams cad du dpal nA ro pa dang mjal ba kho nar lung bstan/ de nas bi kra ma la shI la'i nA ro pa'i gtsug lag khang shar
khri sgo brtsegs pa zhes yod pa der bzhugs te/ dgyes rdor rgyud gzigs/ rgyud kyi chings 'chad lugs thams cad paNDYi ta gzhan las nA ro pa lhag par mkhyen nas shin tu ngo
mtshar/ ga na bzhugs kyang btsal dgos snyam pa ka li zhal blta ba ste 'bras dkar mo bre gsum dang nya sha zhig chas su bsnams te tshol du phyin pas ma rnyed par rigs ngan
gyi grong du tshud/ der rgyal pos btson du bzung / zhag gsum nas btang / rgyal po de 'tsho ba'i yo byad ni sbyin sreg gi thab khung du rlung g.yab kyis g.yabs pas me 'byung
/ de'i gseb nas zas sna tshogs pa gzar bus bcus nas 'ong ba gzigs/ bla ma rnams rgyal po de'ang nA ro'i sprul pa yin gsung ngo / /de nas ma rnyed par dpal penda pa
chung ba byon pa dang thug de sa mkhan du byas nas btsal yang ma rnyed/ penda pa log bla ma rang gis smyon pa 'khyam pa lta bur nags gseb dur khrod bas mtha' thams cad nyul
bas/ nyin gcig tsandan gyi sdong po zhig gi steng na/ dgyes pa rdo rje lha dgu'i dkyil 'khor 'ja' tshon gyi gur phub pa lta bu snang la rang bzhin med pa/ sdong po la
ma reg reg la khad pa de'i bcom ldan 'das ma lhan cig skyes ma'i thugs kar uShTa sngags kyi 'khor lo spu shad kyis bris pa lta bu sgor re ba skus mi sgrib pa zhal gzigs/
yang btsal bas shel gyi pha bong la nA ro gshegs pa'i zhabs rjes rnyed/ da de myur bar mjal 'ong snyam drod pa skyes te/ de kho na'i mdun du maNDYal 'bul gyin gsol ba btab
nas zhag bdun song ba dang / dpal nA ro pa dngos su de'ang mi lpags kyi g.yang gzhi gsol ba/ thod pa dang kha TsAM ga bsnams shing / sku gcer bu stag sham ral pa'i thor
tsugs rus pa'i rgyan drug gis brgyan pa dpal he ru ka'i

chas su zhugs pa zhig byon/ rab tu dga' ches yun ring po sdug bsngal bzhin du btsal ba'i yus kyis brnangs te lus sku la btsun mo lta bur 'khyud de ngus nas rje btsun thugs
rje re chung zhes zhus/ de nas gser lhag thams cad maNDYal du phul bas ma bzhes/ nan gyis zhus pas bzhes te/ spyan zim mdzad/ bla ma dkon mchog mchod cig gsung nam mkha'
la gtor song bas/ 'phangs snyam shar bas mod la/ khyod 'dod na slar yang yod do gsungs ma god par gtad/ 'di thams cad gser gling yin mod gsungs zhabs brdabs pas sa gzhi thams
cad gser du song / der tshogs 'khor shoms gsung / 'di na nya khog gcig las mi 'dug zhus pas/ de dum bu drug cur gtugs la la ba'i khung du shing los gtums la cung zad
zhog gsungs bzhag de nas cung zad song ba dang dbye bas bza' ba dang bca' ba'i rigs sna drug cu/ ro brgya dang ldan pa mang po zhig tu song 'dug pas/ der tshogs kyi 'khor
lo mdzad de/ rang grol ye shes nyi ma yis/ /puShpa ha ri'i dgon pa ru/ /bhU ti'i ma rig mun sel la/ /ye shes snang bas khyab par gyis/ /zhes bla mas lung bstan pa yin pas
puShpa ha rir 'gro gsungs byon/ der mkha' 'gro snyan rgyud/ rang lugs bde mchog 'khor lo'i slob bshad kyi rtse mor phyin pa/ gzhan yang bsre 'pho'i man ngag lhag ma lus
pa/ ro snyoms sogs sngar ma gnang ba dang gnang ba rnams snying por bsgril te gnang der zla ba gsum bzhugs zer/ de dus bla ma 'di ma rnyed pas sbyangs/ da bod du log mi
'gro bla ma 'di rang gi drung du sdod snyam thugs la shar bas/ slob dpon spyod pa bas shar phyogs kyi rgyud byin gyis brlabs pa yin/ slob dpon 'phags pas lho phyogs kyi
rgyud byin gyis brlabs/ rgyal po indra bhU tis nub phyogs kyi rgyud byin gyis brlabs/ ngas byang phyogs pa ta'i rgyud kha ba can byin gyis brlabs pa yin pas/ khyod 'di ru
ma sdod bod du song zhig byang phyogs kha ba can gdul bya snod ldan yod do gsungs te/ bla ma rang phyogs las rnam rgyal gyi spyod pa la zhugs te mi snang bar gyur to/ /de
nas gser lhag ma rnams kyis rten mahA bo dhi sogs la mchod pa mdzad dgongs/ de'i dus su rdo rje gdan gyi dus mchod dang 'dzom/ der nyin mo mis mchod pa 'bul/ nub mo mi
ma yin gyis mchod pa 'bul ba yin pas/ de'i dus su nub mo ku co chen po byung / nang par bltas pas srin

po shin tu che ba zhig shi de'i gdong pa rang la'ang mtho bcu drug 'dug nas/ thams cad langs dogs skrag nas yod pa'i tshe/ lo tsA bas penda pa la ngas bsgoms pa'i nus pa bstan
nam byas pas/ gdam ngag gi rtsal ci 'dug lta yi gyis gsungs/ der lus pande pa la bcol nas srin po'i ro la grong 'jug mdzad nas bas mthar dor/ der thams cad kyis lo tsA
ba grub thob tu shes nas bkur sti bgyis so/ /de nas bal por sleb dus dur khrod ra ma do lir bla ma me mnyam rdo rje tshogs 'khor mdzad 'dug pas/ de kri ya zhus pa'i bla
ma yin pas des bos byon/ rnal 'byor pa de rnams tshogs mgyogs par gyis/ 'phyis na mkha' 'gro ma'i bar chad 'ong zer/ de rnams la 'di 'dra ba'i rnal 'byor pa 'ong ba/ mkha'
'gro ma la 'dzem pa/ mkha' 'gro mas byin gyis rlob dngos grub ster ba yin mod/ nga'i bla ma rnams zhing skyong gi mkha' 'gro ma dngos su gral la sgrig pa yin te snyam
nA ro mai tri dran du song rgya gar du log dgongs tho rangs mnal lam la/ shing lo gyon pa'i bud med cig sngas su 'ongs nas phyag spyi bor bzhag da rgya gar du ma ldog bod
na gdul bya yod/ de'i bar du bar chad mi 'byung zer ba dang / bal yul rin chen tshul gyi gtsug lag khang na bzhugs pa'i tshe/ tho rangs mnal lam la jo bo mai tri pa sengge
la chibs nas byon te/ skye med mtshon pa'i brda bstan/ yi ge med pa'i chos gsungs/ brjod du med pa'i don rtogs/ sngar ma shar ba'i nyams shar ba rmis/ mnal sad pa dang
rje btsun mai tri pa dran du song / de nas rim pas bod du phebs/ bu slob rnams kyis gzhi len phun sum tshogs pa bgyis/ de'ang rgya gar du byon thebs dang po la lo bcu dgu
bar pa la drug de res rgya gar rang du lo gcig bzhugs/ dgung lo bcu gnyis nas lnga bcu rtsa gnyis kyi bar la sbyangs pa mdzad pas lo bzhi bcu/ dpal nA ro pa rang bsten
pa la snga phyi bsdoms pas/ lo bcu drug dang zla ba bdun du bsten/ dus skad cig mi 'bral 'grogs pa'i phyir/ /dang / nga mar ston chos kyi blo gros 'di/ /tshe sum gnyis rgya
gar yul du bskyal/ /lo bzhi bcu'i bar du thos bsam byas/ /dus na ning gdug pa sbrul gyi lo/ /cho 'phrul rta yi zla ba la/ /

mi kho bo lam du zhugs nas mchi/ /dang / dus gzhes ning rgya gar 'gro ba'i tshe/ /longs spyod 'byor pas phongs dus su/ /rin chen gser gyis yol mo bkang / /dang / rgya gar yul
du lan gsum phyin/ /lus srog la ma bltas dam chos btsal/ /zhes gsungs so/ /'byon thebs bar pa log nas rngog ston mgo yags la sogs pa rjes su bzung / phyi ma 'byon dus
rje btsun mi la zhabs phyir 'byon pa skad dang / mar pa'i nyer dgu pa la mi la 'khrungs pa dang / phyi ma 'byon pa bzhi bcu rtsa gnyis pa la byed pa mar pa'i dgung lo so
gcig pa la jo bo bod du 'byon pa rnams dus mi 'grig des na rje btsun rang gi mgur dang bstun na lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa la byon/ rtsa gnyis pa la rgya gar du bzhugs/ nga gsum
pa la phyir 'khor/ de nas jo mo bdag med ma khab tu bzhes/ der gzhan gyi tha mal pa 'jig rten la zhen pa zhig tu rtog go /skal ldan rnams la skal ba ji lta ba'i lam ston
par mdzad pa las rngog chos sku rdo rje la dgyes rdor/ gur/ mahA ma yA/ gdan bzhi rtsa bshad 'grel pa man ngag dang bcas pa gnang / rjes kyi brgyud pa bdun tshun rdo rje
dril bu 'dzin shes pas chog kho bo rang gis byin gyis rlob pa yin gsung / mes tshon po la bde dgyes gsang gsum ma yA sangs rgyas thod pa man ngag dang bcas pa gnang /
dol gyi mtshur ston dbang nge la gsang ba 'dus pa lugs gsum/ rtsa rgyud sgron gsal/ rgyud phyi rtsa 'grel/ bskyed rdzogs kyi man ngag dgyes rdor sogs gnang / 'di gsum la
bshad rgyun mu tig star la rgyus pa lta bu'i bka' babs gzhan yang 'dam snying drung gi mar pa mgo yags/ dol pa gag ston/ gra'i me'u chung / chu god dpal le/ dge bshes khe
gad/ mjal ba la snga ba klog skya/ gnyal gyi shud kyi lba ba can/ la yag pa ba rang lba ba can/ 'phrang gi rgya ston zhig po/ gtsang rong rgya mkhar gyi zhang ston no/ /khe
gad ni lo tsA ba 'khor lo grags kyi yab/ rje btsun grongs nas rgyud rgyud 'grel gyi rgya dpe phal cher 'di'i lag tu byung / mar pa bya ze ba/ myang sgom sprang ltag lha
rje se rings/ de dag rgyud dbang man ngag gis rjes su bzung ba khong rang tsho nas mi thog 'ga' zung gi bar du 'chad nyan gyi rgyun byung ba rkyang / zhang ston gyis mar
mes gnyis ka la gtugs/ gzhan lho pa te sgom ni/ rje btsun gyi chibs kha ba sku lus 'di khas mkha' spyod byon pa/ chos 'brel ba tsam gyi

slob ma/ rtsa mi lo tsA/ mar do/ spu sreng lo chung sogs mang ngo / /jo mo gzhan brgyad de tshogs kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i tshe dgyes rdor sprul pa'i lha dgur dngos su ston/
gtso mo'i sras su mdo sde 'khrungs/ dgung lo nyer gcig pa la rtas brdab pas dbu chag rgyud man ngag la sbyangs pa che/ grong 'jug nus pas bod du gdul bya med pas grong 'jug
btub pa'i mi ro ma rnyed nas phug ron gyi ro la grong 'jug mdzad/ rgya gar shar phyogs su bram ze gzhon nu'i ro la grong 'jug gyis la 'phrin las mdzod bla ma gsungs pa
las phyis thos pa'i lo rgyus med/ gzhan 'khor gyi bdag med ma bzhi tsam la sras drug sras mo gcig ste bdun yod zer/ sras mya ngan las 'das pa'i gong du rje btsun mi las
gtugs nas lo bzhi tsam/ yi chad brgyad kyi sgo nas tshar bcad/ sras kyi che 'don mdzad pa'i dus nas rjes su bzung / che 'don nas lo gnyis tsam la sras gshegs/ de dus rje
mar pa dgung lo don drug tsam mo/ /mi la la bde dgyes gsang 'dus/ gdan bzhi/ sangs rgyas thod pa/ mahA ma yA rnams kyi rgyud dbang sgrub thabs rim pa gnyis dang bcas pa
snying po don gyi skor rnams mthar phyin pa gnang yang / sgrub rgyud kyi bka' babs pas brgyud 'dzin rgyas kyang bshad rgyun bde mchog las ma dar ro/ /rje mar pas rgya gar
na gdan bzhi ka'i dpe nA ro pa min pa la med gsungs/ bla ma gro bo lung na chos gsung dus/ snga sde sgang na jo bo khyung pa bya ba 'gos kyi slob ma zhig gdan bzhi 'grel
pa lugs 'chad pa la/ bla ma'i gsung nas nga cag dmag drang dgos gsungs/ de ci lags zhus pas/ rgya gar na gdan bzhi ka shes pa gzhan med par bod du gdan bzhi ka 'chad pa
des gsungs/ de khong gis gsan nas khong gsung ba mad de mchi/ dka' ba mdzad pa yin gsungs 'phro bcad/ rje btsun gdan bzhi'i rgyud gsum 'chad pa na mkha' 'gro ma rnams thib
se nyan pa la 'ong gsungs/ de lta bu'i rje btsun de rgyud man ngag gi rgya mtshor bzhugs pa la bod rnams kyi bsod nams la bum pa gang ba tsam zhig dar ba yin/ de nas rje
mar pas grong 'jug kyang 'ga' re mdzad de bstan/ sku'i bkod pa'ang du mar snang / ting nge 'dzin gyi dkyil 'khor sprul nas mngon sum du ston/ sa thams cad rdzogs kyang
sa bcu pa'i tshul 'dzin/ brgyad cu rtsa brgyad pa la yum bdag med ma 'od kyi gong bur

byas te thugs khar bsdus/ 'gro don gzhan che bar dgongs pa dang / sku gdung gi gdul bya gzigs nas sku spyi bo nas 'od dang bcas te bla ma yi dam mkha' 'gro'i tshogs kyis gdugs
rgyal mtshan rol mo sgra mchod pa'i sprin dang lhan du gshegs/ sku gdung gi gdung rnams rngog mdo sdes sras bya ring 'khor lo la blus te da lta gzhung spre zhing na dngul
gyi gdung rten bzhengs/ de'ang gser gyi gdung khang du bzhugs su gsol lo/ /rje btsun 'di la thams cad du 'phags pa kun tu bzang po dang / Dombi he ru ka'i sprul par
grags so/ /rngog chos sku rdo rje ni/ rngog lo tsA ba khu dbon dang yab tshan dang po/ 'brog pa yin la/ 'khrungs sa gzhung ri bo/ sngags rnying ma slob tu gtsang sgyer phu'i
dge bshes sgyer chung pa can du byon/ sgyer phu'i chag lo dang yang mjal/ bye ma lung pa las mtshan brjod gsan/ de dus dge bshes sgyer chung pas rje mar pa'i bsngags
pa brjod pas mtshan thos pa rang la dad pa'i spu long g.yos/ chos 'phro myur bar zhus nas gzhung du log rta zhig khyer nas lho gro bo lung du byon/ rta phul bas/ khyod kyi
rta phul ba de phyag rten yin na ches/ 'bul ba yin na chung gsung / de'i dus rngog rang gis dgung lo bcu drug tsam/ rje mar pa zhe drug tsam yin/ thog mar bdag med lha
mo bco lnga zhus nyams su blangs ring por ma thog par lha mo bco lnga'i dkyil 'khor dngos su gzigs/ bla ma la bdag skal bar ldan nam/ chos 'di byin rlabs che bar yin zhus
pas/ gnyis ka yin gsung / de nas gzhung du na ma zlum po zhig gi khar gnas gzhi khyung lta bu zhig btab pas zlum khyung du grags par lan grangs du ma spyan drangs/ ka ca
spong thag lan gsum byas nas dgyes rdor rtsa 'grel ma yA gdan bzhi yongs rdzogs so so'i man ngag khyad par bsre 'pho gnad kyi mtshams sbyor rnams gnang / 'dis thos pa dang
bsgrub pa stabs su mdzad pas ye shes kyi sku brnyes/ 'chad nyan mdzad pas slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa thon/ dgung lo drug cu rtsa gcig pa la dben gnas nas ston btsas
ma rnga ba'i dus gsung chen pos bos te/ nga'i phyi la su 'gro 'dod shog gsungs pa la gzhan su'ang ma byung bar kun gyis mthong bar nam mkha' la gshegs so/ /'di mkha' spyod
chung ngu yin snyam gleng ba ni log rtog ste/ mi las ser

ba phab dus bya byi'i ro spungs pa dum zhig thugs dam la bzhugs te se khol gtogs pas gnam la di ri rir zhes 'phur song zhes grags la/ rgya gar gyi slob dpon nag po spyod pas
kyang bsad pa nus te slar gso mi nus zhes smra na bsad gso nus pa'i rnal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po gang du byon pa'i mkha' spyod kyang 'og min zhes grags pas bcu pa
rnams sangs rgyas byed pa der ro/ /de la slob ma rams/ spa/ rngog rgyang / sum pa/ lho pa sogs mang / de las rams klu gong pa de gzhung lugs mtha' dag la sbyangs pa'i mkhas
pa rgya gar gyi paNDYi ta 'bum phrag gsum pa'ang rtsod pas pham par byas/ des bla ma chos rdor la gtugs/ de dus gzhung mdar bla ma la sgugs gra byur sar khong gis bla
ma yin pa skad byas de sngon la byon pas btson la shor/ bla ma la skyon ma byung bas shin tu mnyes/ chos gsung dus gzhan gyi 'dres byung na nga la rje mar pa'i gsung gtsang
ma de zhus byas zhu phod byas chog des dgyes rdor la bshad pa shin tu gtsang / des dbon po ram rdo rje btsan sogs dang / mkhas pa rgya nam/ de'i slob ma tre bo mgon po
ba/ de'i slob ma gnyan rdo rje sengge/ de'i slob ma snye mdo thams cad mkhyen pa/ de'i sras kun dga' don grub sogs de lugs 'dzin/ sras ni mdo sde/ las stod kyi spug ye
rgyal gyi skye ba/ rngog ston dang spa mo chos brtson gnyis kyi sras mar pa mjal/ 'di dgung lo brgyad lon pa na rje mar pa gshegs/ bcu gsum la yab gshegs/ de dus yab la dbang
rgyud man ngag gsan yang brgyud pa 'ded pa tsam las med pas/ yab gshegs gdong zhal chems la dgyes rdor ram/ ma hA ma yA spa la nyon sogs byung / man ngag ni chos rdor
gyis brjed thor btab ste rmo mo zhig la bu 'di lo bco brgyad lon dus sprod gsungs pas/ dpe 'di la rngog pa'i bsre 'phor grags/ gsung bzhin ram can byon/ des dang dod ma
byas pas ma mgu bar log rngog dang spa la gsan zer/ gzhan yang bla ma mang du bsten/ de dus kyi gsang sngags pa la mkhyen pa che bar grags/ dgung lo bdun cu rtsa bdun gyi
bar du dbang dang rgyud gdams pa la 'chad nyan mdzad/ 'grel pa rin chen rgyan 'dra brtsams/ 'di la bla ma chos rdor

gyis mdzad pa rin po che'i rgyan bya ba zhig yod/ dpe khams su shor nas de dang 'dra ba zhig byed gsungs pas de ltar grags so zer ba blun gtam yin/ rje yab sras kyi bka' yang
dag pa'i tshad ma lus lta bu de la rgyan btags pa 'dra bar 'di mdzad/ gzhan gur/ sambu Ti dang / mtshan brjod la'ang mdzad/ man ngag gi yi ge'ang mang ngo / /de la slob
ma rtsags chos kyi rgyal po/ mgar bkra shis rin chen/ 'tsho'u dar re/ mal yer pa ba/ tre po mgon po/ ngor rje kun dga' 'od/ shen rdo rje sengge/ mnyam med shAkya ye shes/
cog ro chos kyi rgyal mtshan/ lha phug mkhar ba/ rngog tsha chos sku/ dran ston mtha' bral/ lho nag gnyal ba rdog rgya tsha rin chen mgon sogs mtha' yas pa zhig byung
/ sras gtsang tsha jo tshul/ mtshan tshul khrims bla ma/ de'i sras rngog kun dga' rdo rje/ 'di byung nas yab kyis dge slong mdzad de ring por ma lon par gshegs pas mes kyis
bskyangs/ dgung lo bcu lon tshe mes gshegs/ bla ma mang po las thos pa mdzad/ 'chad nyan legs par byas/ slob ma mang du thon/ spre zhing btab/ bdun cu rtsa brgyad pa la
gshegs/ de'i sras gzi brjid grags pa/ yab zhe drug bzhes pa la 'khrungs chos rnams yab dang lo ras sogs las gsan/ bya 'dul gyi slob ma 'char ba la bsnyen par rdzogs/ brgyad
cu bzhugs/ 'chad nyan mdzad slob ma'ang legs par thon/ khong gi gcung po rgyal po dga'i sras bla ma rin chen bzang po/ khu bo la rngog chos/ gzhan yang mang du bsten/
zul phur bsnyen par rdzogs/ nyer bdun bzhes pa la khu bo grongs khams su byon/ tshal pas bla mar khur/ bka' bstan 'gyur ro cog bzhengs/ 'chad nyan dar/ bdun cu rtsa bdun
la gshegs/ rin chen bzang po'i gcung po la sras lnga byung ba'i che ba slob dpon chos kyi rgyal mtshan khu bo sogs las thos pa mdzad/ so bdun pa la rin chen bzang po gshegs/
khams dar rtse mdo thug byon/ bstan pa bskyangs/ 'phrin las che/ bdun cu rtsa bdun pa la grongs de'i gcung po sengge 'bum gyi sras don grub dpal/ de'i sras byang chub
dpal/ de rin po che chos rgyal ba gshegs pa'i phyi lo 'khrungs/ sum cu rtsa dgu'i bar du yab kyi nye gnas

dang / slob gnyer sbrags pas rngog chos la mkhas pa chen por gyur dus chos ma chag par gsungs/ bdag po drung chen pa'i bka' skyon byung bas zhur byon pa la/ rje tsong kha pa
dang lam du mjal chos zhib tu drir byung ba la lan 'debs mdzad pas mkhyen rab che bas bsngags pa brjod/ de nyid kyi slob ma 'bras spungs chos rje bkra shis dpal ldan pa
dang mkhan chen padma bzang po/ gtsang chung chos kyi grags pa la gtug bcug des 'ur langs/ stag lung ngag dbang grags pa/ ches sangs rgyas rgyal mtshan/ bdag po grags pa
'byung gnas/ byams gling pa chen po bsod nams rnam rgyal/ 'gos gzhon nu dpal/ khrus khang lo tsA ba sogs mang pos zhabs la btugs/ lhag par 'brug pa rgyal dbang chos rje/
zlum khyung pa dang sna ra ba sogs rtsa ba'i grwa pa bzang la mang ba thon/ phyag dpe brtag gnyis kyi gzhung rdo rje mar grags pa gcig la chos tshar re la mtshan ma re btab
pa'i grangs brgya dang brgyad cu rtsa gnyis yod/ rang lo brgyad cu rtsa bdun pa la gshegs/ gdan sa dbon byang chub dpal grub pas bzung / mdo sde'ie sras rgyal tsha thogs
med grags pa/ yab las sngags gzhung mkhas par bslabs/ yi ge'ang du ma mdzad/ bshad pa'i 'phrin las che/ de'i sras rgyal tsha ra mo dang rdo rje sengge/ dang po phya pa'i
jo sras shig yin/ rdo rje sengge la gtsang pa rgya ras sogs kyis gtugs/ de lta bu chos sku rdo rje rjes 'brang dang bcas pas bshad pa mdzad pa las rgya shin tu che bar
'phel zhing brgyud pa snga phyi rnams kyis brtsams pa'i rgyud 'grel gyis kyang lung pa thams cad gang ngo / /mes ni myang stod stag tshal du 'khrungs/ rje mar pa la 'bul
mo che lan gsum mdzad pas zhabs tog gis mnyes pa yin/ gnas gzhi ba tho btab/ brtag gnyis la Tikka mdzad/ dgyes bde gsang gsum ma yA thod pa rnams la bshad grwa btsugs/
sku khams bzang ba'i tshe zhag bdun bdun tsam mnal gcig la 'gro/ rong ngur smrig tu gshin po rjes su 'dzin pa la phebs pa zhig la khong chang gsol gyin gzims rang bzhugs/
dge bshes gzhan rnams cho ga mdzad pas yon bdag blo ma bde/ gzhan rnams kyis khrel bgad byas pa dang / yon bdag gis thugs dam mdzad par zhu yang yang byas pas/ kho re tsho

ngas khyed kyi de min da lta grong gong ma ya gir rgan mo zhig sna khrag 'dzags te shi song / de tshun gyi yar 'dren byas yod gsung / ltar song bas ji lta ba bzhin 'dug nas
thams cad yid ches/ phyis nga zhag nyi shu rtsa gcig nyal/ de nas ma longs na ro 'di bsregs gsungs pa la/ zhag bcu dgu song nas dbon po zhig gis log mi srid snyam bsgul
bas shangs nas khrag mang po brdol te sku mdangs yal lo zer/ zhang ston gyis kyang mar mes gnyis ka la gtugs/ mas rang gi dbon mes kun po sogs na rim yang legs par byung
zhing / zhang ston gyi slob ma ye shes snying po/ de las zhang ston kun dga' grags sogs mes lugs kyi bshad rgyun da lta'i bar du'ang yod/ 'tshur ston dbang nge ni dol gyi
mda' 'tshur gyi rigs sngags 'chang shin tu mthu che ba zhig gi sras su 'khrungs/ dge bshes lce ba sogs las slob gnyer la brtson 'grus chen po mdzad sku bsod rgyas/ 'bum
bzheng pa'i yig mkhan dang 'phros gtam la da lta gsang ba 'dus pa la su mkhas dris pas/ khong rnams na re/ mar pa lho brag pa mkhas zer/ de nas lho brag par 'bul ba mdzad/
