khyad par mar pa mon nag la mthu mdzad dus bkod pa la de shi bas mthus bla ma mnyes par byas pa yin/ dol mdar gdan drangs/ gsang ba 'dus pa lugs gnyis/ ye shes zhabs lugs
la/ dza ya na dang / thag na dang / snyim pa'i me tog dang bcas pa'i bshad pa'i srol gsum mnga'/ de rnams la rgyud don man ngag tu bsgril nas bshad pa med pas 'phags lugs
la gtsigs che/ lugs bzhi ka gsan/ bshad pa byas pa'i slob ma khams pa ro mnyam rdo rje/ 'khon gad pa kIrti/ mtshes ston bsod nams rgyal mtshan gsum gtso bo/ khams pa
ro mnyam rdo rjes rgya gar du mai tri pa la gsang 'dus zhu snyam phyin pas gshegs nas ma mjal/ gzhan nyan sa ma rnyed bod du log rje mar pa las nyan snyam pa la lam du a
tsa ra gnyis dang mnyam du byung / gar 'gro gsungs pas 'tshur la 'dus pa nyan du 'gro zer/ rje mar pa'ang gshegs nas mi 'dug pas 'tshur gyi drung du byon/ 'khon gad pa kIrti
dang mnyam du nyan/ 'khon gad pa kIrtis/ mdar sengge rgyal mtshan la 'phags skor 'gos nas brgyud pa mkhas par lobs/ man ngag la ma 'gu bar

'tshur la bzhugs pa thos nas gsan/ nyams len mdzad pas sgyu ma lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin skyes/ des byang khang pa bsod nams rin chen/ khong gnyis ma gcig pa'i spun/ sngar byang
khang pa slob dpon/ phyis 'khon la 'dus pa gsan pa yin/ 'di la sba ba sbubs su nub/ gtsug tor 'phags/ des thur la ba tshul khrims skyabs la/ de mdo rgyud kun la mkhas
pa lo bcu gnyis bsgoms pas grub pa brnyes/ des thad dpe ba 'phags pa skyabs la slob gnyer mthar phyin/ nyams rtogs khyad par can skyes/ des gser sdings pa gzhon nu 'od la/
des 'dul 'dzin chen po jo bo'i lam rim la mkhas pa zhig shab kyi sna rings su klas mo che bas zhabs tog mdzad/ khong gi ston pas 'phags skor mi mkhyen nam zhus pas/ 'phags
skor mkhan po gar bdog gsungs pas/ khong na re/ lha sa'i rgan mos lha sa mi mthong / thur la na gsang sngags kyi sdong po 'phags skor mkhas pa 'phags pa skyabs bzhugs
pa ma gsan nam gsung / cung skyengs pa zhig byung / tshur log slob dpon gtsang pa la ngo chen bcol/ 'phags pa'i gsung gis kho bo lam thogs pa zhig bgyi gsung gsang 'dus
gzhung bshad man ngag thams cad tshang bar gnang / gzhan yang mang du zhus/ bla ma mang du bsten/ kha che paN chen dang klas mo cher mjal/ gser sdings btab/ mkhas pa thams
cad kyi dri sa/ mi chen thams cad kyi gtugs sar gyur/ de la nyid kyi slob ma mgar grags pa dbang phyug bya ba'i sring mo la sras skyes thob kyi shes rab 'gran du med pa
zhig byung nas bdag rkyen mdzad/ sbyangs pa mthar phyin byed du bcug mtshan chos sku 'od zer/ 'dis chos ci zhus pa thams cad lan res 'dzin nus pa yin zer/ dus 'khor sogs
rgyud sde la mkhas pa chen po de la 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtshos gsan/ bu ston gyi bla ma rdo rje rgyal mtshan la dus 'khor gsan pa'i tshe/ kho bo yo ga'i chos 'di rnams
nyan par 'dod de nyan sa ma rnyed zhus pas/ 'o na nged kyi mched grogs 'phags 'od yon tan rgya mtsho zhes bya ba zhig skyid mkhar mda' na yod/ de la zhus gsung / zha
lur phebs 'phral rtsad bcad pas mtshan mthun pa zhig dang nor/ phyis ma nor ba rtsad chod/ yang na nged der yong / yang na 'dir phebs dgos zhus pas/ 'phags pa'i gsung

nas khong chos sde chen po'i bdag po yin pas nga'i spe'u 'dir ga na shong / nga rang khong gi thad du 'gro gsungs nas zha lur phebs/ spyir yo ga dus 'khor sogs chos mang du
gsan/ khyad par 'dus pa gsan pa'i tshe/ khyod mkhas pa yin pas rgya ba'i rgya lugs/ gar pa'i gar lugs la sogs pa mi dgos gsungs/ bshad pa yam me zhig byas nas chos thob
che bar bya gsungs pa la/ bdag chos 'di la shin tu mos pa zhig lags pas bshad pa dpyis phyin pa zhig zhu zhus pas/ a pa 'o na de tsug gis mi 'ong / sngon la rim lnga'i khrid
bya/ de rting bshad pa ma byas na rgyud la go ba legs po mi 'char gsungs/ zla ba drug gi bar du mtshams bsdams rim lnga bskyangs/ rtags tshul dang mthun pa byung / bshad
pa mthar phyin/ 'byon khar phyag na gang yod kyi 'bul ba phul bas/ nga la mi dgos khyod rang sde gog 'dzin pa la dgos/ nga'i chos rnams ma shi'i bar du 'chad dgos gsungs/
yo ga dang 'phags dus la yig cha rtsom dgos pa'i bka' rgya bsdams/ bu ston gyi zhal nas ngas kyang bsgoms na man lung gu ru lta bu zhig 'ong ste/ 'phags pa'i gsung ma
chog pas mi tshe bshad pa la skyel dgos byung gsung ngo / /bu ston la dpal ldan bla ma dam pa dang shar pa ye shes rgya mtsho gnyis kyis gsan nas/ sa skya pa rnams la da
lta 'dus pa de gnyis las brgyud/ yang bu'i dngos slob dag las red mda' ba/ de las tsong kha pas gsan te nyams bzhes kyi snying po 'di la mdzad/ des nang mchod kyi ka pa
la bdud rtsis bkang ba zhig slob bu'i dbus su phyar nas/ 'di sus 'thungs pa la nga'i rgyud kyi bka' babs gsungs pa la/ gzhan sus kyang len ma nus/ snar thang pa shes rab
'byung gnas kyis blangs/ de la mkhas grub rjes khrel bgad byas zhes grags kyang / des gtsang de las dbur stod kyi rgyud stod smad gyes/ 'di dag mar pa'i brgyud 'dzin ngo
ma yin no/ /gzhan ma yA/ gdan bzhi/ sangs rgyas thod pa gsum sus 'chad kyang rjes btsun mar pa rang la thug pa'o/ /de'ang bu nas thugs sras lo tsA ba/ de las sku zhang chos
rje rnams las bdag cag rang la brgyud do// // ! bla ma mar pa'i sgrub rgyud kyi bka' babs pa rje btsun mi la 'khrungs yul gung thang smad kyi lung phran/ pha lnga'i nang
nas ko ran de'i rtsa bya

bar/ rigs khyung po/ yab mi la shes rab rgyal mtshan/ yum myang bza' dkar rgyan gyi sras su lcam sring gnyis 'khrungs/ ming po'i mtshan thos pa dga' sring mo la pe ta mgon
skyid du btags/ sku chung ngu'i dus nas yab gshegs/ de'i kha chems 'jog lugs nor ba dang / a mas lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi las mi 'gro bas/ a khu'i bu'i chung ma byed dgos byas
pa la ma nyan pas nor rdzas thams cad a khu dang a nes bgos/ g.yog bcol shin tu kha nyen/ dang po gser g.yu'i ral pa nyi le ba/ phyis shig sro'i ral pa nyi le ba zhig byung
/ mi rnams kyi gtam skad la'ang mi bdag bdag tu re/ bdag po sgo phyir bton zhes gleng / der lo bcu drug 'gro dus kha chems rgyus yod rnams bos ston mo bshams/ khyad
par a khu a ne la gzug 'dren byas/ mas da bus khyim so zin pa 'dug pas nor rnams phyir sprod dgos pa'i rgyu mtshan gleng bas/ a khu a ne za ba la mthun nas har langs rgyab/
sgos lcag gis brdungs/ zhang po kha zhan pas lab ma nus/ gzhan mi rnams zas ngo bltas nas cang mi lab/ der mas thos pa dga' la klog slobs zer/ lo tsA ba glan chung la
skra bcad/ khong la 'bri klog dang phyag na rdo rje las kyi rdo rje'i lugs zhib mo phag mo sogs gsan zer glan lo'i phyag rdor lo rgyus las byung / slob dpon gyi zla la skyid
ston zhig la phyin/ mi rnams glu len pa la sems 'phros nas chang gis kyang gzi/ glu len cing 'ongs pa mas thos nas/ pha mi la shes rab rgyal mtshan la bu khyod 'dra skye
ba/ nged rang ma smad kyi 'khos khyer 'di la glu dran pa 'dug ge zer brgyal/ sangs ba'i thabs byas nas ma ci gsung byed byas pas/ dbus gtsang du song la mthu mkhas pa
zhig slobs la dgra thams cad kha phung la thong zer/ bya yi/ cha rkyen bsgrubs byas/ ma rang gi lto skal zhang pos 'debs pa zhig yod pa de'i phyed btsongs/ rta bzang po
zhig dang tshos ltang drug gzhan yang zong 'dra ba byung nas mnga' ris stod nas dbus gtsang du mthu slob tu 'gro mi lnga tsam grogs su byon/ dgung lo bco brgyad pa la mas
dpal thang sgrol ba tshun bskyal/ lam du mthu su che rtsad bcad pas/ yar klungs na gnyags g.yung ston khro rgyal bya ba yod/ de che zer ba rim par gsan nas de rang la gtad
de byon/ de la dngos po gang yod phul/ 'di min

lus ngag yid gsum yang 'bul/ bdag la yul mi khyim mtshes skyid du 'phangs pa 'ga' bdog pa mthu mthil phyin pa zhu byas pas/ kha pho che bar mdzad/ khong lnga dang mnyam du
mthu zab zab 'dra bar mang po bslabs/ grogs po rnams mgu nas log rje btsun gyis khong tsho bskyal nas log byon pas/ bla ma nas khyod mi 'gro ba ci yin zer/ der bla ma rang
gis gnang ba'i rdzong de rnams phyag rten du btang nas/ ngas yul du mthu'i rtags ma thon par log na a ma nga'i mdun du lceb nas 'chi sdod pa yod/ mthu rtags thon pa zhig
zhu byas pas/ glen pa khyod dang po nas de skad zer/ brtag pa myur ba zhig bya gsung grwa pa stobs che la mgyogs pa zhig yod pa de bden rdzun ltar btang / kho 'khor nas
thos pa dga' bden par 'dug zer/ 'o na gtsang rong gi lha rje ye shes gzungs dang nga gnyis blo mthun pa'i grogs po byas/ mthu dang ser ba brjes/ nga'i thad du mthu slob
pa byung na khong can gtong / khong gi rtsar ser ba slob tu byung na nga can gtong bar byas pa yin 'bul chas dang / nga'i bu 'di snying rje bar yod pas mthu gsha' ma zhig
slobs shig zer ba'i yi ge mdzad de brdzangs/ khu lung du lha rje ye shes gzungs la yi ge gtad 'bul ba phul nas/ sgrub khang lag mthus glags mi rnyed pa zhig bzos/ der drag
sngags gza' gdong dmar nag zhus nas bsgrubs/ zhag bdun song ba dang bla ma byon/ sngar yin na des chog gi yod gsungs pa la/ thag ring gi mthu lags pas rgyun bsring pa
lags zhus pas/ bden yong gsungs/ yang bdun song ba'i nyin bla ma byon nas/ mdang dam can rnams kyis mi mgo sum cu rtsa lnga dkyil 'khor gyi mthar spungs/ ngo so zla ba bzhin
'phyar nas slebs byung / bsgral rgyu gnyis 'dug pa bsgral lam gsung / snying tshim gyi rten du gzhog pa zhu/ da chos skyong la gtang rag thong gsungs/ mtshams thon btang
/ de'i tshe a khu'i bu la chung ma blangs nas bag ston byed pa'i mi tshogs pa'i khyim rdib nas ma smad la gnag pa'i mi sum cu rtsa lnga shi a khu dang a ne lus/ der lha
rje la gnubs kyi ma phur gshin gsum sgyu 'phrul dang bcas pa bslabs shing bzhugs pa'i phyi lo ma'i yi ge slebs/ mthu'i rtags thon byung tshul/ da dung ser ba gyang

rim pa dgu yod zer ba phob zer ba dang / zhing phyed po btsongs pa'i rin gser rang srang bdun byung ba dbus kyi bya bral zhig la dmod btsugs nas brtags pas 'phrod par go yi
ge gab yig gser bem po la sbas/ des rtsad bcad pas chod nas yi ge gtad/ de bla ma'i yum gyis dgongs nas gser rnams gnang byung / slar ser ba zhu ba la gnyags kyi drung du
byon/ der gu lang 'byung ba'i 'khrugs ser chen po gnang nas/ thun dong du 'brug ldir glog g.yo/ sngar gyi gra pa de grogs su btang byung nas ser ba phab pas/ gyang rim
gsum yod zer ba babs/ ma dang 'phrad 'dod kyang khong gnyis khyi ra bas mthong bas bros/ kho stobs che bas mgyogs pas yul mi'i dmag gis bcar bcar tshun bsdad de snying tshim
bsgrubs/ de nas bla ma rnam gnyis kyi phyag phyir lo 'ga' shas gsan pa mdzad/ der mi mang po bsad pa'i sdig pa yod/ de tsug byas sbyang dgos snyam yod pa dang / gnyags
kyi yon bdag bzang po zhig na ba'i sngas bsrungs la bla ma byon/ der phan ma thogs par kho shi bas bla ma thugs skyo nas log phebs pa'i dus/ thos pa dga' nged rang gnyis
pos sdig pa chen po bsags yod pas/ yang na khyod kyis chos gsha' ma zhig gyis la nga drongs/ ngas brgyags skyel/ yang na ngas chos bsha' ma zhig byas khyod drang / khyod
kyis 'di kun skyongs la nga la brgyags skyol gsungs pas/ skabs rnyed nas bdag gis chos bya bar zhus pas/ 'o na de kha gyis/ khyod na so'ang gzhon/ snying rus kyang che
bar 'dug pas gsungs/ dbus kyi gos snam legs bsdus pa mdzo gcig rgyab stsal te gtsang du byon/ gnubs mjal/ myang stod rgyang khar du sgyer ston dbang nge bya ba yod pas der
song la rdzogs chen zhus gsungs/ der byon khong rang gi gdam ngag gang yod gnang / des khor re bya bar ngab mi byang chub rgyal po sgyu 'phrul yang dag bdud rtsi rnams
la mkhas pa zhig yod pa der brdzangs/ des yar 'brog ngor mar pa 'byung nge bya ba ma mo mkhan zhig gi rtsar brdzangs nas tshul de bzhin gyis bla ma dgu bsten/ khong gis gtsang
rong gi 'bre ston lha dga' la gtad de brdzangs/ der rdzogs pa chen po gsan/ de yan du bla ma re'i rtsar lo gcig

tsam gnyis tsam bzhugs/ yongs dril lo bco lnga tsam/ rang rang gi chos la slob gnyer slob dpon dang mnyam zer zer byas sbyangs pa che/ bskyed rim la nus pa thon kyang thugs
ma tshim/ der 'bre ston gyis nangs shig gung thang pa zhes bos nas/ lags zhus tsa na/ 'a cag gnyis khyod kyis chos nyan lo tsam/ ngas bshad lo tsam 'dis mi phan/ rdzogs
chen dang sgyu 'phrul yang lta dgongs kyi don ston tsam/ spyi'i rnam pa las rgyud thog tu khel ba dka' ba 'dug da lta lho brag chu khyer bya ba de na rgya gar gyi grub thob
nA ro pa dang mai tri pa'i dngos kyi slob ma rgya gar du yun ring por bzhugs/ dka' ba mang du spyad pa mar pa lo tsA zhes bya ba zhig yod/ de la gsang sngags byin rlabs
kyi lam rten 'brel lus la bsgrigs pas rtogs pa sems la 'char ba zhig yod 'dug nged rang pha spad der 'gro dgos pa min nam gsungs/ rje lo tsA ba'i mtshan thos pa tsam gyis
lus ba spu zing / mchi ma lhug par shor/ da lta rang de'i drung du sleb na bsam pa 'khrungs te/ cis kyang 'thad zhus/ dpon slob bsdebs nas byon/ 'brog tu bla ma bsnyung
nas mkha' 'gro ma dga' 'am ci tsug yin/ nga ma tshud par 'dug khyod rang song gsungs/ sman thang brgyud de byon/ de ring 'byor rgyu mdang dgongs de rje lo tsA ba la bla
ma nA ro pas gnang ba yin snyam pa'i rin po che bai DUrYa'i rdo rje phun sum tshogs pa dri mas nogs pa zhig byung bas khrus mdzad de/ rgyal mtshan gyi rtse la 'char bas
'od kyis phyogs bcur khyab pa zhig rmis/ de dang dus mtshungs yum bdag med ma la/ bla ma nA ro pas bla ma la gnang ba yin snyam pa'i shel gyi mchod rten dri mas nogs pa zhig
bla mas khrus byas pha ri'i rtse mor bskyal ba la thams cad kyis phyag mchod pa byed/ de'i dkon gnyer bud med gnyis kyis byed pa zhig byung nas nang par bla ma la zhus
pas/ rmi lam nying 'khrul la gtad pa ci yod gsungs/ der bsu ba la 'phral phru slog pa skad mdzad de byon/ der mjal de kha la snang ba 'gyur yang ngo ma shes/ mjal sna bcol
bas khru'i 'phro 'di slog chang 'di 'thung / khong gi mjal sna ngas bya'o gsungs/ dum zhig na byis pa snum ral shig ge ba zhig 'bod du byung / khong gis go chod 'dug
ngas kyang go chod pa byed bsam rems pas phru lhag ma med par lhogs/ /chang yang lhag ma med pa gsol bas

rten 'brel 'grig yud tsam zhig la dpon slob gnyis kyis slog pa'i zhing de da lta ni mi lag mang pos kyang nyin gcig la zin dka'o/ /de nas bla ma mjal ba dang / da gi'i de khar
'dug pa dang zil che nas tshom me lus pas/ khyod bden rngog gis kyang ngo ma shes/ mar pa lo tsA nga rang yin gsungs te/ lte ba gung thang smad du bcad/ /slob gnyer dbus
gtsang phyogs su bgyis/ /sgyer ston ngab mis dbu mdzad nas/ /rong ston lha dga' yan chad du/ /drin can gyi bla ma bcu tsam bzhugs/ /chos ni rgyud sde snga 'gyur zhus/
/lta dgongs kyi chos la mkhyen pa che/ /khyad par lha rje gnubs chung la/ /drag sngags gza' gdong dmar nag zhus/ /khong sgrub 'phrin gyi phyag len mkhas na yang / /mi kho
bo'i sgro 'dogs cung ma chod/ /rje nA ro mai tris byin brlabs pa/ /lus rten 'brel gnad du bsnun pa yis/ /sems chos nyid ma dang sprod pa zhig /lho chu khyer gyi phu na
bzhugs so skad/ /pha lo tsA'i snyan pa rgyang nas 'khums/ /mtshan thos pa tsam gyis ba spu g.yos/ /lam dka' ba spyad de spyan sngar phyin/ /zhal mthong ba rang gis snang
ba 'gyur/ /khong tshe rabs kyi bla ma yin pa 'dra/ /der bdag la stod nas 'ongs pa'i mi sdig po che zhig lags pas bla mas thugs rjes gzung nas tshe gcig lus gcig la sangs
rgya ba'i gdam ngag cig gnang bar zhu byas pas/ gdam ngag yod/ sangs rgya mi rgya khyod rang gi snying rus la rag las gsungs/ nangs par nas nang mir tshud/ yum shin tu byams/
de dus lho brag la kha bas bla ma'i grwa pa rdung 'tshog mang du byas pas mthu gyis gsungs byas/ khong rnams nang 'dzings mi 'ga' shi bla ma la babs dgos byung bas ming
du mthu chen du btags/ der sdig pa byang ba'i ched dang sras la 'bogs dgongs/ ri zur gcig tu mkhar gyi rmang zlum po zhig brtsigs/ thog so gnyis tsam longs pa dang de
bshig zla gam/ de'ang bshig gru gsum/ de'ang bshig nas da lta'i sras mkhar 'di'i rmang bting / thog so bdun tshar ba dang khyams rtsig tu bcug de thams cad la mi la rang
min pa rdo ra mgo tsam zhig dang / sa khyem gang skyel rogs med/ de'i bar la chos gnang la re nas/ rngog mes 'tshur sogs dbang gsan pa la byon pa'i zlar

'tshangs pas/ gral nas bton phyag 'bebs 'chi ba la gtugs pa/ dus rgyun du'ang rkyen phra mo re la bsnyad btags nas bka' skyon phyag 'bebs mdzad de yi chad thengs bdun song
gi bar la yum la'ang ma zhus/ de nas rgyab la sgal mig gsum rdol ba bstan nas chos zhu ba'i rogs la sbran pas yum spyan chab shor/ bla ma la zhus pas sgal ba rang byung med
dam gsungs/ sngar rta bong la sgal pa byung zer ba thos/ mi la sgal pa byung zer ba ma thos/ sgal pa byung bar ma zad gsum yang rdol 'dug zhus pas/ khrid shog gsungs/
rgyab rmar song ba de gzigs phul bas/ 'di bzhin gyis la sa skyol gsungs/ ci la phan zhus pas rma la sa mi 'chor ba la phan gsungs/ der yang dad pa skad cig kyang ma log bdag
gis sdig pa de tsam byas rting 'di la lam bgrod pa zhig ma byung na 'gro sa dmyal ba min pa med/ tshe gcig la sangs rgya ba'i lam bla ma gzhan la med pas bla mas ci gsung
bsgrubs te mnyes pa zhig bya dgos bsam pa kho na byung / der rma rnams 'grams 'khrugs nas na tsha mi bzod/ yum la zhus pas re zhig ngal gsos gsungs/ rma 'grams pa drag
nas mthu chen da las gyis gsungs/ rgyab kyi rma ma drag pas sa rdo pang du gzung zhing bskyal te las mdzad/ khyams longs nas bla mas gdam ngag mi gnang ba 'dra bsam thugs
mug nas byon/ slar bsam mno btang nas log de dus yum gyis ma phod par byin rlabs rten 'ga' dang phyag tham yig rdzus bskur te rngog can brdzangs/ khong gi gra rigs dol
yas pho yas mo bas brdungs pa la ser ba phob gsungs phab/ rgan mo zhig la gnas tshang bcol ba de ngu / snying rje nas khyod kyi zhing ji lta bu zhig yod gsungs/ 'di 'dra
yod zer gru gsum mchu ring zhig bris pas/ de ma thag tu sla nga bkab sdigs mdzub mdzad pas mo'i zhing ma la gnod pa med pa snum srug ge 'dug sla ngas ma khyab pa'i mchu
lhag pa chu log gis gnan/ gzhan yul de grog shul du btang / phyi than bzhag pas khong rnams rngog la babs/ ser ba'i dus de'i sris kho bo'i thog 'di la'ang yul der ser ba
thu bas zhing thams cad bcom nas rgan mo'i zhing de la skyon med/ mchu chu log gis mnan pa zhig kyang byung ngo / /de nas lam du bya byi'i ro bsdus pas steng g.yogs

ltem gang ba byung / de bla ma'i spyan sngar dkyil 'khor gyi stegs bu yod pa'i khar spungs nas bshums pas ci'ang mi lto/ jo bo nA ro pa'i bu brgyud la sdig po che btsan thabs
su sangs rgya ba yod pa yin gsungs/ cung zad dgongs pa la bzhugs pa'i mthar se gol gtogs pas thams cad nam mkha' la dir rgyab ste 'phur/ de dag gi bya rjes stegs bu la
byung ba da lta'i bar du yod de/ des bla ma yab sras la yid ches/ rngog gis gdam ngag gnang yang bla ma'i bkas ma grol bas myong ba ma skyes sras che 'don gyi dus su bla
ma'i spyan sngar byon/ che 'don tshar/ grwa pa bying gyes/ dbu che rags pa yod pa'i dgongs shig tshogs 'khor byed gsungs/ der bying tshogs/ dbyug pa zhig sku gzhogs su bzhag
pas/ yum gyis dgongs nas rgyang bskyed de bzhugs/ der mar pas phyag sdigs mdzub mdzad rngog la gtad de spyan hur phyung nas/ chos sku rdo rje zer ba ma bcol ba byed
mkhan khyed mthu chen la dbang bskur man ngag ster ba'i rgyu mtshan ci yin gsungs/ rngog bred nas de ltar byas chog pa'i bla ma rang gi phyag tham dang byin rlabs rten rnams
gnang byung ba lags zhus pas/ mthu chen de khyod la sus bskur gsungs/ bred nas bdag la yum gyis gnang ba lags zhus nas rgya mthongs su mchongs te phyir byon/ yum la phyag
'bebs mdzad du phebs pas yum gyis sgor byon bcad de bzhugs pas/ phyag srad srad pa zhig mdzad bzhugs gdan khar bzhugs/ rngog la nga'i byin rlabs rten rnams da lta rang
long shog gsungs 'byon par chas te phyir thon pa na/ a bo mthu chen gyis na bza' la 'jus nas phyag phyir 'gro bar zhus pas/ a bo mthu chen ngas khrid rung da res kyi 'di
dang 'dra/ bla mas rjes su 'dzin te 'ong / yus kyis mi 'dzin na gdod bla ma'i gnang ba zhus te phan gdags so gsung ba la/ phung po nga 'dra ba/ nga rang sdug pa ma zad
yum dang bla ma la'ang 'di lta bu'i 'o brgyal byung / nga skye ba phyi mar chos dang mjal ba zhig thugs rjes 'dzin dgos zhes lceb par brtsams pa na/ bla mas bu de 'dra ma
byed/ gsang sngags bla med kyi lugs la phung po sangs rgyas kyi bdag nyid yin pas de la brnyas na rtsa ltung phog mdo lugs la'ang rang srog rang gis gcod pa sdig pa che
shos su gsungs pa yin/ de ltar ma byed gsungs pa'i ring bla ma thugs sos

nas bdag med ma shog gsungs/ yum byon pas rngog la sogs pa gar song / bla ma rngog sku chas len du chas pa la mthu chen zhu ba 'di ltar 'bul ba la lan 'di ltar 'debs kyin bzhugs
gda' zhus pas/ 'o na shog gyis gsungs/ a bo mthu chen gyis nga 'dra ba bla ma thugs sos nas kyang sku drung du 'gror med la/ phyin na bka' skyon dang phyag 'bebs myong
ba las med pa zhes brgyal brgyal bshums pas/ bla ma rngog gis khyod yar song la bla ma'i spyan sngar mthu chen phyin e chog ltos/ de min ngas 'dir ma bsdad na 'dis gang
min byas dogs 'dug des zhus pas/ bla ma mar pa'i zhal nas/ da res 'bod pa'i mgron gyi gtso bo a bo mthu chen yin/ bdag med ma rang song la bos shog gsungs der yum rang
phebs/ mthu chen da khyod rang ngu mi dgos thugs rjes gting nas 'dzin par 'dug de'i rtags la da res mgron gyi gtso bo mthu chen yin/ khyod rang song la bos shig gsung 'dug
pa gsungs pas/ yum gyis sems gso yin nam/ bden nam the tshom me ba la drung du bslebs/ der bu chen der yod kun yang 'dzom zin 'dug de'i tshe bla ma thugs zhi bar bzhugs
nas/ brtags brtags na rang re kun la skyon med/ ngas ni mthu chen gyi sdig pa sbyong ba'i phyir byas/ bdag med ma ni spyir bud med sems chung / khyad par snying rje che
bar 'dug pas kho la snying rje nas yig brdzus bskur/ rngog gis yi ge bskur nas de ltar byed pa bden mod/ 'on kyang byin rlabs rten tshar cig 'dir skyol/ phyis khyod rang
la ster gsungs/ de'ang khyod bu slob las dang po pa rnams dad pa ma log ngas 'dod pas kun nas blangs pa'i las yin na zhi bas bcol bas chog ste min/ bu 'di la yid chad chen
po lan dgu thongs na lam lhag med du sangs rgya ba yin pa la/ da lan the ba'i brgyad las ma thongs pas da dung dka' ba spyod pa cung zad dgos/ 'di ngas skal ldan du shes
nas phru slog pa'i zol gyis bsu ru phyin gsungs/ gral de nyid du skra bcad mtshan mnal lam bzhin rdo rje rgyal mtshan zhes btags/ dge bsnyen dang byang chub sems kyi sdom
pa gnang ste/ gsang sngags kyi dbang bskur ni sang gnangs nas rim bzhin bya'o gsungs pas/ nga'i 'di rmi lam yin nam mngon sum yin/ rmi lam yin na gnyid ma sad na dga'
ste snyam pa 'khrungs nas

tshogs kyi 'khor lo la dgyes par rol/ der sang nas sa chog gnangs sta gon zhag gsum pa dngos gzhi mdzad pa'i dkyil 'khor bstan pa'i dus/ 'dir mtshon byed dpe'i dkyil 'khor
yin/ mtshon bya don gyi dkyil 'khor 'di na zhes bar snang la dpal 'khor lo sdom pa drug cu rtsa gnyis kyi dkyil 'khor rten brten par bcas pa mngon sum du bzhugs pa mjal/
gsang mtshan 'dogs pa'i dus sa gsum gyi mkha' 'gro ma nam mkha'i sprin phung tsam gyis mgrin gcig tu bzhad pa'i rdo rje zhes btags so/ /dbang gong ma gnyis kyang dngos dbang
du mdzad/ dbang dus su dpe'i ye shes gzigs pas 'jig rten chos mchog gi rtogs pa brnyes pa yin gsung / de nas brtsams te dgyes pa rdo rje/ ma hA ma yA/ gdan bzhi/ sangs
rgyas thod pa/ gsang ba 'dus pa/ de dag gi rgyud rgyud 'grel dbang sgrub thabs rim pa gnyis/ don mthar thug ston pa'i snying po skor/ khyad par khyad chos bsre 'pho gnad
kyi mtshams sbyor la smar khrid du mdzad/ lho brag stag nya'i brag la sgom du bcug go /tshar gcod la lo bzhi/ rjes 'dzin mdzad nas lo gnyis dang zla ba brgyad bzhugs/ lo
tsam bzhugs rgyu'i nang la mkha' 'gro snyan rgyud kyi gdam ngag gnang / dpal nA ro pas mdzad pa lta bu'i tshogs kyi 'khor lo dgyes pa'i rdo rje la brten nas mdzad pas/
mes rngog 'tshur mi la mgo yags la sogs thams cad kyis dgyes rdor sprul pa'i lha dgu dngos su gzigs/ gzhan bde mchog 'khor lo la sogs pa'i yi dam du mar snang ba/ zad par
sa la sogs pa'i rdzu 'phrul/ grong 'jug mdzad pa la sogs che ba'i yon tan sangs rgyas dang mnyam par gzigs pas/ ci gsung ba'i bka' la skad cig kyang mi 'gong ba'i dam bca'
mdzad de/ pha sku drin can gyi zhabs drung du/ /lo drug zla mthong brgyad du bsdad/ /lus dang grib ma bzhin du 'grogs/ /nor zang zing gi 'bul ba ma mchis te/ /lus kyi
zhabs tog rdul du brlag /dang / thugs gting nas mnyes pa'i gnad ka des/ /rgyud zab mo dgyes pa'i rdo rje dang / /byin rlabs can gyi bde mchog dang / /snying po mahA ma yA'i
rgyud/ /dpal nam mkha' lta bu'i gsang 'dus dang / /bka' srung can gyi gdan bzhi dang / /sprul pa sangs rgyas thod pa'i rgyud/ /don mthar

thug ston pa snying po'i skor/ /bka' rgya mtsho ltar zab rgyud 'grel las/ /bcud nor bu rin chen gting nas blangs/ /gnad zab dgu'i don snying phyung ba rnams/ /gser zhun ma
lta bur dril nas gnang / /phri bsnan lhag chad yod re zhes/ /DA ki dpang btsugs dbu snyung bzhes/ /de nas bla ma la zhus te yar log rngog la phyag skyel du byon/ de nas yul
du sleb dus yum shi sring mo 'khyar/ khang zhing mthus 'jigs nas bdag med du lus 'dug der skyo shas gting nas langs a ma'i rus bu rnyed/ de la glan lo'i dbon po'i rtsar
byon tsha tsha btab/ yon du dkon mchog brtsegs pa'i mdo lus 'dug pa de phul/ dgong gcig bzhugs/ rkang btsugs phug tu byon/ der a nes kha cang bgyis te zhing thabs kyis
phral/ rin sprad pa bsnams te brag dkar rta sor byon/ 'tsho ba phye dri yod tsam lo gsum/ ci'ang med pa zwa rang gi tshod ma la brten pa lo drug ste dgu rtse gcig tu bsgoms/
sgom la bogs che bsam pa ma byung / der khyi ra bas mthong lus dka' thub kyis gdungs pas mi yin nam 'dre yin zer/ de dag las 'phros thos nas pe tas rnyed/ mdzes se dang
gnyis kyis rtsam chang sha dang bcas pa dum zhig phul te zos pas sgom mi nus pa snyam byed/ gegs 'di las che ba mi yong dgongs te bla mas gnang ba'i shog dril bltas pas/
sngar rtsa nang du rlung sems 'du rgyu zas ngan pas ma lhongs pa des bslang bar shes/ de'i lugs bzhin bcos pas skyon 'dzin yon tan du ngo 'phrod nas/ byang chub kyi sems
rang byung gis gyen du log gsang gnas kyi rtsa mdud grol/ sa dang po dang gnyis pa non/ de nas lo tsam du brtson par mdzad pas lte ba'i rtsa mdud grol/ de nas brag dmar
chong lung la sogs par byon/ lhag par la phyir byon nas lha chen po tshogs kyi bdag po dam la btags/ slob brgyud rnams kyi sbyin bdag byed par khas blangs rang srog mdongs
gsol du phul/ de nas rtsar mar skor cig byon/ dgun de gshen rdor mo shAkya gu Na sogs ban skyes drug chos zhu bar 'ong ba'i lugs byas/ 'tsho chas nyung ngu zhig las bsnams
ma byon/ khong tsho la sgang nas log de dgong nas kha mo che bab/ sos zla ba lnga pa tsam las lam ma bye/ der bu slob rnams kyis grongs yod snyam gshegs rdzongs la
dmigs mchod pa byas/ de nas

sos khong rnams kyis spur ram spur rus gang rnyed snyam ltar 'ongs pas gsa' zhig pha bong nas bya ra byed pa mthong / de nas ngu ba dang gsung thos chas cung zad las ma zad
par 'dug pas ting nge 'dzin gyis 'tsho bar shes/ dad pa lhag par skyes/ mchi ma lhug par shor/ nan gyis yul du gdan drangs/ der bsu mi rnams bro rtse bas thugs nyams 'ur
ba skad mdzad de/ pha bong 'dam bzhin brdzis/ de dus snying ka'i rtsam mdud grol sa drug pa non pa yin te/ stod byang chub sems kyi rgyun 'bab bde/ /smad dwangs ma'i thig
les gang bas bde/ /bar dkar dmar thug phrad rtse bas bde/ /de nas mi ma yin gyi gdul bya phal btul nas mi'i gdul bya 'dus pa'i thog ma/ ra la'i phu za 'og phug tu bzhugs
dus/ yul de'i phyugs rdzi rnams drung du byung ba'i byis pa zhig rje btsun mthong ba tsam gyis lus skyi bung / sems tshe 'di'i snang ba 'gags/ khrong nge lus/ de nas brtsams
te yang yang chos nyan du 'ong ba la ma khus sdang po byas phru slog tu bcug de'i dus chung ngu la mdze nad byung / der rje btsun gyis sgom bzlas 'dra bslabs/ de'i
tshe mdzo ki bzhi byung ba'i rgan pas grogs byas rgya gar du 'khrid par brtsams/ byis pa de phar 'gro dus rje btsun thugs dam la bzhugs gsungs/ des phug pa'i sgo brtsigs
lo gcig tsam 'gor te mdze nad gsos/ tshur log mi la gar bzhugs rtsad bcad pas/ dang po de skad zer ba zhig 'dug da gar song ngam ma shes zer/ sngar gyi shul du bltas pas
phug pa'i sgo brtsigs brtsigs par 'dug gshegs yod snyam bshig pas rje btsun sku khrong nge bzhugs/ khyod kyis don 'grub bam/ 'grub zhus/ der rje btsun la skra bcad/ mtshan
rdo rje grags pa de khar bzhag dge bsnyen dang sems bskyed/ bde mchog 'khor lo'i dbang bskur/ bsre 'pho'i man ngag stsal te sgom du bcug pas bde drod bsam gyis mi khyab
pa skyes pas ras rkyang mdzad/ thams cad kyis ras chung pa zhes snyan pa'i dril bsgrags so/ /de nas thugs sras bu slob phal cher 'dus/ de nas chu bar du byon/ sman lung
du bzhugs dus bkra shis tshe ring mas g.yos nas/ nam mkha'i lha phran man/ sa 'og lto 'phye yan/ gdon chen bco brgyad kyis gtsos pa'i snang srid kyi lha 'dre ma tshogs pa
med/ de las shin tu 'jigs shing mi bsrun pa'i sha za ma lnga/ keng rus bzhed pa'i bud

med ri rab pang du bteg nas rdeg par rtsom/ dmar mo khrag 'dzag ce spyang gi gdong can rgya mtsho hub kyis 'thung / gshin rje gzugs 'chang ba nyi zla cha lang bzhin du rdeb/
sol ba'i bud med gad brgyangs can gza' skar thang la 'bebs/ shin tu mdzes pa lha mo'i gzugs kyis yid bslu/ gzhan yang gzugs med lag pa rkyong ba/ rtsi shing nags tshal
'gul ba/ sa rdo ri brag bgad pa/ phyogs bzhi 'obs kyis bskor/ mtshams bzhi gyad kyis srung ba/ nam mkha' me dang sa gzhi chus gtams pa/ mi sdug pa'i gzugs bred dgu tshogs/
mi bzad pa'i mtshon srid dgu 'phen/ mi snyan pa'i tshig dgu smra/ bar chad lung bstan gyis glu len/ mi bsrun pa'i bya ba yod dgus bsam gtan gyi drod nyul du byung ba rnams
gsung ngag bden pa'i tshig gis bkrol/ phyag rgya gnyan po'i zil 'og tu mnan/ rang rtags srog gi snying po bzhes/ bka' 'bangs bgyid par brtsis la phab/ lhag par bkra shis
tshe ring mas gtsos pa rnams la lta ba dbu mar gtan la phab/ sgom pa lam gyi rim par bskyed rdzogs kyi gnad bcun/ spyod pa 'phrang sgrol gnad kyi bar dor phye nas bstan/
bka' gsang snyan rgyud kyi gdams pa rnams gnyer gtad/ rje btsun nyid kyi las kyi phyag rgyar bzhes/ phyi rab rnams kyi mgon skyabs dpung gnyen du 'gyur bar mdzad pas/
nga'i bstan pa mi ma yin tshe ring ma dang / mi dbus pa ston pa des 'dzin pa yin gsungs/ de'i dus mgrin pa longs spyod kyi 'khor lo dwangs mas gang bas sa brgyad kyi rtogs
pa brnyes/ de nas gangs ti se'i bar du byon/ der bon po ming sring btul/ nus pa che shos/ sring mo de'ang bon rang gi lo rgyus la/ bsam yas su 'khrungs pa co sa bon mo/
bla ma tshe dbang rig 'dzin gyi yum tshe'i rig 'dzin brnyes pa de yin/ nA ro bon chung de'i slob ma yin zer/ stag la me 'bar gyi sprul pa yin yang zer/ ming po rdzu 'phrul
gyis btul/ sring mo phyag rgyar mdzad de dwangs ma dbang du bsdus pas thul/ thong la'i la thog tu dam pa sangs rgyas dang rdzu 'phrul 'gran/ spangs rtogs mtshungs par
zhal bzhes/ rje ras chung pa rgya gar du brdzangs pa la ston pa dar blo'i rtsod lan ma thebs pas yin/ thos pa'ang gal che zer ba byung / rje btsun yab sras zab mo'i gdams
pa len rgyu la dgongs/ tshur 'khor dus ras chung pa

nga rgyal skyes pa g.yag ru che ru ma song / rje btsun chung du ma song bar de'i nang du 'khrul 'khor ldem me bzhugs pa dang / dpe la chags pa rkyang ma brgya bu brgya/ spyang
ki ma brgya bu brgya'i 'bros 'ded/ rje btsun rang gi sku'i rtsa 'khor bde dgyes gsang 'dus gdan thod ma yA drug tu bstan pa dang / dkar brgyud bla ma dang sngags kyi
dkyil 'khor sogs dang / pha bong rta ltar zhon nas rgyug pa/ chu ltar 'phyar ba/ 'dam ltar rdzi ba sogs sku gsung thugs kyi bkod pa mtha' yas pa bstan nas nga rgyal lhag
ma med par mdzad/ de'i skabs su dpral ba'i rtsa mdud grol bas sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpar gyur pa'i tshul bstan/ sa bcu pa la rjes thob de bzhin gshegs pa rnams dang khyad
par med kyang / zhes gsungs pa'i rgyu mtshan gyis so/ /bal po rdzong du dharma bo dhi/ shI la bha ro gnyis kyi phyag bzhes/ de nas mi ring bar dbus pa ston pa rje btsun
rang gi rdzu 'phrul gyis thugs bsgyur nas bkug mjal dus chang bzhes 'phro de gnang bas lhag ma med par bzhes pas brgyud pa zin par dgongs/ bsod nams tshogs chen bsags
las byung / /sems can kun gyi rin po che/ /zhes bsgrags/ de la bde mchog lha bcu gsum gyi dbang bskur ba'i dus na nga mi la rgas pas mi longs/ bum pa khyod rang song la bskur
cig gsungs pas bum pa nam mkha' la 'phags te dbang bskur/ bsre 'pho gnad kyi mtshams sbyor bstan te sgom bcug pas thun mong dang khyad par gyi nyams mod la skyes/ gzhan
yang gdam ngag legs par gnang / ras chung pas rdo rje phag mo bris thang la rab gnas zhus pas/ ye shes pa dam tshig pa 'di la bzhugs/ dga' ston du me tog 'di bzhes gsungs
pas/ ye shes kyi lha dngos su byon te de la thim/ bris sku dbu seng byas te me tog bzhes zhes grag go /mthar gshegs pa'i tshe sa bcu gnyis kyi dbang phyug brnyes mod
kyang / lam gnyis lhag mar las pa skad mdzad de/ 'di nas mngon par dga' ba'i zhing du byon nas/ der yongs su sbyong ba mdzad do zhes zhal gyis bzhes la/ mya ngan las 'das
nas ras chung pa byon pa la lam du dngos su bsu ba/ rjes ma spur gyi rtsar phebs dus 'khor gsar pa rnams kyis ma btang bar ras chung pa yus nas brgyal/ brgyal sangs

ba dang spur khang nang na me rang 'bar ba de'i dbus su phyag gcig gis me lce mnan/ gcig gis zhal 'gram skyor te/ kho re tsho de skad ma byed dang / 'bag brgya bas sengge gcig
dga' ba de ras chung pa yin yar thong / ras chung pa rang yang de ltar yus mi dgos gsung mtha' tshig gi mgur gsungs/ slar spur du song / der gdung rnams ring bsrel gyi
gong bu gcig tu byas te yal/ lha dang mkha' 'gro'i mchod pa blos mi 'khyud pa byung / bod du kun mthun snang grub pa'i rdzu 'phrul ston pa 'di las lhag pa'ang lta ci/ mnyam
pa'ang ma byung ngo / /slob ma nyi ma lta bu gcig zla ba lta bu gcig rgyu skar lta bu nyer gsum ste grub thob nyer lnga/ phyir mi ldog thob pa'i rtogs ldan brgya/ drod
thob pa'i skyes bu rtsa brgyad/ lam sna zin pa'i rnal 'byor pho mo stong rtsa gcig chos 'brel thob pas ngan song gi rgyun lam chad pa brtsis las 'das pa 'ongs zhes bcom
ldan 'das mas lung bstan pa ltar byung ngo / /de'i sras kyi thu bo zla ba lta bu ni rje btsun ras chung pa ste/ yul gung thang 'phrang rar yab gnyan dar ma grags zhes bya
ba'i sras su 'khrungs/ mtshan rdo rje grags pa zer/ sku 'bras gtsang bas lha'i bu 'dra/ der klog yig mkhas par bslabs/ dgung lo brgyad la yab gshegs/ yum a khus bsdus/
de chos la mi dga' bas ma'ang de dbang song nas shin tu sdang / der klog bklags pas za yon phun sum tshogs pa byung / de bsnams za 'og phug tu mi la'i rtsar byon/ de nas
ma khus dbang med khrid nas phru slog tu bcug pas mdzes zin/ de nas ma khus kyang mi la'i rtsar rgyug zer/ der rje btsun gyis glan lugs kyi phyag na rdo rje gnang bzlas
pa byas pas thu ru red/ zhang po'i sa gung thang tsher yul bya bar phyin nas khang gog cig tu bsdad yod pas/ dzo ki bzhi byung ba'i rgan pa de snying rje che/ des khrid nas
rgya gar du byon/ lam du 'phral skad sbyangs/ thugs rab che bas skad kyang mthar thug pa zhig mkhyen/ lam yang yun ring ba 'gor/ ta pa sa ta'i grong khyer bla ma ba la
tsandra bzhugs par brtol/ las kyi rdo rje'i sgrub thabs 'bring po yi ge bcu pa'i dbang sgrub thabs gnang / zla ba gsum song ba dang lus thams cad phus btab pa bzhin skrangs/
nad zug tshugs thabs med pa byung / rnag khrag chu ser yang gang min nas rdol ba'i phol mig mang po byung nas/ bla ma la mi sos pa 'dra na zhus pas/ dmangs po

yul 'tshol ba bya ba'am/ pham po srid tshol ba bya ba yin/ dang po 'di tshugs 'ong gsungs/ bla mas kyang zhag bdun mtshams gcod grogs mdzad/ de nas brtson pas mnal lam du la
zhig la mi mang po 'gro yi 'dug ci la 'gro dris pas/ nged rnams gung thang gi gnyan rdo rje grags la gnod pa'i klu bskyas byed par ltar 'gro ba yin zer/ mnyam por phyin
pas ri mthon po zhig gi khar bslebs dus/ lung pa zhig nas sbal sbrul mang po phyung phyung zer zhing 'gro /bya mang pos phyi nas yar 'ded byed cing la brgal song / mnal
sad pa na ngo gdong yang 'jam nyal nyal 'dug lus thams cad bde sangs song / brgyugs pas kyang de khar 'dug nas/ yul na ni mdzes thu lum song zer ba yod/ pha dar ma grags
la bu ma skyes ri shi byas nas te te mang du brdungs/ nangs par bla ma la zhus pas sos pa yin/ da dung log nyen yod pas srung ba byed dgos gsungs/ bsrung ba'i ched du zla
phyed mtshams bcad/ de grol 'phral bod du byon/ bsod snyoms mdzad/ gser srang phyed dang bzhi rnyed pa 'bul du byon/ de res gdam ngag lhag ma med pa gsan/ ti bu dang yud
cig mjal/ de nas 'khor te rje btsun la gtugs nas dbang gdam ngag mang po gsan/ bsgoms pas gtum mo'i drod rtags thon/ ras chen ras chung zhes yab dang mtshungs pa'i grags
pa thob/ bla ma'i khrid gsar pa rnams kyi slob dpon mdzad/ de nas rje btsun gyis brdzangs nas rgya gar du phyi ma byon/ der bla ma ti bu dang mjal/ ba la tsandra'ang de'i
slob ma paNDYi ta zla ba bzang po yin/ de las nA ro mai tri nas brgyud pa'i gdams pa/ gzhan yang de nyid kyi yab ga ya dha ra paN chen mkhas la man ngag che bas de'i gdams
pa sogs gsan/ de'i dus grub thob a mo gha badzwa yis/ bod phrug snying rje bar 'dug ste tshe zhag bdun las mi 'dug pa zer/ thugs dngangs te bla ma la zhus pas/ grub pa'i
rgyal mo zhes pa tshe dpag med dngos su mjal ba zhig yod pas spyan drang gi gsungs/ tshogs dang gser gyi maNDYal bshams gsol ba btab pas shing spangs gser gyi maNDYal
de nyid du byon/ tshe dpag tu med pa'i sgrub thabs phyi nang gsang ba de kho na nyid las tshogs rta mgrin la sogs pa'i sham bu dang bcas pa gnang / zhag bdun gnyid med du
bsgrubs nas ma gcig gis

khyod lo ji tsam thub par 'dod gsungs/ shi'ang mi lto snyam pa tshun zhus pas/ bod ngan pa/ bsam pa mtho dma' nges pa med/ bu pha'i tshe dang mnyam pa zhig bya yi gsungs/ brgyad
cu rtsa brgyad thub par lung bstan/ de nas gdam ngag rnams tshang bar byas nas log 'byon khar ti bus khyod kyis sgra mi shes pa'i skyon gyis dpe 'di rnams bod skad
du ji lta bar bsgyur med pa 'dra ste/ lam du mkha' 'gro ma zhig gis zhus dag byed par 'gyur ro sogs zhal bkod thems par stsal/ ma gcig 'di de dus skal ba dang ldan pa rnams
rjes su 'dzin/ gzhan phal pas mthong bar mi nus pa zhig go /ji ltar gsung pa bzhin bal por phebs dus bha ri mas bsus te dpe rnams kyi lhag chad bsal tshur byon thugs la
khengs pa cung zad 'khrungs pa/ rje btsun gyis rdzu 'phrul bstan de bzlog bla ma la gdams pa yar skyes su phul ba/ de yang / lus med mkha' 'gro'i chos skor la/ /lhag chad
nor 'khrul mkha' 'gros bsal/ /zab dang yang zab bka' rgyas btab/ /'chi med bdud rtsi'i bcud len dang / /gzhan yang gser dang 'dra ba'i chos/ /ngo sprod gnad kyi bar do
dang / /bsam gtan thun 'jog gdam ngag dang / /brda don gsum dang rin chen lnga/ /nyams su len pa'i chos drug dang / /zhes bya ba rnams so/ /gzhan/ bod phrug rgya gar phyin
pa la/ /gdams pa bdag rang che'o snyam/ /zhes gsungs/ de nas nya ma rnams rje btsun yab las sras ngo mtshar che ba skad zer bas sdig tu 'gyur snyam nan gyis zhus/ snye
nam drod phug tu mkha' 'gro snyan rgyud kyi gdam ngag rnams phri bsnan lhag chad med par gnang / rje btsun gyis mar pa la gsan pa thams cad thugs sras ras chung pa la tshang
bar bzhugs skad/ de nas dbus la byon sum 'phreng du a su mjal ba la 'gyur gyi do ha gsan/ yar klungs su rje btsun sku mtshar ba dang / dbus mo'i gsol nyams nang 'dzom
lo gsum pho brang skyor ldem du grags par rgyal po'i sras tshab mdzad/ rje btsun gyis mdze por sprul nas g.yu bslangs/ ras chung pa gtong phod che bas sbyin/ des yab yum
khros te slar rje btsun gyi drung du bzhugs/ g.yu sprang po la sbyin pa mi las lon/ /do nub bde mchog gi dbang yon mdzod/ /gsungs/ de nas re zhig na/ da ni ras chung dbus
su song / /dbu ru byang ngos 'grims la

bzhud/ /dang / dge bshes 'ga' la phan thogs par 'gyur/ sham po'i gangs/ byar po'i nags/ dgon pa rdo bod mtshams su thob/ /de na gdul bya snod ldan yod/ /yos bu'i lo rta zla
ba'i tshes bcu bzhi tshun la 'dir slebs pa gyis gsung ba bzhin/ rdze btsun gyis kyang lam du skal ldan mang po rjes su bzung ste/ bla ma'i bkas ro snyoms da lta ston pa'i
dus min pas bod yul gyi brag mkha' 'gro ma dang lha 'dre thams cad 'du ba zhig yod pa der sbos/ mi rabs gsum nas chos 'di'i bdag po 'ong / de la gtod cig gyis gsung pa
bzhin lho brag mkhar chur byon/ ro snyoms dang sangs rgyas thos chog gter du sbas/ sham por phebs/ der mkha' 'gro ma btsun chung du grags pa des sleb/ blon la spyan drangs/
grub pa'i rgyal mos tshe dpag tu med pa sgrub pa'i gnas su lung bstan/ tshul nges pa med par de'i sprul pa'i bud med re rje btsun gyi bstan pa nam gnas tshun 'ong gsung
/ de nas byar po nags su phebs/ 'di yan du rje btsun gyis mos pas spyod pa'i sa pa kho na'i tshul bzung / 'dir chos nyid kyi bden pa gzigs te yun ring por ma lon par sa
bcu pa'i dbang phyug tu gyur pas/ rje btsun gyis nga'i bu bdud kyis khyer/ bdud sus khyer/ mi la'i bdud kyis khyer ro gsungs de nas gnyal lo ro rang du bzhugs te 'phrin
las yun ring du bskyangs nas mthar tshe gong gi phug pa/ grub rgyal ma dang mi la gnyis kas lcang lo can dang khyad par med par lung bstan pa'i gnas de nyid nas sku lus ma
spangs par mkha' spyod du byon pa yin la/ da lta'ang lcang lo can na btsun mo lnga brgya'i dbus su rdo rje 'chang ye shes kyi skur bzhugs pa yin no/ /de ltar spyan 'dren
pa'i mkha' 'gro btsun chung ma tshogs kyi dbus nas mkha' spyod du byon/ slob ma lo gtsang ra dang byes 'gol ba bzhi la lho'i bu bzhi/ khyung tshang pa/ 'brog sgom/ bur
sgom/ rta shod ras pa la byang gi bu chen bzhi/ gzhan la stod pa gnyan chos skyabs sogs tshad med pa thon/ rje zla 'od gzhon nu/ sne'u zur pa/ bya yul pa sogs dge ba'i bshes
gnyen du mas kyang gtsug gi nor bur bsten no/ /de'i slob ma tsa'i rgyal ba lo/ 'khrungs sa gnyal stod/ mdo rgyud la sbyangs/ rje btsun gyi tshogs pa rnams kyi dpon du
lo nyi shu rtsa lnga bzhugs/ gtsang pa ni/ la stod gcung / sum

pa nye'u mkhar pa/ yab sum pa dbang phyug yum rma mo khyi khar gyi sras su 'khrungs/ khyim thab byed 'jug rtsis la bros nas myang stod stag tshal du stod lung rgya dmar ba
dpon slob phebs pa'i sar byon/ mdo'i sbyangs pa dang / rngog jo sras mdo sde la dgyes rdor rgyud bslabs/ rje ras chung pa'i snyan pa la gtad de byon/ phyag g.yas pa'i srin
lag mar mer phul/ lo nyi shu rtsa gcig gzims g.yog mdzad/ khong med par su la'ang chos mi gnang zhes zer grags/ bsre 'pho gnad kyi mtshams sbyor rang yang tshar drug cu
rtsa bzhi gsan/ chu bo ganggA tshun la gdam ngag che bar grags/ ting nge 'dzin grub pas mngon shes rdzu 'phrul la thogs pa med do/ /byes 'gol ba ni/ mkha' 'gro btsun chung
ma ming sring gnyis yod pa'i ming po/ mtshan ston pa yang dag dpal zer/ rje btsun gyi spyan sngar chos sgor zhugs/ mtshan chos kyi grags par btags/ gdam ngag dang nus
pas grub thob kyi grags pa thon/ 'di gsum la sku mched gsum zer/ de dag gi sras kyi thu bo grub thob gling yin/ gzhan ri thub mang du byung / byar por shes snang ba ni/ nye
gnas rin chen grags rang yin/ 'phrin las kyang legs par byung ngo / /khyung tshang pa/ 'khrungs yul stod lung / bya 'dul las rab tu byung / rgya dmar ba las bsnyen par
rdzogs/ pa tshab las dbu ma gsan pas bsten long ma byung bar dar yon tan grags las bzed pa/ dbang rdor las spyod 'jug rgya dmar ba las tshad ma dang rang rgyud/ se las phar
phyin mtshan brjod/ phug pa ba las ra li/ jo bsod las bde mchog dang kri ya/ lho pa las kha rag skor/ rwa lo las dus 'jigs dgra nag 'char pa las bka' gdams/ 'khon phu
ba lcam sring las lam 'bras/ rgya las rim lnga/ rngog las dgyes rdor bslabs/ yang dag pa'i gdam ngag la blo ma rdzogs/ 'bri sgom gling kha pa'i rtsar byon/ khong gis dbus
pa glen/ slob dpon ras chung pa 'dra ba dbus su bzhugs pa la mi zhu ba 'di nas yar 'ong ba gsungs/ bden dgongs ras chung pa'i drung du snga 'gros btang / byon pas/ nga'i
rmi lam du zla ba rang gcig nas nyi ma 'od dang ldan par 'ong bar yod zer/ zla ba de khyod kyis bsngags pa'i slob ma kho yin/ nyi ma khyod rang du 'dug zhag bcu dgu la
snyan rgyud rdzogs par gnang / phyis

lan gnyis mjal/ de nas bsgrubs pas spangs rtogs kyi yon tan bsam gyis mi khyab/ de'i slob ma dge sdings pa/ shangs pa mar ston/ rta sgom gsum la zhang los gtugs/ gzhung ma
byung nas thugs the tshom pa na/ dge sdings pa nas ma cig ong jo bla ma'i gsang yum yin/ khong la yod srid der song gsungs/ lan gnyis byon pas yod pa'i sgros kyang mi gsungs/
phyis kha che paN chen la bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan grub pa dpal bzang po/ 'dul spyod legs par bslabs/ kho thag ma chod par ma cig gi drung du byon pas/ da res dgyes
bzhin du gnang bas thugs tshim/ de nas kyang thos pas mi ngoms nyid dang ni zhes pa'i skabs bal por paN chen ratna rakShi ta la sgra tshad bslabs/ rgyud 'grel pa dang bcas
pa nyis brgya tsam/ dbang yongs su rdzogs pa brgyad cu rtsa bzhi gsan/ lar chos zhus pa'i bla ma bdun cu yod/ 'gyur yang mang bar mdzad/ chos rje sa paN dang phyag bris
gtong res mdzad pa na'ang chos rje pas bkur sti che bar 'dug go /des sba'i sngags 'chang dha ra shrI rnying ma ba/ des khong rang gi sras chos rje bsod nams rgyal mtshan/
des khong rang gi sras mo ye shes kun ldan/ phyis kun ldan ras mar grags pa/ de la kun spangs pa bde legs rin chen pas gsan/ de la mkhas btsun gzi brjid pas zhu/ khong
gis zhu dus ma cig kun ldan rang bzhugs pa gsan nas la phyir byon/ mjal nas yongs rdzogs gsan/ mkhas btsun pa nas/ ding sang sha ra rab 'byams pa/ gtsang smyon he ru kas
rtsal du bton pa las mched pa dang / gtsang chen chos kyi dbang phyug nas mched pa gnyis su gyes/ bde legs pas gnas rnying mkhan po gangs can kun dga' dpal la/ des 'brug
pa rgyal dbang chos rje la gdams te/ mya ngan las 'da' kha'i zhal chems la ras chung snyan rgyud kyi dpe 'di ra lung du chos rje kun dga' dpal 'byor la phul gsung / kun
spangs dpon slob gnyis ka stod 'brug tu zhal gyis bzhes pa zhig rgyal ba'i dbang pos dpal 'brug pa rin po che ngag dbang chos kyi rgyal po/ de las kho bos thob bo/ /ngom
rdzong ston pa ni/ gcen lung pa/ sngags rnying ma lugs kyi ston pa/ rje btsun gyi bka'i bsdu ba po/ mar pa mgo yags kyis kyang gdam ngag bum pa gang byo lon pa 'di las rtsa
ba med

pa'i snyan rgyud cig byung ba la ngom rdzong snyan rgyud du grags/ de mya ngan las 'das nas spur bzhugs sindhu ra bre gang min pa spur rus kyi rigs ma byung zer ro// gzhan
zhi ba 'od kyis brag rgya shar du bsgrub pa mdzad/ brag ri zang thal nas mkha' spyod du byon/ khyi ra ras pa mkha' spyod 'grub/ srid gsum lus ma spangs par mkha' spyod du
song / lcam lhan cig skyes pa'i sgron ma ni rje btsun bzhugs rin drung nyid na bzhugs dpe gnyer mdzad/ gshegs gshegs tshun bzhugs/ de nas 'dir byon/ 'dir bzhugs/ 'dir gshegs
med/ rje zla 'od gzhon nu'i zhal nas/ de ni kho bo la thugs rtsigs che/ gdam ngag 'di lta bu zhus shig gsungs khungs ston/ don la chos bdag mkha' 'gro yin/ dpe khyer
nas u rgyan du log pa'o gsung ngo / /rje btsun gyi sras nyi ma lta bu ni chos kyi rgyal po dwags po lha rje/ mar pas/ rgod de la bu gcig byung ba de/ /'gran gyi do med zhig
'ong ba yin/ /zhes gsungs pa de'o/ /de 'ang sngon gyi sems dpa' me tog zla mdzes/ thub pa'i spyan sngar zla 'od gzhon nur gyur pa/ snying rje padma dkar po'i mdo las/
kun dga' bo nga 'das nas ma 'ongs pa'i dus na byang phyogs kyi rgyud du dge slong 'tsho byed ces bya ba sngon gyi rgyal ba la lhag par bya ba byas pa/ sangs rgyas brgya
stong mang po la bsnyen bkur byas pa/ dge ba'i rtsa ba bskyed pa/ lhag pa'i bsam pa bskyed pa/ theg pa chen po la yang dag par zhugs pa/ skye bo mang po la phan pa dang bde
ba'i phyir zhugs pa/ mang du thos pa/ byang chub sems dpa'i sde snod 'dzin pa/ theg pa chen po'i bsngags pa brjod pa/ theg pa chen po yang dag par ston pa zhig 'byung
bar 'gyur te/ zhes lung bstan pa'i skyes bu de 'khrungs pa'i yul ni/ gnyal bud nyi'i bye brag ser lung / de nyid kyi yab mes kyis brtsigs pa'i gnas gzhi ser kha yod pa de
yin/ gdung rus snyi ba/ yab snyi ba rgyal po dang yum dal bza' gnyis la sras gsum 'khrungs pa/ bar ma zhang dar ma grags/ dgung lo sum cu rtsa gnyis kyi bar du rten khyim
pa/ sman gyi 'gro don kho na mdzad/ de'ang rgya gar gyi mkhas pa skye med sogs rgya dkar nag bal po/ lhag par bod kyi sman pa pi dzi la thug spyir sman gyi slob dpon sum
cu bsten/ bstan bcos yan lag brgyad pa la mkhas pa dpe med pa/ slob ma'ang zhang

nag dang grum pa lha rje sogs mang du thon pa/ gso spyad mdzad pa'i dus na'ang dge ba'i bshes gnyen sha ra ba sogs bsten/ thos pa legs par mdzad pa zhig ste/ so gnyis pa'i
dus jo mo dang sras kun grongs nas dwags por byon/ dbrongs ka bya ba'i gnas gzhir mang yul ba blo ldan shes rab kyis mkhan po byas/ zhang zhung pa shes rab snying po bya
bas las slob byas/ khong mtshan nyid pa yin/ yid bde ba byang chub sems dpa' bya ba bla ma mi la'i yang slob ma yin pa zhig gis gsang ston byas te tshigs rdzogs su bsnyen
par rdzogs/ der mkhan slob gnyis las 'dul ba legs par bslabs/ mkhan po las zangs dkar lugs kyi bde mchog gi skor bslabs/ bcas pa la srog las gces pa bzung bas gar byon yang
btsun pa'i dper 'dren/ byang chub sems dpas gdam ngag cig btab byung bas zhag bdun bdun tsam ting nge 'dzin la 'byams 'gro ba byung / ci tsam thub bltas pas zhag bcu
gsum tsam thub/ de nas ngas rab tu byung nas de'i bya ba gnyis la ma 'bad na mi 'ong dgongs te dbur stod du byon/ der dge bshes smyug rum pa'i spyan sngar bzhugs nas lam
rim zla ba dgu bskyangs/ thugs la 'khrungs/ de'i dus na dge bshes rgya yon bdag de smyug rum pa dang gnyis blo mthun mdzad nas gra pa rnams khong la zhu 'jug khong rang dben
pa mdzad nas sgrub pa mdzad kyin 'dug pa la thugs shin tu dad nas mjal bar 'dod de/ bskor ba byas gsol ba nyi tshe btab pas/ dus lan gcig khong gis mkhyen nas nang du
bkug de nas mar lam rim chung du bskyangs/ thugs la btags/ lo gsum bsten/ thugs kyi dgongs pa longs/ dge bshes rgya yon bdag de dbu ru stod kyi bka' gdams pa zhig la thugs
tshod ma thob yin/ de ltar bsnyen par rdzogs nas dwags dang dbu ru'i bar la lo skor tsam zhig sbyangs pa mdzad/ skyes bu gsum gyi lam gyi rim pa ma nor ba thugs su chud/
des gzhan gyi 'dren pa mdzad pa la mtshungs pa med pa sengge'i sgra bsgrags pa yin no/ /de nas nam zla dpyid dus shig mtshams thon nas lcags ri'i lho phyogs su skyo sangs
la byon pas/ sprang po gsum gyi gcig na re/ 'o skol gsum 'dra ba'i bsod nams chung ba yong ba/ tshol ma dgos par zan chen po dang / lo ma'i tshod ma phor pa re btung
rgyu yod na zer/ gcig na re yid smon byed na de 'dras gar phyin/ mnga'

bdag rtse lde la byed pa yin mod zer/ gcig na re rtse lde la'ang 'chi ba 'ong / byed rang byed na mi la ras pa la byed pa yin mod/ lus la gos mi dgos/ 'tsho ba mkha' 'gro mas
'dren/ gnas 'pho skyas byed pa na nam mkha' la 'phur nas 'gro/ skye shi'i 'jigs pa med pa de yin na dga' mod zer shugs ring nar nar/ mchi ma rtsig rtsig 'dug der sngar
nas dad pa'i kha la lhag par drung du 'gro 'dod pa byung / sprang po la ston mo byin/ bla ma rnams la dgongs pa zhus/ de'i nub mo dkon mchog la mchod pa byas gsol ba btab
pas/ rmi lam na rag dung ring mo zhig bus pas skad dzambu'i gling thams cad du thos pa zhig 'dug ding sang dbus gtsang na dung 'di las skad che ba med byas pa zhig rmis/
yang nam mkha' rten med la rnga bo che btags nas brdungs pas sgra chen po byung / de la ri dwags mang po nyan 'dug mi mang po dpag tu med pa 'dug pa la/ mon mo lta bu zhig
nas/ mi 'di rnams la rnga brdungs/ ri dwags 'di tsho la 'di byin zer 'o ma thod phor gang btang / 'dis 'di tsam mi khyed byas pas/ khyod rang 'thung dang 'dir ma zad
rigs drug gi sems can thams cad khyed de 'ong zer/ nga ni nyi ma nub phyogs su 'gro zer song ba rmis bla ma rnams kyis zangs nged kyis brdungs pas zangs skad mis 'don zhig
'ong bar 'dug gsungs/ 'gong ston bya ba yul phyogs gcig pa zhig yod pa de lam grogs la khrid de la stod kyi phyogs su gtad de byon/ sang sleb zer bar 'chi la thug pa zhig
byung / 'gong ston lam du lus/ spro bde bkra shis sgang du mjal/ chang thod phor gang gnang ba btungs pas rten 'brel 'grig dpal 'khor lo sdom pa'i dbang bskur/ rdo rje
rnal 'byor ma'i sgo nas byin gyis brlabs/ bsre 'pho gnad kyi mtshams sbyor khrid du bstan/ de bsgoms pas yun mi ring bar rtsa rlung gi drod rtags shar/ lcam lhan cig skyes
pa'i sgron ma dpe gnyer mdzad pas chos 'di dang 'di zhus zhes ngas bstan pas/ rje btsun gyi dbang lung man ngag bum pa gang byor lon gsungs/ lo gsum las ma bzhugs/ lo
bcu gnyis na rtogs pa thun mong ma yin pa shar ba'i lung bstan/ lo drug tu bka' gdams kyi khrod du tshud/ bya cha chos spyod

la g.yengs/ des sngar gyi sa mA dhi stong / thugs ma bde nas da nga la sgom gyi skal ba med pa yin nam/ de na bka' gdams kyi bla ma rnams kyi sar 'gro dgos snyam pa la/ yang
thugs dgongs btang bas/ nga'i bla ma rje btsun de sangs rgyas yin/ khong gi zhal nas/ phyag rgya chen po sgom dus su/ /lus ngag dge sbyor ma brtson zhig /mi rtog ye shes
yal nyen yod/ /gsung ba de 'di yin 'dug da ni dmyal bar song rung bla ma de rang la bltos pa 'cha' ba yin/ kho rang mkhyen snyam pa'i blo bcos ma ma yin pa zhig skyes nas/
blo khel nges su bkal nas gsol ba btab pas/ dar cig na rje btsun mdun du yer gyis byon pa'i snang ba shar/ de nas lo drug gnyal se ba lung du bsgoms pas drod dang ting
nge 'dzin yang klong du tshud/ phyag rgya chen po'i gnas lugs bcos min du gzigs nas/ rang rig ye shes 'od gsal 'di/ /yod med mtha' las 'das pa zhig /sogs kyi mgur gsungs
nas/ bo dhi tsitta'i 'phreng ba rdog po nyi shu rtsa gcig yod pa phyag gis glang ma'i sdong po de la bsdams te/ dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyis nga lung bstan na/ shing
'di las shing khyod skye bar gyur cig gal te ma bstan na mi skye bar gyur cig gsungs pas/ mod de la yal ga dang yal ga khri'u/ 'dab ma dang bcas pa sngo khrung nge skyes
pas/ de phan de'i 'khris na gnas gzhi yod pa'i bka' gdams pa'i btsun pa rnams kyis bya cha chos spyod mi nus pa zer sdig gsog gi yod pa'i 'phro chad/ dad dad mos mos
su gyur/ de dus sho sgom byang yes bya ba'i bshes gnyen de phyag phyir 'brangs/ der thugs so ma gsod nas bros te 'ol 'gar byon/ de'i ri khrod du lo bdun bzhugs/ phyag rgya
chen po'i rtogs pa sgom med du na 'phos/ der yang zang zing gi 'du long che nas gzhan zhig tu gshegs dgongs/ dbyar 'o de gung rgyal gyi gangs la bzhugs pa'i tho rangs
shig btsad po'i gzugs dar gyi thod chen po bcings pa/ mgul du g.yu chen po btags pa zhig byung nas/ 'dir bzhugs na yon bdag ni ngas byed pa yin te da mi bzhugs na nga'i bu
dwags lha sgam po can du bzhud cig khos khyod kyi zhabs tog byed par 'gyur ro zer/ de nas dwags lha sgam por phebs/ bla mas lung bstan pa'i

gnas su mkhyen/ thog mar zangs lung du gdan phab 'jag spyil bzos/ chu'i bcud len mdzad dgongs nas len du btang tsa na/ ras sgom ras pa na re/ chu ga na'ang mi 'dug zer/ kha
rtsang brag rtsar bting bzhag pa'i stan de sol dang gsungs/ bltas pas chu khog ma'i kha tsam zhig rdol nas 'dug 'di la gting ji tsam yod snyam lag pa brkyang bas gting mi
'dug der lo bcu gnyis su 'dag sbyar mdzad de bzhugs dgos dgongs tsa na/ bud med lus la thal ba byugs pa lag na rma bya'i sgro bzung ba zhig na re/ bcu gnyis 'dag sbyar
byas pa bas/ /bcu gnyis bstan pa spel na dga'/ /zer/ de nas zhag 'ga' lon tsa na gtsang gi klog skya ston pa byung / de nas rgyal ba khyung tshang pa/ dge bshes gnyan nag
gnyags dmar po rnams rim par byung / de rnams kyi khrid tshar ba na dbus gtsang khams gsum gyi snod dang ldan pa'i mi rnams dus gcig la 'dus pa lta bur tshogs/ gdam ngag
btab pas ring por ma lon par nyams myong khyad par can rtsa rlung gi yon tan mngon par shes pa drug ka dus gcig shar ba dpag tu med pa byung / de thams cad kyang ma dag
pa'i dngos po mi 'chang zhing / sbyangs pa'i yon tan la gnas pa sha stag ste/ ting nge 'dzin rgyal po'i mdo las/ skyes bu dam pa mya ngan yongs 'das nas/ /ma rungs dus na
bdag gis mdo 'di gzung / /nas/ de yi tshe na ting 'dzin 'dzin pa dag /lnga brgya las ni mi nyung der 'byung ste/ /mdo sde mchog 'di rgya cher bzung ba la/ /de dag sngon
du 'dren pa gzhon nu yin/ /zhes gsungs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' sangs rgyas la ma 'ongs pa'i dus mdo sde zab mo 'dzin pa la smon lam btab pa de rnams so/ /mdo ting nge 'dzin
rgyal pos brjod bya logs pa zhig bstan pa lta bur po to ba gsung zer te/ mdo 'dir sgyu ma lta bu/ dpa' bar 'gro ba/ rdo rje lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin zhib mor bstan pas/
rdo rje theg pa'i phyag rgya chen po dang mdor rgyas tsam du zad do/ /sku'i bkod pa du mar ston pa zad pas chu me dang nam mkha'/ gshegs bzhud nam mkha' la mdzad pa/ phug
pa cher ma song / sku sgam po'i ri dang mnyam pa phug tu bzhugs pa/ ye shes sems dpa' dngos su rten la bstim pa sogs rdzu 'phrul ni mo'o 'gal gyi bu

lta bu/ skye ba gcig gis thogs pa'i byang chub sems dpar zhal gyis bzhes pa ste/ ting nge 'dzin rgyal po las/ ye shes bla med 'di ni rab bsgrubs nas/ /phyi dus mod la de ni
'jig rten du/ /rgyal ba dri med 'od ces bya bar 'gyur/ /zla 'od gzhon nur gyur pa bdag nyid kyi/ /lung bstan 'di thos dga' ba rgyas gyur te/ /zhes dang / snying rje padma
dkar po las kyang / byang chub sems dpa' byed pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba rgya chen po rnam pa sna tshogs bsags nas 'chi ba'i dus byas ma thag tu nub phyogs su sangs rgyas kyi
zhing bye ba brgya stong 'das pa na de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dpag med kyi sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'jig rten gyi khams bde ba can du skye bar 'gyur te/ 'jig rten gyi khams yon
tan thams cad kyi brgyan pa zhes bya bar de bzhin gshegs pa 'od dri ma med pa zhes bya bar 'gyur ro/ /kun dga' bo dge slong 'tsho byed de'ang nga'i bstan pa 'di yangs
shing rgyas par byed par 'gyur gyi/ kun dga' bo khyod mya ngan ma byed cig ces gsungs so/ /dus de'i tshe khams pa mi gsum gyis dam tshig gi rdzas cung zad cig gsol bas nyams
'ur/ de dge skos kyis thos nas khong gsum bskrad pas sgam po'i lha mchod thams cad mgo rting log rjes ci yin gsung / rgyu mtshan gsol bas/ khong tsho mi 'dug na nga'ang
mi sdod gsung dra chung rgyab tu bsnams/ sba mkhar phyag tu bzung nas phebs pas gling gi smad du khong gsum dang mjal/ pha bong steng ma'i khar bla mas bro 'khrabs te
yar shog gsungs/ 'og ma'i khar khong gsum gyis bro 'khrabs te yar 'ong zhu bas pha bong gnyis ka zhabs kyis 'dam brdzis pa ltar gyur to/ /der lo bcu gnyis 'gro don mdzad/
bdun cu rtsa lnga pa la gshegs/ slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa las mchog gyur dngos kyi gdan sa sgom tshul/ sras kyi thu bo khams pa mi gsum/ 'ba' rom pa la sogs sgam po'i
grub thob bco brgyad du grags pa rnams so/ /mar mi la gdan sa'i ka dpe ma med/ sgom pa chen po rje zla 'od gzhon nu rang gi gdan sar mnga' gsol ba yin/ de'ang rje sgam
po pa'i gcen po rgya pa se re dang / yum tshe lcam gnyis la sgom pa sku mched gsum 'khrungs pa'i bar pas mi chos gzung / bgres pa tshul khrims snying po/ chung ba shes rab
byang chub/

dang po dgung lo bcu bdun pa la/ dge bshes mnga' ris pa la rab tu byung / lo nyi shu pa la sha ba pa gling du bsnyen par rdzogs/ rjes gdam ngag thams cad gnang / lam phug dang
sha 'ug stag sgo sogs su bsgrub pa mdzad/ dgung lo so lnga pa la gdan sar dbang bskur/ de'i dus da nga rgas pas khyed rang rnams tshul khrims snying po la btud cig gsung
/ dpal khams pa chen pos kyang bla ma gnyis par bkur na gzhan rnams lta ci/ sgam po'i nang rten mchod khang grub nas/ stod lung du gnas brtan shes rab grags kyis spyan
drangs/ 'tshur lha lung gi dgon pa btab/ dbus gtsang khams gsum gyi grwa pa tshad che ba 'dus/ lha sar phebs pa'i tshe/ lha sa sde 'khrug gi skyon gyis re srul du song
'dug pa gso bar mi nus sam snyam pa byung ba'i tshe/ mnal lam du rje sgam po pas khyed kyis nga 'jog phod dam gsungs pa byung / jo bo shAkya'i sku yis dngos su spyan chab
phyung bas/ de nyid du bzhugs nas zhig gsos mdzad/ gser ston la sogs pa'i srol btsugs/ 'dis sgam po pa lung bstan du/ de nga'i sku gdung gi mchod rten zhig cing ral ba mthong
nas gser gyis brgyan par byed cing / gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / dar dang / dril bu g.yer kha'i dra ba g.yog pa dang / de bzhin gshegs pa'i sku gzugs
dang / mchod rten gyi khang pa dang / mchod rten rnams sengge'i rgyal mtshan gyis brgyan te/ lha dang mi rnams dga' ba skye zhing / de yongs su skyong ba dang / nga'i
bstan pa yongs su bskyang ba dang / sems ma dad pa rnams dad par bya ba dang / dad pa rnams phyir zhing 'phel ba dang / skye bo mang po'i dge ba'i rtsa ba tshogs bsags
pa'i phyir lo lnga pa byed du 'jug par 'gyur ro zhes bstan pa 'di yin zer ro/ /phyag sor ba dang gtsang nag pa sogs kyis zhabs la btud/ lnga bcu rtsa bzhi pa la gshegs/ gdan
sa gcung sgom chung gis lo gnyis bzung zhe bzhi pa la gshegs/ de'i gdan sa khu dbon gsum ka'i sras dwags po 'dul 'dzin gyis bskyangs te/ de ni sha mi 'dul 'dzin gyi slob
ma la 'dul ba la mkhas pa chen po sde snod gzhan gnyis kyang legs par thugs su chud pa 'dis mchod khang chen mo btab/ bar du 'bri gung gling pas gdan sa yud cig dang
/ 'brug pa rgyal dbang rjes lo drug gzhan spyan snga sgom pa nyid kyi

dbon rim par byon pa/ dkar brgyud kun gyi gtsug rgyan sgam po pa zhes grags so/ /rje zla 'od gzhon nus zangs lung nas lung bstan/ skye bo ye shes rdo rjes gnas kyi sgo phye
ba nas/ ding sang gi bar du 'gro ba rnams kyi bsod nams kyi myu gu skye ba'i zhing / ji tsam du nyung ba'i dus na'ang sgom chen stong phrag tsam 'khor mor tshogs pas sgrub
brgyud kyi srog shing tshugs pa'i phyir/ sgrub brgyud bstan pa'i srog shing tsa ri ba zhes bya'o/ /rje tshul khrims snying po'i slob ma'i thu bo 'gro ba'i mgon po g.yu
brag pa yin te/ yul lha sa'i tsha ba gru/ sngags rigs su 'khrungs/ chos kyi bag chags bzang / bye'u ston pa la sdud pa/ gshen la mtshan brjod/ rngog la mdo sde dgyes rdor/
gur ma yA/ gsang ldan/ sam bu lo tsA la mngon pa dang tshad ma bslabs/ bco brgyad pa la pha tshan gyi brnyas pa byung bas mthu lo gsum bsgrubs nas tshar bcad/ khams su
byon/ nyi shu rtsa bzhi la mnal lam du rna nas rna khrag mang po 'dzag pa'i mthar sbrul 'dra ba'i sems can ring mo zhig thon nas nub phyogs su rgyang ring por song / der
khyod dang yun ring 'grogs te da ni mi phrad snyam pa byung / gser g.yu 'dor/ 'khor ba las yid byung nas mthu mdzad 'phro'i bca' gzhi bshig pas slob ma zhig yod pas slob
dpon de 'dra ma byed zer du byung / nyer drug pa la dkon mchog brtsegs pa gzigs pas dad pa chen po 'khrungs/ mkhan po dge ba'i bshes gnyen mkhar sgo ba dang / slob dpon
grab mkhar ba/ gsang ston gzung ljang mdo ba rnams kyis byas te bsnyen par rdzogs/ mtshan brtson 'grus grags par gsol/ lo gcig cog pu dang stan gcig mdzad/ dpal rga lo sog
tu phebs pa mjal te rim pas gdam ngag gsan/ rgya gar gyi mkhas pa bai ro tsa na dang mjal/ rang yul du log bsgoms pas thig le'i gegs byung / rga lo thag ring / yer pa ba
la gtugs/ lo gsum song ba dang rga lo mjal gdam ngag lhag ma zhus/ dgung lo so gsum pa la/ slob dpon sgom pa lha sar zhig gsos mdzad pa'i tshe mjal/ lhan cig skyes sbyor
gnang nas bsgoms pas sngar gyi sgom thams cad shes pa kha phyir bltas su 'dug da ni sgom mkhan rang gtan la 'bebs par 'dug snyam dga'/ rtogs pa'i sa mtshams ma phyed pa
la ban da bun dar song /

slob dpon la zhus pas gsol ba drag tu thob/ nged kyi 'di byin rlabs la brten pa yin/ de rang phyag rgya chen por bya dgos gsungs nas gdam ngag zhig gnang ste bsgoms pas/ sems
ma bcos pa nam mkha' lta bu'i ngang nas shes rab kyi me mched kyin 'dug de tsug yin snyam rong rong byung zhus pas/ brtag dpyad ma mdzad brtags dpyad kyis sgrib pa yin
gsung / yang bsgoms pas sngar bzhin shes rab rong rong byung ba de brtag dpyad du 'dug pas de'i rjes su ma 'brangs par glod kyin bzhag pas rtogs pa lhag gis shar/ sngar
gyi rtogs pa thams cad dang mi 'dra ba zhig gting nas byung / de zhus pas/ 'o de tsug 'ong yu bu la dkar brgyud kyi byin rlabs de tsug yong ba yin/ da 'ur gyis song ba yin
gsung / nga rang yid ches pas mos gus kyang sngar dang mi 'dra ba zhig byung / de nas sngar rlung rtsol byed byed pa de goms pa'i shugs kyis sems ma bcos par 'jog pa 'di
la rlung rtsol ma byas na ma bde ba byung nas zhus pas/ de legs kyi gsung rlung skye med kyi gdams pa gnang / de yer pa pa'i rlung 'od gsal du gzhug pa'i thog tu sing gis
song nas rlung dang phyag rgya chen po gcig tu 'dres/ de nas zla ba phyed lon tsa na rtogs pa ni ma 'gyur/ sngar gyi rtogs pa dang 'dra ba'i nyams myong rnams mi 'dug
nas/ lam rtogs pa'ang 'grib pa 'am snyam pa byung nas zhus pas/ rtogs pa shing 'dra/ nyams myong spre'u 'dra ba yin pas cang mi lto yi gsung / thabs lam ma bcun pa'i phyag
rgya chen po bskyang ba de rtogs pa mtho mtho byas kyang nyams myong gi rtsal med par sa gcig pur rdugs nas sdod par 'dug nas/ 'brong bu lkug par gcig pur bzhugs te thabs
lam skye med bsgoms te nyams myong 'ur gyis 'phel/ rtogs pa dang nyams myong 'dres/ de nas bla ma 'ol dga' ba dang mjal nas byang chub sems la bogs thon/ de dus longs
spyod de tsam med/ rgod ma dkar mo zhig yod pa nye gnas la bskyon te gtsug lag khang gi sa dros gsungs pas/ kho'i yid la ci'ang med par 'di tsam pa'i blo rgya byed pa bsam
nas mas 'khor tshad cig bskor te mtho btab pas rten 'brel 'grig gung thang gtsug lag khang dbu rtse glo 'bur khyams ra lha chen dpal 'bar la sogs pa'i rten gsum bzhengs/
de nas tshal

btab/ gzhan phan rlabs chen gyi spyod pa 'khrug pa mang po mdzad/ gnas bdun du sku 'gyur ba bdun bstan nas mtshan bdun thogs te/ skal ldan rnams byang chub kyi myur lam la
bkod/ chos skyong bya rog ma ci bsgo bsgrub pa yin zhes grags/ sku 'bum bzhengs/ dgung lo don gcig bzhes pa la gshegs/ de'i dngos kyi gdan sa mnyam med shAkya'i ye shes kyis
mdzad/ gzhan nam mkha' 'od/ nyi ma 'od/ 'dul ba 'od/ shAkya 'od bzhi slob ma'i mchog tu grags pa'i nam mkha' 'od kyis lha ri kha dang / kong po'i lha ri gyang tho/ 'brog
yang steng / nyi ma 'od kyis phyug kha/ 'dul ba 'od kyis kha rag tu klu btul dgon pa btab/ de'i dbon po'i ring la ban khri tsam tshogs zer/ shAkya 'od kyis byang du dgon
pa btab bo/ /gzhan mar pa 'od la sogs pa bstan pa la bya ba byed pa'i skyes bu rim par byon pas tshal pa dkar brgyud ces lugs kyis 'od khyab par byung ngo / /khams pa
mi gsum gyi gsal stong shwa re pa la 'phrin las cher ma byung zhes grags la/ dbu se ni/ mdo khams tre shod gangs kyi ra bar/ yab rdo rje mgon gyi sras su 'khrungs yab la
grub skor phran dang / rgya gar gyi bla ma bai ro tsa na mjal/ bcu drug bzhes tshe tre bo mchog gi bla ma la rab tu byung / mtshan chos kyi grags par gsol/ jo bo'i slob
ma yol chos dbang byon pa mjal/ bcu dgu pa la dbus su byon/ nyi shu pa la stod lung rgya dmar ba dang / de'i slob ma phywa ba chos kyi sengge la mtshan nyid/ sha ra ba dpon
slob lo drug bsten bka' gdams/ pa tshab la dbu ma/ mal 'dul 'dzin gyi mkhan po byas/ ye shes blo gros kyis slob dpon/ mal gyi gcung pos gsang ston byas te bsnyen par rdzogs
'dul ba nyan/ rga lo tsA ba dang a seng gnyis rgyal na bzhugs pa la sbyor drug dang mgon po bya rog ma gsan/ sum cu pa la sgam por byon/ chos rje khu dbon mjal/ thog
mar lam rim bskyangs/ de nas dbang zhus thabs lam gyi gdam ngag gnang nas bsgoms pas/ sgom chen brgyad brgya'i nang nas sgom sran che bar grags/ ting nge 'dzin gyi yon
tan dpag tu med pa/ lo rer ras chung pa mjal chos drug dang thun 'jog sogs 'ga' re gsan/ gzhan sden phug pa/ mes tshon po'i slob ma rkyang mo spang kha ba/ gshen rdo rje
sengge/

dar yul ba sogs mang du bsten/ sgam po pas lung bstan nas/ 'ol dga'i brag gu ri bo che'i brag phug cig tu bzhugs pas/ bud med cig na re/ nga'i ma jo 'ong ngo khyod ma bzhugs
zer bas/ byams snying rje byang chub kyi sems la gnad du bsnun zla ba bcu bzhir bzhugs pas drod klong du tshud/ rtags ngo mtshar nges shes khyad par can skyes/ de nas chos
rje ja lkog na bzhugs dus rtogs pa phul bas khyod kyi don de nor 'dug nga khyod la re che ba yin pas/ da dung sgoms gsungs/ zla ba drug bsgoms pas sngar gyi de las ma
'gyur/ yang zhus pas phyag spyi bor bzhag bu 'khor ba dang 'brel thag chod pa yin no gsungs/ de nas mon rgyal pos sbyin bdag byas sha 'ug stag sgor byon/ 'khor 'das dbyer
med du song / de nas gnas nges med du byon gyin bsgrub pa mdzad/ lnga bcu pa la khams su byon nas kam po gnas nang du bzhugs/ de nas tre bor byon dge 'dun stong tsam 'dus/
de nas sgom tshul gyi zhal nas/ khyod khams su skyid sdug ci byung yang yar shog gsung ba'i bka' sgrub pa dang / gzhung 'tshur gyi bar 'dir dgon pa 'debs pa dang / dwags
lha sgam por gser gyi glegs bam brgya 'bul ba dang / bla ma zhang gi 'khrug pa la mi rnams mi dga' bar 'dug pas/ khong la 'khrug pa mi mdzad pa'i zhu ba 'bul ba rnams
la byon/ zhang la zhu ba phul bas de nas 'khrug pa ma mdzad/ 'tshur phur dgon pa btab/ brgyad cu rtsa bzhi bzhes pa la gshegs/ de'i slob ma sangs rgyas ras chen lo dgu bzhes
pa'i tshe/ zangs ri ras pa'i rtsar byon/ ras chung pa'i gdam ngag gsan/ bde gsal mi rtog pa'i nyams khor yug tu shar/ na bza' ras rkyang du mdzad pas ras chen du grags/
lo bco lnga pa la bla ma gshegs/ de nas phag gru sogs dang / lhag par sgam po gnas nang du byon nas dus gsum mkhyen pa bsten/ gdam ngag rdzogs par gsan/ de'i slob ma
spom brag pa yin te/ 'bri rgyal dam pa chos 'phyug bya bar 'khrungs/ bcu bzhi bzhes pa la ras chen pa'i snyan pa gsan nas 'bob pa skar sgang du sangs rgyas ras chen mjal/
phyag na rdo rje dngos yin pa'i snang ba shar/ gdam ngag rdzogs/ spel sgo dgon par lo bcu drug tu bsgrub pa mdzad dag pa'i snang ba shar/ snyan pas phyogs thams cad du khyab/
de nas khra shod

sbom brag tu dgon pa btab/ smar khams su gshegs/ de'i slob ma rin po che karma pa ste/ 'bri lung dam pa chos phyug tu rtsad po u'i rigs/ yab rgya dbang tshur tsha srang dar
gyi sras su 'khrungs/ mtshan chos 'dzin du btags/ lo dgu dang bcu pa la gsung rab mang po klog pa tsam gyis thugs su chud/ sems nyid gshis 'gyur ba med par rang bzhin du
gnas/ ngo cung zad ma mkhyen pa rin po che spom brag pas ngo sprad/ de nas gdam ngag gnang ba'i dbu tshugs/ de nas ka thog pa byams 'bum dang / lcang mang phu pa la bsnyen
par rdzogs/ mtshan chos kyi bla mar gsol/ lo bcu bar med par nyams len bskyangs pas mthar phyin/ khams su grwa pa lnga brgya tsam 'dus/ ljang yul gyi bar du drag po'i
las kyi nus pa bstan nas lam rgya btsugs/ 'tshur phur lo drug bzhugs gangs dkar ma dang thang lha sogs lha chen thams cad bran du bkol/ snyan pa'i grags pa thon/ hor rgyal
pos gser yig pa btang nas gdan 'dren du byung / rgya yul du byon/ lam du sems can mang po'i don mdzad/ rgya yul du chu la bskyur ba sogs mang po byung ba rnams zil gyis
mnan/ karma pa'i snyan pa je che la song / khyad par mkhar zhig tu bcug khro chus sgo bsdams nas gsol zas med par bzhag kyang nyam nga ba med pa'i cho 'phrul bstan pas/
go po las kyang zhabs la gtugs/ bod yul la sogs gar bde bar chos spyod cing nged la smon lam bzang po thob zer nas 'ja' sa bzang po bsgrags/ cong to mkhar nas 'tshur phu'i
bar phebs lam la lo brgyad song / mtshur phur phebs nas lha chen gyis thog drangs rten gsum mang du bzhengs/ 'di'i dbon brgyud kyis bstan pa 'dzin pa zhig 'ong rgyu dngos
de snye mo gya pa'i ru ba dang thug pa'i 'thab gral du gshegs/ des grub chen rang mi gshegs gong du grub thob u rgyan pa rgya nag tu 'byon pa'i lam dbus brgyud rtsis la/
pag shis chos skyong rnams la u rgyan pa 'dir gdan drongs gsung / u rgyan pas kyang mkhyen nas 'tshur phur phyogs byon/ der karma pa'i gsung nas/ gya ba byang pas gyu
ba byas/ /zhwa nag po can gyi brgyud pa bcad/ /'on kyang nyi ma la stod kyi phyogs nas zhwa nag po'i brgyud pa 'dzin pa zhig 'ong / de'i bar du nged kyi rgyal tshab khyod
kyis byed dgos gsung / zhwa nag gser mdongs dbu nas phud de grub thob pa la bskyon/ lde mig ka to ra gang dbu

thog tu bzhag ste/ rgyal ba rgya mtsho'i dbang yin gsungs bskur/ grub thob pas kyang zhal gyis bzhes/ sku gsum ngo sprod cig gsan/ der zhag gsum las ma bzhugs/ phyis mjal ba
med do/ /de nas karma pa ring por ma lon par gshegs so/ /de'ang dbon brgyud kyis bstan pa zin pa med nas sprul pa'i sku rim par byon pa 'di byung ba yin zhes grag go /de'i
sprul pa'i sku rang byung rdo rje ni/ 'khrungs yul mi la'i yul rtsa phu'i gangs zhur mo'i 'gram du zhi byed pa zhig gi sras su 'khrungs/ lo lnga lon pa na grub chen u
rgyan pa mjal/ grub chen pa'i gsung nas sang nga'i bla ma karma pa 'byon pa yod gsungs nas stan mthon po bshams/ der grub chen pa'i drung du phyin pa na stan de la 'dzem
pa med par 'dzegs te bzhugs/ grub chen pas byis pa khyod nga'i bla ma'i gdan la sdod pa ci yin gsungs pas/ bla ma de nga yin te/ da khyod la re dgos par 'dug zer nas zhol
gyis babs/ u rgyan pa la phyag mdzad/ der dbu skra bcad rang byung rdo rjer gsol/ dge bsnyen/ byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa/ dbang man ngag rim par gnang / dgung lo
bdun pa la kun ldan shes rab la dge tshul bsgrubs/ de nas 'tshur phur pag shi'i slob ma gnyan ras la chos gsan/ gzhan gnam mtsho ba/ gsang phu gling smad pa shAkya gzhon
nu/ snye mdo pa kun dga' don grub sogs bsten/ mdo sngags kun la mkhas par sbyangs/ dgung lo bco brgyad pa la mkhan po gzhon nu byang chub dang / slob dpon dge 'dun rin
chen pas byas te bsnyen par rdzogs/ hor rgyal po'i spyan 'dren byung nas thegs/ snga ma la phyir phebs/ phyi ma rgya yul rang du gshegs/ chos rje nyid zla ba'i dkyil 'khor
nang du bzhugs pa bstan pas rgyal po 'khor bcas shin tu dad/ de nas zhwa nag po can dang / rtogs ldan grags pa sengge la zhwa dmar po gnang bas zhwa dmar ba byung / de'i
sprul sku mkha' spyod dbang po/ de nas zhwa dmar nag gi sprul pa'i sku gnyis su gyes te/ dang po ni ma byon pa'i sangs rgyas sengge/ slob dpon padmas rgyal ba mchog dbyangs
yin pa dang / lhag par sprul pa'i na rim bcu gcig mtshan gsol te lung bstan/ de dag las rol pa'i rdo rje/ hor rgyal po the mur gan dang / de'i sprul pa'i sku gong ma
ye dbang gis spyan drangs te rgya yul du phebs dus/ rgya'i yul 'od kyis khengs pa dang / gzims khang la 'ja'i ka ba zug pa

sprin gyi gseb tu sangs rgyas dang byang sems mngon sum du byon pa/ lha'i bu dang bu mo rnams kyis nam mkha' nas mngon sum du mchod pa 'bul ba la sogs pa'i rdzu 'phrul dang
ngo mtshar ba'i ltas dpag tu med pa bstan pas rgyal po 'khor dang bcas pa dad pa lhag par spel nas yang dag pa'i lam la bkod/ gong nas mtshan de bzhin gshegs par gsol lo/
/de nas rim par byon pas dbus gtsang khams su karma kaM tshang pa zhes bya ba'i lugs dar ro/ /chos kyi rgyal po zla 'od gzhon nu'i sras kyi thu bo dpal phag mo gru pa ni/
yul 'dod khams kyi lho rgyud 'bri lung rme shod kyi stag ngos sab khang bya bar/ gdung rus dbas we na 'phan thog gi rigs/ yab dbas we na a dar bya ba dang / yum re dbye
bza' btsun ne bya ba sras su bltams/ de dus yum gyi rmi lam du gser gyi rdo rje rtse dgu pa zhig skyes pa thu bar bzhag pa las phyogs bcur 'od zer 'phros pa rmis/ dgung
lo dgu pa la bya khyi lha khang bya bar mkhan po lhing nge yan thub bu tshul khrims bya ba dang / slob dpon lhing nge 'od zer rgyal mtshan las rab tu byung / mtshan rdo
rje rgyal por gsol/ yi ge ma bslabs par mkhyen pas mkhan po dngul 'bum bzheng pa'i zhabs tog mdzad/ khams rang du slob dpon bcu drug tsam bsten/ gzhan la spyod 'jug lan 'ga'
re bshad/ mkhan slob thugs mnyes pas dbus su rdzong bar zhal 'cham ste/ dbas chen po dang stabs su byon/ khong la rdzas chen po mnga' ba dang gcig byas chog pa byung
/ sog gi mer nag khar phebs pa'i tshe dbus gtsang gi phyogs thams cad nag po ra ri zhig gis khengs 'dug pa la/ mi g.yo ba'i sku chung ngu zhig gi ral gris bcad nas phyogs
thams cad skya bsang la song ba'i snang ba byung / dgung lo bcu dgu pa stod lung du 'byor/ rgya dmar pa'i sar gzhi phab/ dbu tshad nyan/ zhar chos pa dge bshes phya pa la
zhus/ de nas khong gi phyag phyir gsang phur phebs/ slob gnyer mthil phyin mdzad pas khams pa gcig la ston pa bzang bar grags/ de dus khams pa sde tshan rnams kyis g.yag
brkus pa phywa pas dgongs nas gzigs su phebs pas/ sta gri bsnams te bdas pas/ slob dpon spyil bur tshud sgo'i ya them la phog pa da lta'ang yod/ de lta bur sdig bsags pa
shin tu byang dka' bar byung

gsung / gzhan yang bya yul pa sogs bsten/ bka' gdams la sogs pa gsan/ nyi shu rtsa lnga pa la zur phur bya 'dul gyis mkhan po/ rgya dmar bas slob dpon/ dmar gyis gsang ston
mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ mkhan slob la 'dul ba/ gsang ston la phar phyin/ myang bran la spyod 'jug sogs gsan/ mkhas pa chen por grags/ dmar chos rgyal ba la bde mchog
sogs dang / dpal rga lo dang mjal mgon po la sogs pa'i skor/ 'jad brag ltag pa dang brdog mun ne la 'phags skor dang mngon pa/ de nas bur du bur sgom nag po la lo ro ras
chung pa'i gdam ngag rnams gsan/ der zla ba brgyad bsgoms pas sku thams cad bde bas gang ba dang / zhabs la tsher ma zug pa'ang bde bar 'char ba byung / de nas sa skyar
byon/ sa chen kun dga' snying po la rgyud sde mang po dang / khyad par lam 'bras sogs bum pa gang byo gsan chos dri ba la dgyes pas lan legs par gsol bas khams pa shes rab
can zhes mnyes/ dpon slob lhan du rdo rje phug tu bsgoms pas rtsa rlung gi drod rtags legs par byung nas/ bla mas mthong lam gyi rtogs pa shar bar ngo sprad/ gzhan yang
'byim lo dang / byang sems zla ba rgyal mtshan bsten/ khong gi zhal nas zla ba mar ngo la mtshams bcad/ yar ngo la chos bshad dbang bskur dang byin rlabs byas na gzhan la
phan che bar 'ong gsung / gzhan yang bla ma mang du bsten/ stod lung du sangs rgyas gnyal chung bya bas khams pa ston pa khyod kyi rjes su mkha' 'gro ma gser gyi rgyan
can bzhi 'brang gi 'dug cing / ngam shod ri'i drung du 'gro ba mang po la phan thogs par 'ong zer lung bstan/ slar yang sa skya pa'i spyan sngar byon dogs pa bcad/ ma cig
zha ma sogs bla ma bcu gsum tsam la gtugs/ lar gdams pa 'di che zer ba la ma gtugs pa med gsung / de dus zhang sum thog pas sa skya pa'i drung nas khrid de yar klungs su
byon/ khong byas btsad po la sogs pa dang yon mchod zhig yong re ba la mthun 'jug ma mdzad pas bla ma zhang cung zad ma mnyes/ zhang la nyes pa med par skur pa chen po zhig
byung bas/ zhang gis nga la ni nyes pa ye med/ 'di 'dra ba'i gtam ji ltar byas na zhi bar 'gyur dris byung bas/ dge ba'i bshes gnyen chen po zhig la brten na zhi bar
'gyur ram gsung / 'o na dge ba'i

bshes gnyen su che zer/ da lta dwags po snyi sgom kho na snyan pa che bar 'dug pa gsungs pas dge bshes khams pas grogs byed na 'gro zer/ der bsdongs te sgam por byon/ de dus
bla ma rin po che 'khor bar 'khyam pa'i rgyu'i gtso bo gang lags zhus pas/ tha mal gyi shes pa ngo ma shes pa yin mod gsungs/ gsung de kho nas bde cham song ba zhig byung
/ de nas dogs gcod ci zhus kyang dge ba'i bshes gnyen chos dri mkhas gsungs nas dgyes dgyes mdzad de gsungs/ der phyag rgya chen po 'di la zer/ snyam pa thams cad zhus
pas/ rtog pa yin mod ka gsungs/ dus lan gcig ngo sprod cig gi rkyen gyis rtogs pa gsha' ma de shar ba bla mas/ dgongs nas phyag rgya chen po bya ba de la zer ba yin gsungs/
de'i tshe sku g.yo 'gul ma nus/ sngar gyi bla ma rnams ci red na bya ba lan 'ga' gsungs/ de nas brtsams te shes rab kyi klong rdol/ chos ci bltas kyang mi go ba ma byung
/ rje sgam po pa gshegs nas lo gcig bzhugs/ de nas yar byon te thugs la bla ma sa skya pa chen po de chos dri ba la dgyes pas da nga la shod rgyu thogs pa med snyam byon/
de res dri ba tsam yang mi mdzad par spyan rtsa 'gyur 'dug pas/ bla ma de myur du grongs par mkhyen/ 'on du phebs tshal sgang du bzhugs/ der slob ma mang du 'dus/ der
tsha rong btsad po'i sgo drung du byon nas/ kho bo tshal sgang du sdod pa de legs/ da phag mo gru'i phu'i nags pha gir bsdad na snyam pas spyan ras kyis btsa' bar zhu bya
ba'i lan bskur bas/ nang du bos them pa mi 'da' ba'i dam bca' yod zhus pas/ kho rang der byon thugs dang bstun chog pa'i zhu ba phul/ de nas dre'u zhig la chibs pas rin
chen spungs pa'i brag rtsa nas 'gro ma phod/ der gdan phab pas mtha' rtsa ba'am phag mo gru par grags/ rgya sgom rmi ras bya ba zhig gis bsdad sar gdan drangs/ sa de nags
kyi snying por gzigs pas/ khyod kyi spyil bu 'di skyid lan gsum gsungs pas bzhed na 'bul zer/ de nyid du kho bo'i gdan long gsungs te gnas bcas/ zla ba rgyal mtshan gyi
gsung ltar mdzad dge 'dun btos che ba tshogs/ gzims skyil nang na bang ba chung ngu nas khal re lhag tsam shong ba zhig las med kyang / grwa mang la brgyags 'gyed ci bcus
kyang zad pa mi 'byung / nor rgyun mas dpon slob brgyad

brgya tsam gyi 'tsho ba sbyor ba yin zer/ dge 'dun rnams shin tu dad pas gzims spyil nas chos khri'i bar gyi lam thams cad du zhwa gos dang dar kha la sogs pa 'ding / der sgom
btab pa thams cad la myong ba phun sum tshogs pa skyes pas phyogs thams cad du snyan pas khyab pas slob ma grwa pa brgyad brgya la gdugs thogs lnga brgya zer ba byung
/ sku lus kyi bkod pa bcu gnyis su ston/ mkha' 'gro ma rnams la rgyud sde gsan pa'i rgyud de'i le'u grangs dang don bsdu ba'i yi ge mdzad/ dus de'i tshe bla ma'i gzims spyil
du bud med tshogs pa'i skad thos nas nye gnas stag lung thang pas ltar yongs pa dang po la ci'ang ma mthong ba dang / yang skabs zhig skad 'dug nas bltas pas bya 'jol
mo zhig phur ba las gzhan ma mthong / der bla ma nyid la zhus pas/ mkha' 'gro ma tshogs pa yin/ khyad par phag mo gru na bu mo lnga gsum bco lnga lon pa zhig yod/ de ni
dpal rdo rje phag mo'i sprul pa'i sku/ khyod rang de phyag rgyar bsten na phung po 'ja' lus su 'gyur ba yin gsung / btsal bas rnyed de lan gnyis su yal bar bor bas/ de mya
ngan las 'das te/ dbu thod grub thob gling gis bcad klad pa bldag rung byon/ thod pa de las kho mo rang gi gnas su 'gro zhes pa'i sgra byung bas tsa rir zhog cig pa'i
bka' gnang / phung po gzhan rnams stag lung thang pa de ma thag tu tshol du song bas yal nas mi 'dug ces grags te/ bcom ldan 'das dpal 'khor lo sdom pa ni bde gshegs phag
gru pa/ mtshan ldan gyi bu mo de rdo rje phag mo dngos su byon par 'dug go /da res stag lung thang pas de go ma chod/ tshul khrims rin po che'i rten 'brel 'grig pas phyis
go chod du song zhes grags so/ /de nas skabs shig grwa pa rnams bsags nas/ grub thob nam mkha' dang mnyam pa zhig tu mis kyang mthong nas 'ong / sprul pa mang po 'gyed
pa dang / mngon shes la sogs pa'i yon tan mang po 'char ba dang / tshe'ang dpag tu med pa thub par 'dug khyed slob ma rnams lta ba dang / mjal ba dang / byin rlabs zhu ru
yod/ chos 'chad pa mi 'ong ba de dang / khyod tsho la chos bshad na tshe thung du 'gro ba 'dug ste chos 'chad pa la 'dam gros gyis gsungs/ grwa pa kun tshogs te gros thag
