ma chod/ dge bshes zhang e nas bos/ khong gis dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad yon tan dang / sprul pa dang / nus pa bsam

gyis mi khyab pa mnga' yang 'o skol dang mjal du med/ chos mi gsung na ci la phan ces gsungs pas thams cad der gros thag chod/ rin po che la zhus pas/ dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro
thams cad mdun ma de la ma mnyes gsung / zhang nas chos bshad pa la mi dgyes pa'i dpa' bo dang mkha' 'gro de bdud rang yin gsung / der bka' bgros snga ma la gdams na spyir
bod/ sgos dkar brgyud kyi bstan pa la ches phan pa zhig yong rgyu yin te bsod nams la ma bskos pa yin gsungs/ de nas grwa pa rnams la dbang byin brlabs rgyud man ngag
thams cad gang la gang 'os pa gnang bas nags khrod de la dpal kun tu bzang po'i nags tshal zhes grags te/ 'og min gyi zhing byas kyang de kha/ rdo rje 'chang byas kyang
bde gshegs phag pho gru pa/ sa bcu pa'i 'khor byas kyang rab tu byung ba brgyad brgya tsam 'dus pa'i skal ldan 'di rnams so zhes lha dang bcas pa'i 'jig rten na grags so/
/dgung lo drug cu rtsa gcig pa la gshegs te ngo mtshar ba'i ltas bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung ngo / /de'i bu chen byon pa ni/ mos gus mthar phyin stag lung pa/ rtogs pa
mthar phyin sna phu pa/ shes rab mthar phyin spar phu pa/ nus mthu mthar phyin mchan bu rgya ras rnams la mthar phyin gyi bu bzhi zer/ skal ldan ye shes sengge/ rtogs ldan
mi nyag sgom rings/ grub thob nyag re se po/ kun ldan gtsang pa ras chung rnams la gdams pa'i bu bzhi zer/ chos rje 'jig rten mgon po/ bandha phug pa/ chos rje lUm/ chos
rje gtum rnams la ro gcig rtogs pa phyed dang bzhi zer/ bla ma dmar pa/ ye phub pa/ dgyer sgom/ bshes gnyen sengge dpal rnams la nye ba'i sras bzhi zer/ gzhan bla ma zhang
/ dge bshes glang / gshen rdo rje sengge la sogs pa slob ma bsam gyis mi khyab pa thon/ /de las stag lung thang pa ni/ g.yang shod bong ra steng du/ yab ban blon 'bar
po'i sras su 'khrungs/ bco brgyad bzhes pa'i tshe/ thang skya lha khang du bla sgang pa'i sar bros/ mkhan po na ston bla sgang pa shes rab rdo rje dang / slob dpon tshar
ston sgo mang pa las rab tu byung / dge bshes brag dgon pa la 'grel chung spyod 'jug bslab btus/ lam sgron sogs gsan rgya gar rang la 'gro dgongs kyang zla bo dang bangs
bsnyags kyis zin nas ma thon/ de nas phag gru'i snyan pa gsan nas 'byon par dam bcas pa'i dus/ mnal lam du skas ring shig la

'dzegs nas byon pas thog khar mthon tsa na mi dkar po chen po zhig gis phyag nas bzung nas ngas ma 'then na mi thon zer ba zhig rmis/ phyis rje phag gru'i gsung nas/ de kho
bo yin gsungs/ khong gi dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bzhi bzhes pa'i dus phag mo grur phebs/ lo drug phag mo grur bzhugs/ nye gnas mdzad/ bla ma'i thugs su byon/ chos gsungs pa
thams cad ma brjed par yi ger btab/ gdam ngag che/ dpal phag mo gru pa gshegs nas zla gcig nas mal gror 'chad ka ba la chos gsan/ de nas slar phag mo gru'i gdung rten gtsug
lag khang bzhengs la byon/ zhang shom rab la mkhan po zhus/ las slob mar pa lam thang pa/ gsang ston zhang ston sgom min pas mdzad de shom rar bsnyen par rdzogs/ stag
lung 'di 'gro mgon rin po ches drug cu bzhes pa/ sa mo glang gi lo sku lus kyi bkod pa bcu gnyis mdzad pa'i tshe sku lus kyi bkod pa gcig gis thang pa la/ khyod kyi 'phrin
las rgyas pa'i sa shig nyi ma byang phyogs pha gi na 'dug rab khyod khams su 'gro thang ba yin pas thengs gcig song / de'i rjes su sngon gyi las kyis bskos pa'i gnas de
dang phrad cing / der 'phrin las rgyas pa yin/ de'ang sa de shin tu rtsub cing mi las gyur pa'i 'dre zhig gis sna drangs pa'i lha 'dre gdug pa can dpag tu med pa gnas pa
sus kyang mi zin pa yin pa la kho bos thams cad zhabs kyis bcags/ lha 'dre thams cad btul byams pa'i las dang ldan par byas yod pas/ da khyod kyis zin pa yin gsungs/ dar
sprad rong gsum dang phod mdo bas stag lung du gdan drangs/ dgung lo so dgu pa la bla brang nag por phyags pheb/ yongs sum cu tsam bzhugs/ sku 'da' khar grwa pa sum stong
lhag tsam 'dus/ ngo mtshar ba'i rdzu 'phrul du ma bstan/ drug cu re dgu pa la gshegs/ dbon rin chen mgon gdan sar bton/ 'dis mchod khang chen mo btab gling dar rgyas su
mdzad/ de'i gdan sa sangs rgyas yar byon/ de la gdan sa zer ba'i dbon po gnyis byung ba nas gcig khams su byon ri bo che btab/ de nas stag lung ya thang ma thang gnyis
su gyes/ gnyis ka ban sum stong brgyad brgya lhag tsam re 'tshog dbus gtsang mdo khams gzhan du'ang grwa pa'i dar rgyas che ste/ ding sang gi bar du dbon brgyud rim par byon/
dus phyis stag lung ngag dbang grags pa zhes bya

ba'i mkhas grub de byon/ snyan pa che bas dbus gtsang gi che dgus btud/ 'bri stag gi chos lugs nyams la khad pa rnams gsos so/ /de dag kyang 'brel tshad don ldan byang chub
sems dpa'i sprul pa kho na'o/ /spar phu ba ni/ g.yor ru grar 'khrungs/ gzhon nu nas thos bsam mdzad/ khyad par phywa pa yun ring du bsten/ khong gi grwa pa'i nang nas shes
rab che bar grags/ a su las do ha gsan/ bla ma yel pa ye shes brtsegs kyi do ha skor rnams gsan pas/ 'di bshad pa rkyang du 'dug nga'i bla ma de dang mjal na nyams myong
khyad par can yong nges bsam/ spar phu ba la 'gro mgon gyi spyan sngar byon pa 'thad zhus pas/ rang re las lhag pa cang yod dam gsungs/ cis kyang 'byon par zhu/ lhag pa'ang
'ong srid zhus pas byon/ 'gro mgon dang mjal/ gsung gleng mang du mdzad/ spar phu ba'i thugs la bla ma 'di sems tsam gyis lta ba 'dzin par 'dug snyam pa byung khrid
btab pas/ 'di la nga rang zhib par 'dug snyam yon tan ma skyes/ tshogs chos gsan pas/ de la mgu bar gyur te log yang bla ma yel pas bla ma rin po che'i drung du mos gus
can la yon tan 'char rgyu zhig yong gi 'dug pa la/ slob dpon pa la ma skyes bar snang bas da dung lan cig gshegs par zhu byas pas rung gsungs/ slob dpon dang 'grogs nas byon/
'gro mgon gyi rten 'brel mdzad nas/ bu ram la padma'i par legs par btab nas drangs pas khong de la chags te ma gsol bar bzhag pa/ yel pa ba bzhengs nas bcag ste drangs/
'gro mgon gyis/ pha rol tu phyin pa dang dbu ma la sogs pa rgyu mtshan nyid kyi chos/ thabs lam gyi bye brag dang phyag rgya chen po la sogs pa 'bras bu sngags kyi chos
thams cad kyang sems rtogs pa'i thabs su gsungs pa kho na yin/ sems rtogs pa la sgom dgos sgoms shig gsungs pas/ ga re gdam ngag ci'ang ma bstan par sgoms shig gsungs
bsam cung zad bsams tsa na gnas lugs kyi don mngon du gyur nas 'gro mgon la gsol 'debs 'dod 'jo'i ba mo mdzad/ spar bu dgon btab tshogs pa lnga brgya tsam 'dus so/ /mchan
bu rgya ras ni/ chos skyong gis rjes su bzung bas grub pa brnyes/ skal ldan ye shes sengge ni mon gar du 'khrungs/ phag mo gru'i ri mthong pa rang gis sgom 'khrungs/ de
nas 'gro mgon

dang mjal/ ngo sprod cig btab pas rtogs pa khyad par can 'khrungs/ skal ldan ye shes sengger grags/ des grwa rabs su zar dgon pa btab/ de'i slob ma g.ya' bzang chos rje yin/
gtsang zhal gyi dmar mor 'khrungs/ sgri nas mkhan po chos ston bya ba zhig la rab tu byung / mtshan chos smon lam du gsol/ de nas 'chad dkar du 'dul ba dang bka' gdams
gsan/ de nas lo bco brgyad pa la rgya dur du byon bsnyen par rdzogs/ lo drug tu 'dul ba la sbyangs pa mdzad pas gnubs 'dul ba 'dzin par grags/ nyer brgyad pa la zar na skal
ldan ye shes sengge bzhugs pa gsan nas der byon/ zhal mjal ba tsam gyis rtogs pa shar/ gdam ngag rdzogs/ so brgyad pa la g.ya' bzang btab/ drug cu rtsa lnga pa la gshegs/
'phrin las shin tu che ba'i slob ma'i mchog sgom bzhir grags pa byung / gdan sa rin chen jo sras/ de'i rjes su rtogs ldan rgyal po dge mdzes 'od/ de'i rjes su mkhar chu
pa chos bsam 'od kyis lo bco brgyad mdzad/ 'di grub thob u rgyan pa la rdo rje rnal 'byor mas lung bstan pa de yin/ de nas rim par brgyud de g.ya' bzang pa zhes grags
so/ /mi nyag sgom rings ni/ 'gro mgon gyi drung na khrid zhu ba'i tshe nangs shig 'gro mgon gyis kho'i mdun du thag pa'i rgya zhig bres/ ral gri zhig zhog gsungs/ de nas
kho'i pha gsod mi zhig yod pa khrid de 'gro mgon byon/ sgom rings zhe sdang skyes nas ral gri khyer brgyugs pas/ 'gro mgon gyis khyod rang gi sems la ltos shig gsungs nas
de nyid du rtogs pa shar/ 'dis 'bri gung btab/ grwa pa brgya tsam 'dus/ skyob pa lung bstan te khong rang gshegs/ nyag re se bo 'gro mgon mjal nas grub pa thob/ khams su
sles dgon btab 'phrin las bskyangs so/ /rin po che rgyal tsha dang / kun ldan gtsang pa ras chung gnyis mched/ gnubs nam mkha' snying po'i brgyud du 'khrungs/ rgyal tshas
bla ma mang po bsten/ sbyangs pa mthar phyin/ lhag par dpal phag mo gru pa la brten nas phyag rgya chen po'i rtogs pa shar ba yin/ kun ldan ni phag mo grur gcen po'i brgyags
skyel ba la byon/ rje btsun mi la'i rnam thar gsung pa dang thug de 'dra ba zhig ngas kyang bya snyam nas chos grwa der mgo lcogs lan gsum byas/ 'gro mgon la gdams
pa zhus nas bsgoms pas rtogs pa shar grub pa brnyes/ mu ge byung ba'i tshe khro phu'i mchod khang gi sgo

la phyag mkhar thug thug mdzad nas rnal 'byor ma rnams/ de ring rnal 'byor pa la bsod snyoms shig zhu'o gsungs pas/ mchod khang gi sgo 'phar nas nas phyir mang du byung / yul
mi thams cad kyis blangs kyang zhag lnga'i bar du nas ma zad pa'i grub rtags bstan/ bdun cu la gshegs/ khong mched kyi dbon po khro phu lo tsA ba/ yab jo phan/ lo bcu
lon pa la rgyal tsha dang kun ldan gyis mkhan slob mdzad de dge tshul bsgrubs/ mtshan byams pa dpal bu btags/ gtsang dkar la gsan pa mang du mdzad/ lce don kun bzang la lo
brgyad cu 'gro ba zhig la rdor dbyings sogs dkyil 'khor lnga brgya lhag tsam zhig gi lag len bslabs/ 'bri mtshams pa zhang dge ba zer ba zhig la lo tsA phul du phyin pa
sbyangs/ bcu dgu pa la rgyal tshas mkhan po/ gtsang dkar gyis slob dpon/ kun ldan ras pas gsang ston mdzad de bsnyen par rdzogs/ gtsang nag la 'dul ba lo gnyis nyan/ kun
ldan dang rgyal tsha la gdam ngag lugs mi 'dra ba brgya dang sum cu rtsa drug bka' babs bcu gsum yod pa gsan/ nyer bzhi pa la bal por chas/ paN chen buddha shrI bsten/ mi
tra dzo ki mjal bod du spyan drangs/ khro phu'i gnas bzhi'i sa byin gyis brlabs/ de rting buddha shrI spyan drangs/ de'i rjes su gro mo brgyud/ bai DUr tshong 'dus su byon/
kha che paN chen spyan drangs/ lha mo che khru brgyad cu pa bzhengs/ sras sems dpa' chen po byung / rtogs pa rgyal tsha la rten nas 'khrungs/ sems dpa' chen po'i slob
ma yang rtse ba rin chen sengge/ de'i slob ma bu ston rin po che/ rgyal tsha dang kun ldan gyis slob ma lce sgom dang / de'i slob ma ma cig re ma yin te/ khro phu dkar
brgyud ces grags pa che'o/ /gshen rdo rje sengge ni/ sa skya pa chen po'i slob ma phag mo gru pa dang mched grogs/ phyis phag mo gru pa la gtugs nas rtogs pa shar ba yin/
'dis dbang sdud byas nas phag gru dbang du bsdus/ de nas slar sa skyar byon/ dmar po skor gsum zhus te kho dbang du bsdus zer ba 'di dang / rga lo la snying rlung byung
nas bod du byon pa sa chen gyis bsal zer ba gnyis ka sngon gyi yi ge khungs ma la mi snang / phyis bris par 'dug pas mi bden no/ /chos rje dmar pas khams su shwa dgon btab/
tshogs pa nyis stong tsam rgyun du 'dus/ de'i rjes su shwa yang dgon pa/ rmog spyan snga rin po che/ shwa dbu rtse pa/ rnal rin chen gling pa sogs mang du byon/ smar dkar
brgyud du

grags so/ /bla ma zhang sum thog pa dang por mched grogs/ phyis zhabs kyi padma bsten pa'o/ /'bri gung 'jig rten mgon po ni/ yul ldan stong rtsod du zhes bya bar/ 'brug rgyal
skyu ru'i gdung / rnying ma'i sngags 'chang zam ma chad pa'i brgyud par yab rdo rje zhes bya ba'i sras su 'khrungs/ dbus gtsang du byon 'gro mgon gyi zhabs drung du phebs
nas zla ba sum cu rtsa gnyis bsten/ de'i tshe rten dge bsnyen na bza' ra thul zhig bzhes pas dge bsnyen ra thul can zhes grags la/ bla ma'ang mnyes/ khyod la sgom chen
bzang po zhig 'ong / sgom chen tsam la bzang ba zhig 'ong zhes lung bstan/ 'gro mgon gshegs nas e chung phug par thugs dam la bzhugs pas glo bur du bsnyun mdze drag po
zhig byung / rdza gseb tu bzhugs te ro sus kyang mi mthong ba zhig bya snyam nas byon par chas/ yi dam spyan ras gzigs kyi sku zhig yod pa la phyi phyag bgyis/ sku shed chung
bas kha bub tu cung zhig lus pa na/ dang por rang gi sdug bsngal bsams/ de nas sems can thams cad kyi sdug bsngal bsams pas snying rje chen po bzod glags med pa zhig
'khrungs/ zhag gsum dro bzhir rgyun chags sa thams cad spyan chab kyis bangs/ klu gdon de 'khor dang bcas pa sku lus las thon song ba gzigs/ sgom ro gcig gi rtogs pa thugs
la 'khrungs pas/ zhag gsum dro bzhi'i nang par na/ /mi kho bo'i las ngan rang sar dag /ces gsungs/ de ltar grub pa brnyes pa'i snyan pas 'ur bslang / gzhan ston mo byed
pa'i gral dbu la spyan drangs pa'i tshe zhig thod pa bsam grub kyi sras mo nam mkha' rgyan gyis sku mdun du gcer brgyugs byas pas/ nga rten dge bsnyen du song bas brnyas
pa yin/ cis kyang rab tu byung dgos 'dug dgongs nas dgung lo so lnga pa la phag mo grur zhang gsum thog pas mkhan po/ ci lung slob dpon/ gnyan pa 'dul 'dzin gyis gsang
ston byas te tshigs rdzogs mdzad/ mtshan rin chen dpal/ gnyal pa 'dul 'dzin la mdo rtsa legs par bslabs/ 'gro mgon gshegs rjes su bla ma zhang gis gral gong du bzhugs/ bsngo
ba tsam mdzad pa las lo bdun du gdan sa med/ de nas chos rje 'dis gdan sa mdzad de longs spyod chung zhing 'o brgyal bar byung / gsol ba btab pas mnal lam du 'gro mgon
byon nas za 'og gi 'bol rnying pa zhig 'dug pa 'di kho rang tsho la gtod la/ khyod rang

dbu ru byang phyogs su song gsungs pa rmis/ mnal sad 'phral bzhengs/ dpon slob lnga bros byon te/ dbur stod du byon pa dang / sgom rings kyis grwa pa rnams spyan 'dren du 'ong
ba dang 'grig 'bri gung du bzhugs/ bstan pa'i rtsa ba dge 'dun de'ang tshul khrims rin po che la rag las par gzigs nas/ dben pa'i gnas su 'dug pa dag kyang bag yangs
su mi 'dug snyan pas ni 'dzam bu'i gling khyab/ stag lung du thang pas spyan drangs/ bla ma'i gdam ngag yod pa'i gleng mo mdzad/ khyod bla ma bsten yun thung gsungs don gtug
la re mdzad pa la/ ja bu ram gyi gnang sbyin thugs rjes bzung sogs sgro 'dogs gcod rgyu med pa mgur du phul/ gnyos rgyal ba lha snang bas ston mo bshams pa'i dus/ 'khor
lhan cig tshogs pa dgu khri la/ /kun 'dus pa'i gtso bo gnyos chen yin/ /de lta bu'i skyob pa 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi sprul pa yin te/ kha che paN chen la singga la'i dgra
bcom pas gser gyi me tog gsum bod du bskur ba'i gcig 'phags pa klu sgrub kyi sprul par gtod cig gsungs pa su yin ma 'tshal/ paN chen glas mo cher bzhugs pa na/ paN chen
la bsnyen par rdzogs pa zhus pa'i mkhan bu rnams la chos gos re gnang gi yod pas/ 'bri gung pa'i khams btsun zhig chos gos la bltas nas bsnyen rdzogs zhus/ de res paN
chen gyi phyag na 'khrol med pas ma gnang bas/ khos dbu tshugs byas paN chen rang gi sku chos dgos zhus 'jus pas/ phyag g.yog rnams khros nas kho brdungs/ kho'i kha snar
khrag mang po shor/ paN chen thugs dam mdzad pa'i tshe/ sgrol dkar mngon sum du byon pa la/ de nas zhag bdun du ma byon/ phyi bshags mdzad gsol ba btab pas zhag bdun song
nas sku rgyab gtad de byon/ 'phags ma bdag gis ci nongs zhus pas/ khyod dpon slob kyis klu sgrub kyi slob ma brdungs pas sdig bsags gsungs/ de mi dran zhus pas/ kha sang
kha sna nas khrag shor shor brdungs pa de yin mod gsung / da de'i sdig pa ji ltar byas nas 'byang / rab tu byung ba lo grangs dang mnyam pa la chos gos byin na 'byang gsungs/
de ltar mdzad pa'i dam bcas te su'i slob ma yin rtsad bcad pas 'bri gung pa'i slob mar 'dug pas skyob pa klu sgrub tu thag chod/ phyis me tog kyang phyag tu phul ba
yin/ paN chen srin po rir bzhugs dus 'tshur 'bri

rgya gsum gyi gdan 'dren byung / paNDYi ta bi bhu ti tsandra spyir phyag rgya chen po ba la skyon/ khyad par de dus phyag rgya ba 'di rdzun che ba yin/ 'o skol bka' gdams pa
gdan 'dren sar byon pa 'thad zhu ba la/ paN chen thugs hur phyung ste/ bi bhU ti bi bhU ti/ de skad ma zer sangs rgyas la 'khrul pa mi mnga'/ 'bri gung pa slob dpon klu
sgrub yin zhes sngar gyi lo rgyus gsungs/ lhag par khyod phyag rgya ba la skur pa btab pas dmyal bar skye bar 'dug sdig pa sbyongs gsungs/ 'o na ji ltar sbyangs zhus pas/
'dir bde mchog gi sku zhig bzhengs gsungs pas bzheng par gsan/ kha che ba yin zer ba'i bzo ba zhig byung / des zhag bdun la bsgrubs nas de nyid la thim pa dpal he ru ka
nyid kyi sprul pa yin zhes grags so/ /'bri gung pas tsa ri'i dag pa shel gyi ri sgo mang mchod rten gyi dbyibs lha nyis stong brgyad brgya'i pho brang du gzigs nas bal po'i
bzo bo mkhas pa bkug ste sgo mang rin po che las bzhengs bdun cu rtsa lnga pa la gshegs/ slob ma grub pa brnyes pa bgrang gis mi lang / gtso bo rje spyan snga/ dbon rin
po che mched/ gnyos mgar chos gsum/ dbon sher 'byung sogs so/ /rje spyan snga ba ni slob dpon padma'i dngos slob a mi byang chub 'dre bkol du grags pa'i gdung rabs/ rlangs
lha gzigs/ yab yon chen rgyal bskyabs kyi sras su bltams/ bcu gsum pa la spyi gnas g.yo bu zhes bya bar rab tu byung / mtshan grags pa 'byung gnas su gsol/ dgung lo
bco lnga pa la bros nas 'bri gung du byon/ chos rje dang mjal/ der phyag dbu la bzhag pa tsam gyis chos thams cad mnyam pa nyid ces bya ba'i ting nge 'dzin 'khrungs/ lo ngo
gsum gzims spyil zur pa zhig tu de bskyangs/ bcu bdun pa la chos rje dwags por 'byon pa'i phyag phyi gzims g.yog mdzad/ de man spyan snga kho nar bzhugs pas spyan snga
bar thogs/ bco brgyad pa la zheng sum thog pas mkhan po/ lha 'bri sgang pas las slob byas te bsnyen par rdzogs/ chos rje'i gdam ngag thams cad tshang bar gsan/ chos rjes
tshogs su byon pa'i na bza' bsnams pa'i mod la khri thog tu bton/ chos rje nyid kyis phyag phul te/ ngas gdan sa brgya 'gyur stong 'gyur du bzang du btang gi gsungs nas
rje spyan snga phag mo grur brdzangs te/ ngam bus tshogs pa 'di tsam bskyangs pa'i phud rje phag mo gru pa la phul ba yin gsungs/

de bzhin de'i ring la gdan sa shin tu dar rgyas che/ lo nyi shu rtsa drug bzhugs/ de nas 'bri gung du dbon rin po che zhi bar gshegs pa'i ma legs skyel du byon dus gcung rin
po che 'bri gung gling pa sogs kyi gdan sar bzhugs dgos pa'i zhu ba phul ba ma bzhes/ tha ma stag lung pa dang bka' gdams pa sogs la rgya 'dre mi byed pa'i rtsis bzung
nas lo nyi shu rtsa gnyis mdzad/ der bzhugs pa'i lo bdun pa la hor dmag 'dam du sleb pa'i 'ur byung / 'bri gung gi dge 'dun rnams bros par rtsom pa'i tshe/ 'jigs mi dgos
gsungs cag ge bzhugs/ de'ang thog mar hor gyi dmag dpon mi li byi byung / sku mthong ba tsam gyis pha dang bu'i 'du shes skyes te phyis 'bul ba skyel bar khas blangs/ de
nas zhag nyer brgyad la dor rtas dmag dpon byas nas slebs byung / khos sgom pa shAkya rin chen gyi lag pa nas bzung nas khrid pas nam mkha' nas rdo'i char pa bab/ kho na
re 'di ci yin zer/ khyod kyis ngam bu'i sgom pa bzungs pas ngam bu ma dgyes/ ngam bu ma dgyes pas gnam ma dgyes te rdo char byung ba yin gsungs/ 'dis ci byed pa yin/ ngam
bu so nam ni mi byed/ gzhan gyi 'bul ba byung ba rnams 'di'i lag tu gtad nas dge 'dun skyong ba yin gsungs pas sgom pa btang gnod pa med par byas so/ /de ltar thams cad
ting nge 'dzin gyi dbang du mdzad pas 'bri gung gi sde'ang cher 'phel/ ban khri tsho bco brgyad 'tshog ces grags pa'ang de dus byung / chos rje sa skya paNDYi tas rje btsun
pa gshegs pa'i gral dbur spyan 'dren mdzad pa'i zhu yig tu'ang / da lta khyod las bzang ba'i dge ba'i bshes gnyen mi 'dug pas zhes bsngags pa yin/ de'i tshe gcung rin
po che la zhen 'then pa 'ga' zhig gis ma gus pa'i rnam 'gyur bstan pas nga 'gro ba yin gsungs ma zad kyi thad du sgar mdzad/ de gcung rin po ches mtshams kyi khul nas gzigs
nas har 'don mdzad bzhugs par zhus pas ma gnang / gcung gis da 'o na khyod rgya gar yul na sku khams bzang 'dug zer na'ang de bar du nga gdan sar la snom ri byas nas dbu
snyung phul bas/ 'o na da gzu ba dgus phul na'ang mi 'gro gsung / dgung lo brgyad cu rtsa gcig pa la gshegs pa yin no/ /bu slob kyang rgyal ba rin po che/ gcung rin po
che/ rgyal ba yang dgon pa sogs mang po byung ngo / /rgyal ba rin po che ni rje spyan snga'i dbon/ dgung lo bcu drug pa la dbus su phebs/ rje spyan sngas byin

brlabs mdzad pas rtogs pa 'khrungs so/ /bcu dgu pa la 'bri gung du byon bsnyen par rdzogs/ sgrub pa mdzad pas sprul bsgyur nus/ rje spyan snga 'bri gung du bzhugs dgos byung
bas dgung lo so gsum pa la thel gyi gdan sar 'bri gung nas bkod de brdzangs/ der g.yog rnams kyis mthong bkur cher ma byas pas/ rje la zhus pas tshes grangs 'di'i nyin
ngas chos rar thog 'bebs/ khyod rang de chos gos kyis bzed la pho gsungs pa de bzhin byung / chos ra thams cad brgyal nas song / thog chos gos kyis gtums te gar 'bo gar 'bo
gsung ba na'ang tshig sgra 'ur sgra 'byin/ mthar chos ra'i mthar bor bas shul mi bzad pa byung / des thams cad kyis grub thob tu shes nas gus pa rnyed/ de'i snyan pa gsan
pas/ hor rgyal po jing gir han gyi bu thu bo hu la'i hu gnam the'i sprul pa yin/ 'brug sgra thos pa dang dngangs skrag bsam gyis mi khyab pa skyes pas rgya nag gi rgyal
sa mi zin par 'dug ces sog yul du bskrad pa bsod nams che nas stod hor gyi yul thams cad kyi bdag byas/ kha che'ang kho'i 'og tu chug pa zhig yod pa des bla'i mchod gnas
su bkur/ 'bul mo che lan gsum rgyab/ stod hor gyi yul du kha che'i bzo bos bsgrubs pa'i sku rigs thams cad 'di'i ring sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la sri zhu chen po byas
so/ /gzhan yang singga la/ ti ra hu ti/ bod ya tshe'i rgyal po kun gyis 'bul ba mang du byas te drug cu rtsa lnga la gshegs/ de'i gdan sar de nyid kyi dbon/ bcu gnyis pa
rin chen rdo rje phebs te/ dbon brgyud rim par spyan snga mdzad/ sa skya nang 'khrugs nas bod bying la 'di'i dbon rigs kyis lung brgyugs pas/ lugs gnyis ka la phag mo gru
pa zhes 'gran zla med pa 'di byung ngo // 'bri gung du skyob pa rang gi gdan sa dbon rin po ches mdzad/ de gshegs nas rje spyan sngas mdzad/ de rjes gcung rin po ches bskyangs
pas 'bri gdan gnyis su gyes/ gnyos lha snang ba nas lha pa mched/ 'di'i nang du man lung gu ru'ang byung ba yin/ sa skya pa dbang che ba'i dus na'ang 'bri gung pa
lung 'og tu ma tshud pas sa 'bri stod smad thams cad du 'thab/ phyis ang len gyis rgya'i dmag bos nas 'bri gung gling log btang / cung zad las ma gnod pa ding sang bar du
dar rgyas dpe med pa 'dis shes

so// dbon sher 'byung skyob pa'i rus dbon/ skyob pa'i spyan sngar bzhugs pa'i tshe/ bla ma'i zhabs tog dang mkhyen pa la mtha' med pas thams cad kyis slob dpon pa zhes zer/
skyob pa gshegs nas ti se/ lho brag mkhar chu sogs su byon/ mkhar chur khyad chos brgya dang dgu bcu pa dgongs gcig tu grags pa yi ger btab/ de nyid du brgya lnga bcur bsdu
ba mdzad/ dwags su byon sgam po'i spyan snga'ang mdzad do/ /de ltar 'bri gung pa dar ba'i sgang la thams cad khong gi khongs su gtogs pa 'dra zhig yod skad do/ /rtogs
pa mthar phyin gling ras pa ni/ 'khrungs yul myang stod bzhengs kyi glang po snar/ gling stod smad gnyis las gling smad pa/ yab rgyal po skyab be/ yum gzus mo dar chung
gi sras su 'khrungs/ mtshan padma rdo rje/ gzhon nu nas bris klog mkhas par mkhyen/ brgyad la lha rje ras sman las sman bslabs/ bcu gsum lon tshe mkhas par gyur/ bcu bdun
pa la khu bo dge ba'i bshes gnyen gling zhes pa bka' gdams pa chen po de la dge bsnyen mdzad/ dpal dbyangs kyi sgron ma rnam drug sogs mang du gsan/ dbus pa zhang bya ba
rwa dang dpyal gnyis ka'i slob ma zhig la phag mo dang / rwa 'bum seng la dus 'khor/ bde mchog 'jigs byed sogs rwa ba'i skor zhib mo gsan/ rje dpon zhig dang rabs chad la
ma 'cham pas mthu mdzad pas de brlag mthu che bar grags/ de nas dge bshes 'om thang pa la rab tu byung / bsod snyoms la byon pas jo mo sman mos brid de tshugs ma zin/ gnyis
po bsdongs nas khyung tshang pa rwa lo'i mchod gnas mdzad pa bsten/ khong gis ras chung ba ma mjal ba 'dra bsam log lta zhig skyes pas/ phyis drod skye ba la gnod par
byung gsungs/ de nas ras chung pa'i dngos slob gnyal lo ro na mang du bzhugs zer ba gsan nas gnyal lor du byon/ tshe gong du rje sum pa la nged thag ring nas chos zhur
'ongs pa yin pas thugs la gdags par zhu byas pas/ thog mar lo la dbang chos zhus/ de nas nga mtshams grol yong gsung ba bzhin/ lo'i spyan sdar byon/ de nas sum pa/ gzhan
byes 'gol ba la'ang gtugs te/ rje ras chung pa'i gdam ngag thams cad kha tshang bar thob pas/ da lta 'dzam bu'i gling na gdams pa nga rang che snyam pa byung / de nas lho
mon du sgom du 'gro bsam pa la/ mnal lam du mi

dkar po zhig byung nas/ sku lus gcer bur phyung mgo mjug yongs la lta nyul zhib bo zhig byas te/ khyod lho mon la ma 'gro/ da ste lo lnga na khyod kyi don 'grub 'ong zer ba
rmis/ des bshol/ de'ang gling la ya mtshan can gyi gtam lnga zhes bya ba yod pa'i dang po ni/ mdo sde dkon mchog brtsegs pa gzigs pas/ sngon sangs rgyas log pa dad sel gyi
bstan pa la dge slong byang chub sems dpa' gnyis kyis bud med kyi 'khor la chos bstan pa la/ gzhan bsam gtan pa drug cus 'khrig pa'i chos kyis bskur pa btab pas dmyal
bar yun ring du sdug bsngal myong / shAkya thub pa'i drung du mir gyur nas las kyi sgrib pa sbyangs nas lnga brgya tha ma la las kyi sgrib pa rgyun chad par lung bstan pa'i
nang nas/ de dag gi 'dren par 'os pa byang chub sems dpa' brtson 'grus 'od bya ba yin par gzigs pa'o// gnyis pa ni/ rje sum pa gshegs nas gdan sa mdzad/ sngar gyi lung
bstan pa de nas lo lnga song ba na ngam shod kyi ri la sgom du 'byon bsam pa ltar byon/ yar klungs gdab kha bya bar sgom chen 'dra ba dang phrad/ 'phros byas pas dpal phag
mo gru pa'i snyan pa gsan pa tsam gyis ba spu g.yos/ spyan sngar da lta rang sleb na bsam pa byung nas tsham tshom med par byon/ 'gro ba'i mgon po chos khrir phebs pa
dang mjal/ sangs rgyas dngos yin/ shing dang bya 'khor 'di kun kyang sprul pa yin/ nga re 'tshengs bsam pa zhig las gzhan tha mal pa'i rtog pa ma 'gyus/ de'i rkyen gyis snang
ba thams cad bun long song nas sgrib byed zhi/ chos thams cad kyi ngang tshul dri ma med pa zhig mthong / sgro 'dogs thams cad cig car du chod de/ dpe yi ge gcig kyang
ma zhus te/ /rgyal ba'i gsung rab rab 'byams la/ /shes pa'i snang ba de nas thob/ /shes rab kyi spyan cig gnang ba 'dra/ /de nas lhan cig skyes sbyor gsan te lo bdun zla
ba bdun zhag bdun gyi mtshams kyi dam bca' phul te/ zhag lnga song ba'i nyin/ phag mo gru'i mkha' 'gro ma de gshegs pa gzigs nas der byon te thod pa bregs/ klad pa bldag
gin byon pa dang / stag lung thang pa thod pa 'breg bsam byon pa lam du 'dzom/ grogs po 'di gsol byas klad pa rtsid khem gang gdengs pas khong zhal yol byas zhal ras la
phog de'i dbang gis stag lung ba'i zhal ngo rim par sku 'bras gtsang

ba yin zer/ de nas 'gro mgon rin po che chos khri khar bur ston zhig gi gral dbu la phebs 'dug pa la/ gral gsham nas thod pa bzed nas bu ram gyi rtsig pa lta bu/ bla ma'i gsol
ras de la rgya phubs bkal ba lta bu zhig byung nas rten 'brel bzang / 'dir ma 'ongs pa na gtsug lag khang rgya phubs can zhig 'byung gsungs/ khyod lo bdun zla ba bdun
zhag bdun du mtshams bcad de sgom par dam bcas nas zhag lnga la grol ba ci yin gsungs pas/ rje yi zhal nas gnyug ma'i don/ /sgoms shig gsungs nas bsgoms lags pas/ /bsgom
bya sgom byed stor nas thal/ /sgom thun mtshams su bzung rgyu yang mi gda'o/ /sogs phul bas/ bla ma mnyes nas rgya gar chu bo ganggA phan chod la sa ra ha chen po rtogs
pa mtho/ de tshun la khyod rtogs pa mtho ba yin gsungs bsngags pa brjod/ rje spyir rnal 'byor pa/ sgos chung ma can la mi mnyes kyang gling ras pa la lhag par mnyes/ der
phag mo gru pas rten 'brel mdzad de jo mo slog de nas sna phu'i bkra shis dge gling gi phug par bzhugs/ phag mo grur chos brda' byung tsam nas de nas byon te chos gsan/ slar
der zlog pa yin zhes u rgyan par gsungs/ bza' btung ci bzhes kyi phud kyis bla ma mchod pas/ 'gro mgon gyi drung na dge ba'i bshes gnyen 'ga' dang bcas te ja gsol ba'i
zhal dkar du tshod ma zhig ling byung / ci yin zhus pas/ gling ras lkugs pa des tshod ma'i phud phul bar 'dug gsung dgyes/ gsum pa ni/ 'gro mgon gshegs nas 'gro don mdzad/
nor byung tshad cha lang chen po zhig la bcal te nam mkha' la 'khrol gyin byon te phag mo grur phul/ tshur log nas bsam yas su zhag sa mdzad pa'i tho rangs/ bud med sngon
mo zhig gis bka' 'gyur ro cog gi glegs bam yin mno ba zhig ljags steng du bzhag byung ba khong du song ba rmis/ de nas bka' 'gyur thams cad thugs la chug bden rdzun
lta ba la tshal du byon nas mnan shar mdzad pas phar zhu dag thub pa byung / /bzhi pa ni/ de nas mdo rgyud mthong tshad la don mi mkhyen pa med nas 'grel pa brtsam dgongs
te/ bde dgyes mtshan brjod la sogs pa la 'grel pa brtsams pas sna phu'i mdo 'phrang po zho rar klog pa'i sde yod pa dag gis skur pa btab/ de gsan nas der byon te gang mi
'thad pa 'dug ces rtsod pas sus kyang lan 'debs ma nus/ de'i tshe thugs khengs pa skyes nas glegs

shing gcig sku mdun gcig sku rgyab/ de glegs thag gis bsdams te nam mkha' la phar bzhud tshur bzhud mdzad de/ nga dam chos kyi po ti zhig tu mi 'dug gam sogs kyi mgur bzhengs
pas/ thub pa'i dbang pos/ gling ras pa de lta bu'i khengs pa ma byed/ nga'ang mthar 'di ltar gyur gsungs mya ngan las 'da' ba'i tshul bstan nas zhi bar gyur/ thams cad
kyis gus pas btud/ grub thob chen po zhes snyan grags kyi gdugs dkar po srid pa'i khongs thams cad gang bar gyur to/ /de nas gnyal lor dbus gtsang kun tu dad pa can spyan
'dren pa rnams kyi ngo bzhin byon/ zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi sgo rnam par phye bar mdzad/ lo ro tshe spong du lo ro zhig po gdan sar bkod/ rje rang dbus gtsang
du gtso bor bzhugs/ skabs shig sna phur dbang bskur zhu ba'i mi 'ga' yod pa zhig la dbang g.yog la zhig po de yod na dgongs pa zhig byung ba/ kho lo ro dol gyi lha rtser
yod pas shes nas 'phur te dbang bskur gyi grabs mdzad sar slebs/ khyod kyis ji ltar 'ongs gsungs/ ri mtho ba rnams la reg la khyad byas te 'phur nas 'ongs zhu'o/ /lnga pa
ni bkra shis dge gling gi phug na bzhugs dus mkha' 'gro ma zhig byung nas/ gling ras pa der ma sdod zer/ phyir byon ma thag brag phug de rdib/ de nas 'jag spyil mdzad de
sgang der bzhugs pa'i skabs/ mkha' 'gro ma lnga rang rtags kyi dbu rgyan re khyer nas grub thob chen po'i dbu la bskyon/ rdo rje 'chang chen po'i rgyal tshab tu mnga' gsol
nas mi snang bar gyur to/ /de ltar drug cu rtsa gcig gi bar du bzhugs nas dbyar zla ra ba'i nyer brgyad la gshegs/ gdung rten la sogs pa legs par bsgrubs so// // ! de'i
slob ma'i gtso bo ni/ chos kyi rje yin te/ de 'khrungs pa'i yul myang stod khu le'i cha/ yab rgya zur so tshab pe dang / yum mar bza' dar skyid/ sras bdun byung ba'i chung
shos te pha ma 'brog pa yin la/ bskyas dang thug bying song yum gcig pur lus pa la gan logs zhes bya ba'i lhas su grod pa sgor mo zhig btsas pas/ yum dngangs te bor
nas 'ongs pa jo jos rtsad bcad pas lo rgyus ji lta ba bshad/ de nyid du jo jos brgyugs phyin pas sbra shul na bya rgod gcig gis grod pa de sos nas rtol/ khye'u zhig 'dug
khong byung ba dang bya rgod de 'phur song / de slob dpon lwa ba pa yin zhes grags so/ /de nas gzhon nu'i

dus su padma sambha wa'i lung bstan/ sa ral zhes pa'i lung gsum mdor/ /nor bu 'dzin pa'i sprul pa 'byung / /pha bong sho 'dra'i kha nas chos 'chad rtsom zhes pa ltar/ der byis
pa rnams khrid pha bong de khrir byas nas chos 'chad pa'i tshul gyis rtse/ nangs shig de'i 'khris kyi rdo la zhabs kyi padmo gnyis shin tu gsal bar bkod/ gcen chen po
skal ldan bya bas dgung lo bcu gnyis pa la khu lung du slob dpon mkhar lung pa can khrid lo brgyad bsten te tshad ma'i grwa sa yin pas/ der sbyangs pa mthar phyin/ grwa
bskor yang mdzad/ slob dpon mnyes nas mtshan shes rab bdud rtsi'i 'khor lor gsol/ gzhan slob dpon rta thang pa la mngon pa/ lhan gyi so dar ma sengge la sgyu 'phrul mdo rgyud
sogs sbyangs/ gzhan yang bla ma 'ga' re bsten/ dgung lo nyer gsum pa la grub thob gling ra lung du phebs pa dang mjal/ gsung gleng tsam mdzad/ de nas dbus su byon/ sna
phur mjal nas dbang rgyud gdam ngag zhus/ zhag bdun nas ras thub/ yang yul du skor cig brgyags len du byon/ phyir sna phur log bla ma 'bul bas mnyes par byas te dgun 'dag
sbyar mdzad de bsgoms pas/ rlung phyi nang bsre nus pa dang / rtsig pa la thogs pa med pa dang / ting nge 'dzin gsal stong nam mkha' dwangs pa lta bu la 'byams nas bsgom
bya sgom byed stor 'gro bar 'dug nas/ bla ma la'ang 'di las med dam snyam mtshams grol ba'i dus zhus pas/ ngo mtshar che rje btsun mi la'ang de ltar byung 'dug gsung
/ bsgom bya sgom byed mi gda' na zhus pas/ bu de kun nyams yin/ rtogs pa bsha' ma zhig da ste lo lnga na 'byung gsungs/ spyir sna phur lo bzhi bzhugs/ gdam ngag thams cad
tshar/ lung bstan nas mkhar chur 'gro ba'i dgongs pa zhus pas/ ro snyoms gter na yod tshul/ de 'don pa khyod yin te da lo res sdod gsungs/ nan gyi zhus pas khrol te rngog
rdo rje sengge la dgyes gdan yA gsum gsan pa la zla ba brgyad tsam thogs/ de'i ring la bla ma mya ngan las 'das nas mi 'dug 'dad dang gdung khang bzheng pa la lo gcig 'gor/
de nas lho brag mkhar chur byon/ lo gsum bzhugs/ dpon slob bdun yod/ 'tsho ba shin tu bkres la kha lhags kyis mnar bas sku'i mdangs shor/ yul mi rnams kyis 'dre mo spun
bdun zhes btags/ der phyag phyi ba rnams kyis rkyen ma theg par log jo kun dga' sgra zer

kho stod pa zhig gis zla re la phye bre do tsam re bskyal/ brgyags thes de kha la mdzad de lcags phur can du 'dag sbyar mdzad nas thugs dam la rtse gcig tu bzhugs pas/ khams
'dus pa zhig langs/ de je thu je thur song lo gsum du ma drag lo gsum pa'i nang du chos skyong mgon pos pha ri'i logs nas sgyogs rgyag lha mo nag mos lha 'dre'i dmag g.yos/
mi reng dmar pos mda' 'phen/ gzhan snang srid kyi lha ma srin sde brgyad tshogs te/ dmag gis bskor nas rgyob cig sod cig zer/ skabs re na ri shing nags tshal thabs cad
bgad/ skabs re na 'gul khyom ldeg brag ri de nyil li li zhig 'gro/ res 'ga' thams cad mgo brnyan can du song nas mtshon cha 'phen pa sogs byung ste bar chad lam du khyer
ba'i go cha sra bas ri btsugs pa bzhin du bzhugs pa'i mthar/ grub thob chen po dran pa'i gdung shugs drag po byung nas gsol ba btab pas mdun du dngos su byon nas byin
gyis brlabs so snyam pa zhig la phyag rgya chen po'i rtogs pa nam mkha' la mdung bskor ba bzhin du song / bar chad de thams cad dngos grub kyi sna 'dren/ bdud rigs de thams
cad dam la thogs nas chos skyong du song bas/ bar chad che dus der chos skyong yang dgra ru langs/ da lta bdud kyang dpal du shar gsung / ro snyoms kyi gter phyung / de
tshe dgung lo so gcig pa'o/ /chos 'di phyis ha bo gangs su rlung jo yes sogs bdun la rten 'brel bsgrigs te bshad pa yin/ de nas dbus gtsang gnyis su byon/ kha rag shar
gyi ri la bzhugs/ khyung btsun ma bka' 'bangs su bcug der mkha' 'gro ma sengge'i gdong pa can yong nas srod la tsa ri trar 'gro bar lan gsum bskul/ mkha' 'gro'i lung bstan
nam bdud kyi bar chad gang yin mi shes dgongs ji snyam ma mdzad/ nam seng khar cung zad mnal du song / sad pa dang kha rag gi ri la nyi ma shar 'dug de'i nyi zer la grub
thob chen po gzi brjid shin tu che ba zhig byon nas/ bu rgya ras ma 'dug sgom du song sogs gsungs te mi snang bar gyur/ der lo ro skal ldan sogs bzhi khrid 'bri gung du
byon/ de nas khong rnams yul la slog rlung thun gcig bzung ste byon pas bod kha gsum du gnyos mgar chos gsum gnas sgo 'byed par 'gro ba dang 'dzom/ khong rnams na re khyod
su yin par gar 'gro zer/ nga gling ras gsus po che'i bu rgya ras mig po che yin/ gnas

tsa ri la sgom du 'gro gsungs nas bsdebs te zhing skyong gis bsus nas ri pa la la byon/ yul stod sbal ba g.yu mtshor sbal pa g.yag shad tsam gyis lam bgags pas/ grogs gzhan
rnams thabs ci drag la gya/ chos rje de'i steng du mchongs te brdzis/ de rdor gyur pa la zhabs kyi padmo 'dam la bkod pa lta bur a rdzog go rdzog byung / de nas cig car
phur byon/ zhing skyong gi dbang mo rdo rje g.yu sgron dam la btags/ phyogs skyong las kyi gshin rjes dge bsnyen blangs/ slar g.yu mtshor byon pa sha skam du khong rnams
dang 'grig de ring gi tshogs 'khor khyed gshoms zer/ rung byas zhing skyong gi ru ba la bslangs nas zas sna tshang sngar ming tsam yang ma thos pa mang po byung ste tshogs
btang lhag ma spungs pas dkar rdog thang du grags/ de nas zhib mo khrag khrig tu phebs dus nyi ma'i dgung la sa rub skar ma khrag khrig byung nas grogs rnams kyi de res
ma bgrod/ chos pa'i tshad rdo bor sa 'dug gsungs te byon pas lha mo re ma ti mjal/ de nas pho brang gi phyogs bzhi'i khri bzhi nas mkha' 'gro ma rnams la chos bshad khyad
par pho brang chen por sprul pa'i lha zhal gzigs/ bcom ldan 'das rdo rje phag mos bstan pa bya rgod kyi nyin lam bco brgyad khyab pa dang / bcom ldan 'das 'khor lo sdom
pas bskal pa bzang po 'di la mos par sangs rgya bar lung bstan/ de nas sindhu ra'i rgya mtshor chu sbur gyi tshul du rdol pa'i mkha' 'gro mas rang gi skra las btags pa'i
mig ra phul/ mkha' 'gro ma gzhan rnams kyis rdo yur ba drangs sgrub phug ngo mtshar ba'ang phul/ de nas yul stod du log sdong po kha TsAM gyi drung du zla ba gsum skyil
krung ma bshig par bzhugs/ sangs rgyas rabs bdun 'jal te rten 'brel gyi gdam ngag gsan/ de nas yar log pa'i lam du rab byung gcig dang rtogs ldan gcig bud med gcig ste bzhi
mnyam du byung / rab byung de gzhan du song / der khong gsum las med nas/ bud med de 'chal gtam gu yangs su smra bas rten gyis lan dgongs bsnyen par rdzogs pa'i thugs
'dod cher yod pa'i gsal btab/ byang 'bri gung du byon/ skyob pa sku mtshams yod pas mjal kha ma byung / phyir log skyob pas dgongs nas zhwa bskur pa lam du 'phrod/ bla ma
zhang gi rtsar byon/ bla ma zhang gis dgongs nas bsu ba rgyas pa mdzad/ de phan rten ras par yod pas dbu skra bsil/

zhang gis mkhan po mdzad/ rtsi 'dul 'dzin gyis slob dpon mdzad tshigs rdzogs bsgrubs/ mtshan ye shes rdo rjer gsol/ de'i tshe bla ma zhang gis rgod ma dkar mo la zhon te chibs
rgyugs byas/ rgya gar gyi nA ro paN chen gyi skra gcod mkhan nga min pa su yod gsungs/ de dus 'bri gung pas gnang ba'i zhwa de gyon nas bzhugs/ zhang log phebs pa'i dus/
zhwa rgod po nam 'phangs spyod pa 'dra ba 'dis rgyal khams 'gengs bsam pa yin te/ rgad po g.yas chung byad pa'i bar la rta rmig 'dra ba bzhes grub 'dug pas da 'dis rgyal
khams gang bar 'gyur gsungs/ slob dpon la 'dul ba gsan/ mkhan po la tshal lugs kyi bskyed rdzogs/ khyad par chos skyong gi skor legs par gsan/ bla ma zhang la brten nas
snying rje'i klong rdol/ khong gis lung bstan klong rdol gyi dgon pa btab/ dbu se mjal gdams pa gsan/ khong gi lung bstan 'brug btab/ chos rje dpon slob rtse bo lar phebs
dus da lta'i gnas yod sar 'brug ma mad dgu babs nas 'dug nam mkhar song / phebs dus 'brug sgra drag po thengs 'gar grags pas dgon pa'i ming 'brug tu btags/ de nas dgon
pa btab/ lo de nyid la spyil bu stong du longs/ de nas kyang de'i ri sul thams cad du dar bas/ tshogs pa la zhag dus byas/ brdar sgang mthon por dar slong ba yin zhes grags/
slob ma khri tsho lnga tsam tshogs zer/ de thams cad la yang dag pa'i gdam ngag byin nas rab 'bring gsum du phye nas 'khor 'gyed dang po btang / rab rnams ni 'ja' lus
brnyes pas steng lha/ 'og klu dang lha min/ bar mi'i 'jig rten gzhan du/ 'bring rnams u rgyan/ shambha la/ singga la/ gser gling zangs gling sogs/ mtha' ma dza lendha
ra nas/ rgya nag po tshun gyi ri bo'i khrod du brdzangs pas thams cad gang bar byas/ 'khor 'gyed gnyis pa la de las kyang gtos mi chung ba bkye/ gsum pa chos rje mya ngan
las 'das nas zhal chems bzhin phyogs phyogs su byon pa de la tha snyad byas pa yin/ rgyu mtshan des dpal 'brug pa'i bstan pas bya rgod kyi nyin lam bco brgyad khyab ces
dang / mi phyed 'brug pa/ 'brug phyed sprang po/ sprang phyed grub thob tu kun la rlung ltar grags so/ /de ltar dgung lo so bzhi nas nga gcig gi bar du 'phrin las

bskyangs/ gling gis lung bstan ra lung btab/ dgung lo lnga bcu rtsa gcig pa la 'brug tu gshegs/ spur zhugs la sbyangs pa'i dus/ thugs ljags spyan gsum/ dbu thod la rigs gsum
mgon po/ sku tshigs pa nyi shu rtsa gcig la spyan ras gzigs nyi shu rtsa gcig gzhan ring bsrel yang mang du byon/ 'brug tu lha mo che bzhengs de'i nang du ljags bzhugs
pas chos brgyud thams cad la 'brug pa zer ba 'di byung ba yin no// de la slob ma dang por che ba spa rkyang gnyis/ bar du che ba rgya 'bras gnyis/ mtha' mar che ba lo rgod
gnyis/ gzhan ras pa gsum/ rnal 'byor gsum/ zhig po gsum sogs dbu che gdugs thog pa nyis stong brgyad brgya byung ba'i spa ri ba/ bla ma zhang gi mchod gshoms pa/ mtshan
ye shes mgon po zer/ zhang gi chos rje la chos skyong gi dbang gnang ba'i dus/ 'di nga'i zla la byung na dgongs/ khong yang bla ma 'di'i phyag phyi la 'gro rgyu byung na
bsam pa zhang gis dgongs nas/ ye shes mgon po rang rgya ras pa'i phyi la rgyug gsung gnang ba sbyin pas chos skyong yang rgya ras pa'i phyi la 'brangs so zer grags so/ /sku
yon che bas mkhyen pa'i mnga' bdag ces thogs/ tsa ris ras chen sogs kyis kyang chung ngu'i gsan sbyong der mdzad/ spa ri byang chub gling dgon btab/ chu bo ri la kha
shar sogs mang du mched/ khong nas brgyud pa la bu rgan du grags/ rkyang mo kha pa bde ba can du sbyangs pa'i ston pa chen po zhig dang por chos rje la rgol 'dod kyis drung
du 'ongs/ zhal mjal ba'i mod la rtogs pa shar/ rkyang mo kha btab/ brgya yags ba grwa pa yin/ chos rje la dbul ba mdzad pa'i dus slob ma gtos che ba yod pas btsun chung
na mnyam brgya phul/ de la chos rjes yags so gsungs pas brgya yags par thogs/ der brgya yags/ 'brog dga' ldan la sogs btab/ 'bras mo pa ni nyid ro pa/ mtshan sangs rgyas
'bum/ chos rje'i gsung la 'dris pa/ nyams bzhes dge sbyor bdun pa la rtsal du bton/ slob ma mkhon sgom la sogs pa mang ngo / /de bzhi nas brgyud pa la bu chen brgyud zer/
ras pa gsum/ g.yag ras/ li ras/ 'gran ras/ g.yag ras kyi slob ma la stod pa bde mchog sangs rgyas/ de'i slob ma sprul sku shes yes/ de'i slob ma rdza ri ras pa/ de'i slob
ma rdza sgo ba shes rab dpal/ de

la skyes mchog smon lam dpal ba dang / 'jam dbyangs pa sogs mang zhig byung / skyes mchog pa'i slob ma la rdza sna pa/ rgyal dbang rjes lung mang bar mtshan gsol ba de sogs
'brog phyogs na shin tu dar/ sgrub skor gyi bka' lung la'ang phan shin tu thogs/ li ras la sgro ston sogs slob ma legs par byung / rnal 'byor gsum ni/ jo yes/ dga' yes/
bde yes gsum/ jo yes chos rje'i bka'i sdud pa po yin pas gdam ngag che/ khong la skyi ston dbyar ras sogs slob ma mang / grar dga' ldan btab/ de dag la sogs pa nyis stong
brgyad brgya'i slob rgyun la bu chung brgyud/ gnyis ka bsdoms pa la bar 'brug ces grags so// // ! lo ras ni 'khrungs sa gzhung gi grags chen/ gdung lo/ yab rnal 'byor dang
/ yum me bza' skyid la sras med nas/ 'brug tu chos rje dang / lha sar jo bo thugs rje chen po la mchod pa rgya chen po byas pas byung ba yin/ mtshan lo bde ba skyong /
chos kyi bag chags bzang bas lo gsum bzhi nas bri klog mkhyen/ sku'i cho bzang bas lo lnga dang drug gnyis la chos la 'bros par brtsams/ yab yum gyi mtha' bzhi shag dar
gyi bu mo jo mor bsus/ bdun pa la bros nas 'brug tu slebs/ der rjes spal ti la gtad nas skyor mo lung du skra bcad/ mtshan grags pa dbang phyug tu gsol/ yul nas bdas mi byung
/ skor cig byon pa na jo mo dang lhan cig rkang pa lcags su bcug kyang ma chags par slar chos rje'i sku drung du byon/ gdam ngag rnams legs par gsan/ de nas yab sras
zhal dan nas chos rje dpon slob gtos che ba gzhung du spyan drangs/ mi rnams kyis 'tshengs pa gsum chos rje dpon slob 'bul bas 'tshengs pa/ mtha' bzhi shag dar nor gyis
'tshengs pa/ khong rang chos mdzad rgyu byung bas 'tshengs pa zer ro/ /de nas chos rjes thugs la btags/ gdam ngag thams cad sba sri med par gnang / dgung lo bcu gsum lon
pa'i tshe kha rag tu byon/ der jo gdan kun rgyal zer ba lo mnyam zhig kyang phyag phyir 'byor/ khong bsod snyoms la song ba'i shul du kha ba chen po bab de la kho ma thar/
bla ma la gsol zas med snyam khos snying rus bskyed 'ongs nas phug pa'i phyi/ chos rjes nang nas brkos pas 'phrod tsam byung / der bsnyun gzhi dam po zhig byung ba sdig
sgrib

dag pa'i rtags bzang / der lo gsum bzhugs/ chos rje gshegs nas gnam mtsho phyug mo'i do la sgom bzhed/ de dus mtsho rul dar ma chags pa la nya pa gzhon nu zhig gis dang blangs
byas/ de'i pho bo na re/ khyod las nga drag ste 'ong zer/ rdzings chung du de btang pas mtsho'i dkyil du slebs pa na rlung dmar 'khrugs/ de'i dbang gis rba klong longs
nas/ nya pa na re ngas ma phyin pa drag byas te khyod ma nyan/ da 'chi ba min pa'i thabs med/ khyod rang thugs dam byed rgyu yod na mdzod zer kho mgo gos kyis gtums nas
'jums nyal song / der chos sku kun bzang ma zhes grags pa'i gsol 'debs de mdzad/ mos gus kyi gdung bas chos rje mngon sum du ko rdzings kyi kha na phebs/ bu 'jigs pa med
do gsung ngo snyam pa zhig la lhags pa 'jam nyal/ do'i rtsa na phebs 'dug pas nya pa'ang yid ches/ der phye khur gcig la bgo bsha' mdzad de lo gnyis kyi gsol brgyags mdzad
rtsis/ lo gcig song ba na dar chags/ phyi do'i sgom chen pa rnams kyis nan gyis spyan drangs do phyir byon/ slar nang du 'dab rtsis sgom chen gzhan 'ga' song zer nas ma
byon par zhwa mo do la byon/ der nye gnas dge 'dun dar zhag shas bsdad nas 'gro rtsis la/ dar btsan thabs su zhig nas nang du lus/ der chas mang bar yod pa kho la gtad
pas sri ma shes par 'dzad/ de dus chos rjes dar yong ltos gsungs/ gzhan mi snang snam bu brkyang ba 'dra zhig mthong / de la chos rjes sna drangs byon/ pha gi'i ru gseb tu
phebs pa'i tshe/ khyed gang nas 'ongs zer/ nged zhwa mo do nas 'ongs byas pas mtsho rul nas sus bgrod rdzun yin zer/ dgong mo ri la phyugs 'tshor 'gro ba rnams log nas/
khong rnams na re/ de ring ru gseb tu btsun pa gnyis ma byung ngam/ de ring las ltad mo che ba 'ong ma myong zer/ ci yin/ zhwa mo do nas khong gnyis chu la ma bying bar
'byon pa mthong zer bas kun dad/ de nas jo mo gangs sogs su rgyun ring bar bzhugs/ u ri btab/ 'phrin las dang po der bskyangs/ gdam ngag gi gtso bo thub lnga la mdzad/ de
nas ring zhig nas tshogs pa dmangs ri la bkye/ brgya lhag tsam shul 'dzin pa la bzhag dpon slob stong lhag tsam gyis gtsang du byon nas rdzong sgo gangs la

bzhugs/ de dang 'go yul du dgon pa mang po btab/ de nas dkar po chos lung btab ste tshogs che tsa na khri tsam/ rgyun du nyis stong lhag pa 'dus te/ 'phrin las bar ba der bskyangs/
brgyad brgya tsam ri la bkye/ chos lung du 'dag sbyar la lnga brgya tsam bcug de lhag stong lhag pa zhig phyag phyir khrid de lho brag mon sogs su byon/ lha khang
du gdan chags/ der gtsug lag khang gi so bran sogs mdzad de/ dpal sengge rir dben pa bsten nas bzhugs pa'i mthar dge slong bslab gtsang stong dang lnga brgya la dpal 'khor
lo sdom pa'i dbang bskur/ de nas gang 'dod pa'i gdam ngag gnang 'phrin las mtha' ma bskyangs te dgung lo drug cu rtsa bzhi pa la zhi bar gshegs so/ /chos rje 'dis dgung
lo bcu bdun pa la chos mdzad zer ba sogs rnam thar chen por lhad shor ba yin zer bas/ 'di ltar rnam thar rnying pa rang du byung bas 'thad do// de la slob ma 'jam dbyangs
mgon po la sogs pa'i mkhas pa rnam gsum/ tsa ri ras chen sogs ras pa rnam gsum/ a lo shAkya gsum ste rnal 'byor rnam gsum sogs mtha' yas pa'i 'jam dbyangs mgon pos myang
smad ku ring 'phrin las bskyangs/ gcod yul zab don thugs snying dang thabs lam rdo rje tshig 'byed kyang 'dis mdzad/ gsang mtshan don yod rdo rje zer ba yin/ phyis rgya
nag ri bo rtse lnga la sku ma spangs par byon/ /sras kyi gtso bo tsa ri ras chen yin/ de 'khrungs sa gzhung dge rong stod sde'i grong smad/ yab rgya smyon pa 'bum zhes
kha drag pa zhig dang / yum gcung bza' sgom ma zhes bya ba lo ras kyi lcam mo gnyis kyi sras su 'khrungs/ nor longs spyod bsam gyis mi khyab pa yod pa la yab snga mor 'das
pa'i dge ba la btang / dgung lo dgu pa la chos rje lo ras la go mi'i dge bsnyen mdzad/ chos rje se mo do la gshegs dus/ bla ma spa ri ba'i sar sdod dge tshul bsgrubs/
slob gnyer gyis gsungs/ bcu gsum pa'i tshe chos rje jo mo gangs la byon pa thos nas phyag phyir byon nye gnas mdzad/ gdam ngag tshang bar gnang / skyor mo lung du byon nas
bsnyen rdzogs bsgrubs/ chos rje gshegs rjes gdan sa mdzad dgos zhus kyang ma gnang ste/ spyan snga ston pa chos lung gi gdan sa la brdzangs/ bla ma bde gshegs lha khang
du bkod/ dgung lo zhe drug pa la gnas mchog dpal gyi tsa rir byon lo

gsum bzhugs/ thams cad kyi mig ltos byas mdzad/ de nas 'khor te ti se la skor cig byon/ de dus sa 'bri'i sa sna na bzhugs pa kun gyis zhabs tog phul phyin bsgrubs/ de nas 'khor
te gdan sa mdzad nas 'phrin las rgya cher bskyangs pa'i slob ma rtogs ldan mgon po ye shes/ grub thob gser sgo ba/ khyi sgom chen po la sogs pa mkhas pa dang grub pa
bsam gyis mi khyab/ de ltar khu dbon gnyis las brgyud pa smad 'brug ces bya/ gtos sa'i dreg pa tsam kun la grags/ phyis rong spang chen du 'khrungs pa'i gtsang chen chos
kyi dbang phyug gis yom chos sdings sogs dwags kong lho rgyud sogs su dgon gnas du ma btab/ rgyal dbang rje la sbyor gtod zhus kyang de nyid ring por ma lon par gshegs nas/
sbrum pa la bde gzar gyis khag pa'i skabs su sbrum pas sprul sku zhwa dmar pa la sbyor gtod byas te chos brgyud de khar 'dug pa'i lugs so/ /rgod tshang pa ni 'khrungs
sa lho la yag gi dol bu chung gi khrar/ yab chu chal mon grags/ yum zug mo dpal rgyan gnyis kyi sras su 'khrungs/ mtshan mgon po rdo rje/ sku phra mo'i dus bro pa'i lad
mo mdzad pas pag shi don grub sengger grags/ der slob dpon zhang la 'grel chung / stong la dbu ma/ yu ba pa la spyod 'jug wa zha la lam rim gsan pas tshar res legs par mkhyen/
de'i tshe gtsang nas glu mkhan bzhi byung / de rnams kyis/ dgon pa ra lung gi chos rje rgya ras la/ /tshe 'di phyi gnyis kyi bde legs yod/ /dam pa'i lha chos shig byed
na de ru gshegs/ /snying nas rang chos shig byed na de ru gshegs/ /zer thos pa'i mod la dad pa bcos min zhig skyes nas yab la zhus te byon/ chos rje mjal phyag rgya chen
po'i sgom khyer thun gcig ma zhig gnang / bsgoms pas zhag bco brgyad la rtogs pa thun mong ma yin pa shar/ 'bri gung sogs bskor slar 'brug tu phebs/ chos rje sku bsnyung
ba'i sku rim thun pa'i khrod du yod pas/ chos rje'i gsung nas thun pa ma gi'i gseb na bstan pa 'dzin pa'i skyes bu zhig yod pa yin gsungs/ gdam ngag chos rje dbon la
bcad pas/ bla ma chos rje ras pa yin/ /drin can sangs rgyas dbon ras yin/ /gsungs/ de nas der bsnyen par rdzogs te/ lho brag mkhar chur sgrub pa lo gsum snyon kha dam la
btags/ pho ma lha khab tu bla ma

sgrub pa lo gsum mdzad pa'i skabs shig chos rje ras pa de sa bcu pa'i byang chub sems dpa' yin snyam pa byung / de ma thag sems sangs rgyas su ngo sprod pa'i bla ma sa bcu
par mthong ba khyod 'dra ba'i log lta can zhes rang la smad/ de nas bla ma la sangs rgyas kyi 'du shes 'bral ma myong / der shig nad thu ba dang 'gro yin 'gro yin la gnyid
du 'gro/ snang ba sbrul gyis ltem gang ba byung bas sa nad kyi dogs pa byung / de nas stod dza landha ra'i bar du bskor/ der mkha' 'gro mas dngos su byin gyis brlabs/ de
nas log tsa ri la byon/ der gnas nang gi sgom chen rnams kyi chas 'dren pa'i khur pa mdzad sku rgyab la sgal ba byung / rnag khrag zhabs rting du nar re 'dzag pa/ de dus
sku lus nang nas nang khrol thams cad thon pa zhig rmis/ 'di mi ldog gam byas pas mi dkar po zhig nas brtson 'grus chung na ldog zer/ de ltar sgrib pa dag pho brang du
sprul pa'i lha zhal nam 'dod gzigs/ der lo bzhugs mdzad/ skus nad kyi dogs pa der grol/ de nas yar byon/ sangs rgyas dbon gyis gsung nas/ da nga'i khrid gnyer la sdod gsung
/ stod du 'gro bar zhus pas/ 'o na de ltar gyis gsung / de nas shrI la byon bsgrub pa mdzad/ lhag par rgod tshang du bzhugs nas mi nga dang gcig bya khyod dang gnyis/
brag 'di dang gsum ming gcig tu ma song tshun mi sgrub ri zhes dam bcas te bsgrubs pas rgod tshang pa zhes mtshan thogs/ der zhig po byang dpal slebs/ sngar brag phug dog
par yod pa la/ snang ba 'di tsho zang nge dang thal le rang du 'dug pa gsung gin gcod cing gshags pas yangs por song / zhig pos 'dir tshang mal bca' sa sogs dgos pa zhus
pas slar cung zad cig brtsigs so/ /de nas grub thob kyi grags pa thon te/ bar 'brog rdor gling / steng 'gro/ gnya' nang bde chen stengs sogs su gtso bo sgrub pa/ seng bar
la chos bshad/ de'ang khrid chen brgyad du mdzad/ skal ba dang ldan pa rnams rjes su bzung ba yin no/ /chos rje 'di'i sku 'khor na sgom ma bzhugs pa rnams ni tha mal pa
skad yin par brdzus pa ma gtogs mkha' 'gro ma 'ba' zhig ste/ nga'i sgom ma sle thul can 'di rnams nyin mo nga la chos nyan/ nub mo nA ro pa'i phyi rten bkra shis sgo mang

la skor ba bskor te u rgyan du tshogs kyi 'khor lo la 'gro ba yin gsungs/ nA ro pa'i phyi rten gsungs pa de ra lung gi mchod rten yin/ de bzhin bden pa grub thob u rgyan pas
chos rje'i khrid gnyer mdzad pa na sgom ma dang grub chen bsres nas chos nyan par dbyes phye/ btsun pa stod/ btsun ma khyams smad du 'jog 'ga' zhig u tshugs kyis gong du
'tshangs pa brdungs pas/ u rgyan du bud med de dag cha lugs de kho na bzhin byung nas rdo char phab dbu chag slar rlung gis gsos pa yin no/ /dgung lo bdun cu la gshegs
so/ /de la slob ma rtogs pa rang dang mnyam pa yang dgon pa/ zhe bcad rang dang mnyam pa spyil dkar ba/ mos gus rang dang mnyam pa ne rings pa bzhi/ gzhan phu ri ba/ ma bdun
pa sogs bsam gyi mi khyab pa zhig byon pa'i/ yang dgon pa ni la stod lho lha gdong du/ sngags brgyud/ yab jo bsam/ yum chos mthong gi sras su 'khrungs/ gdung rus stong
/ phul dmar ba/ ko brag pa sa paN/ rje spyan snga ba/ drod chung ba sogs bsten/ khyad par rgod tshang pa sku drin che shos su 'dzin pas rjes 'jug rnams de'i lugs 'dzin/
mkhas pa dang grub par bod kyi mi gcig la kun mthun grub bo/ /de'i slob ma spyan snga rin ldan ding rir 'khrungs/ lha gdong na sprul pa'i sku bzhugs zhes gsan nas mos gus
skyes/ dgung lo bcu gcig pa zhig gis phyag phyir byon/ de nas ma gshegs par spyan sngar bzhugs pas spyan snga zhes grags so/ /de'i slob ma zur phug pa rin chen dpal bzang
/ de'i slob ma chos rje 'ba' ra ba ste/ shangs kyi chab lung par dpon 'bum zhes pa'i sras su 'khrungs/ gzhon nu nas chos rje bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan pa'i
gsol bya ba mdzad/ gsan pa'ang legs par mdzad/ de nas nges 'byung drag po 'khrungs nas chos la bros zur phug pa las dkar brgyud kyi gdam ngag gsan te bsgoms pas rtogs pa
mchog tu gyur/ 'ba' ra brag tu don grub sdings btab/ de las slob brgyud kyis bod kun bkang / yang slob mon rtse ba zhes pa las mched nas 'brog dbus kong po sogs su dar/ dbus
smyon kun dga' bzang po las kyang

mang du mched/ gdan sa ni dbon brgyud kyis bzung ste/ de dag las kyang grub pa'i skyes bu tshad med pa byung ste stod 'brug gi rkang 'ba' ra ba la thug go /u rgyan pa ni zur
tsho'i go lung du yab jo phan/ rus rgyud mched bzhi byung ba'i bgres shos go lung pa zhang mdo sde dpal/ de 'og gzhon nu dpal/ de 'og mi chos pa/ chung shos sengge dpal
yin/ des lo bdun nas rgod tshang pa bhu Tar byon pa la dge bsnyen blangs/ de nas bcu drug gi bar du ma phur/ bde dgyes/ phyag rdor/ yo ga rgyud phyag len dang bcas pa la
bslabs/ bcu drug pa la bo dong er byon/ bo dong rin rtse la mngon pa gong 'og tshad ma rnam nges/ shes rab 'grel chung bslabs te 'chad rtsod rtsom gsum la 'gran zla med
par grags/ jo jo mdo sde dpal la 'grel chung gsan/ 'dul ba'i skor gzigs pas bag chags mthun par 'dug khyad par las brgya rtsa gcig pa gzigs pa tsam gyis thugs la chud/ dgung
lo nyi shu pa la bo dong rin rtses mkhan po/ zhang bsam gling pas slob dpon/ slob dpon bsod 'od pas gsang ston mdzad nas tshigs rdzogs bsgrubs/ mtshan rin chen dpal du
gsol/ de nas lo bcu gnyis su stan gcig pa'i b.ratal zhugs gzung sha'ang ma gsol/ bo dong rin rtse la dus 'khor 'bro lugs/ go lung pa mdo sde dpal la chag lugs legs par
sbyangs/ khong gis dus 'khor ba sangs rgyas rdo rje la rtsa mi lugs nyon gsungs/ rong la brdzangs/ zla ba bcu gcig tu phran dang bcas pa gsan/ der khong chos bcag nas ser
chags la byon pas cung zad ma gus/ lhag par rgyud 'di la rdzogs pa'i rim pa 'di min pa zhig 'ong thang snyam pa dang / dka' gnad mang po sus kyang dogs pa ma chod par yod
pas shambha la rang du 'gro dgongs/ de la chos rje rgod tshang pa'i grwa pa rnams rkang sho rgod 'dug pas zla bo 'ong / sngar skor cig shog gsung ba yod snyam chos rje
snye nam bde chen steng du bzhugs pa mjal/ rgod tshang pas sang gi nyi ma la las can gyi slob ma zhig 'ong ba yin gsungs/ mjal nas slob dpon jo btsun zhes dgyes dgyes mdzad/
der dpon slob 'phros la lo rgyus zhus pas/ ji 'dra ji 'dra la ma bde gsungs/ 'di lta bu la ma

bde zhus pas/ de 'di dang 'di min nam gsungs pas ma bde ba phal cher khrol/ sman min 'ga' zhig phyis shes par 'gyur ro gsungs/ der 'di lta bu'i dus kyi 'khor lo mkhas par mkhyen
pa su la gsan zhus pas/ ngas gzhan la ma zhus shrI rir bsdad dus bud med dmar mo zhig gis po ti byin/ de mid pa'i snang ba byung nas chos gang la'ang mi shes pa ma
byung ba yin gsungs/ 'o na bdag la dus kyi 'khor lo'i dbang gnang dgos zhus pas/ slob dpon jo btsun rang gsol ba thob cig gsungs/ der gsol ba btab pas tho rangs rmi lam du
dus 'khor ba sangs rgyas rdo rje yin no snyam pa zhig gis dkyil 'khor gyi las rim rgyas pa byas te dbang bskur rdzogs par sbyin pa rmis/ gnyid sad dus nyi ma shar 'bol
song snang / drung du phyin pas slob dpon jo btsun thugs tshim mam gsung / tshim lags zhus te/ de phyin nas chos rje sangs rgyas dngos su gzigs pa yin/ der bka' las shambha
la na las 'brel mi 'dug dngos kyi las 'brel u rgyan du 'dug der song gsung / thog mar byang mi med kyi thang la zla ba dgu bzhugs/ de nas ti se/ mar yul/ ga sha dza landhara'i
bar du byon/ de nas grogs mched lnga yod pa'i gsum snod min par mkhyen nas slog dpal yes khrid de u rgyan du byon/ lam du cho 'phrul bsam gyis mi khyab pa byung
/ khyad par chos rje'i drung du sgom ma brdungs pa rnams kyis rdo char phab/ b.ratal zhugs kyis zil gyis mnan te u rgyan mthil du brtol/ he ru ka rang byung gi pho brang
de thog mar ka ma dha ko zhes pa'i gangs ri zhig tu gzigs/ de nas dhU ma tha lar smad 'tshong ma zhig gis thug pa phor gang byin pa 'thungs pas skad cig la lus mi gcig pa
bcu bdun blangs pa'i snang ba byung / de sangs pa na sngar gyi gangs sogs thams cad dkyil 'khor gyi 'khor lo mngon sum lta bur gzigs/ khyad par bcom ldan 'das mas rdo rje
gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub stsal/ smad 'tshong ma des kyang gdams pa dang / reg pa med pa'i rdo'i 'og tu lo gcig bsgoms na rgya gar gyi grub thob brgyad cu rtsa bzhi'i gcig
dang mnyam par 'gyur zhes lung bstan/ gzhan yang rnal 'byor ma bzhi dang mjal te/ dpal yes skyel ba la bod du log 'byon dgos byung ba yin/ tshur lam kha che brgyud bla chen
de khyim gyi bla mchod du bzung / khong chos byed zer khrid byon pa

lam du rgod tshang pa gshegs pa gzigs te slar slog chos rje rang rdo rje gling du byon/ rgod tshang pa'i nang rten gdan sa la sogs pa'i bca' bkod mdzad/ 'phrin las che bas
phyis mnga' ris rgyal po 'khor bcas rab tu byung / rgya gar rdo rje gdan du byon/ rgyal po shing gtan can ra ma pA las sbyin bdag byas/ tshogs bdag dam la btags/ phyag rgya
chen po dang kun rdzob byang chub sems zung 'jug gi rtogs pas phu grol mda' grol du song / de phyin spyan zur gyis gzigs pa tsam gyis kyang nad dang gdon las grol bar
byed nus/ lha 'dre mi gsum zil gyis mnan/ mdo rgyud 'di mi mkhyen bya ba med/ khyad par rgya nag tu byon/ lam du karma pas bstan pa 'dzin rogs bcol rgya nag tu rgyal po hu
pi li se chen han gyis spyan drangs pa bzhin byon/ lo gcig la phyir log dngos po khab tsam yang ma bsnams/ dgung lo bdun cu pa la gshegs/ bsnyen sgrub stsal ba'i slob ma
rin po che mkhar chu ba/ karma pa rang byung rdo rje/ bla ma dbu ma ba/ mkhas btsun bsod nams 'od zer/ rtogs ldan zla ba sengge/ rtogs ldan g.yag mgo ba/ chos rje kun dga'
don grub/ grub thob tsha chung ba/ shong rdo rje rgyal mtshan/ shong blo brtan sogs bsam gyis mi khyab pa gsungs la ngas rdo rje gsum gyi bsnyen sgrub 'di kha bshad na
lung pa grub thob kyis 'gengs pa yin te/ 'brug pa'i zhen byas khrid chen brgyad po 'di rang bshad ces gsungs/ rtogs ldan zla seng pa ni grub chen pa'i gsung la 'dris pas
zin bris phal cher khong gis btab/ de'i slob ma mching bu'i mkhan po byang chub sengge/ de'i slob ma 'phags mchog bsod nams dpal te/ dang por chos rje gangs pa la btugs/
khrid zhabs phal cher ma tshar ba la bla ma grongs/ mkhan chen byang chub sengge la btugs chu bar du bsgoms pas rtogs pa brnyes pa yin/ de la rgod phrug grags pa 'byung
gnas/ de'i slob ma kha rag pa rgya mtsho dpal/ de'i slob ma kha rag grub chen bsod nams rgyal po/ de las rgyal dbang rjes gsan no/ /spyil dkar bas 'bri mtshams su ba ri
spyil dkar btab/ 'od gsal 'khor yug tu mnga'/ sku tshe phal sgrub pa la bskyal ba yin// ne rings pa ni/ rgod tshang pa rang gis mjal ba pha grub pa zhig po'i dbon po yin/
rgod tshang pa la gdams

pa gsan/ grub pa brnyes/ phal cher sku mtshams rang la bzhugs pas ne rings chos rje sbas pas che zer/ 'phags pa rin po che rgya 'khor nas byang lam du phebs dus bod bying bsu
ba la byon/ khong ma byon par chos rje shAkya dpal brdzangs/ shin tu grang / lhag par kha ba chen po zhig byung bas thams cad 'o brgyal/ khong dpon slob cog bu mdzad/
na bza' srab pa 'phags pas ltar gnang bas cog pu'i mtha' skor thag zhags tsam gyi kha ba zhu nas snum rug ge byung / des 'phags pa dgyes nas che bstod du gangs can shAkya'i
dpal du btags/ 'di gnas rnying pa'i zhal ngo yin/ khong gi rjes su chos rje kun dga' dpal la'ang gangs can kun dga' dpal zhes zer/ khong dang mtshan mthun pas mon rtse
ba'i slob ma kun dga' dpal la'ang gangs can kun dga' dpal zer ba byung / de dus gnas rnying stod 'brug tu yod zer/ ne rings pa rang gi dbon rgyud kyang legs par byung ba
tsa ri ti se sogs 'dzin pa la do gal che bar mdzad pa yin no/ /de lta bu'i chos rje rgod tshang pa dpon slob brgyud pa dang bcas pa la stod 'brug ces grags shing / gnam
gyi skar ma tsam zhes mang ba'i dper kun gleng ba 'di'o/ /chos rje gtsang pa rgya ras kyi sku dngos kyi gdan sa ba ni sangs rgyas dbon yin/ de ni chos rje'i gcen po lha gnyan
la sras gnyis byung ba'i che shos yin/ chung ba dbon stag go chos rje 'brug tu bzhugs pa'i dus nye gnas la de ring chos skyong 'go ba'i mi zhig 'ong gtor ma grabs gyis
gsungs/ de'i nyin byon dbu skra bcad/ mtshan dar ma sengge/ de nyid du chos skyong gi dbang gnang / gzhan gdams pa rim gyis gsan/ bsnyen sgrub mdzad/ bsnyen par rdzogs/
chos skyong dam la thogs/ sde brgyad las la bkol ba yin te/ chos rje dpon slob gzhung du byon pa'i tshe 'brug gi gnas brtan du bzhag shing gtos che ba bsags pas/ chos rje
phyir byon dus mi gcig gis bsags pa'i shing rang mang gsungs/ der lung pa'i phyugs rdzi zhig der slebs nas shing khong gcig pu min/ mi mgo sna tshogs byas pa rkyang gis
bsags so zer/ phyis 'brug tu zhing gcig slog pa'ang nye gnas la tsha ba 'phyi ba zhig gyis/ de bar ma 'ong gsung pa/ khos tshad la khyer phyin pas zhing gi steng srog chags
sna tshogs kyis gang nas phal cher slog zin 'dug de nas mi snang bas 'phro dum zhig lus/ gzhan

yang khyi nag pha jo zer ba'i mgon khyi zhig yod pa'i mgul du yi ge btags de btang bas gar brdzangs par slebs te/ tshur yig lan yang de kha la bskur bas chog de thams cad chos
skyong gi sprul pa yin/ dus rgyun du'ang gsung bcad mdzad de bsnyen sgrub rang mdzad/ de'i dbang gis nus pa rdzu 'phrul thogs med mnga'/ 'byung ba la rang dbang thob
pas zhu mkhan brag tu bla ma sgrub pa mdzad pa'i tshe brag la phyag gis 'jus pa'i rjes/ ra lung du sbyin sreg mdzad pa'i rdo la phyag rjes/ ra lung gi sgom sde la chu gnod
zhi ba'i phyir zhabs rjes/ stag ri'i dben gnas rgyun du brtan pa'i phyir dang chos rdzong sogs te zhabs rjes bdun bzhag stag rir gsang spyod la byon pa na/ bu mo rus pa'i
rgyan gyis brgyan pa gsum byung nas/ khyod rgya gar yul du 'byon tsa na/ /nged mi 'gyur bu mo spun gsum gyis/ /lam byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed pa/ /de thugs la gsal
lam lo tsA ba/ /zhes zer ba'i mod la rje mar pa 'khrungs pa'i skabs shin tu gsal por dran/ chos rje'i slob ma phyi tshar rnams kyi gdam ngag rdzogs par mdzad/ nyid kyi
slob ma 'gro sgom zhig pos lho kha bzhi dbang du bsdus/ ra lung gi phyi rten bzhengs pa'i ganydzyi ra bskyon pa la stag ri nas rdzu 'phrul gyis rkyang la chibs te byon/ der
rab tu gnas pa'i dus dkar brgyud kyi bla ma rnams dngos su byon pa gzigs/ drug cu re gcig la zhi bar gshegs so/ /gzhon nu sengge gcen lha btsan gyis sras gnyis byung ba'i
che ba yin/ chung ba rin chen dpal lo/ /dgung lo brgyad pa la chos rje'i drung du rab tu byung / rtsa gsum pa la bsnyen par rdzogs/ so gsum pa la gdan sar byon/ rje khu
dbon gnyis kyi gdam ngag bum pa gang byo yod/ rtsa rlung gi nus pa che/ 'di'i ring la lho 'brug thub/ 'brug la gling log byung / dgung lo drug cu re bdun pa la gshegs/
zhal slob kyang grub thob g.yu mo che ba la sogs thon// slob dpon rin dpal gyi sras po nyi ma sengge bcu gcig pa la chos rje gzhon nu la rab tu byung / rtogs pa mchog tu
gyur/ bcu drug pa la gdan sar phebs dgung lo so bdun pa la gshegs/ sengge shes rab dbon stag gi sras su mched gnyis 'khrungs pa'i gcen po/ dgung lo drug nas ting nge 'dzin
rang 'khrungs/ bcu gcig pa la chos rje gzhon nu la rab tu byung /

dgung lo dgu pa la la yag gangs phug tu chos rje pa la dbang bskur zhus pa'i dril bu'i sgra la brten nas rtogs pa 'khrungs/ bco brgyad pa la rtsa rlung gi khrid bskyangs pa'i
bde drod bsam gyis mi khyab/ zhabs la rma byung ba'i dus khrag med par 'o ma 'dzags/ rtsa gcig pa la grub thob u rgyan pas gsol ba btab nas rgod tshang pa'i gdan sa la
byon/ phyis 'phrin las shin tu che/ dpang lo tsA ba'i dbu skra gcod mkhan yin/ 'ga' zhig tu rdo rje gling pa/ 'ga' zhig tu rgyal sras byang gling pa zhes zer/ zhe gcig pa
la gshegs/ 'dis ra lung gi gdan sa ma mdzad/ gdam ngag rnams la sku drin che ba yin/ /sengge rin chen ni rdor gling pa'i gcung po sangs rgyas dbon gyi sprul par grags/
dgung lo bcu gcig pa la nyi ma sengge las rab tu byung / chos rje sku mched la gdam ngag rdzogs par gsan/ bcu gsum lon pa nas tshogs pa bskyangs/ 'di'i dus tsa ri rnying
ma nas 'brug pa'i las tshan bsdus/ des kong kha dwags zhabs rnams su rims nad me ltar 'bar/ yon bdag rnams gros byas/ rkyen pa rgyal po stag rdo rjes gtsos/ ri ba zhu bar
'ongs ba na/ chos rje'i bka' las ri thebs mi gtong gsungs/ rgyal po lceb par chas pa na zhal gyis bzhes te rgyal po la 'gro mgon 'doms gsungs pas/ bsod nams rgyal mtshan
gral gsham na 'dug pa yid la 'thad nas 'dams pas 'dam kha ma log gsungs/ gnas rnying mar mi gtong / nga la khye'u khrag mdog sha'i ral pa can zhig gi phul ba'i gnas/ rib

/ ne rings u ri rnams nas las 'dzin bos te ci ga car dpal gyi nags ljongs bzung ba yin/ 'dis spos skya btab/ der bzhugs pas mtshan ldan spos skya pa zhes grags so/ /lnga
cu rtsa drug pa la gshegs/ /de'i slob ma sangs rgyas dga' bde/ mtshan gzhan rtogs ldan lo ro ras par grags pa des rje ras chung pa'i gdan sa rnams bskyangs/ chos rje spos

rgyal po ste/ shangs su 'khrungs/ yab la rab tu byung / dgung lo nyer lnga pa la gdan sar bzhugs/ hor rgyal po thu'o hun the'i mur gyis bla'i mchod gnas su bzung / gtsug lag

rtse sogs gtos che/ yab sras de gnyis kyis gsung rab phal cher gos shog la gser du bzhengs/ glegs thag la sogs pa'ang si ta'u la byas so// de la slob ma mkhan po rdo
rje rin chen dang / bla chen bsam rgyal kha che ba zhes bon nus pa can chos lugs su 'gyur ba de gnyis gtso bo/ gzhan lha khab 'jig rten blos btang sogs mang ngo / /dgung
lo so bzhi la gshegs/ 'di chos rje'i sprul par grags// de'i sras blo gros sengge lhor 'khrungs/ yab gshegs pa sngas/ yab tshan ring por 'gro ba'i dbon po kun dga' sengge

ye shes

la gshegs/de'i gcung po shes rab bzang po spyan ras gzigs kyi sprul par grags/2nd 'Brug chen rGyal ba'i dbang po Kun dga' dpal 'byor'di'i sras dpal rgyal ba'i dbang po yin/

/ zhal chems la nged kyi 'dad kyi gral dbu rin po che 'brug pa la zhus/ rngog rin po che bdun brgyud

skad gnyis shan sbyar gyi bshad pa zhib

la thob kyi/ gzhan mched pa ni mi snang ngo / /yul pha yul dang 'brel ba'i gzhis dgon de/ /sems chos brgyad kyi khol po byed byed nas/ /don chung la tshe zhabs 'dzad pa'i
rgyu/ /gsung / gdan sa'i 'dzin skyong bor/ phyogs bral gyi bstan pa skyong bzhed/ khor yug cog bu pa'i srol gtod/ gtsang chen chos kyi dbang phyug gis gdan drangs/ tsa

btsun kun dga' bzang mo/ chos rje

'chi med grub pa sogs la zla ba gsum du khrid chen brgyad gnang / khyad chos su byung bas zin bris btab/ tsa ri la jo bzang rdor 'dzin la sogs pa'i gnang bkod mdzad/ sgam pordbon
rin po che bskos/ bya yul du sprul sku 'byung bar lung bstan/ ra lung du byon/ dgung lo zhe dgu pa la gshegs so/mKhan po bSam gtan/de la slob ma mkhan po bsam gtan
pa dang / thel mkhan chen dpal ldan rgyal mtshan nam/ lhun sde rab 'byams par grags pa gnyis la mkhan po rnam gnyis/ dge slong rin rnam pa dang bsod mchog pa gnyis la dge
slong rnam gnyis/ bla ma kun dga' bsam gtan pa dang rin chen dbang po gnyis la bla ma rnam gnyis/ lha btsun kun dga' chos rgyam dang sna phu rtogs ldan gnyis la rtogs ldan
rnam gnyis/ shar kha ras pa dang / gangs khrod ras pa gnyis la ras pa rnam pa gnyis/ sngags 'chang rgyal mtshan lhun grub la mthu bo che mi gcig zer/ gzhan 'bri gung
dbon rin po che/ 'ba' ra ba'i dbon po mnyam med nam mkha' rin chen/ gtsang smyon/ zhal snga 'phags pa lha sogs mtha' yas/ lha btsun kun dga' chos rgyal las sgrub grwa du
ma mched/ gzhan bsam gyis mi khyab bo/rJe 'Brug pa chen po Ngag dbang chos rgyal/de'i rigs kyi dbon chos kyi sras su gyur ba ni rje 'brug pa chen po ste/ yab rgyal dbang

bsur byon/ lho gro bo lung du rab tu byung / mtshan ngag dbang chos kyi rgyal po gsol/ de nyin nas brtsams te lo gcig gis ring la 'brug rngog gi dbang rgyud man ngag rdzogs
par mdzad/ ra lung du phebs nas mdo sde'i lung gsan/ rje gshegs nas grub chen shAkya 'phel pa la 'brug skor gyi lhag ma lag len la dogs gcod zhib mo mdzad/ bcu bzhi
la gdan sar bton/ mchod rten chen mo'i rab gnas kyi skabs sangs rgyas dbon gyis ma 'ongs pa'i dus 'di la zhig gsos dgos pa yong / de dus kho bo rang slebs nas byed gsungs
pas/ mchod rten phyed zhig pa zhig gsos mdzad pas dbon ras kyi sprul pa'i skur shes/ gzhan stag lung ngag dbang grags pa/ sku zhang chos rje mkhyen rab mchog grub/ chos
rje lhun bde ba sogs bla ma mang du bsten/ bde mchog la sogs pa'i rgyud man ngag mang du gsan/ ra lung kha ro

la sogs su lo dgu tsam bsgrub pa mdzad/ ngo mtshar ba zhal du mi gleng sbed/ phyag rgya chen po'i rtogs pa shar/ 'phrin las mkha' 'gro chos skyong gis sgrub/ ting nge 'dzin

pa/ tshogs chen mkhan po nam mkha' bkra shis dang / dge 'dun sgang mkhan po rin chen bkra shis pa sogs bstan 'dzin sbyin bdag che dgus btud pa/ thog de la dbus gtsang du
che bar grags so/ /ting ting rdor 'dzin pa sogs zhabs tog can/ thal ru rtogs ldan sogs grub thob tu grags pa/ rdo rje 'dzin pa chos kyi mgon po sogs mthu stobs can/ gzhan

bka' lung legs par stsal te/ dgung lo so brgyad la zhi bar gshegs/ /'jam pa'i dbyangs chos kyi grags pa ni/ yul lho rgyud/ yab gong ma bkra shis dar rgyas bya ba bod yul
lho rgyud 'bangs mi khyim khri phrag gsum tsam la dbang sgyur ba de dang / yum thams cad mkhyen pa rdo rje gdan pa kun dga' rnam rgyal gyi lcam dkar mo gnyis kyi sras su
'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu gcig la rgyal dbang rje'i grwa rigs 'dzom pa rgyun du chos rgyal lhun po zhes pa'i pho brang du dge 'dun brgyad brgya tsam gyis lo gcig gi bar du rab
tu byung bar gsol ba 'debs pa la bsdad/ de nas 'brug pa rin po che phebs/ gdams

pa legs par gsan zhing / slob dpon dus zhabs shAkya dbang phyug tu byas pa snye mo ru pa'i dge bshes sbyangs pa can zhig la rgyud dang tha snyad la gsan pa mdzad/ gzhan dge
slong rin chen rnam rgyal pa la rgyal dbang rje nas brgyud sgrub bka'/ grub chen shAkya 'phel ba'i slob ma 'gro mgon chos skyabs pa las khrid dpe logs su ma lus pa'i phyag
bzhes su lon pa dang / gzhan yang zhwa dmar nag sogs bla ma du ma la gsar rnying bka' gsum gyi gdam ngag ci'ang gsan/ ting nge 'dzin la rtsal 'byongs pas zhabs rjes phyag
rjes/ bar snang la skyil krung 'cha'/ rdo rje dril bu bar snang la bzhag khro bo rdo rje shugs dngos su phebs/ lhag par ras chung zhabs kun gyis mthong bar zla ba gsum
bya bral gyi zol gyis gdams pa gnang bar byon/ phyis yi ger btab pa bde mchog mai tri lugs kyi snyan rgyud yin/ su kha sidhis lung bstan bkra shis mthong smon btab pa sogs
ngo mtshar bsam gyis mi khyab pa bstan te zhe lnga pa la mya ngan las 'das so/ /de'i slob ma la cig car rdor 'dzin bstan pa rgya mtsho/ bshad pa'i bka' 'dzin rdo rje
gling pa yon tan ye shes rdo rje 'chang mngon sum pa de yin/ sgrub bka' 'dzin pa la su kha siddhis/ mi tra lo yi sprul pa yis/ /khyod kyi sgrub brgyud rgyas par byed/ /ces
lung bstan pa'i rje btsun mi tra dzo ki'i sprul pa ni bdag cag la bka' drin chen po sbyin pa po kun spangs rin po che'am/ mtshan gzhan sgyu ma'i gar mkhan du grags pa de
yin/ lo'i sprul pa ni/ dmar DA ki ras chen du grags pa khong yin par bka' stsal/ sku dngos kyi gdan sa gcung paNDYi ta bkra shis rnam rgyal lnga rig pa de'o/ /sras gnyis/
gzhan rje de la thug tsam yang gdam ngag gi gnad zin pas phyis gzhan gyi 'dren pa byed pa 'ba' zhig byung bas 'phrin las shin tu che/ de ltar dbon ras nas 'di'i bar du
byon pa rjes 'brang dang bcas pa la gdan sa brgyud ces bya ste/ sgra bsgyur mar mi ras chung nas brgyud pa'i gdams pa kho na nyams su len cing lag len gyi 'phrang la brdar
bas/ don brgyud gdams pa'i mnga' bdag 'brug pa zhes bstod ra bgyis so// // ! 'dir 'bad dge ba'i sprin dkar ni/ /srid pa'i mtha' mnyam 'phel 'gyur bas/ /thar pa'i shul
ring bgrod rnams la/ /gdung sel mchog tu gyur cig gu /de ltar bstan pa spyi'i chos 'byung bstan pa'i padmo rgyas pa'i nyin byed ces

bya ba/ gong dkar nas sde srid rin po che ma'i bkas rtsom dgos zhes bskul ba ltar/ phal cher gtam phyogs lhung gi rjes su 'brang bas zer tshad 'chad dka' la/ gzu bor gnas pa
dag gis rnal mar brjod pa rnams phyogs gcig tu bya ba'i bar seng la bris pa las rdzogs pa lo ro'i rong / dron dbang sgyur du grub pa 'dis thams cad du bstan pa dang bstan
'dzin gyi skyes bu byon te/ srid zhu gong nas gong du 'phel bar gyur cig/ //sarba manggalaM// //rab dkar don brgyud gzhung lugs gangs ri'i spor/ /kun mkhyen bla ma mi
yi sengge de'i/ /mtshungs bral theg mchog lta ba'i nga ro'i dbyangs/ /bka' 'bum khrigs su sdeb pa'i mu tig phreng / 1 /'ga' zhig bzhan dbang kha thor gyur pa'i rigs/ /lhag
bsam 'bum ldan mdzod khri thabs mkhas mchog /bstan don gser gyi gnya' shing phrag par brgyan/ /'dzad med par gzhi'i 'khrul 'khor 'di bsgrubs dges/ 2 /pha ma 'brel thogs
mkha' mnyam 'gro kun dang / /khyad par sku gshegs dpal ldan de nyid kyi/ /tshe rabs nyes pa'i phung po yongs gzhil te/ /sku bzhi'i dbang phyug da lar 'du bar smon/ /ces
mi rje mchog nas bkas bskul ba ltar/ ngag gi dbang po bde ba'i rdo rjes so// //
